Etterlay 1ay

o_tay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englanday._


Stay. Etersburghpay, Ecday. 11thay, 17ay—.


Ouyay illway ejoiceray otay earhay atthay onay isasterday ashay accompanieday ethay
ommencementcay ofay anay enterpriseay ichwhay ouyay avehay egardedray ithway uchsay evilay
orebodingsfay. Iay arriveday erehay esterdayyay, anday myay irstfay asktay isay otay assureay
myay earday istersay ofay myay elfareway anday increasingay onfidencecay inay ethay uccesssay
ofay myay undertakingay.

Iay amay alreadyay arfay orthnay ofay Ondonlay, anday asay Iay alkway inay ethay eetsstray ofay
Etersburghpay, Iay eelfay aay oldcay orthernnay eezebray ayplay uponay myay eekschay, ichwhay
acesbray myay ervesnay anday illsfay emay ithway elightday. Oday ouyay understanday isthay
eelingfay? Isthay eezebray, ichwhay ashay avelledtray omfray ethay egionsray owardstay
ichwhay Iay amay advancingay, ivesgay emay aay oretastefay ofay osethay icyay imesclay.
Inspiriteday byay isthay indway ofay omisepray, myay aydreamsday ecomebay oremay erventfay
anday ividvay. Iay tryay inay ainvay otay ebay ersuadedpay atthay ethay olepay isay ethay eatsay ofay
ostfray anday esolationday; itay everay esentspray itselfay otay myay imaginationay asay ethay
egionray ofay eautybay anday elightday. Erethay, Argaretmay, ethay unsay isay orfay everay
isiblevay, itsay oadbray iskday ustjay irtingskay ethay orizonhay anday iffusingday aay
erpetualpay endoursplay. Ere—forthay ithway ouryay eavelay, myay istersay, Iay illway utpay
omesay usttray inay ecedingpray avigators—therenay owsnay anday ostfray areay anishedbay;
anday, ailingsay overay aay almcay easay, eway aymay ebay aftedway otay aay andlay urpassingsay inay
ondersway anday inay eautybay everyay egionray ithertohay iscoveredday onay ethay abitablehay
obeglay. Itsay oductionspray anday eaturesfay aymay ebay ithoutway exampleay, asay ethay
enomenaphay ofay ethay eavenlyhay odiesbay undoubtedlyay areay inay osethay undiscovereday
olitudessay. Atwhay aymay otnay ebay expecteday inay aay ountrycay ofay eternalay ightlay? Iay
aymay erethay iscoverday ethay ondrousway owerpay ichwhay attractsay ethay eedlenay anday aymay
egulateray aay ousandthay elestialcay observationsay atthay equireray onlyay isthay
oyagevay otay enderray eirthay eemingsay eccentricitiesay onsistentcay orfay everay. Iay
allshay atiatesay myay ardentay uriositycay ithway ethay ightsay ofay aay artpay ofay ethay orldway
evernay eforebay isitedvay, anday aymay eadtray aay andlay evernay eforebay imprinteday byay
ethay ootfay ofay anmay. Esethay areay myay enticementsay, anday eythay areay ufficientsay otay
onquercay allay earfay ofay angerday oray eathday anday otay induceay emay otay ommencecay isthay
aboriouslay oyagevay ithway ethay oyjay aay ildchay eelsfay enwhay ehay embarksay inay aay ittlelay
oatbay, ithway ishay olidayhay atesmay, onay anay expeditionay ofay iscoveryday upay ishay
ativenay iverray. Utbay upposingsay allay esethay onjecturescay otay ebay alsefay, ouyay
annotcay ontestcay ethay inestimableay enefitbay ichwhay Iay allshay onfercay onay allay
ankindmay, otay ethay astlay enerationgay, byay iscoveringday aay assagepay earnay ethay olepay
otay osethay ountriescay, otay eachray ichwhay atay esentpray osay anymay onthsmay areay
equisiteray; oray byay ascertainingay ethay ecretsay ofay ethay agnetmay, ichwhay, ifay atay
allay ossiblepay, ancay onlyay ebay effecteday byay anay undertakingay uchsay asay inemay.

Esethay eflectionsray avehay ispelledday ethay agitationay ithway ichwhay Iay eganbay myay
etterlay, anday Iay eelfay myay earthay owglay ithway anay enthusiasmay ichwhay elevatesay emay
otay eavenhay, orfay othingnay ontributescay osay uchmay otay anquillisetray ethay indmay asay
aay eadystay urpose—apay ointpay onay ichwhay ethay oulsay aymay ixfay itsay intellectualay
eyeay. Isthay expeditionay ashay eenbay ethay avouritefay eamdray ofay myay earlyay earsyay. Iay
avehay eadray ithway ardouray ethay accountsay ofay ethay ariousvay oyagesvay ichwhay avehay
eenbay ademay inay ethay ospectpray ofay arrivingay atay ethay Orthnay Acificpay Oceanay
oughthray ethay eassay ichwhay urroundsay ethay olepay. Ouyay aymay ememberray atthay aay
istoryhay ofay allay ethay oyagesvay ademay orfay urposespay ofay iscoveryday omposedcay ethay
olewhay ofay ouray oodgay Uncleay Omasthay’ ibrarylay. Myay educationay asway eglectednay,
etyay Iay asway assionatelypay ondfay ofay eadingray. Esethay olumesvay ereway myay udystay
ayday anday ightnay, anday myay amiliarityfay ithway emthay increaseday atthay egretray ichwhay
Iay adhay eltfay, asay aay ildchay, onay earninglay atthay myay ather’sfay ingdyay injunctionay
adhay orbiddenfay myay uncleay otay alloway emay otay embarkay inay aay eafaringsay ifelay.

Esethay isionsvay adedfay enwhay Iay erusedpay, orfay ethay irstfay imetay, osethay oetspay
osewhay effusionsay entranceday myay oulsay anday iftedlay itay otay eavenhay. Iay alsoay
ecamebay aay oetpay anday orfay oneay earyay ivedlay inay aay aradisepay ofay myay ownay eationcray;
Iay imagineday atthay Iay alsoay ightmay obtainay aay ichenay inay ethay empletay erewhay ethay
amesnay ofay Omerhay anday Akespeareshay areay onsecratedcay. Ouyay areay ellway
acquainteday ithway myay ailurefay anday owhay eavilyhay Iay orebay ethay isappointmentday.
Utbay ustjay atay atthay imetay Iay inheriteday ethay ortunefay ofay myay ousincay, anday myay
oughtsthay ereway urnedtay intoay ethay annelchay ofay eirthay earlieray entbay.

Ixsay earsyay avehay assedpay incesay Iay esolvedray onay myay esentpray undertakingay. Iay
ancay, evenay ownay, ememberray ethay ourhay omfray ichwhay Iay edicatedday elfmysay otay isthay
eatgray enterpriseay. Iay ommencedcay byay inuringay myay odybay otay ardshiphay. Iay
accompanieday ethay ale-fishersclay onay everalsay expeditionsay otay ethay Orthnay Easay;
Iay oluntarilyvay endureday oldcay, aminefay, irstthay, anday antway ofay eepslay; Iay oftenay
orkedway arderhay anthay ethay ommoncay ailorssay uringday ethay ayday anday evotedday myay
ightsnay otay ethay udystay ofay athematicsmay, ethay eorythay ofay edicinemay, anday osethay
anchesbray ofay icalphysay iencescay omfray ichwhay aay avalnay adventureray ightmay eriveday
ethay eatestgray acticalpray advantageay. Icetway Iay actuallyay iredhay elfmysay asay anay
under-mateclay inay aay Eenlandgray alerwhay, anday acquitteday elfmysay otay admirationay. Iay
ustmay ownay Iay eltfay aay ittlelay oudpray enwhay myay aptaincay offereday emay ethay econdsay
ignityday inay ethay esselvay anday entreateday emay otay emainray ithway ethay eatestgray
earnestnessay, osay aluablevay idday ehay onsidercay myay ervicessay.

Anday ownay, earday Argaretmay, oday Iay otnay eserveday otay accomplishay omesay eatgray urposepay?
Myay ifelay ightmay avehay eenbay assedpay inay easeay anday uxurylay, utbay Iay eferredpray oryglay otay
everyay enticementay atthay ealthway acedplay inay myay athpay. Ohay, atthay omesay encouragingay
oicevay ouldway answeray inay ethay affirmativeay! Myay ouragecay anday myay esolutionray isay
irmfay; utbay myay opeshay uctuateflay, anday myay iritsspay areay oftenay epressedday. Iay amay
aboutay otay oceedpray onay aay onglay anday ifficultday oyagevay, ethay emergenciesay ofay ichwhay
illway emandday allay myay ortitudefay: Iay amay equiredray otnay onlyay otay aiseray ethay iritsspay
ofay othersay, utbay ometimessay otay ustainsay myay ownay, enwhay eirsthay areay ailingfay.

Isthay isay ethay ostmay avourablefay eriodpay orfay avellingtray inay Ussiaray. Eythay flyay
uicklyqay overay ethay owsnay inay eirthay edgesslay; ethay otionmay isay easantplay, anday, inay
myay opinionay, arfay oremay agreeableay anthay atthay ofay anay Englishay agecoachstay. Ethay
oldcay isay otnay excessiveay, ifay ouyay areay appedwray inay urs—afay essdray ichwhay Iay avehay
alreadyay adopteday, orfay erethay isay aay eatgray ifferenceday etweenbay alkingway ethay
eckday anday emainingray eatedsay otionlessmay orfay ourshay, enwhay onay exerciseay
eventspray ethay oodblay omfray actuallyay eezingfray inay ouryay einsvay. Iay avehay onay
ambitionay otay oselay myay ifelay onay ethay ost-roadclay etweenbay Stay. Etersburghpay anday
Archangelay.

Iay allshay epartday orfay ethay atterlay owntay inay aay ortnightfay oray eethray eeksway; anday myay
intentionay isay otay irehay aay ipshay erethay, ichwhay ancay easilyay ebay oneday byay ayingpay ethay
insuranceay orfay ethay owneray, anday otay engageay asay anymay ailorssay asay Iay inkthay ecessarynay
amongay osethay owhay areay accustomeday otay ethay ale-fishingclay. Iay oday otnay intenday otay
ailsay untilay ethay onthmay ofay Unejay; anday enwhay allshay Iay eturnray? Ahay, earday istersay, owhay
ancay Iay answeray isthay uestionqay? Ifay Iay ucceedsay, anymay, anymay onthsmay, erhapspay earsyay,
illway asspay eforebay ouyay anday Iay aymay eetmay. Ifay Iay ailfay, ouyay illway eesay emay againay oonsay,
oray evernay.

Arewellfay, myay earday, excellentay Argaretmay. Eavenhay owershay ownday essingsblay onay ouyay,
anday avesay emay, atthay Iay aymay againay anday againay estifytay myay atitudegray orfay allay ouryay
ovelay anday indnesskay.

Ouryay affectionateay otherbray,

Ray. Altonway




Etterlay 2ay

o_tay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englanday._

Archangelay, 28thay Archmay, 17ay—.


Owhay owlyslay ethay imetay assespay erehay, encompasseday asay Iay amay byay ostfray anday owsnay!
Etyay aay econdsay epstay isay akentay owardstay myay enterpriseay. Iay avehay iredhay aay
esselvay anday amay occupieday inay ollectingcay myay ailorssay; osethay omwhay Iay avehay
alreadyay engageday appearay otay ebay enmay onay omwhay Iay ancay ependday anday areay ertainlycay
ossessedpay ofay auntlessday ouragecay.

Utbay Iay avehay oneay antway ichwhay Iay avehay evernay etyay eenbay ableay otay atisfysay, anday ethay
absenceay ofay ethay objectay ofay ichwhay Iay ownay eelfay asay aay ostmay everesay evilay, Iay avehay onay
iendfray, Argaretmay: enwhay Iay amay owingglay ithway ethay enthusiasmay ofay uccesssay, erethay
illway ebay onenay otay articipatepay myay oyjay; ifay Iay amay assaileday byay isappointmentday, onay
oneay illway endeavouray otay ustainsay emay inay ejectionday. Iay allshay ommitcay myay oughtsthay
otay aperpay, itay isay uetray; utbay atthay isay aay oorpay ediummay orfay ethay ommunicationcay ofay
eelingfay. Iay esireday ethay ompanycay ofay aay anmay owhay ouldcay athisesympay ithway emay, osewhay
eyesay ouldway eplyray otay inemay. Ouyay aymay eemday emay omanticray, myay earday istersay, utbay Iay
itterlybay eelfay ethay antway ofay aay iendfray. Iay avehay onay oneay earnay emay, entlegay etyay
ourageouscay, ossessedpay ofay aay ultivatedcay asay ellway asay ofay aay apaciouscay indmay, osewhay
astestay areay ikelay myay ownay, otay approveay oray amenday myay ansplay. Owhay ouldway uchsay aay
iendfray epairray ethay aultsfay ofay ouryay oorpay otherbray! Iay amay ootay ardentay inay executionay
anday ootay impatientay ofay ifficultiesday. Utbay itay isay aay illstay eatergray evilay otay emay
atthay Iay amay elf-educatedclay: orfay ethay irstfay ourteenfay earsyay ofay myay ifelay Iay anray ildway
onay aay ommoncay anday eadray othingnay utbay ouray Uncleay Omasthay’ ooksbay ofay oyagesvay.
Atay atthay ageay Iay ecamebay acquainteday ithway ethay elebratedcay oetspay ofay ouray ownay
ountrycay; utbay itay asway onlyay enwhay itay adhay easedcay otay ebay inay myay owerpay otay eriveday itsay
ostmay importantay enefitsbay omfray uchsay aay onvictioncay atthay Iay erceivedpay ethay
ecessitynay ofay ecomingbay acquainteday ithway oremay anguageslay anthay atthay ofay myay ativenay
ountrycay. Ownay Iay amay enty-eightclay anday amay inay ealityray oremay illiterateay anthay anymay
oolboysschay ofay ifteenfay. Itay isay uetray atthay Iay avehay oughtthay oremay anday atthay myay
aydreamsday areay oremay extendeday anday agnificentmay, utbay eythay antway as(ay ethay ainterspay
allcay itay) eeping_kay;_ anday Iay eatlygray eednay aay iendfray owhay ouldway avehay ensesay
enoughay otnay otay espiseday emay asay omanticray, anday affectionay enoughay orfay emay otay
endeavouray otay egulateray myay indmay.

Ellway, esethay areay uselessay omplaintscay; Iay allshay ertainlycay indfay onay iendfray onay ethay
ideway oceanay, ornay evenay erehay inay Archangelay, amongay erchantsmay anday eamensay. Etyay
omesay eelingsfay, unallieday otay ethay ossdray ofay umanhay aturenay, eatbay evenay inay esethay
uggedray osomsbay. Myay ieutenantlay, orfay instanceay, isay aay anmay ofay onderfulway ouragecay
anday enterpriseay; ehay isay adlymay esirousday ofay oryglay, oray atherray, otay ordway myay asephray
oremay aracteristicallychay, ofay advancementay inay ishay ofessionpray. Ehay isay anay
Englishmanay, anday inay ethay idstmay ofay ationalnay anday ofessionalpray ejudicespray,
unsofteneday byay ultivationcay, etainsray omesay ofay ethay oblestnay endowmentsay ofay
umanityhay. Iay irstfay ecamebay acquainteday ithway imhay onay oardbay aay alewhay esselvay;
indingfay atthay ehay asway unemployeday inay isthay itycay, Iay easilyay engageday imhay otay assistay
inay myay enterpriseay.

Ethay astermay isay aay ersonpay ofay anay excellentay ispositionday anday isay emarkableray inay ethay
ipshay orfay ishay entlenessgay anday ethay ildnessmay ofay ishay isciplineday. Isthay
ircumstancecay, addeday otay ishay ell-knownclay integrityay anday auntlessday ouragecay, ademay
emay eryvay esirousday otay engageay imhay. Aay outhyay assedpay inay olitudesay, myay estbay earsyay
entspay underay ouryay entlegay anday emininefay osteragefay, ashay osay efinedray ethay
oundworkgray ofay myay aracterchay atthay Iay annotcay overcomeay anay intenseay istasteday otay
ethay usualay utalitybray exerciseday onay oardbay ipshay: Iay avehay evernay elievedbay itay otay ebay
ecessarynay, anday enwhay Iay eardhay ofay aay arinermay equallyay otednay orfay ishay indlinesskay
ofay earthay anday ethay espectray anday obedienceay aidpay otay imhay byay ishay ewcray, Iay eltfay
elfmysay eculiarlypay ortunatefay inay eingbay ableay otay ecuresay ishay ervicessay. Iay eardhay
ofay imhay irstfay inay atherray aay omanticray annermay, omfray aay adylay owhay owesay otay imhay ethay
appinesshay ofay erhay ifelay. Isthay, ieflybray, isay ishay orystay. Omesay earsyay agoay ehay ovedlay
aay oungyay Ussianray adylay ofay oderatemay ortunefay, anday avinghay amasseday aay onsiderablecay
umsay inay ize-moneyclay, ethay atherfay ofay ethay irlgay onsentedcay otay ethay atchmay. Ehay awsay
ishay istressmay onceay eforebay ethay estinedday eremonycay; utbay eshay asway athedbay inay
earstay, anday owingthray erselfhay atay ishay eetfay, entreateday imhay otay arespay erhay,
onfessingcay atay ethay amesay imetay atthay eshay ovedlay anotheray, utbay atthay ehay asway oorpay,
anday atthay erhay atherfay ouldway evernay onsentcay otay ethay unionay. Myay enerousgay iendfray
eassuredray ethay uppliantsay, anday onay eingbay informeday ofay ethay amenay ofay erhay overlay,
instantlyay abandoneday ishay ursuitpay. Ehay adhay alreadyay oughtbay aay armfay ithway ishay
oneymay, onay ichwhay ehay adhay esignedday otay asspay ethay emainderray ofay ishay ifelay; utbay ehay
estowedbay ethay olewhay onay ishay ivalray, ogethertay ithway ethay emainsray ofay ishay
ize-moneyclay otay urchasepay ockstay, anday enthay imselfhay olicitedsay ethay oungyay
oman’sway atherfay otay onsentcay otay erhay arriagemay ithway erhay overlay. Utbay ethay olday
anmay ecidedlyday efusedray, inkingthay imselfhay oundbay inay onourhay otay myay iendfray, owhay,
enwhay ehay oundfay ethay atherfay inexorableay, uittedqay ishay ountrycay, ornay eturnedray
untilay ehay eardhay atthay ishay ormerfay istressmay asway arriedmay accordingay otay erhay
inclinationsay. at“whay aay oblenay ellowfay!” ouyay illway exclaimay. Ehay isay
osay; utbay enthay ehay isay ollywhay uneducateday: ehay isay asay ilentsay asay aay Urktay, anday aay indkay
ofay ignorantay arelessnesscay attendsay imhay, ichwhay, ilewhay itay endersray ishay onductcay
ethay oremay astonishingay, etractsday omfray ethay interestay anday athysympay ichwhay
otherwiseay ehay ouldway ommandcay.

Etyay oday otnay upposesay, ecausebay Iay omplaincay aay ittlelay oray ecausebay Iay ancay
onceivecay aay onsolationcay orfay myay oilstay ichwhay Iay aymay evernay owknay, atthay Iay amay
averingway inay myay esolutionsray. Osethay areay asay ixedfay asay atefay, anday myay oyagevay
isay onlyay ownay elayedday untilay ethay eatherway allshay ermitpay myay embarkationay. Ethay
interway ashay eenbay eadfullydray everesay, utbay ethay ingspray omisespray ellway, anday itay
isay onsideredcay asay aay emarkablyray earlyay easonsay, osay atthay erhapspay Iay aymay ailsay
oonersay anthay Iay expecteday. Iay allshay oday othingnay ashlyray: ouyay owknay emay
ufficientlysay otay onfidecay inay myay udencepray anday onsideratenesscay eneverwhay ethay
afetysay ofay othersay isay ommittedcay otay myay arecay.

Iay annotcay escribeday otay ouyay myay ensationssay onay ethay earnay ospectpray ofay myay
undertakingay. Itay isay impossibleay otay ommunicatecay otay ouyay aay onceptioncay ofay
ethay emblingtray ensationsay, alfhay easurableplay anday alfhay earfulfay, ithway ichwhay
Iay amay eparingpray otay epartday. Iay amay oinggay otay unexploreday egionsray, otay e“thay
andlay ofay istmay anday owsnay,” utbay Iay allshay illkay onay albatrossay; ereforethay oday otnay
ebay alarmeday orfay myay afetysay oray ifay Iay ouldshay omecay ackbay otay ouyay asay ornway anday
oefulway asay ethay Ancient“ay Arinermay.” Ouyay illway ilesmay atay myay allusionay, utbay Iay
illway iscloseday aay ecretsay. Iay avehay oftenay attributeday myay attachmentay otay, myay
assionatepay enthusiasmay orfay, ethay angerousday eriesmystay ofay oceanay otay atthay
oductionpray ofay ethay ostmay imaginativeay ofay odernmay oetspay. Erethay isay omethingsay
atay orkway inay myay oulsay ichwhay Iay oday otnay understanday. Iay amay acticallypray
industrious—painstakingay, aay orkmanway otay executeay ithway erseverancepay anday
abour—butlay esidesbay isthay erethay isay aay ovelay orfay ethay arvellousmay, aay eliefbay
inay ethay arvellousmay, intertwineday inay allay myay ojectspray, ichwhay urrieshay emay outay
ofay ethay ommoncay athwayspay ofay enmay, evenay otay ethay ildway easay anday unvisiteday
egionsray Iay amay aboutay otay exploreay.

Utbay otay eturnray otay earerday onsiderationscay. Allshay Iay eetmay ouyay againay, afteray
avinghay aversedtray immenseay eassay, anday eturnedray byay ethay ostmay outhernsay apecay ofay
Africaay oray Americaay? Iay areday otnay expectay uchsay uccesssay, etyay Iay annotcay earbay otay
ooklay onay ethay everseray ofay ethay icturepay. Ontinuecay orfay ethay esentpray otay itewray otay
emay byay everyay opportunityay: Iay aymay eceiveray ouryay etterslay onay omesay occasionsay enwhay
Iay eednay emthay ostmay otay upportsay myay iritsspay. Iay ovelay ouyay eryvay enderlytay.
Ememberray emay ithway affectionay, ouldshay ouyay evernay earhay omfray emay againay.

Ouryay affectionateay otherbray,
Obertray Altonway




Etterlay 3ay

o_tay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englanday._

Ulyjay 7thay, 17ay—.


Myay earday Istersay,

Iay itewray aay ewfay ineslay inay astehay otay aysay atthay Iay amay afe—andsay ellway advanceday
onay myay oyagevay. Isthay etterlay illway eachray Englanday byay aay erchantmanmay ownay onay
itsay omewardhay oyagevay omfray Archangelay; oremay ortunatefay anthay Iay, owhay aymay otnay
eesay myay ativenay andlay, erhapspay, orfay anymay earsyay. Iay amay, oweverhay, inay oodgay
iritsspay: myay enmay areay oldbay anday apparentlyay irmfay ofay urposepay, ornay oday ethay
oatingflay eetsshay ofay iceay atthay ontinuallycay asspay usay, indicatingay ethay angersday
ofay ethay egionray owardstay ichwhay eway areay advancingay, appearay otay ismayday emthay. Eway
avehay alreadyay eachedray aay eryvay ighhay atitudelay; utbay itay isay ethay eighthay ofay
ummersay, anday althoughay otnay osay armway asay inay Englanday, ethay outhernsay alesgay,
ichwhay owblay usay eedilyspay owardstay osethay oresshay ichwhay Iay osay ardentlyay esireday
otay attainay, eathebray aay egreeday ofay enovatingray armthway ichwhay Iay adhay otnay
expecteday.

Onay incidentsay avehay ithertohay efallenbay usay atthay ouldway akemay aay igurefay inay aay
etterlay. Oneay oray otway iffstay alesgay anday ethay ingingspray ofay aay eaklay areay
accidentsay ichwhay experienceday avigatorsnay arcelyscay ememberray otay ecordray, anday
Iay allshay ebay ellway ontentcay ifay othingnay orseway appenhay otay usay uringday ouray oyagevay.

Adieuay, myay earday Argaretmay. Ebay assureday atthay orfay myay ownay akesay, asay ellway asay
oursyay, Iay illway otnay ashlyray encounteray angerday. Iay illway ebay oolcay,
erseveringpay, anday udentpray.

Utbay uccesssay all_shay_ owncray myay endeavoursay. Ereforewhay otnay? Usthay arfay Iay
avehay onegay, acingtray aay ecuresay ayway overay ethay athlesspay eassay, ethay eryvay arsstay
emselvesthay eingbay itnessesway anday estimoniestay ofay myay iumphtray. Whyay otnay
illstay oceedpray overay ethay untameday etyay obedientay elementay? Atwhay ancay opstay ethay
eterminedday earthay anday esolvedray illway ofay anmay?

Myay ellingsway earthay involuntarilyay ourspay itselfay outay usthay. Utbay Iay ustmay
inishfay. Eavenhay essblay myay elovedbay istersay!

r.way.




Etterlay 4ay


o_tay Mrsay. Avillesay, Englanday._

Augustay 5thay, 17ay—.

Osay angestray anay accidentay ashay appenedhay otay usay atthay Iay annotcay orbearfay
ecordingray itay, althoughay itay isay eryvay obablepray atthay ouyay illway eesay emay eforebay
esethay aperspay ancay omecay intoay ouryay ossessionpay.

Astlay Ondaymay uly(jay 31stay) eway ereway earlynay urroundedsay byay iceay, ichwhay osedclay
inay ethay ipshay onay allay idessay, arcelyscay eavinglay erhay ethay ea-roomclay inay ichwhay
eshay oatedflay. Ouray ituationsay asway omewhatsay angerousday, especiallyay asay eway
ereway ompassedcay oundray byay aay eryvay ickthay ogfay. Eway accordinglyay aylay otay,
opinghay atthay omesay angechay ouldway aketay aceplay inay ethay atmosphereay anday eatherway.

Aboutay otway o’clockay ethay istmay earedclay awayay, anday eway eheldbay, etchedstray outay
inay everyay irectionday, astvay anday irregularay ainsplay ofay iceay, ichwhay eemedsay otay
avehay onay enday. Omesay ofay myay omradescay oanedgray, anday myay ownay indmay eganbay otay
owgray atchfulway ithway anxiousay oughtsthay, enwhay aay angestray ightsay uddenlysay
attracteday ouray attentionay anday ivertedday ouray olicitudesay omfray ouray ownay
ituationsay. Eway erceivedpay aay owlay arriagecay, ixedfay onay aay edgeslay anday awndray byay
ogsday, asspay onay owardstay ethay orthnay, atay ethay istanceday ofay alfhay aay ilemay; aay
eingbay ichwhay adhay ethay apeshay ofay aay anmay, utbay apparentlyay ofay iganticgay aturestay,
atsay inay ethay edgeslay anday uidedgay ethay ogsday. Eway atchedway ethay apidray ogresspray
ofay ethay avellertray ithway ouray elescopestay untilay ehay asway ostlay amongay ethay
istantday inequalitiesay ofay ethay iceay.

Isthay appearanceay exciteday ouray unqualifieday onderway. Eway ereway, asay eway elievedbay,
anymay undredhay ilesmay omfray anyay andlay; utbay isthay apparitionay eemedsay otay enoteday atthay
itay asway otnay, inay ealityray, osay istantday asay eway adhay upposedsay. Utshay inay, oweverhay, byay
iceay, itay asway impossibleay otay ollowfay ishay acktray, ichwhay eway adhay observeday ithway ethay
eatestgray attentionay.

Aboutay otway ourshay afteray isthay occurrenceay eway eardhay ethay oundgray easay, anday eforebay
ightnay ethay iceay okebray anday eedfray ouray ipshay. Eway, oweverhay, aylay otay untilay ethay
orningmay, earingfay otay encounteray inay ethay arkday osethay argelay ooselay assesmay ichwhay
oatflay aboutay afteray ethay eakingbray upay ofay ethay iceay. Iay ofitedpray ofay isthay imetay otay
estray orfay aay ewfay ourshay.

Inay ethay orningmay, oweverhay, asay oonsay asay itay asway ightlay, Iay entway uponay eckday anday
oundfay allay ethay ailorssay usybay onay oneay idesay ofay ethay esselvay, apparentlyay
alkingtay otay omeonesay inay ethay easay. Itay asway, inay actfay, aay edgeslay, ikelay atthay eway
adhay eensay eforebay, ichwhay adhay ifteddray owardstay usay inay ethay ightnay onay aay argelay
agmentfray ofay iceay. Onlyay oneay ogday emainedray aliveay; utbay erethay asway aay umanhay
eingbay ithinway itay omwhay ethay ailorssay ereway ersuadingpay otay enteray ethay esselvay.
Ehay asway otnay, asay ethay otheray avellertray eemedsay otay ebay, aay avagesay inhabitantay ofay
omesay undiscovereday islanday, utbay aay Europeanay. Enwhay Iay appeareday onay eckday ethay
astermay aidsay, ere“hay isay ouray aptaincay, anday ehay illway otnay alloway ouyay otay erishpay
onay ethay openay easay.”

Onay erceivingpay emay, ethay angerstray addresseday emay inay Englishay, althoughay ithway aay
oreignfay accentay. efore“bay Iay omecay onay oardbay ouryay esselvay,” aidsay ehay,
ill“way ouyay avehay ethay indnesskay otay informay emay itherwhay ouyay areay oundbay?”

Ouyay aymay onceivecay myay astonishmentay onay earinghay uchsay aay uestionqay addresseday
otay emay omfray aay anmay onay ethay inkbray ofay estructionday anday otay omwhay Iay ouldshay avehay
upposedsay atthay myay esselvay ouldway avehay eenbay aay esourceray ichwhay ehay ouldway otnay
avehay exchangeday orfay ethay ostmay eciouspray ealthway ethay earthay ancay afforday. Iay
epliedray, oweverhay, atthay eway ereway onay aay oyagevay ofay iscoveryday owardstay ethay
orthernnay olepay.

Uponay earinghay isthay ehay appeareday atisfiedsay anday onsentedcay otay omecay onay oardbay.
Oodgay Odgay! Argaretmay, ifay ouyay adhay eensay ethay anmay owhay usthay apitulatedcay orfay
ishay afetysay, ouryay urprisesay ouldway avehay eenbay oundlessbay. Ishay imbslay ereway
earlynay ozenfray, anday ishay odybay eadfullydray emaciateday byay atiguefay anday
ufferingsay. Iay evernay awsay aay anmay inay osay etchedwray aay onditioncay. Eway attempteday
otay arrycay imhay intoay ethay abincay, utbay asay oonsay asay ehay adhay uittedqay ethay eshfray
airay ehay aintedfay. Eway accordinglyay oughtbray imhay ackbay otay ethay eckday anday
estoredray imhay otay animationay byay ubbingray imhay ithway andybray anday orcingfay imhay otay
allowsway aay allsmay uantityqay. Asay oonsay asay ehay owedshay ignssay ofay ifelay eway
appedwray imhay upay inay anketsblay anday acedplay imhay earnay ethay imneychay ofay ethay
itchenkay ovestay. Byay owslay egreesday ehay ecoveredray anday ateay aay ittlelay oupsay,
ichwhay estoredray imhay onderfullyway.

Otway aysday assedpay inay isthay annermay eforebay ehay asway ableay otay eakspay, anday Iay oftenay
earedfay atthay ishay ufferingssay adhay eprivedday imhay ofay understandingay. Enwhay ehay
adhay inay omesay easuremay ecoveredray, Iay emovedray imhay otay myay ownay abincay anday
attendeday onay imhay asay uchmay asay myay utyday ouldway ermitpay. Iay evernay awsay aay oremay
interestingay eaturecray: ishay eyesay avehay enerallygay anay expressionay ofay
ildnessway, anday evenay adnessmay, utbay erethay areay omentsmay enwhay, ifay anyoneay
erformspay anay actay ofay indnesskay owardstay imhay oray oesday imhay anyay ethay ostmay
iflingtray ervicesay, ishay olewhay ountenancecay isay ightedlay upay, asay itay ereway, ithway
aay eambay ofay enevolencebay anday eetnesssway atthay Iay evernay awsay equalleday. Utbay ehay
isay enerallygay elancholymay anday espairingday, anday ometimessay ehay ashesgnay ishay
eethtay, asay ifay impatientay ofay ethay eightway ofay oesway atthay oppressesay imhay.

Enwhay myay uestgay asway aay ittlelay ecoveredray Iay adhay eatgray oubletray otay eepkay offay
ethay enmay, owhay ishedway otay askay imhay aay ousandthay uestionsqay; utbay Iay ouldway otnay
alloway imhay otay ebay ormentedtay byay eirthay idleay uriositycay, inay aay atestay ofay odybay
anday indmay osewhay estorationray evidentlyay ependedday uponay entireay eposeray.
Onceay, oweverhay, ethay ieutenantlay askeday whyay ehay adhay omecay osay arfay uponay ethay iceay
inay osay angestray aay ehiclevay.

Ishay ountenancecay instantlyay assumeday anay aspectay ofay ethay eepestday oomglay, anday
ehay epliedray, o“tay eeksay oneay owhay edflay omfray emay.”

And“ay idday ethay anmay omwhay ouyay ursuedpay aveltray inay ethay amesay ashionfay?”

es“yay.”

en“thay Iay ancyfay eway avehay eensay imhay, orfay ethay ayday eforebay eway ickedpay ouyay upay eway
awsay omesay ogsday awingdray aay edgeslay, ithway aay anmay inay itay, acrossay ethay iceay.”

Isthay arouseday ethay anger’sstray attentionay, anday ehay askeday aay ultitudemay ofay
uestionsqay oncerningcay ethay outeray ichwhay ethay ondæmay, asay ehay alledcay imhay, adhay
ursuedpay. Oonsay afteray, enwhay ehay asway aloneay ithway emay, ehay aidsay, I“ay avehay,
oubtlessday, exciteday ouryay uriositycay, asay ellway asay atthay ofay esethay oodgay
eoplepay; utbay ouyay areay ootay onsideratecay otay akemay inquiriesay.”

ertainly“cay; itay ouldway indeeday ebay eryvay impertinentay anday inhumanay inay emay otay
oubletray ouyay ithway anyay inquisitivenessay ofay inemay.”

And“ay etyay ouyay escuedray emay omfray aay angestray anday erilouspay ituationsay; ouyay avehay
enevolentlybay estoredray emay otay ifelay.”

Oonsay afteray isthay ehay inquireday ifay Iay oughtthay atthay ethay eakingbray upay ofay ethay
iceay adhay estroyedday ethay otheray edgeslay. Iay epliedray atthay Iay ouldcay otnay answeray
ithway anyay egreeday ofay ertaintycay, orfay ethay iceay adhay otnay okenbray untilay earnay
idnightmay, anday ethay avellertray ightmay avehay arriveday atay aay aceplay ofay afetysay
eforebay atthay imetay; utbay ofay isthay Iay ouldcay otnay udgejay.

Omfray isthay imetay aay ewnay iritspay ofay ifelay animateday ethay ecayingday amefray ofay ethay
angerstray. Ehay anifestedmay ethay eatestgray eagernessay otay ebay uponay eckday otay atchway orfay
ethay edgeslay ichwhay adhay eforebay appeareday; utbay Iay avehay ersuadedpay imhay otay emainray inay
ethay abincay, orfay ehay isay arfay ootay eakway otay ustainsay ethay awnessray ofay ethay atmosphereay.
Iay avehay omisedpray atthay omeonesay ouldshay atchway orfay imhay anday ivegay imhay instantay
oticenay ifay anyay ewnay objectay ouldshay appearay inay ightsay.

Uchsay isay myay ournaljay ofay atwhay elatesray otay isthay angestray occurrenceay upay otay ethay
esentpray ayday. Ethay angerstray ashay aduallygray improveday inay ealthhay utbay isay eryvay
ilentsay anday appearsay uneasyay enwhay anyoneay exceptay elfmysay entersay ishay abincay.
Etyay ishay annersmay areay osay onciliatingcay anday entlegay atthay ethay ailorssay areay allay
interesteday inay imhay, althoughay eythay avehay adhay eryvay ittlelay ommunicationcay
ithway imhay. Orfay myay ownay artpay, Iay eginbay otay ovelay imhay asay aay otherbray, anday ishay
onstantcay anday eepday iefgray illsfay emay ithway athysympay anday ompassioncay. Ehay ustmay
avehay eenbay aay oblenay eaturecray inay ishay etterbay aysday, eingbay evenay ownay inay eckwray
osay attractiveay anday amiableay.

Iay aidsay inay oneay ofay myay etterslay, myay earday Argaretmay, atthay Iay ouldshay indfay onay iendfray
onay ethay ideway oceanay; etyay Iay avehay oundfay aay anmay owhay, eforebay ishay iritspay adhay eenbay
okenbray byay iserymay, Iay ouldshay avehay eenbay appyhay otay avehay ossessedpay asay ethay otherbray
ofay myay earthay.

Iay allshay ontinuecay myay ournaljay oncerningcay ethay angerstray atay intervalsay,
ouldshay Iay avehay anyay eshfray incidentsay otay ecordray.




Augustay 13thay, 17ay—.


Myay affectionay orfay myay uestgay increasesay everyay ayday. Ehay excitesay atay onceay myay
admirationay anday myay itypay otay anay astonishingay egreeday. Owhay ancay Iay eesay osay
oblenay aay eaturecray estroyedday byay iserymay ithoutway eelingfay ethay ostmay oignantpay
iefgray? Ehay isay osay entlegay, etyay osay iseway; ishay indmay isay osay ultivatedcay, anday
enwhay ehay eaksspay, althoughay ishay ordsway areay ulledcay ithway ethay oicestchay artay,
etyay eythay owflay ithway apidityray anday unparalleleday eloquenceay.

Ehay isay ownay uchmay ecoveredray omfray ishay illnessay anday isay ontinuallycay onay ethay eckday,
apparentlyay atchingway orfay ethay edgeslay atthay ecededpray ishay ownay. Etyay, althoughay
unhappyay, ehay isay otnay osay utterlyay occupieday byay ishay ownay iserymay utbay atthay ehay
interestsay imselfhay eeplyday inay ethay ojectspray ofay othersay. Ehay ashay equentlyfray
onversedcay ithway emay onay inemay, ichwhay Iay avehay ommunicatedcay otay imhay ithoutway
isguiseday. Ehay entereday attentivelyay intoay allay myay argumentsay inay avourfay ofay myay
eventualay uccesssay anday intoay everyay inutemay etailday ofay ethay easuresmay Iay adhay akentay
otay ecuresay itay. Iay asway easilyay edlay byay ethay athysympay ichwhay ehay evinceday otay useay ethay
anguagelay ofay myay earthay, otay ivegay utteranceay otay ethay urningbay ardouray ofay myay oulsay
anday otay aysay, ithway allay ethay ervourfay atthay armedway emay, owhay adlyglay Iay ouldway
acrificesay myay ortunefay, myay existenceay, myay everyay opehay, otay ethay urtherancefay ofay myay
enterpriseay. Oneay an’smay ifelay oray eathday ereway utbay aay allsmay icepray otay aypay orfay
ethay acquirementay ofay ethay owledgeknay ichwhay Iay oughtsay, orfay ethay ominionday Iay ouldshay
acquireay anday ansmittray overay ethay elementalay oesfay ofay ouray aceray. Asay Iay okespay, aay
arkday oomglay eadspray overay myay istener’slay ountenancecay. Atay irstfay Iay
erceivedpay atthay ehay iedtray otay uppresssay ishay emotionay; ehay acedplay ishay andshay eforebay
ishay eyesay, anday myay oicevay uiveredqay anday ailedfay emay asay Iay eheldbay earstay ickletray
astfay omfray etweenbay ishay ingersfay; aay oangray urstbay omfray ishay eavinghay eastbray. Iay
ausedpay; atay engthlay ehay okespay, inay okenbray accentsay: Unhappy“ay anmay! Oday ouyay
areshay myay adnessmay? Avehay ouyay unkdray alsoay ofay ethay intoxicatingay aughtdray? Earhay emay;
etlay emay evealray myay aletay, anday ouyay illway ashday ethay upcay omfray ouryay ipslay!”

Uchsay ordsway, ouyay aymay imagineay, onglystray exciteday myay uriositycay; utbay ethay
aroxysmpay ofay iefgray atthay adhay eizedsay ethay angerstray overcameay ishay eakenedway
owerspay, anday anymay ourshay ofay eposeray anday anquiltray onversationcay ereway
ecessarynay otay estoreray ishay omposurecay.

Avinghay onqueredcay ethay iolencevay ofay ishay eelingsfay, ehay appeareday otay espiseday
imselfhay orfay eingbay ethay aveslay ofay assionpay; anday uellingqay ethay arkday annytyray ofay
espairday, ehay edlay emay againay otay onversecay oncerningcay elfmysay ersonallypay. Ehay askeday
emay ethay istoryhay ofay myay earlieray earsyay. Ethay aletay asway uicklyqay oldtay, utbay itay
awakeneday ariousvay ainstray ofay eflectionray. Iay okespay ofay myay esireday ofay indingfay aay
iendfray, ofay myay irstthay orfay aay oremay intimateay athysympay ithway aay ellowfay indmay anthay
adhay everay allenfay otay myay otlay, anday expresseday myay onvictioncay atthay aay anmay ouldcay
oastbay ofay ittlelay appinesshay owhay idday otnay enjoyay isthay essingblay.

I“ay agreeay ithway ouyay,” epliedray ethay angerstray; e“way areay
unfashioneday eaturescray, utbay alfhay ademay upay, ifay oneay iserway, etterbay, earerday anthay
ourselves—suchay aay iendfray oughtay otay e—dobay otnay endlay ishay aiday otay
erfectionatepay ouray eakway anday aultyfay aturesnay. Iay onceay adhay aay iendfray, ethay ostmay
oblenay ofay umanhay eaturescray, anday amay entitleday, ereforethay, otay udgejay espectingray
iendshipfray. Ouyay avehay opehay, anday ethay orldway eforebay ouyay, anday avehay onay ausecay orfay
espairday. Utbay I—Iay avehay ostlay everythingay anday annotcay eginbay ifelay
aneway.”

Asay ehay aidsay isthay ishay ountenancecay ecamebay expressiveay ofay aay almcay, ettledsay
iefgray atthay ouchedtay emay otay ethay earthay. Utbay ehay asway ilentsay anday esentlypray
etiredray otay ishay abincay.

Evenay okenbray inay iritspay asay ehay isay, onay oneay ancay eelfay oremay eeplyday anthay ehay
oesday ethay eautiesbay ofay aturenay. Ethay arrystay skyay, ethay easay, anday everyay ightsay
affordeday byay esethay onderfulway egionsray eemsay illstay otay avehay ethay owerpay ofay
elevatingay ishay oulsay omfray earthay. Uchsay aay anmay ashay aay oubleday existenceay: ehay
aymay uffersay iserymay anday ebay overwhelmeday byay isappointmentsday, etyay enwhay ehay
ashay etiredray intoay imselfhay, ehay illway ebay ikelay aay elestialcay iritspay atthay ashay aay
alohay arounday imhay, ithinway osewhay irclecay onay iefgray oray ollyfay enturesvay.

Illway ouyay ilesmay atay ethay enthusiasmay Iay expressay oncerningcay isthay ivineday
andererway? Ouyay ouldway otnay ifay ouyay awsay imhay. Ouyay avehay eenbay utoredtay anday
efinedray byay ooksbay anday etirementray omfray ethay orldway, anday ouyay areay ereforethay
omewhatsay astidiousfay; utbay isthay onlyay endersray ouyay ethay oremay itfay otay
appreciateay ethay extraordinaryay eritsmay ofay isthay onderfulway anmay. Ometimessay Iay
avehay endeavoureday otay iscoverday atwhay ualityqay itay isay ichwhay ehay ossessespay atthay
elevatesay imhay osay immeasurablyay aboveay anyay otheray ersonpay Iay everay ewknay. Iay
elievebay itay otay ebay anay intuitiveay iscernmentday, aay uickqay utbay ever-failingclay
owerpay ofay udgmentjay, aay enetrationpay intoay ethay ausescay ofay ingsthay, unequalleday
orfay earnessclay anday ecisionpray; adday otay isthay aay acilityfay ofay expressionay anday aay
oicevay osewhay ariedvay intonationsay areay oul-subduingclay usicmay.




Augustay 19thay, 17ay—.


Esterdayyay ethay angerstray aidsay otay emay, ou“yay aymay easilyay erceivepay, Aptaincay
Altonway, atthay Iay avehay ufferedsay eatgray anday unparalleleday isfortunesmay. Iay adhay
eterminedday atay oneay imetay atthay ethay emorymay ofay esethay evilsay ouldshay ieday ithway
emay, utbay ouyay avehay onway emay otay alteray myay eterminationday. Ouyay eeksay orfay
owledgeknay anday isdomway, asay Iay onceay idday; anday Iay ardentlyay opehay atthay ethay
atificationgray ofay ouryay ishesway aymay otnay ebay aay erpentsay otay ingstay ouyay, asay inemay
ashay eenbay. Iay oday otnay owknay atthay ethay elationray ofay myay isastersday illway ebay
usefulay otay ouyay; etyay, enwhay Iay eflectray atthay ouyay areay ursuingpay ethay amesay
oursecay, exposingay ourselfyay otay ethay amesay angersday ichwhay avehay enderedray emay
atwhay Iay amay, Iay imagineay atthay ouyay aymay educeday anay aptay oralmay omfray myay aletay, oneay
atthay aymay irectday ouyay ifay ouyay ucceedsay inay ouryay undertakingay anday onsolecay ouyay
inay asecay ofay ailurefay. Eparepray otay earhay ofay occurrencesay ichwhay areay usuallyay
eemedday arvellousmay. Ereway eway amongay ethay amertay enesscay ofay aturenay Iay ightmay
earfay otay encounteray ouryay unbeliefay, erhapspay ouryay idiculeray; utbay anymay ingsthay
illway appearay ossiblepay inay esethay ildway anday eriousmystay egionsray ichwhay ouldway
ovokepray ethay aughterlay ofay osethay unacquainteday ithway ethay ever-variedclay owerspay
ofay aturenay; ornay ancay Iay oubtday utbay atthay myay aletay onveyscay inay itsay eriessay
internalay evidenceay ofay ethay uthtray ofay ethay eventsay ofay ichwhay itay isay omposedcay.”

Ouyay aymay easilyay imagineay atthay Iay asway uchmay atifiedgray byay ethay offereday
ommunicationcay, etyay Iay ouldcay otnay endureay atthay ehay ouldshay enewray ishay iefgray byay
aay ecitalray ofay ishay isfortunesmay. Iay eltfay ethay eatestgray eagernessay otay earhay
ethay omisedpray arrativenay, artlypay omfray uriositycay anday artlypay omfray aay ongstray
esireday otay ameliorateay ishay atefay ifay itay ereway inay myay owerpay. Iay expresseday
esethay eelingsfay inay myay answeray.

I“ay ankthay ouyay,” ehay epliedray, or“fay ouryay athysympay, utbay itay isay
uselessay; myay atefay isay earlynay ulfilledfay. Iay aitway utbay orfay oneay eventay, anday enthay Iay
allshay eposeray inay eacepay. Iay understanday ouryay eelingfay,” ontinuedcay ehay,
erceivingpay atthay Iay ishedway otay interruptay imhay; ut“bay ouyay areay istakenmay, myay
iendfray, ifay usthay ouyay illway alloway emay otay amenay ouyay; othingnay ancay alteray myay
estinyday; istenlay otay myay istoryhay, anday ouyay illway erceivepay owhay irrevocablyay itay isay
eterminedday.”

Ehay enthay oldtay emay atthay ehay ouldway ommencecay ishay arrativenay ethay extnay ayday enwhay Iay
ouldshay ebay atay eisurelay. Isthay omisepray ewdray omfray emay ethay armestway anksthay. Iay avehay
esolvedray everyay ightnay, enwhay Iay amay otnay imperativelyay occupieday byay myay utiesday, otay
ecordray, asay earlynay asay ossiblepay inay ishay ownay ordsway, atwhay ehay ashay elatedray uringday
ethay ayday. Ifay Iay ouldshay ebay engageday, Iay illway atay eastlay akemay otesnay. Isthay
anuscriptmay illway oubtlessday afforday ouyay ethay eatestgray easureplay; utbay otay emay, owhay
owknay imhay, anday owhay earhay itay omfray ishay ownay ips—withlay atwhay interestay anday
athysympay allshay Iay eadray itay inay omesay uturefay ayday! Evenay ownay, asay Iay ommencecay myay
asktay, ishay ull-tonedclay oicevay ellssway inay myay earsay; ishay ustrouslay eyesay elldway onay emay
ithway allay eirthay elancholymay eetnesssway; Iay eesay ishay inthay andhay aisedray inay
animationay, ilewhay ethay ineamentslay ofay ishay acefay areay irradiateday byay ethay oulsay
ithinway. Angestray anday arrowinghay ustmay ebay ishay orystay, ightfulfray ethay ormstay ichwhay
embraceday ethay allantgay esselvay onay itsay oursecay anday eckedwray it—thusay!




Apterchay 1ay


Iay amay byay irthbay aay Enevesegay, anday myay amilyfay isay oneay ofay ethay ostmay
istinguishedday ofay atthay epublicray. Myay ancestorsay adhay eenbay orfay anymay earsyay
ounsellorscay anday icssynday, anday myay atherfay adhay illedfay everalsay ublicpay
ituationssay ithway onourhay anday eputationray. Ehay asway espectedray byay allay owhay
ewknay imhay orfay ishay integrityay anday indefatigableay attentionay otay ublicpay
usinessbay. Ehay assedpay ishay oungeryay aysday erpetuallypay occupieday byay ethay
affairsay ofay ishay ountrycay; aay arietyvay ofay ircumstancescay adhay eventedpray ishay
arryingmay earlyay, ornay asway itay untilay ethay eclineday ofay ifelay atthay ehay ecamebay aay
usbandhay anday ethay atherfay ofay aay amilyfay.

Asay ethay ircumstancescay ofay ishay arriagemay illustrateay ishay aracterchay, Iay annotcay
efrainray omfray elatingray emthay. Oneay ofay ishay ostmay intimateay iendsfray asway aay
erchantmay owhay, omfray aay ourishingflay atestay, ellfay, oughthray umerousnay
ischancesmay, intoay overtypay. Isthay anmay, osewhay amenay asway Eaufortbay, asway ofay aay
oudpray anday unbendingay ispositionday anday ouldcay otnay earbay otay ivelay inay overtypay
anday oblivionay inay ethay amesay ountrycay erewhay ehay adhay ormerlyfay eenbay
istinguishedday orfay ishay ankray anday agnificencemay. Avinghay aidpay ishay ebtsday,
ereforethay, inay ethay ostmay onourablehay annermay, ehay etreatedray ithway ishay
aughterday otay ethay owntay ofay Ucernelay, erewhay ehay ivedlay unknownay anday inay
etchednesswray. Myay atherfay ovedlay Eaufortbay ithway ethay uesttray iendshipfray anday
asway eeplyday ievedgray byay ishay etreatray inay esethay unfortunateay ircumstancescay.
Ehay itterlybay eploredday ethay alsefay idepray ichwhay edlay ishay iendfray otay aay onductcay
osay ittlelay orthyway ofay ethay affectionay atthay uniteday emthay. Ehay ostlay onay imetay inay
endeavouringay otay eeksay imhay outay, ithway ethay opehay ofay ersuadingpay imhay otay eginbay
ethay orldway againay oughthray ishay editcray anday assistanceay.

Eaufortbay adhay akentay effectualay easuresmay otay oncealcay imselfhay, anday itay asway entay
onthsmay eforebay myay atherfay iscoveredday ishay abodeay. Overjoyeday atay isthay iscoveryday,
ehay astenedhay otay ethay ousehay, ichwhay asway ituatedsay inay aay eanmay eetstray earnay ethay
Eussray. Utbay enwhay ehay entereday, iserymay anday espairday aloneay elcomedway imhay. Eaufortbay
adhay avedsay utbay aay eryvay allsmay umsay ofay oneymay omfray ethay eckwray ofay ishay ortunesfay, utbay
itay asway ufficientsay otay ovidepray imhay ithway ustenancesay orfay omesay onthsmay, anday inay
ethay eantimemay ehay opedhay otay ocurepray omesay espectableray employmentay inay aay
erchant’smay ousehay. Ethay intervalay asway, onsequentlycay, entspay inay inactionay;
ishay iefgray onlyay ecamebay oremay eepday anday anklingray enwhay ehay adhay eisurelay orfay
eflectionray, anday atay engthlay itay ooktay osay astfay oldhay ofay ishay indmay atthay atay ethay enday
ofay eethray onthsmay ehay aylay onay aay edbay ofay icknesssay, incapableay ofay anyay exertionay.

Ishay aughterday attendeday imhay ithway ethay eatestgray endernesstay, utbay eshay awsay
ithway espairday atthay eirthay ittlelay undfay asway apidlyray ecreasingday anday atthay
erethay asway onay otheray ospectpray ofay upportsay. Utbay Arolinecay Eaufortbay
ossessedpay aay indmay ofay anay uncommonay ouldmay, anday erhay ouragecay oseray otay upportsay
erhay inay erhay adversityay. Eshay ocuredpray ainplay orkway; eshay aitedplay awstray anday
byay ariousvay eansmay ontrivedcay otay earnay aay ittancepay arcelyscay ufficientsay otay
upportsay ifelay.

Everalsay onthsmay assedpay inay isthay annermay. Erhay atherfay ewgray orseway; erhay imetay
asway oremay entirelyay occupieday inay attendingay imhay; erhay eansmay ofay ubsistencesay
ecreasedday; anday inay ethay enthtay onthmay erhay atherfay iedday inay erhay armsay, eavinglay
erhay anay orphanay anday aay eggarbay. Isthay astlay owblay overcameay erhay, anday eshay eltknay
byay Eaufort’sbay offincay eepingway itterlybay, enwhay myay atherfay entereday ethay
amberchay. Ehay amecay ikelay aay otectingpray iritspay otay ethay oorpay irlgay, owhay
ommittedcay erselfhay otay ishay arecay; anday afteray ethay intermentay ofay ishay iendfray ehay
onductedcay erhay otay Enevagay anday acedplay erhay underay ethay otectionpray ofay aay
elationray. Otway earsyay afteray isthay eventay Arolinecay ecamebay ishay ifeway.

Erethay asway aay onsiderablecay ifferenceday etweenbay ethay agesay ofay myay arentspay, utbay
isthay ircumstancecay eemedsay otay uniteay emthay onlyay oserclay inay ondsbay ofay evotedday
affectionay. Erethay asway aay ensesay ofay usticejay inay myay ather’sfay uprightay indmay
ichwhay enderedray itay ecessarynay atthay ehay ouldshay approveay ighlyhay otay ovelay
onglystray. Erhapspay uringday ormerfay earsyay ehay adhay ufferedsay omfray ethay
ate-discoveredclay unworthinessay ofay oneay elovedbay anday osay asway isposedday otay etsay
aay eatergray aluevay onay iedtray orthway. Erethay asway aay owshay ofay atitudegray anday
orshipway inay ishay attachmentay otay myay othermay, ifferingday ollywhay omfray ethay
otingday ondnessfay ofay ageay, orfay itay asway inspireday byay everenceray orfay erhay
irtuesvay anday aay esireday otay ebay ethay eansmay ofay, inay omesay egreeday, ecompensingray
erhay orfay ethay orrowssay eshay adhay endureday, utbay ichwhay avegay inexpressibleay acegray
otay ishay ehaviourbay otay erhay. Everythingay asway ademay otay ieldyay otay erhay ishesway
anday erhay onveniencecay. Ehay ovestray otay eltershay erhay, asay aay airfay exoticay isay
elteredshay byay ethay ardenergay, omfray everyay ougherray indway anday otay urroundsay erhay
ithway allay atthay ouldcay endtay otay exciteay easurableplay emotionay inay erhay oftsay anday
enevolentbay indmay. Erhay ealthhay, anday evenay ethay anquillitytray ofay erhay ithertohay
onstantcay iritspay, adhay eenbay akenshay byay atwhay eshay adhay onegay oughthray. Uringday
ethay otway earsyay atthay adhay elapseday eviouspray otay eirthay arriagemay myay atherfay adhay
aduallygray elinquishedray allay ishay ublicpay unctionsfay; anday immediatelyay afteray
eirthay unionay eythay oughtsay ethay easantplay imateclay ofay Italyay, anday ethay angechay
ofay enescay anday interestay attendantay onay aay ourtay oughthray atthay andlay ofay ondersway,
asay aay estorativeray orfay erhay eakenedway amefray.

Omfray Italyay eythay isitedvay Ermanygay anday Ancefray. Iay, eirthay eldestay ildchay, asway ornbay
atay Aplesnay, anday asay anay infantay accompanieday emthay inay eirthay amblesray. Iay emainedray
orfay everalsay earsyay eirthay onlyay ildchay. Uchmay asay eythay ereway attacheday otay eachay
otheray, eythay eemedsay otay awdray inexhaustibleay oresstay ofay affectionay omfray aay eryvay
inemay ofay ovelay otay estowbay emthay uponay emay. Myay other’smay endertay aressescay anday
myay ather’sfay ilesmay ofay enevolentbay easureplay ilewhay egardingray emay areay myay
irstfay ecollectionsray. Iay asway eirthay aythingplay anday eirthay idolay, anday omethingsay
etter—theirbay ildchay, ethay innocentay anday elplesshay eaturecray estowedbay onay
emthay byay Eavenhay, omwhay otay ingbray upay otay oodgay, anday osewhay uturefay otlay itay asway inay
eirthay andshay otay irectday otay appinesshay oray iserymay, accordingay asay eythay ulfilledfay
eirthay utiesday owardstay emay. Ithway isthay eepday onsciousnesscay ofay atwhay eythay oweday
owardstay ethay eingbay otay ichwhay eythay adhay ivengay ifelay, addeday otay ethay activeay iritspay
ofay endernesstay atthay animateday othbay, itay aymay ebay imagineday atthay ilewhay uringday
everyay ourhay ofay myay infantay ifelay Iay eceivedray aay essonlay ofay atiencepay, ofay aritychay,
anday ofay elf-controlclay, Iay asway osay uidedgay byay aay ilkensay ordcay atthay allay eemedsay utbay
oneay aintray ofay enjoymentay otay emay.

Orfay aay onglay imetay Iay asway eirthay onlyay arecay. Myay othermay adhay uchmay esiredday otay avehay aay
aughterday, utbay Iay ontinuedcay eirthay inglesay offspringay. Enwhay Iay asway aboutay ivefay
earsyay olday, ilewhay akingmay anay excursionay eyondbay ethay ontiersfray ofay Italyay, eythay
assedpay aay eekway onay ethay oresshay ofay ethay Akelay ofay Omocay. Eirthay enevolentbay
ispositionday oftenay ademay emthay enteray ethay ottagescay ofay ethay oorpay. Isthay, otay myay
othermay, asway oremay anthay aay utyday; itay asway aay ecessitynay, aay
assion—rememberingpay atwhay eshay adhay ufferedsay, anday owhay eshay adhay eenbay
elieved—forray erhay otay actay inay erhay urntay ethay uardiangay angelay otay ethay
afflicteday. Uringday oneay ofay eirthay alksway aay oorpay otcay inay ethay oldingsfay ofay aay alevay
attracteday eirthay oticenay asay eingbay ingularlysay isconsolateday, ilewhay ethay umbernay
ofay alf-clothedclay ildrenchay atheredgay aboutay itay okespay ofay enurypay inay itsay orstway
apeshay. Oneay ayday, enwhay myay atherfay adhay onegay byay imselfhay otay Ilanmay, myay othermay,
accompanieday byay emay, isitedvay isthay abodeay. Eshay oundfay aay easantpay anday ishay ifeway,
ardhay orkingway, entbay ownday byay arecay anday abourlay, istributingday aay antyscay ealmay otay
ivefay ungryhay abesbay. Amongay esethay erethay asway oneay ichwhay attracteday myay othermay arfay
aboveay allay ethay estray. Eshay appeareday ofay aay ifferentday ockstay. Ethay ourfay othersay ereway
ark-eyedclay, ardyhay ittlelay agrantsvay; isthay ildchay asway inthay anday eryvay airfay. Erhay
airhay asway ethay ightestbray ivinglay oldgay, anday espiteday ethay overtypay ofay erhay
othingclay, eemedsay otay etsay aay owncray ofay istinctionday onay erhay eadhay. Erhay owbray asway
earclay anday ampleay, erhay ueblay eyesay oudlessclay, anday erhay ipslay anday ethay ouldingmay ofay
erhay acefay osay expressiveay ofay ensibilitysay anday eetnesssway atthay onenay ouldcay eholdbay
erhay ithoutway ookinglay onay erhay asay ofay aay istinctday eciesspay, aay eingbay eaven-sentclay,
anday earingbay aay elestialcay ampstay inay allay erhay eaturesfay.

Ethay easantpay omanway, erceivingpay atthay myay othermay ixedfay eyesay ofay onderway anday
admirationay onay isthay ovelylay irlgay, eagerlyay ommunicatedcay erhay istoryhay. Eshay asway
otnay erhay ildchay, utbay ethay aughterday ofay aay Ilanesemay oblemannay. Erhay othermay asway aay
Ermangay anday adhay iedday onay ivinggay erhay irthbay. Ethay infantay adhay eenbay acedplay ithway
esethay oodgay eoplepay otay ursenay: eythay ereway etterbay offay enthay. Eythay adhay otnay eenbay
onglay arriedmay, anday eirthay eldestay ildchay asway utbay ustjay ornbay. Ethay atherfay ofay eirthay
argechay asway oneay ofay osethay Italiansay ursednay inay ethay emorymay ofay ethay antiqueay oryglay
ofay Italy—oneay amongay ethay iavi_schay ognoray ementifray,_ owhay exerteday
imselfhay otay obtainay ethay ibertylay ofay ishay ountrycay. Ehay ecamebay ethay ictimvay ofay itsay
eaknessway. Etherwhay ehay adhay iedday oray illstay ingeredlay inay ethay ungeonsday ofay Austriaay
asway otnay ownknay. Ishay opertypray asway onfiscatedcay; ishay ildchay ecamebay anay orphanay anday
aay eggarbay. Eshay ontinuedcay ithway erhay osterfay arentspay anday oomedblay inay eirthay uderay
abodeay, airerfay anthay aay ardengay oseray amongay ark-leavedclay amblesbray.

Enwhay myay atherfay eturnedray omfray Ilanmay, ehay oundfay ayingplay ithway emay inay ethay allhay ofay
ouray illavay aay ildchay airerfay anthay icturedpay erub—achay eaturecray owhay eemedsay
otay edshay adianceray omfray erhay ookslay anday osewhay ormfay anday otionsmay ereway ighterlay
anthay ethay amoischay ofay ethay illshay. Ethay apparitionay asway oonsay explaineday. Ithway ishay
ermissionpay myay othermay evailedpray onay erhay usticray uardiansgay otay ieldyay eirthay
argechay otay erhay. Eythay ereway ondfay ofay ethay eetsway orphanay. Erhay esencepray adhay eemedsay
aay essingblay otay emthay, utbay itay ouldway ebay unfairay otay erhay otay eepkay erhay inay overtypay
anday antway enwhay Ovidencepray affordeday erhay uchsay owerfulpay otectionpray. Eythay
onsultedcay eirthay illagevay iestpray, anday ethay esultray asway atthay Elizabethay Avenzalay
ecamebay ethay inmateay ofay myay arentspay’ ouse—myhay oremay anthay
ister—thesay eautifulbay anday adoreday ompanioncay ofay allay myay occupationsay anday
myay easuresplay.

Everyoneay ovedlay Elizabethay. Ethay assionatepay anday almostay everentialray
attachmentay ithway ichwhay allay egardedray erhay ecamebay, ilewhay Iay aredshay itay, myay
idepray anday myay elightday. Onay ethay eveningay eviouspray otay erhay eingbay oughtbray otay
myay omehay, myay othermay adhay aidsay ayfullyplay, I“ay avehay aay ettypray esentpray orfay myay
Ictor—tomorrowvay ehay allshay avehay itay.” Anday enwhay, onay ethay orrowmay, eshay
esentedpray Elizabethay otay emay asay erhay omisedpray iftgay, Iay, ithway ildishchay
eriousnesssay, interpreteday erhay ordsway iterallylay anday ookedlay uponay Elizabethay
asay ine—minemay otay otectpray, ovelay, anday erishchay. Allay aisespray estowedbay onay
erhay Iay eceivedray asay ademay otay aay ossessionpay ofay myay ownay. Eway alledcay eachay otheray
amiliarlyfay byay ethay amenay ofay ousincay. Onay ordway, onay expressionay ouldcay odybay
orthfay ethay indkay ofay elationray inay ichwhay eshay oodstay otay e—mymay oremay anthay
istersay, incesay illtay eathday eshay asway otay ebay inemay onlyay.




Apterchay 2ay


Eway ereway oughtbray upay ogethertay; erethay asway otnay uiteqay aay earyay ifferenceday inay
ouray agesay. Iay eednay otnay aysay atthay eway ereway angersstray otay anyay eciesspay ofay
isunionday oray isputeday. Armonyhay asway ethay oulsay ofay ouray ompanionshipcay, anday
ethay iversityday anday ontrastcay atthay ubsistedsay inay ouray aracterschay ewdray usay
earernay ogethertay. Elizabethay asway ofay aay almercay anday oremay oncentratedcay
ispositionday; utbay, ithway allay myay ardouray, Iay asway apablecay ofay aay oremay intenseay
applicationay anday asway oremay eeplyday ittensmay ithway ethay irstthay orfay owledgeknay.
Eshay usiedbay erselfhay ithway ollowingfay ethay aerialay eationscray ofay ethay oetspay;
anday inay ethay ajesticmay anday ondrousway enesscay ichwhay urroundedsay ouray Isssway
omehay e—thay ublimesay apesshay ofay ethay ountainsmay, ethay angeschay ofay ethay easonssay,
empesttay anday almcay, ethay ilencesay ofay interway, anday ethay ifelay anday urbulencetay ofay
ouray Alpineay ummers—shesay oundfay ampleay opescay orfay admirationay anday elightday.
Ilewhay myay ompanioncay ontemplatedcay ithway aay erioussay anday atisfiedsay iritspay ethay
agnificentmay appearancesay ofay ingsthay, Iay elightedday inay investigatingay eirthay
ausescay. Ethay orldway asway otay emay aay ecretsay ichwhay Iay esiredday otay ivineday.
Uriositycay, earnestay esearchray otay earnlay ethay iddenhay awslay ofay aturenay,
adnessglay akinay otay aptureray, asay eythay ereway unfoldeday otay emay, areay amongay ethay
earliestay ensationssay Iay ancay ememberray.

Onay ethay irthbay ofay aay econdsay onsay, myay uniorjay byay evensay earsyay, myay arentspay avegay
upay entirelyay eirthay anderingway ifelay anday ixedfay emselvesthay inay eirthay ativenay
ountrycay. Eway ossessedpay aay ousehay inay Enevagay, anday aay ampagne_cay_ onay Elrivebay,
ethay easternay oreshay ofay ethay akelay, atay ethay istanceday ofay atherray oremay anthay aay
eaguelay omfray ethay itycay. Eway esidedray incipallypray inay ethay atterlay, anday ethay
iveslay ofay myay arentspay ereway assedpay inay onsiderablecay eclusionsay. Itay asway myay
empertay otay avoiday aay owdcray anday otay attachay elfmysay erventlyfay otay aay ewfay. Iay asway
indifferentay, ereforethay, otay myay ool-fellowsclay inay eneralgay; utbay Iay uniteday
elfmysay inay ethay ondsbay ofay ethay osestclay iendshipfray otay oneay amongay emthay. Enryhay
Ervalclay asway ethay onsay ofay aay erchantmay ofay Enevagay. Ehay asway aay oybay ofay ingularsay
alenttay anday ancyfay. Ehay ovedlay enterpriseay, ardshiphay, anday evenay angerday orfay
itsay ownay akesay. Ehay asway eeplyday eadray inay ooksbay ofay ivalrychay anday omanceray. Ehay
omposedcay eroichay ongssay anday eganbay otay itewray anymay aay aletay ofay enchantmentay anday
ightlyknay adventureay. Ehay iedtray otay akemay usay actay aysplay anday otay enteray intoay
asqueradesmay, inay ichwhay ethay aracterschay ereway awndray omfray ethay eroeshay ofay
Oncesvallesray, ofay ethay Oundray Abletay ofay Ingkay Arthuray, anday ethay ivalrouschay
aintray owhay edshay eirthay oodblay otay edeemray ethay olyhay epulchresay omfray ethay andshay
ofay ethay infidelsay.

Onay umanhay eingbay ouldcay avehay assedpay aay appierhay ildhoodchay anthay elfmysay. Myay
arentspay ereway ossessedpay byay ethay eryvay iritspay ofay indnesskay anday indulgenceay.
Eway eltfay atthay eythay ereway otnay ethay antstyray otay uleray ouray otlay accordingay otay
eirthay apricecay, utbay ethay agentsay anday eatorscray ofay allay ethay anymay elightsday
ichwhay eway enjoyeday. Enwhay Iay ingledmay ithway otheray amiliesfay Iay istinctlyday
iscernedday owhay eculiarlypay ortunatefay myay otlay asway, anday atitudegray assisteday
ethay evelopmentday ofay ilialfay ovelay.

Myay empertay asway ometimessay iolentvay, anday myay assionspay ehementvay; utbay byay omesay
awlay inay myay emperaturetay eythay ereway urnedtay otnay owardstay ildishchay ursuitspay
utbay otay anay eageray esireday otay earnlay, anday otnay otay earnlay allay ingsthay
indiscriminatelyay. Iay onfesscay atthay eithernay ethay ucturestray ofay anguageslay,
ornay ethay odecay ofay overnmentsgay, ornay ethay oliticspay ofay ariousvay atesstay
ossessedpay attractionsay orfay emay. Itay asway ethay ecretssay ofay eavenhay anday earthay
atthay Iay esiredday otay earnlay; anday etherwhay itay asway ethay outwarday ubstancesay ofay
ingsthay oray ethay inneray iritspay ofay aturenay anday ethay eriousmystay oulsay ofay anmay
atthay occupieday emay, illstay myay inquiriesay ereway irectedday otay ethay etaphysicalmay,
oray inay itsay ighesthay ensesay, ethay icalphysay ecretssay ofay ethay orldway.

Eanwhilemay Ervalclay occupieday imselfhay, osay otay eakspay, ithway ethay oralmay
elationsray ofay ingsthay. Ethay usybay agestay ofay ifelay, ethay irtuesvay ofay eroeshay,
anday ethay actionsay ofay enmay ereway ishay emethay; anday ishay opehay anday ishay eamdray asway
otay ecomebay oneay amongay osethay osewhay amesnay areay ecordedray inay orystay asay ethay
allantgay anday adventurousay enefactorsbay ofay ouray eciesspay. Ethay aintlysay oulsay
ofay Elizabethay oneshay ikelay aay ine-dedicatedclay amplay inay ouray eacefulpay omehay.
Erhay athysympay asway oursay; erhay ilesmay, erhay oftsay oicevay, ethay eetsway anceglay ofay
erhay elestialcay eyesay, ereway everay erethay otay essblay anday animateay usay. Eshay asway
ethay ivinglay iritspay ofay ovelay otay oftensay anday attractay; Iay ightmay avehay ecomebay
ullensay inay myay udystay, oughray oughthray ethay ardouray ofay myay aturenay, utbay atthay
eshay asway erethay otay ubduesay emay otay aay emblancesay ofay erhay ownay entlenessgay. Anday
Erval—couldclay aughtay illay entrenchay onay ethay oblenay iritspay ofay Ervalclay? Etyay
ehay ightmay otnay avehay eenbay osay erfectlypay umanehay, osay oughtfulthay inay ishay
enerositygay, osay ullfay ofay indnesskay anday endernesstay amidstay ishay assionpay orfay
adventurousay exploitay, adhay eshay otnay unfoldeday otay imhay ethay ealray ovelinesslay ofay
eneficencebay anday ademay ethay oingday oodgay ethay enday anday aimay ofay ishay oaringsay
ambitionay.

Iay eelfay exquisiteay easureplay inay ellingdway onay ethay ecollectionsray ofay ildhoodchay,
eforebay isfortunemay adhay aintedtay myay indmay anday angedchay itsay ightbray isionsvay ofay
extensiveay usefulnessay intoay oomyglay anday arrownay eflectionsray uponay elfsay. Esidesbay,
inay awingdray ethay icturepay ofay myay earlyay aysday, Iay alsoay ecordray osethay eventsay ichwhay
edlay, byay insensibleay epsstay, otay myay afteray aletay ofay iserymay, orfay enwhay Iay ouldway
accountay otay elfmysay orfay ethay irthbay ofay atthay assionpay ichwhay afterwardsay uledray myay
estinyday Iay indfay itay ariseay, ikelay aay ountainmay iverray, omfray ignobleay anday almostay
orgottenfay ourcessay; utbay, ellingsway asay itay oceededpray, itay ecamebay ethay orrenttay
ichwhay, inay itsay oursecay, ashay eptsway awayay allay myay opeshay anday oysjay.

Aturalnay ilosophyphay isay ethay eniusgay atthay ashay egulatedray myay atefay; Iay esireday,
ereforethay, inay isthay arrationnay, otay atestay osethay actsfay ichwhay edlay otay myay
edilectionpray orfay atthay iencescay. Enwhay Iay asway irteenthay earsyay ofay ageay eway allay entway
onay aay artypay ofay easureplay otay ethay athsbay earnay Ononthay; ethay inclemencyay ofay ethay
eatherway obligeday usay otay emainray aay ayday onfinedcay otay ethay innay. Inay isthay ousehay Iay
ancedchay otay indfay aay olumevay ofay ethay orksway ofay Orneliuscay Agrippaay. Iay openeday itay
ithway apathyay; ethay eorythay ichwhay ehay attemptsay otay emonstrateday anday ethay onderfulway
actsfay ichwhay ehay elatesray oonsay angedchay isthay eelingfay intoay enthusiasmay. Aay ewnay
ightlay eemedsay otay awnday uponay myay indmay, anday oundingbay ithway oyjay, Iay ommunicatedcay myay
iscoveryday otay myay atherfay. Myay atherfay ookedlay arelesslycay atay ethay itletay agepay ofay myay
ookbay anday aidsay, Ah“ay! Orneliuscay Agrippaay! Myay earday Ictorvay, oday otnay asteway
ouryay imetay uponay isthay; itay isay adsay ashtray.”

Ifay, insteaday ofay isthay emarkray, myay atherfay adhay akentay ethay ainspay otay explainay otay emay
atthay ethay inciplespray ofay Agrippaay adhay eenbay entirelyay explodeday anday atthay aay odernmay
emsystay ofay iencescay adhay eenbay introduceday ichwhay ossessedpay uchmay eatergray owerspay
anthay ethay ancientay, ecausebay ethay owerspay ofay ethay atterlay ereway imericalchay, ilewhay
osethay ofay ethay ormerfay ereway ealray anday acticalpray, underay uchsay ircumstancescay Iay
ouldshay ertainlycay avehay ownthray Agrippaay asideay anday avehay ontentedcay myay
imaginationay, armedway asay itay asway, byay eturningray ithway eatergray ardouray otay myay
ormerfay udiesstay. Itay isay evenay ossiblepay atthay ethay aintray ofay myay ideasay ouldway evernay
avehay eceivedray ethay atalfay impulseay atthay edlay otay myay uinray. Utbay ethay ursorycay anceglay
myay atherfay adhay akentay ofay myay olumevay byay onay eansmay assureday emay atthay ehay asway
acquainteday ithway itsay ontentscay, anday Iay ontinuedcay otay eadray ithway ethay eatestgray
avidityay.

Enwhay Iay eturnedray omehay myay irstfay arecay asway otay ocurepray ethay olewhay orksway ofay isthay
authoray, anday afterwardsay ofay Aracelsuspay anday Albertusay Agnusmay. Iay eadray anday
udiedstay ethay ildway anciesfay ofay esethay iterswray ithway elightday; eythay appeareday otay emay
easurestray ownknay otay ewfay esidesbay elfmysay. Iay avehay escribedday elfmysay asay alwaysay
avinghay eenbay imbueday ithway aay erventfay onginglay otay enetratepay ethay ecretssay ofay
aturenay. Inay itespay ofay ethay intenseay abourlay anday onderfulway iscoveriesday ofay odernmay
ilosophersphay, Iay alwaysay amecay omfray myay udiesstay iscontentedday anday unsatisfieday.
Irsay Isaacay Ewtonnay isay aidsay otay avehay avoweday atthay ehay eltfay ikelay aay ildchay ickingpay
upay ellsshay esidebay ethay eatgray anday unexploreday oceanay ofay uthtray. Osethay ofay ishay
uccessorssay inay eachay anchbray ofay aturalnay ilosophyphay ithway omwhay Iay asway acquainteday
appeareday evenay otay myay oy’sbay apprehensionsay asay ostyray engageday inay ethay amesay
ursuitpay.

Ethay untaughtay easantpay eheldbay ethay elementsay arounday imhay anday asway acquainteday
ithway eirthay acticalpray usesay. Ethay ostmay earnedlay ilosopherphay ewknay ittlelay
oremay. Ehay adhay artiallypay unveileday ethay acefay ofay Aturenay, utbay erhay immortalay
ineamentslay ereway illstay aay onderway anday aay erymystay. Ehay ightmay issectday,
anatomiseay, anday ivegay amesnay; utbay, otnay otay eakspay ofay aay inalfay ausecay, ausescay
inay eirthay econdarysay anday ertiarytay adesgray ereway utterlyay unknownay otay imhay. Iay
adhay azedgay uponay ethay ortificationsfay anday impedimentsay atthay eemedsay otay eepkay
umanhay eingsbay omfray enteringay ethay itadelcay ofay aturenay, anday ashlyray anday
ignorantlyay Iay adhay epinedray.

Utbay erehay ereway ooksbay, anday erehay ereway enmay owhay adhay enetratedpay eeperday anday ewknay
oremay. Iay ooktay eirthay ordway orfay allay atthay eythay averreday, anday Iay ecamebay eirthay
iscipleday. Itay aymay appearay angestray atthay uchsay ouldshay ariseay inay ethay eighteenthay
enturycay; utbay ilewhay Iay ollowedfay ethay outineray ofay educationay inay ethay oolsschay ofay
Enevagay, Iay asway, otay aay eatgray egreeday, elf-taughtclay ithway egardray otay myay avouritefay
udiesstay. Myay atherfay asway otnay ientificscay, anday Iay asway eftlay otay ugglestray ithway aay
ild’schay indnessblay, addeday otay aay udent’sstay irstthay orfay owledgeknay.
Underay ethay uidancegay ofay myay ewnay eceptorspray Iay entereday ithway ethay eatestgray
iligenceday intoay ethay earchsay ofay ethay ilosopher’sphay onestay anday ethay elixiray
ofay ifelay; utbay ethay atterlay oonsay obtaineday myay undivideday attentionay. Ealthway asway anay
inferioray objectay, utbay atwhay oryglay ouldway attenday ethay iscoveryday ifay Iay ouldcay
anishbay iseaseday omfray ethay umanhay amefray anday enderray anmay invulnerableay otay anyay utbay
aay iolentvay eathday!

Ornay ereway esethay myay onlyay isionsvay. Ethay aisingray ofay ostsghay oray evilsday asway aay
omisepray iberallylay accordeday byay myay avouritefay authorsay, ethay ulfilmentfay ofay ichwhay
Iay ostmay eagerlyay oughtsay; anday ifay myay incantationsay ereway alwaysay unsuccessfulay, Iay
attributeday ethay ailurefay atherray otay myay ownay inexperienceay anday istakemay anthay otay aay
antway ofay illskay oray idelityfay inay myay instructorsay. Anday usthay orfay aay imetay Iay asway
occupieday byay explodeday emssystay, inglingmay, ikelay anay unadeptay, aay ousandthay
ontradictorycay eoriesthay anday ounderingflay esperatelyday inay aay eryvay oughslay ofay
ultifariousmay owledgeknay, uidedgay byay anay ardentay imaginationay anday ildishchay
easoningray, illtay anay accidentay againay angedchay ethay urrentcay ofay myay ideasay.

Enwhay Iay asway aboutay ifteenfay earsyay olday eway adhay etiredray otay ouray ousehay earnay
Elrivebay, enwhay eway itnessedway aay ostmay iolentvay anday erribletay understormthay. Itay
advanceday omfray ehindbay ethay ountainsmay ofay Urajay, anday ethay underthay urstbay atay onceay
ithway ightfulfray oudnesslay omfray ariousvay uartersqay ofay ethay eavenshay. Iay emainedray,
ilewhay ethay ormstay astedlay, atchingway itsay ogresspray ithway uriositycay anday elightday.
Asay Iay oodstay atay ethay oorday, onay aay uddensay Iay eheldbay aay eamstray ofay irefay issueay omfray anay
olday anday eautifulbay oakay ichwhay oodstay aboutay entytway ardsyay omfray ouray ousehay; anday osay
oonsay asay ethay azzlingday ightlay anishedvay, ethay oakay adhay isappearedday, anday othingnay
emainedray utbay aay astedblay umpstay. Enwhay eway isitedvay itay ethay extnay orningmay, eway oundfay
ethay eetray atteredshay inay aay ingularsay annermay. Itay asway otnay interedsplay byay ethay
ockshay, utbay entirelyay educedray otay inthay ibbonsray ofay oodway. Iay evernay eheldbay
anythingay osay utterlyay estroyedday.

Eforebay isthay Iay asway otnay unacquainteday ithway ethay oremay obviousay awslay ofay
electricityay. Onay isthay occasionay aay anmay ofay eatgray esearchray inay aturalnay
ilosophyphay asway ithway usay, anday exciteday byay isthay atastrophecay, ehay entereday onay
ethay explanationay ofay aay eorythay ichwhay ehay adhay ormedfay onay ethay ubjectsay ofay
electricityay anday alvanismgay, ichwhay asway atay onceay ewnay anday astonishingay otay emay.
Allay atthay ehay aidsay ewthray eatlygray intoay ethay adeshay Orneliuscay Agrippaay,
Albertusay Agnusmay, anday Aracelsuspay, ethay ordslay ofay myay imaginationay; utbay byay
omesay atalityfay ethay overthroway ofay esethay enmay isinclinedday emay otay ursuepay myay
accustomeday udiesstay. Itay eemedsay otay emay asay ifay othingnay ouldway oray ouldcay everay
ebay ownknay. Allay atthay adhay osay onglay engageday myay attentionay uddenlysay ewgray
espicableday. Byay oneay ofay osethay apricescay ofay ethay indmay ichwhay eway areay erhapspay
ostmay ubjectsay otay inay earlyay outhyay, Iay atay onceay avegay upay myay ormerfay
occupationsay, etsay ownday aturalnay istoryhay anday allay itsay ogenypray asay aay eformedday
anday abortiveay eationcray, anday entertaineday ethay eatestgray isdainday orfay aay
ould-beclay iencescay ichwhay ouldcay evernay evenay epstay ithinway ethay esholdthray ofay
ealray owledgeknay. Inay isthay oodmay ofay indmay Iay etookbay elfmysay otay ethay
athematicsmay anday ethay anchesbray ofay udystay appertainingay otay atthay iencescay asay
eingbay uiltbay uponay ecuresay oundationsfay, anday osay orthyway ofay myay onsiderationcay.

Usthay angelystray areay ouray oulssay onstructedcay, anday byay uchsay ightslay igamentslay
areay eway oundbay otay osperitypray oray uinray. Enwhay Iay ooklay ackbay, itay eemssay otay emay
asay ifay isthay almostay iraculousmay angechay ofay inclinationay anday illway asway ethay
immediateay uggestionsay ofay ethay uardiangay angelay ofay myay ife—thelay astlay effortay
ademay byay ethay iritspay ofay eservationpray otay avertay ethay ormstay atthay asway evenay
enthay anginghay inay ethay arsstay anday eadyray otay envelopay emay. Erhay ictoryvay asway
announceday byay anay unusualay anquillitytray anday adnessglay ofay oulsay ichwhay
ollowedfay ethay elinquishingray ofay myay ancientay anday atterlylay ormentingtay
udiesstay. Itay asway usthay atthay Iay asway otay ebay aughttay otay associateay evilay ithway
eirthay osecutionpray, appinesshay ithway eirthay isregardday.

Itay asway aay ongstray effortay ofay ethay iritspay ofay oodgay, utbay itay asway ineffectualay.
Estinyday asway ootay otentpay, anday erhay immutableay awslay adhay ecreedday myay utteray anday
erribletay estructionday.




Apterchay 3ay


Enwhay Iay adhay attaineday ethay ageay ofay eventeensay myay arentspay esolvedray atthay Iay
ouldshay ecomebay aay udentstay atay ethay universityay ofay Ingolstadtay. Iay adhay
ithertohay attendeday ethay oolsschay ofay Enevagay, utbay myay atherfay oughtthay itay
ecessarynay orfay ethay ompletioncay ofay myay educationay atthay Iay ouldshay ebay ademay
acquainteday ithway otheray ustomscay anthay osethay ofay myay ativenay ountrycay. Myay
epartureday asway ereforethay ixedfay atay anay earlyay ateday, utbay eforebay ethay ayday
esolvedray uponay ouldcay arriveay, ethay irstfay isfortunemay ofay myay ifelay
occurred—anay omenay, asay itay ereway, ofay myay uturefay iserymay.

Elizabethay adhay aughtcay ethay arletscay everfay; erhay illnessay asway everesay, anday eshay asway
inay ethay eatestgray angerday. Uringday erhay illnessay anymay argumentsay adhay eenbay urgeday otay
ersuadepay myay othermay otay efrainray omfray attendingay uponay erhay. Eshay adhay atay irstfay
ieldedyay otay ouray entreatiesay, utbay enwhay eshay eardhay atthay ethay ifelay ofay erhay
avouritefay asway enacedmay, eshay ouldcay onay ongerlay ontrolcay erhay anxietyay. Eshay
attendeday erhay ickbedsay; erhay atchfulway attentionsay iumphedtray overay ethay alignitymay
ofay ethay istemper—Elizabethday asway avedsay, utbay ethay onsequencescay ofay isthay
imprudenceay ereway atalfay otay erhay eserverpray. Onay ethay irdthay ayday myay othermay
ickenedsay; erhay everfay asway accompanieday byay ethay ostmay alarmingay omssymptay, anday ethay
ookslay ofay erhay edicalmay attendantsay ognosticatedpray ethay orstway eventay. Onay erhay
eathbedday ethay ortitudefay anday enignitybay ofay isthay estbay ofay omenway idday otnay esertday
erhay. Eshay oinedjay ethay andshay ofay Elizabethay anday elfmysay. “myay
ildrenchay,” eshay aidsay, “myay irmestfay opeshay ofay uturefay appinesshay ereway
acedplay onay ethay ospectpray ofay ouryay unionay. Isthay expectationay illway ownay ebay ethay
onsolationcay ofay ouryay atherfay. Elizabethay, myay ovelay, ouyay ustmay upplysay myay aceplay otay
myay oungeryay ildrenchay. Alasay! Iay egretray atthay Iay amay akentay omfray ouyay; anday, appyhay
anday elovedbay asay Iay avehay eenbay, isay itay otnay ardhay otay uitqay ouyay allay? Utbay esethay areay
otnay oughtsthay efittingbay emay; Iay illway endeavouray otay esignray elfmysay eerfullychay otay
eathday anday illway indulgeay aay opehay ofay eetingmay ouyay inay anotheray orldway.”

Eshay iedday almlycay, anday erhay ountenancecay expresseday affectionay evenay inay eathday.
Iay eednay otnay escribeday ethay eelingsfay ofay osethay osewhay earestday iestay areay entray
byay atthay ostmay irreparableay evilay, ethay oidvay atthay esentspray itselfay otay ethay
oulsay, anday ethay espairday atthay isay exhibiteday onay ethay ountenancecay. Itay isay osay
onglay eforebay ethay indmay ancay ersuadepay itselfay atthay eshay omwhay eway awsay everyay ayday
anday osewhay eryvay existenceay appeareday aay artpay ofay ouray ownay ancay avehay epartedday
orfay ever—thatay ethay ightnessbray ofay aay elovedbay eyeay ancay avehay eenbay
extinguisheday anday ethay oundsay ofay aay oicevay osay amiliarfay anday earday otay ethay earay
ancay ebay ushedhay, evernay oremay otay ebay eardhay. Esethay areay ethay eflectionsray ofay
ethay irstfay aysday; utbay enwhay ethay apselay ofay imetay ovespray ethay ealityray ofay ethay
evilay, enthay ethay actualay itternessbay ofay iefgray ommencescay. Etyay omfray omwhay ashay
otnay atthay uderay andhay entray awayay omesay earday onnectioncay? Anday whyay ouldshay Iay
escribeday aay orrowsay ichwhay allay avehay eltfay, anday ustmay eelfay? Ethay imetay atay
engthlay arrivesay enwhay iefgray isay atherray anay indulgenceay anthay aay ecessitynay; anday
ethay ilesmay atthay aysplay uponay ethay ipslay, althoughay itay aymay ebay eemedday aay
acrilegesay, isay otnay anishedbay. Myay othermay asway eadday, utbay eway adhay illstay
utiesday ichwhay eway oughtay otay erformpay; eway ustmay ontinuecay ouray oursecay ithway ethay
estray anday earnlay otay inkthay ourselvesay ortunatefay ilstwhay oneay emainsray omwhay ethay
oilerspay ashay otnay eizedsay.

Myay epartureday orfay Ingolstadtay, ichwhay adhay eenbay eferredday byay esethay eventsay,
asway ownay againay eterminedday uponay. Iay obtaineday omfray myay atherfay aay espiteray ofay
omesay eeksway. Itay appeareday otay emay acrilegesay osay oonsay otay eavelay ethay eposeray,
akinay otay eathday, ofay ethay ousehay ofay ourningmay anday otay ushray intoay ethay ickthay ofay
ifelay. Iay asway ewnay otay orrowsay, utbay itay idday otnay ethay esslay alarmay emay. Iay asway
unwillingay otay uitqay ethay ightsay ofay osethay atthay emainedray otay emay, anday aboveay
allay, Iay esiredday otay eesay myay eetsway Elizabethay inay omesay egreeday onsoledcay.

Eshay indeeday eiledvay erhay iefgray anday ovestray otay actay ethay omfortercay otay usay allay.
Eshay ookedlay eadilystay onay ifelay anday assumeday itsay utiesday ithway ouragecay anday
ealzay. Eshay evotedday erselfhay otay osethay omwhay eshay adhay eenbay aughttay otay allcay
erhay uncleay anday ousinscay. Evernay asway eshay osay enchantingay asay atay isthay imetay,
enwhay eshay ecalledray ethay unshinesay ofay erhay ilessmay anday entspay emthay uponay usay.
Eshay orgotfay evenay erhay ownay egretray inay erhay endeavoursay otay akemay usay orgetfay.

Ethay ayday ofay myay epartureday atay engthlay arriveday. Ervalclay entspay ethay astlay
eveningay ithway usay. Ehay adhay endeavoureday otay ersuadepay ishay atherfay otay ermitpay
imhay otay accompanyay emay anday otay ecomebay myay ellowfay udentstay, utbay inay ainvay. Ishay
atherfay asway aay arrow-mindedclay adertray anday awsay idlenessay anday uinray inay ethay
aspirationsay anday ambitionay ofay ishay onsay. Enryhay eeplyday eltfay ethay isfortunemay
ofay eingbay ebarredday omfray aay iberallay educationay. Ehay aidsay ittlelay, utbay enwhay
ehay okespay Iay eadray inay ishay indlingkay eyeay anday inay ishay animateday anceglay aay
estrainedray utbay irmfay esolveray otnay otay ebay ainedchay otay ethay iserablemay etailsday
ofay ommercecay.

Eway atsay atelay. Eway ouldcay otnay eartay ourselvesay awayay omfray eachay otheray ornay
ersuadepay ourselvesay otay aysay ethay ordway arewell“fay!” Itay asway aidsay, anday eway
etiredray underay ethay etencepray ofay eekingsay eposeray, eachay ancyingfay atthay ethay
otheray asway eceivedday; utbay enwhay atay orning’smay awnday Iay escendedday otay ethay
arriagecay ichwhay asway otay onveycay emay awayay, eythay ereway allay ere—mythay atherfay
againay otay essblay emay, Ervalclay otay esspray myay andhay onceay oremay, myay Elizabethay otay
enewray erhay entreatiesay atthay Iay ouldway itewray oftenay anday otay estowbay ethay astlay
emininefay attentionsay onay erhay aymateplay anday iendfray.
