Iay ewthray elfmysay intoay ethay aisechay atthay asway otay onveycay emay awayay anday indulgeday inay
ethay ostmay elancholymay eflectionsray. Iay, owhay adhay everay eenbay urroundedsay byay
amiableay ompanionscay, ontinuallycay engageday inay endeavouringay otay estowbay utualmay
easure—Iplay asway ownay aloneay. Inay ethay universityay itherwhay Iay asway oinggay Iay
ustmay ormfay myay ownay iendsfray anday ebay myay ownay otectorpray. Myay ifelay adhay ithertohay
eenbay emarkablyray ecludedsay anday omesticday, anday isthay adhay ivengay emay invincibleay
epugnanceray otay ewnay ountenancescay. Iay ovedlay myay othersbray, Elizabethay, anday
Ervalclay; esethay ereway old“ay amiliarfay acesfay,” utbay Iay elievedbay elfmysay
otallytay unfitteday orfay ethay ompanycay ofay angersstray. Uchsay ereway myay eflectionsray asay
Iay ommencedcay myay ourneyjay; utbay asay Iay oceededpray, myay iritsspay anday opeshay oseray. Iay
ardentlyay esiredday ethay acquisitionay ofay owledgeknay. Iay adhay oftenay, enwhay atay omehay,
oughtthay itay ardhay otay emainray uringday myay outhyay oopedcay upay inay oneay aceplay anday adhay
ongedlay otay enteray ethay orldway anday aketay myay ationstay amongay otheray umanhay eingsbay.
Ownay myay esiresday ereway ompliedcay ithway, anday itay ouldway, indeeday, avehay eenbay ollyfay otay
epentray.

Iay adhay ufficientsay eisurelay orfay esethay anday anymay otheray eflectionsray uringday myay
ourneyjay otay Ingolstadtay, ichwhay asway onglay anday atiguingfay. Atay engthlay ethay
ighhay itewhay eeplestay ofay ethay owntay etmay myay eyesay. Iay alighteday anday asway
onductedcay otay myay olitarysay apartmentay otay endspay ethay eveningay asay Iay easedplay.

Ethay extnay orningmay Iay eliveredday myay etterslay ofay introductionay anday aidpay aay isitvay otay
omesay ofay ethay incipalpray ofessorspray. Ance—orchay atherray ethay evilay
influenceay, ethay Angelay ofay Estructionday, ichwhay asserteday omnipotentay aysway overay emay
omfray ethay omentmay Iay urnedtay myay eluctantray epsstay omfray myay ather’sfay
oor—ledday emay irstfay otay May. Empekray, ofessorpray ofay aturalnay ilosophyphay. Ehay
asway anay uncouthay anmay, utbay eeplyday imbueday inay ethay ecretssay ofay ishay iencescay. Ehay
askeday emay everalsay uestionsqay oncerningcay myay ogresspray inay ethay ifferentday anchesbray
ofay iencescay appertainingay otay aturalnay ilosophyphay. Iay epliedray arelesslycay, anday
artlypay inay ontemptcay, entionedmay ethay amesnay ofay myay alchemistsay asay ethay incipalpray
authorsay Iay adhay udiedstay. Ethay ofessorpray aredstay. ave“hay ouyay,” ehay
aidsay, eally“ray entspay ouryay imetay inay udyingstay uchsay onsensenay?”

Iay epliedray inay ethay affirmativeay. Every“ay inutemay,” ontinuedcay May. Empekray ithway
armthway, every“ay instantay atthay ouyay avehay astedway onay osethay ooksbay isay utterlyay
anday entirelyay ostlay. Ouyay avehay urdenedbay ouryay emorymay ithway explodeday emssystay
anday uselessay amesnay. Oodgay Odgay! Inay atwhay esertday andlay avehay ouyay ivedlay,
erewhay onay oneay asway indkay enoughay otay informay ouyay atthay esethay anciesfay ichwhay ouyay
avehay osay eedilygray imbibeday areay aay ousandthay earsyay olday anday asay ustymay asay eythay
areay ancientay? Iay ittlelay expecteday, inay isthay enlighteneday anday ientificscay
ageay, otay indfay aay iscipleday ofay Albertusay Agnusmay anday Aracelsuspay. Myay earday
irsay, ouyay ustmay eginbay ouryay udiesstay entirelyay aneway.”

Osay ayingsay, ehay eppedstay asideay anday otewray ownday aay istlay ofay everalsay ooksbay
eatingtray ofay aturalnay ilosophyphay ichwhay ehay esiredday emay otay ocurepray, anday
ismissedday emay afteray entioningmay atthay inay ethay eginningbay ofay ethay ollowingfay
eekway ehay intendeday otay ommencecay aay oursecay ofay ectureslay uponay aturalnay
ilosophyphay inay itsay eneralgay elationsray, anday atthay May. Aldmanway, aay ellowfay
ofessorpray, ouldway ecturelay uponay emistrychay ethay alternateay aysday atthay ehay
omitteday.

Iay eturnedray omehay otnay isappointedday, orfay Iay avehay aidsay atthay Iay adhay onglay
onsideredcay osethay authorsay uselessay omwhay ethay ofessorpray eprobatedray; utbay Iay
eturnedray otnay atay allay ethay oremay inclineday otay ecurray otay esethay udiesstay inay anyay
apeshay. May. Empekray asway aay ittlelay uatsqay anmay ithway aay uffgray oicevay anday aay
epulsiveray ountenancecay; ethay eachertay, ereforethay, idday otnay epossesspray emay inay
avourfay ofay ishay ursuitspay. Inay atherray aay ootay ilosophicalphay anday onnectedcay aay
ainstray, erhapspay, Iay avehay ivengay anay accountay ofay ethay onclusionscay Iay adhay omecay
otay oncerningcay emthay inay myay earlyay earsyay. Asay aay ildchay Iay adhay otnay eenbay
ontentcay ithway ethay esultsray omisedpray byay ethay odernmay ofessorspray ofay aturalnay
iencescay. Ithway aay onfusioncay ofay ideasay onlyay otay ebay accounteday orfay byay myay
extremeay outhyay anday myay antway ofay aay uidegay onay uchsay attersmay, Iay adhay etrodray ethay
epsstay ofay owledgeknay alongay ethay athspay ofay imetay anday exchangeday ethay
iscoveriesday ofay ecentray inquirersay orfay ethay eamsdray ofay orgottenfay alchemistsay.
Esidesbay, Iay adhay aay ontemptcay orfay ethay usesay ofay odernmay aturalnay ilosophyphay.
Itay asway eryvay ifferentday enwhay ethay astersmay ofay ethay iencescay oughtsay
immortalityay anday owerpay; uchsay iewsvay, althoughay utilefay, ereway andgray; utbay ownay
ethay enescay asway angedchay. Ethay ambitionay ofay ethay inquireray eemedsay otay imitlay
itselfay otay ethay annihilationay ofay osethay isionsvay onay ichwhay myay interestay inay
iencescay asway ieflychay oundedfay. Iay asway equiredray otay exchangeay imeraschay ofay
oundlessbay andeurgray orfay ealitiesray ofay ittlelay orthway.

Uchsay ereway myay eflectionsray uringday ethay irstfay otway oray eethray aysday ofay myay
esidenceray atay Ingolstadtay, ichwhay ereway ieflychay entspay inay ecomingbay
acquainteday ithway ethay ocalitieslay anday ethay incipalpray esidentsray inay myay ewnay
abodeay. Utbay asay ethay ensuingay eekway ommencedcay, Iay oughtthay ofay ethay informationay
ichwhay May. Empekray adhay ivengay emay oncerningcay ethay ectureslay. Anday althoughay Iay
ouldcay otnay onsentcay otay ogay anday earhay atthay ittlelay onceitedcay ellowfay eliverday
entencessay outay ofay aay ulpitpay, Iay ecollectedray atwhay ehay adhay aidsay ofay May.
Aldmanway, omwhay Iay adhay evernay eensay, asay ehay adhay ithertohay eenbay outay ofay owntay.

Artlypay omfray uriositycay anday artlypay omfray idlenessay, Iay entway intoay ethay ecturinglay
oomray, ichwhay May. Aldmanway entereday ortlyshay afteray. Isthay ofessorpray asway eryvay
unlikeay ishay olleaguecay. Ehay appeareday aboutay iftyfay earsyay ofay ageay, utbay ithway anay
aspectay expressiveay ofay ethay eatestgray enevolencebay; aay ewfay eygray airshay overedcay ishay
emplestay, utbay osethay atay ethay ackbay ofay ishay eadhay ereway earlynay ackblay. Ishay ersonpay
asway ortshay utbay emarkablyray erectay anday ishay oicevay ethay eetestsway Iay adhay everay eardhay.
Ehay eganbay ishay ecturelay byay aay ecapitulationray ofay ethay istoryhay ofay emistrychay anday
ethay ariousvay improvementsay ademay byay ifferentday enmay ofay earninglay, onouncingpray
ithway ervourfay ethay amesnay ofay ethay ostmay istinguishedday iscoverersday. Ehay enthay ooktay
aay ursorycay iewvay ofay ethay esentpray atestay ofay ethay iencescay anday explaineday anymay ofay
itsay elementaryay ermstay. Afteray avinghay ademay aay ewfay eparatorypray experimentsay, ehay
oncludedcay ithway aay anegyricpay uponay odernmay emistrychay, ethay ermstay ofay ichwhay Iay
allshay evernay orgetfay:

e“thay ancientay eacherstay ofay isthay iencescay,” aidsay ehay,
omised“pray impossibilitiesay anday erformedpay othingnay. Ethay odernmay astersmay
omisepray eryvay ittlelay; eythay owknay atthay etalsmay annotcay ebay ansmutedtray anday atthay
ethay elixiray ofay ifelay isay aay imerachay utbay esethay ilosophersphay, osewhay andshay eemsay
onlyay ademay otay abbleday inay irtday, anday eirthay eyesay otay orepay overay ethay icroscopemay oray
uciblecray, avehay indeeday erformedpay iraclesmay. Eythay enetratepay intoay ethay ecessesray
ofay aturenay anday owshay owhay eshay orksway inay erhay iding-placesclay. Eythay ascenday intoay ethay
eavenshay; eythay avehay iscoveredday owhay ethay oodblay irculatescay, anday ethay aturenay ofay
ethay airay eway eathebray. Eythay avehay acquireday ewnay anday almostay unlimiteday owerspay;
eythay ancay ommandcay ethay understhay ofay eavenhay, imicmay ethay earthquakeay, anday evenay
ockmay ethay invisibleay orldway ithway itsay ownay adowsshay.”

Uchsay ereway ethay ofessor’spray ords—ratherway etlay emay aysay uchsay ethay ordsway ofay
ethay ate—enouncedfay otay estroyday emay. Asay ehay entway onay Iay eltfay asay ifay myay oulsay
ereway applinggray ithway aay alpablepay enemyay; oneay byay oneay ethay ariousvay eyskay ereway
ouchedtay ichwhay ormedfay ethay echanismmay ofay myay eingbay; ordchay afteray ordchay asway
oundedsay, anday oonsay myay indmay asway illedfay ithway oneay oughtthay, oneay onceptioncay,
oneay urposepay. Osay uchmay ashay eenbay oneday, exclaimeday ethay oulsay ofay
Ankenstein—morefray, arfay oremay, illway Iay achieveay; eadingtray inay ethay epsstay
alreadyay arkedmay, Iay illway ioneerpay aay ewnay ayway, exploreay unknownay owerspay, anday
unfolday otay ethay orldway ethay eepestday eriesmystay ofay eationcray.

Iay osedclay otnay myay eyesay atthay ightnay. Myay internalay eingbay asway inay aay atestay ofay
insurrectionay anday urmoiltay; Iay eltfay atthay orderay ouldway encethay ariseay, utbay Iay
adhay onay owerpay otay oducepray itay. Byay egreesday, afteray ethay orning’smay awnday,
eepslay amecay. Iay awokeay, anday myay esternight’syay oughtsthay ereway asay aay eamdray.
Erethay onlyay emainedray aay esolutionray otay eturnray otay myay ancientay udiesstay anday otay
evoteday elfmysay otay aay iencescay orfay ichwhay Iay elievedbay elfmysay otay ossesspay aay
aturalnay alenttay. Onay ethay amesay ayday Iay aidpay May. Aldmanway aay isitvay. Ishay
annersmay inay ivatepray ereway evenay oremay ildmay anday attractiveay anthay inay ublicpay,
orfay erethay asway aay ertaincay ignityday inay ishay ienmay uringday ishay ecturelay ichwhay inay
ishay ownay ousehay asway eplacedray byay ethay eatestgray affabilityay anday indnesskay. Iay
avegay imhay ettypray earlynay ethay amesay accountay ofay myay ormerfay ursuitspay asay Iay adhay
ivengay otay ishay ellowfay ofessorpray. Ehay eardhay ithway attentionay ethay ittlelay
arrationnay oncerningcay myay udiesstay anday iledsmay atay ethay amesnay ofay Orneliuscay
Agrippaay anday Aracelsuspay, utbay ithoutway ethay ontemptcay atthay May. Empekray adhay
exhibiteday. Ehay aidsay atthay ese“thay ereway enmay otay osewhay indefatigableay ealzay
odernmay ilosophersphay ereway indebteday orfay ostmay ofay ethay oundationsfay ofay eirthay
owledgeknay. Eythay adhay eftlay otay usay, asay anay easieray asktay, otay ivegay ewnay amesnay
anday arrangeay inay onnectedcay assificationsclay ethay actsfay ichwhay eythay inay aay
eatgray egreeday adhay eenbay ethay instrumentsay ofay ingingbray otay ightlay. Ethay
abourslay ofay enmay ofay eniusgay, oweverhay erroneouslyay irectedday, arcelyscay everay
ailfay inay ultimatelyay urningtay otay ethay olidsay advantageay ofay ankindmay.” Iay
istenedlay otay ishay atementstay, ichwhay asway eliveredday ithoutway anyay esumptionpray
oray affectationay, anday enthay addeday atthay ishay ecturelay adhay emovedray myay
ejudicespray againstay odernmay emistschay; Iay expresseday elfmysay inay easuredmay
ermstay, ithway ethay odestymay anday eferenceday ueday omfray aay outhyay otay ishay
instructoray, ithoutway ettinglay escapeay inexperience(ay inay ifelay ouldway avehay
ademay emay ashameday) anyay ofay ethay enthusiasmay ichwhay imulatedstay myay intendeday
abourslay. Iay equestedray ishay adviceay oncerningcay ethay ooksbay Iay oughtay otay
ocurepray.

I“ay amay appyhay,” aidsay May. Aldmanway, o“tay avehay ainedgay aay
iscipleday; anday ifay ouryay applicationay equalsay ouryay abilityay, Iay avehay onay oubtday ofay
ouryay uccesssay. Emistrychay isay atthay anchbray ofay aturalnay ilosophyphay inay ichwhay ethay
eatestgray improvementsay avehay eenbay anday aymay ebay ademay; itay isay onay atthay accountay atthay
Iay avehay ademay itay myay eculiarpay udystay; utbay atay ethay amesay imetay, Iay avehay otnay
eglectednay ethay otheray anchesbray ofay iencescay. Aay anmay ouldway akemay utbay aay eryvay orrysay
emistchay ifay ehay attendeday otay atthay epartmentday ofay umanhay owledgeknay aloneay. Ifay ouryay
ishway isay otay ecomebay eallyray aay anmay ofay iencescay anday otnay erelymay aay ettypay
experimentalistay, Iay ouldshay adviseay ouyay otay applyay otay everyay anchbray ofay aturalnay
ilosophyphay, includingay athematicsmay.”

Ehay enthay ooktay emay intoay ishay aboratorylay anday explaineday otay emay ethay usesay ofay ishay
ariousvay achinesmay, instructingay emay asay otay atwhay Iay oughtay otay ocurepray anday
omisingpray emay ethay useay ofay ishay ownay enwhay Iay ouldshay avehay advanceday arfay enoughay inay
ethay iencescay otnay otay erangeday eirthay echanismmay. Ehay alsoay avegay emay ethay istlay ofay
ooksbay ichwhay Iay adhay equestedray, anday Iay ooktay myay eavelay.

Usthay endeday aay ayday emorablemay otay emay; itay ecidedday myay uturefay estinyday.




Apterchay 4ay


Omfray isthay ayday aturalnay ilosophyphay, anday articularlypay emistrychay, inay ethay
ostmay omprehensivecay ensesay ofay ethay ermtay, ecamebay earlynay myay olesay occupationay.
Iay eadray ithway ardouray osethay orksway, osay ullfay ofay eniusgay anday iscriminationday,
ichwhay odernmay inquirersay avehay ittenwray onay esethay ubjectssay. Iay attendeday ethay
ectureslay anday ultivatedcay ethay acquaintanceay ofay ethay enmay ofay iencescay ofay ethay
universityay, anday Iay oundfay evenay inay May. Empekray aay eatgray ealday ofay oundsay ensesay
anday ealray informationay, ombinedcay, itay isay uetray, ithway aay epulsiveray
iognomyphysay anday annersmay, utbay otnay onay atthay accountay ethay esslay aluablevay. Inay
May. Aldmanway Iay oundfay aay uetray iendfray. Ishay entlenessgay asway evernay ingedtay byay
ogmatismday, anday ishay instructionsay ereway ivengay ithway anay airay ofay anknessfray anday
oodgay aturenay atthay anishedbay everyay ideaay ofay edantrypay. Inay aay ousandthay aysway
ehay oothedsmay orfay emay ethay athpay ofay owledgeknay anday ademay ethay ostmay abstruseay
inquiriesay earclay anday acilefay otay myay apprehensionay. Myay applicationay asway atay
irstfay uctuatingflay anday uncertainay; itay ainedgay engthstray asay Iay oceededpray anday
oonsay ecamebay osay ardentay anday eageray atthay ethay arsstay oftenay isappearedday inay ethay
ightlay ofay orningmay ilstwhay Iay asway etyay engageday inay myay aboratorylay.

Asay Iay applieday osay oselyclay, itay aymay ebay easilyay onceivedcay atthay myay ogresspray
asway apidray. Myay ardouray asway indeeday ethay astonishmentay ofay ethay udentsstay, anday
myay oficiencypray atthay ofay ethay astersmay. Ofessorpray Empekray oftenay askeday emay,
ithway aay slyay ilesmay, owhay Orneliuscay Agrippaay entway onay, ilstwhay May. Aldmanway
expresseday ethay ostmay eartfelthay exultationay inay myay ogresspray. Otway earsyay
assedpay inay isthay annermay, uringday ichwhay Iay aidpay onay isitvay otay Enevagay, utbay asway
engageday, earthay anday oulsay, inay ethay ursuitpay ofay omesay iscoveriesday ichwhay Iay
opedhay otay akemay. Onenay utbay osethay owhay avehay experienceday emthay ancay onceivecay
ofay ethay enticementsay ofay iencescay. Inay otheray udiesstay ouyay ogay asay arfay asay
othersay avehay onegay eforebay ouyay, anday erethay isay othingnay oremay otay owknay; utbay inay
aay ientificscay ursuitpay erethay isay ontinualcay oodfay orfay iscoveryday anday onderway.
Aay indmay ofay oderatemay apacitycay ichwhay oselyclay ursuespay oneay udystay ustmay
infalliblyay arriveay atay eatgray oficiencypray inay atthay udystay; anday Iay, owhay
ontinuallycay oughtsay ethay attainmentay ofay oneay objectay ofay ursuitpay anday asway
olelysay appedwray upay inay isthay, improveday osay apidlyray atthay atay ethay enday ofay otway
earsyay Iay ademay omesay iscoveriesday inay ethay improvementay ofay omesay emicalchay
instrumentsay, ichwhay ocuredpray emay eatgray esteemay anday admirationay atay ethay
universityay. Enwhay Iay adhay arriveday atay isthay ointpay anday adhay ecomebay asay ellway
acquainteday ithway ethay eorythay anday acticepray ofay aturalnay ilosophyphay asay
ependedday onay ethay essonslay ofay anyay ofay ethay ofessorspray atay Ingolstadtay, myay
esidenceray erethay eingbay onay ongerlay onducivecay otay myay improvementsay, Iay oughtthay
ofay eturningray otay myay iendsfray anday myay ativenay owntay, enwhay anay incidentay
appenedhay atthay otractedpray myay aystay.

Oneay ofay ethay enomenaphay ichwhay adhay eculiarlypay attracteday myay attentionay asway
ethay ucturestray ofay ethay umanhay amefray, anday, indeeday, anyay animalay endueday ithway
ifelay. Encewhay, Iay oftenay askeday elfmysay, idday ethay inciplepray ofay ifelay oceedpray?
Itay asway aay oldbay uestionqay, anday oneay ichwhay ashay everay eenbay onsideredcay asay aay
erymystay; etyay ithway owhay anymay ingsthay areay eway uponay ethay inkbray ofay ecomingbay
acquainteday, ifay owardicecay oray arelessnesscay idday otnay estrainray ouray
inquiriesay. Iay evolvedray esethay ircumstancescay inay myay indmay anday eterminedday
enceforththay otay applyay elfmysay oremay articularlypay otay osethay anchesbray ofay
aturalnay ilosophyphay ichwhay elateray otay iologyphysay. Unlessay Iay adhay eenbay
animateday byay anay almostay upernaturalsay enthusiasmay, myay applicationay otay isthay
udystay ouldway avehay eenbay irksomeay anday almostay intolerableay. Otay examineay ethay
ausescay ofay ifelay, eway ustmay irstfay avehay ecourseray otay eathday. Iay ecamebay
acquainteday ithway ethay iencescay ofay anatomyay, utbay isthay asway otnay ufficientsay; Iay
ustmay alsoay observeay ethay aturalnay ecayday anday orruptioncay ofay ethay umanhay odybay.
Inay myay educationay myay atherfay adhay akentay ethay eatestgray ecautionspray atthay myay
indmay ouldshay ebay impresseday ithway onay upernaturalsay orrorshay. Iay oday otnay everay
ememberray otay avehay embledtray atay aay aletay ofay uperstitionsay oray otay avehay earedfay
ethay apparitionay ofay aay iritspay. Arknessday adhay onay effectay uponay myay ancyfay, anday
aay urchyardchay asway otay emay erelymay ethay eceptacleray ofay odiesbay eprivedday ofay
ifelay, ichwhay, omfray eingbay ethay eatsay ofay eautybay anday engthstray, adhay ecomebay
oodfay orfay ethay ormway. Ownay Iay asway edlay otay examineay ethay ausecay anday ogresspray ofay
isthay ecayday anday orcedfay otay endspay aysday anday ightsnay inay aultsvay anday
arnel-housesclay. Myay attentionay asway ixedfay uponay everyay objectay ethay ostmay
insupportableay otay ethay elicacyday ofay ethay umanhay eelingsfay. Iay awsay owhay ethay
inefay ormfay ofay anmay asway egradedday anday astedway; Iay eheldbay ethay orruptioncay ofay
eathday ucceedsay otay ethay oomingblay eekchay ofay ifelay; Iay awsay owhay ethay ormway
inheriteday ethay ondersway ofay ethay eyeay anday ainbray. Iay ausedpay, examiningay anday
analysingay allay ethay inutiaemay ofay ausationcay, asay exemplifieday inay ethay angechay
omfray ifelay otay eathday, anday eathday otay ifelay, untilay omfray ethay idstmay ofay isthay
arknessday aay uddensay ightlay okebray inay uponay e—amay ightlay osay illiantbray anday
ondrousway, etyay osay implesay, atthay ilewhay Iay ecamebay izzyday ithway ethay immensityay
ofay ethay ospectpray ichwhay itay illustrateday, Iay asway urprisedsay atthay amongay osay
anymay enmay ofay eniusgay owhay adhay irectedday eirthay inquiriesay owardstay ethay amesay
iencescay, atthay Iay aloneay ouldshay ebay eservedray otay iscoverday osay astonishingay aay
ecretsay.

Ememberray, Iay amay otnay ecordingray ethay isionvay ofay aay admanmay. Ethay unsay oesday otnay
oremay ertainlycay ineshay inay ethay eavenshay anthay atthay ichwhay Iay ownay affirmay isay
uetray. Omesay iraclemay ightmay avehay oducedpray itay, etyay ethay agesstay ofay ethay
iscoveryday ereway istinctday anday obablepray. Afteray aysday anday ightsnay ofay
incredibleay abourlay anday atiguefay, Iay ucceededsay inay iscoveringday ethay ausecay ofay
enerationgay anday ifelay; aynay, oremay, Iay ecamebay elfmysay apablecay ofay estowingbay
animationay uponay ifelesslay attermay.

Ethay astonishmentay ichwhay Iay adhay atay irstfay experienceday onay isthay iscoveryday
oonsay avegay aceplay otay elightday anday aptureray. Afteray osay uchmay imetay entspay inay
ainfulpay abourlay, otay arriveay atay onceay atay ethay ummitsay ofay myay esiresday asway ethay
ostmay atifyinggray onsummationcay ofay myay oilstay. Utbay isthay iscoveryday asway osay
eatgray anday overwhelmingay atthay allay ethay epsstay byay ichwhay Iay adhay eenbay
ogressivelypray edlay otay itay ereway obliterateday, anday Iay eheldbay onlyay ethay esultray.
Atwhay adhay eenbay ethay udystay anday esireday ofay ethay isestway enmay incesay ethay eationcray
ofay ethay orldway asway ownay ithinway myay aspgray. Otnay atthay, ikelay aay agicmay enescay, itay
allay openeday uponay emay atay onceay: ethay informationay Iay adhay obtaineday asway ofay aay
aturenay atherray otay irectday myay endeavoursay osay oonsay asay Iay ouldshay ointpay emthay
owardstay ethay objectay ofay myay earchsay anthay otay exhibitay atthay objectay alreadyay
accomplisheday. Iay asway ikelay ethay Arabianay owhay adhay eenbay uriedbay ithway ethay eadday
anday oundfay aay assagepay otay ifelay, aideday onlyay byay oneay immeringglay anday eeminglysay
ineffectualay ightlay.

Iay eesay byay ouryay eagernessay anday ethay onderway anday opehay ichwhay ouryay eyesay
expressay, myay iendfray, atthay ouyay expectay otay ebay informeday ofay ethay ecretsay ithway
ichwhay Iay amay acquainteday; atthay annotcay ebay; istenlay atientlypay untilay ethay enday
ofay myay orystay, anday ouyay illway easilyay erceivepay whyay Iay amay eservedray uponay atthay
ubjectsay. Iay illway otnay eadlay ouyay onay, unguardeday anday ardentay asay Iay enthay asway,
otay ouryay estructionday anday infallibleay iserymay. Earnlay omfray emay, ifay otnay byay myay
eceptspray, atay eastlay byay myay exampleay, owhay angerousday isay ethay acquirementay ofay
owledgeknay anday owhay uchmay appierhay atthay anmay isay owhay elievesbay ishay ativenay owntay
otay ebay ethay orldway, anthay ehay owhay aspiresay otay ecomebay eatergray anthay ishay aturenay
illway alloway.

Enwhay Iay oundfay osay astonishingay aay owerpay acedplay ithinway myay andshay, Iay esitatedhay
aay onglay imetay oncerningcay ethay annermay inay ichwhay Iay ouldshay employay itay.
Althoughay Iay ossessedpay ethay apacitycay ofay estowingbay animationay, etyay otay
eparepray aay amefray orfay ethay eceptionray ofay itay, ithway allay itsay intricaciesay ofay
ibresfay, usclesmay, anday einsvay, illstay emainedray aay orkway ofay inconceivableay
ifficultyday anday abourlay. Iay oubtedday atay irstfay etherwhay Iay ouldshay attemptay ethay
eationcray ofay aay eingbay ikelay elfmysay, oray oneay ofay implersay organizationay; utbay myay
imaginationay asway ootay uchmay exalteday byay myay irstfay uccesssay otay ermitpay emay otay
oubtday ofay myay abilityay otay ivegay ifelay otay anay animalay asay omplexcay anday onderfulway
asay anmay. Ethay aterialsmay atay esentpray ithinway myay ommandcay ardlyhay appeareday
adequateay otay osay arduousay anay undertakingay, utbay Iay oubtedday otnay atthay Iay ouldshay
ultimatelyay ucceedsay. Iay eparedpray elfmysay orfay aay ultitudemay ofay eversesray; myay
operationsay ightmay ebay incessantlyay affledbay, anday atay astlay myay orkway ebay
imperfectay, etyay enwhay Iay onsideredcay ethay improvementay ichwhay everyay ayday akestay
aceplay inay iencescay anday echanicsmay, Iay asway encourageday otay opehay myay esentpray
attemptsay ouldway atay eastlay aylay ethay oundationsfay ofay uturefay uccesssay. Ornay
ouldcay Iay onsidercay ethay agnitudemay anday omplexitycay ofay myay anplay asay anyay
argumentay ofay itsay impracticabilityay. Itay asway ithway esethay eelingsfay atthay Iay
eganbay ethay eationcray ofay aay umanhay eingbay. Asay ethay inutenessmay ofay ethay artspay
ormedfay aay eatgray indrancehay otay myay eedspay, Iay esolvedray, ontrarycay otay myay irstfay
intentionay, otay akemay ethay eingbay ofay aay iganticgay aturestay, atthay isay otay aysay,
aboutay eightay eetfay inay eighthay, anday oportionablypray argelay. Afteray avinghay
ormedfay isthay eterminationday anday avinghay entspay omesay onthsmay inay uccessfullysay
ollectingcay anday arrangingay myay aterialsmay, Iay eganbay.

Onay oneay ancay onceivecay ethay arietyvay ofay eelingsfay ichwhay orebay emay onwardsay, ikelay
aay urricanehay, inay ethay irstfay enthusiasmay ofay uccesssay. Ifelay anday eathday
appeareday otay emay idealay oundsbay, ichwhay Iay ouldshay irstfay eakbray oughthray, anday
ourpay aay orrenttay ofay ightlay intoay ouray arkday orldway. Aay ewnay eciesspay ouldway essblay
emay asay itsay eatorcray anday ourcesay; anymay appyhay anday excellentay aturesnay ouldway
oweay eirthay eingbay otay emay. Onay atherfay ouldcay aimclay ethay atitudegray ofay ishay
ildchay osay ompletelycay asay Iay ouldshay eserveday eirsthay. Ursuingpay esethay
eflectionsray, Iay oughtthay atthay ifay Iay ouldcay estowbay animationay uponay ifelesslay
attermay, Iay ightmay inay ocesspray ofay imetay although(ay Iay ownay oundfay itay impossibleay)
enewray ifelay erewhay eathday adhay apparentlyay evotedday ethay odybay otay orruptioncay.

Esethay oughtsthay upportedsay myay iritsspay, ilewhay Iay ursuedpay myay undertakingay
ithway unremittingay ardouray. Myay eekchay adhay owngray alepay ithway udystay, anday myay
ersonpay adhay ecomebay emaciateday ithway onfinementcay. Ometimessay, onay ethay eryvay
inkbray ofay ertaintycay, Iay ailedfay; etyay illstay Iay ungclay otay ethay opehay ichwhay ethay
extnay ayday oray ethay extnay ourhay ightmay ealiseray. Oneay ecretsay ichwhay Iay aloneay
ossessedpay asway ethay opehay otay ichwhay Iay adhay edicatedday elfmysay; anday ethay oonmay
azedgay onay myay idnightmay abourslay, ilewhay, ithway unrelaxeday anday eathlessbray
eagernessay, Iay ursuedpay aturenay otay erhay iding-placesclay. Owhay allshay onceivecay
ethay orrorshay ofay myay ecretsay oiltay asay Iay abbledday amongay ethay unhalloweday ampsday
ofay ethay avegray oray orturedtay ethay ivinglay animalay otay animateay ethay ifelesslay
ayclay? Myay imbslay ownay embletray, anday myay eyesay imsway ithway ethay emembranceray; utbay
enthay aay esistlessray anday almostay anticfray impulseay urgeday emay orwardfay; Iay eemedsay
otay avehay ostlay allay oulsay oray ensationsay utbay orfay isthay oneay ursuitpay. Itay asway
indeeday utbay aay assingpay ancetray, atthay onlyay ademay emay eelfay ithway enewedray
acutenessay osay oonsay asay, ethay unnaturalay imulusstay easingcay otay operateay, Iay adhay
eturnedray otay myay olday abitshay. Iay ollectedcay onesbay omfray arnel-housesclay anday
isturbedday, ithway ofanepray ingersfay, ethay emendoustray ecretssay ofay ethay umanhay
amefray. Inay aay olitarysay amberchay, oray atherray ellcay, atay ethay optay ofay ethay ousehay,
anday eparatedsay omfray allay ethay otheray apartmentsay byay aay allerygay anday aircasestay,
Iay eptkay myay orkshopway ofay ilthyfay eationcray; myay eyeballsay ereway artingstay omfray
eirthay ocketssay inay attendingay otay ethay etailsday ofay myay employmentay. Ethay
issectingday oomray anday ethay aughter-houseclay urnishedfay anymay ofay myay aterialsmay;
anday oftenay idday myay umanhay aturenay urntay ithway oathinglay omfray myay occupationay,
ilstwhay, illstay urgeday onay byay anay eagernessay ichwhay erpetuallypay increaseday, Iay
oughtbray myay orkway earnay otay aay onclusioncay.

Ethay ummersay onthsmay assedpay ilewhay Iay asway usthay engageday, earthay anday oulsay, inay
oneay ursuitpay. Itay asway aay ostmay eautifulbay easonsay; evernay idday ethay ieldsfay
estowbay aay oremay entifulplay arvesthay oray ethay inesvay ieldyay aay oremay uxuriantlay
intagevay, utbay myay eyesay ereway insensibleay otay ethay armschay ofay aturenay. Anday ethay
amesay eelingsfay ichwhay ademay emay eglectnay ethay enesscay arounday emay ausedcay emay alsoay
otay orgetfay osethay iendsfray owhay ereway osay anymay ilesmay absentay, anday omwhay Iay adhay
otnay eensay orfay osay onglay aay imetay. Iay ewknay myay ilencesay isquietedday emthay, anday Iay
ellway ememberedray ethay ordsway ofay myay atherfay: I“ay owknay atthay ilewhay ouyay areay
easedplay ithway ourselfyay ouyay illway inkthay ofay usay ithway affectionay, anday eway allshay
earhay egularlyray omfray ouyay. Ouyay ustmay ardonpay emay ifay Iay egardray anyay
interruptionay inay ouryay orrespondencecay asay aay oofpray atthay ouryay otheray utiesday
areay equallyay eglectednay.”

Iay ewknay ellway ereforethay atwhay ouldway ebay myay ather’sfay eelingsfay, utbay Iay ouldcay
otnay eartay myay oughtsthay omfray myay employmentay, oathsomelay inay itselfay, utbay ichwhay
adhay akentay anay irresistibleay oldhay ofay myay imaginationay. Iay ishedway, asay itay
ereway, otay ocrastinatepray allay atthay elatedray otay myay eelingsfay ofay affectionay
untilay ethay eatgray objectay, ichwhay allowedsway upay everyay abithay ofay myay aturenay,
ouldshay ebay ompletedcay.

Iay enthay oughtthay atthay myay atherfay ouldway ebay unjustay ifay ehay ascribeday myay eglectnay
otay icevay oray aultinessfay onay myay artpay, utbay Iay amay ownay onvincedcay atthay ehay asway
ustifiedjay inay onceivingcay atthay Iay ouldshay otnay ebay altogetheray eefray omfray
ameblay. Aay umanhay eingbay inay erfectionpay oughtay alwaysay otay eservepray aay almcay anday
eacefulpay indmay anday evernay otay alloway assionpay oray aay ansitorytray esireday otay
isturbday ishay anquillitytray. Iay oday otnay inkthay atthay ethay ursuitpay ofay owledgeknay
isay anay exceptionay otay isthay uleray. Ifay ethay udystay otay ichwhay ouyay applyay ourselfyay
ashay aay endencytay otay eakenway ouryay affectionsay anday otay estroyday ouryay astetay orfay
osethay implesay easuresplay inay ichwhay onay alloyay ancay ossiblypay ixmay, enthay atthay
udystay isay ertainlycay unlawfulay, atthay isay otay aysay, otnay efittingbay ethay umanhay
indmay. Ifay isthay uleray ereway alwaysay observeday; ifay onay anmay alloweday anyay ursuitpay
atsoeverwhay otay interfereay ithway ethay anquillitytray ofay ishay omesticday
affectionsay, Eecegray adhay otnay eenbay enslaveday, Arcæsay ouldway avehay aredspay ishay
ountrycay, Americaay ouldway avehay eenbay iscoveredday oremay aduallygray, anday ethay
empiresay ofay Exicomay anday Erupay adhay otnay eenbay estroyedday.

Utbay Iay orgetfay atthay Iay amay oralizingmay inay ethay ostmay interestingay artpay ofay myay
aletay, anday ouryay ookslay emindray emay otay oceedpray.

Myay atherfay ademay onay eproachray inay ishay etterslay anday onlyay ooktay oticenay ofay myay
ilencesay byay inquiringay intoay myay occupationsay oremay articularlypay anthay eforebay.
Interway, ingspray, anday ummersay assedpay awayay uringday myay abourslay; utbay Iay idday otnay
atchway ethay ossomblay oray ethay expandingay eaves—sightslay ichwhay eforebay alwaysay
ieldedyay emay upremesay elight—soday eeplyday asway Iay engrosseday inay myay
occupationay. Ethay eaveslay ofay atthay earyay adhay itheredway eforebay myay orkway ewdray earnay
otay aay oseclay, anday ownay everyay ayday owedshay emay oremay ainlyplay owhay ellway Iay adhay
ucceededsay. Utbay myay enthusiasmay asway eckedchay byay myay anxietyay, anday Iay appeareday
atherray ikelay oneay oomedday byay averyslay otay oiltay inay ethay inesmay, oray anyay otheray
unwholesomeay adetray anthay anay artistay occupieday byay ishay avouritefay employmentay.
Everyay ightnay Iay asway oppresseday byay aay owslay everfay, anday Iay ecamebay ervousnay otay aay ostmay
ainfulpay egreeday; ethay allfay ofay aay eaflay artledstay emay, anday Iay unnedshay myay ellowfay
eaturescray asay ifay Iay adhay eenbay uiltygay ofay aay imecray. Ometimessay Iay ewgray alarmeday atay
ethay eckwray Iay erceivedpay atthay Iay adhay ecomebay; ethay energyay ofay myay urposepay aloneay
ustainedsay emay: myay abourslay ouldway oonsay enday, anday Iay elievedbay atthay exerciseay anday
amusementay ouldway enthay ivedray awayay incipientay iseaseday; anday Iay omisedpray elfmysay
othbay ofay esethay enwhay myay eationcray ouldshay ebay ompletecay.




Apterchay 5ay


Itay asway onay aay earydray ightnay ofay Ovembernay atthay Iay eheldbay ethay accomplishmentay
ofay myay oilstay. Ithway anay anxietyay atthay almostay amounteday otay agonyay, Iay
ollectedcay ethay instrumentsay ofay ifelay arounday emay, atthay Iay ightmay infuseay aay
arkspay ofay eingbay intoay ethay ifelesslay ingthay atthay aylay atay myay eetfay. Itay asway
alreadyay oneay inay ethay orningmay; ethay ainray atteredpay ismallyday againstay ethay
anespay, anday myay andlecay asway earlynay urntbay outay, enwhay, byay ethay immerglay ofay ethay
alf-extinguishedclay ightlay, Iay awsay ethay ullday ellowyay eyeay ofay ethay eaturecray
openay; itay eathedbray ardhay, anday aay onvulsivecay otionmay agitateday itsay imbslay.

Owhay ancay Iay escribeday myay emotionsay atay isthay atastrophecay, oray owhay elineateday
ethay etchwray omwhay ithway uchsay infiniteay ainspay anday arecay Iay adhay endeavoureday otay
ormfay? Ishay imbslay ereway inay oportionpray, anday Iay adhay electedsay ishay eaturesfay asay
eautifulbay. Eautifulbay! Eatgray Odgay! Ishay ellowyay inskay arcelyscay overedcay
ethay orkway ofay usclesmay anday arteriesay eneathbay; ishay airhay asway ofay aay ustrouslay
ackblay, anday owingflay; ishay eethtay ofay aay earlypay itenesswhay; utbay esethay
uxurianceslay onlyay ormedfay aay oremay orridhay ontrastcay ithway ishay ateryway eyesay,
atthay eemedsay almostay ofay ethay amesay olourcay asay ethay un-whiteclay ocketssay inay ichwhay
eythay ereway etsay, ishay ivelledshray omplexioncay anday aightstray ackblay ipslay.

Ethay ifferentday accidentsay ofay ifelay areay otnay osay angeablechay asay ethay eelingsfay
ofay umanhay aturenay. Iay adhay orkedway ardhay orfay earlynay otway earsyay, orfay ethay olesay
urposepay ofay infusingay ifelay intoay anay inanimateay odybay. Orfay isthay Iay adhay
eprivedday elfmysay ofay estray anday ealthhay. Iay adhay esiredday itay ithway anay ardouray
atthay arfay exceededay oderationmay; utbay ownay atthay Iay adhay inishedfay, ethay eautybay
ofay ethay eamdray anishedvay, anday eathlessbray orrorhay anday isgustday illedfay myay
earthay. Unableay otay endureay ethay aspectay ofay ethay eingbay Iay adhay eatedcray, Iay
ushedray outay ofay ethay oomray anday ontinuedcay aay onglay imetay aversingtray myay
ed-chamberclay, unableay otay omposecay myay indmay otay eepslay. Atay engthlay assitudelay
ucceededsay otay ethay umulttay Iay adhay eforebay endureday, anday Iay ewthray elfmysay onay ethay
edbay inay myay othesclay, endeavouringay otay eeksay aay ewfay omentsmay ofay orgetfulnessfay.
Utbay itay asway inay ainvay; Iay eptslay, indeeday, utbay Iay asway isturbedday byay ethay ildestway
eamsdray. Iay oughtthay Iay awsay Elizabethay, inay ethay oomblay ofay ealthhay, alkingway inay
ethay eetsstray ofay Ingolstadtay. Elightedday anday urprisedsay, Iay embraceday erhay,
utbay asay Iay imprinteday ethay irstfay isskay onay erhay ipslay, eythay ecamebay ividlay ithway
ethay uehay ofay eathday; erhay eaturesfay appeareday otay angechay, anday Iay oughtthay atthay Iay
eldhay ethay orpsecay ofay myay eadday othermay inay myay armsay; aay oudshray envelopeday erhay
ormfay, anday Iay awsay ethay ave-wormsclay awlingcray inay ethay oldsfay ofay ethay annelflay.
Iay artedstay omfray myay eepslay ithway orrorhay; aay oldcay ewday overedcay myay oreheadfay, myay
eethtay atteredchay, anday everyay imblay ecamebay onvulsedcay; enwhay, byay ethay imday anday
ellowyay ightlay ofay ethay oonmay, asay itay orcedfay itsay ayway oughthray ethay indowway
uttersshay, Iay eheldbay ethay etch—thewray iserablemay onstermay omwhay Iay adhay
eatedcray. Ehay eldhay upay ethay urtaincay ofay ethay edbay; anday ishay eyesay, ifay eyesay eythay
aymay ebay alledcay, ereway ixedfay onay emay. Ishay awsjay openeday, anday ehay utteredmay omesay
inarticulateay oundssay, ilewhay aay ingray inkledwray ishay eekschay. Ehay ightmay avehay
okenspay, utbay Iay idday otnay earhay; oneay andhay asway etchedstray outay, eeminglysay otay
etainday emay, utbay Iay escapeday anday ushedray ownstairsday. Iay ooktay efugeray inay ethay
ourtyardcay elongingbay otay ethay ousehay ichwhay Iay inhabiteday, erewhay Iay emainedray
uringday ethay estray ofay ethay ightnay, alkingway upay anday ownday inay ethay eatestgray
agitationay, isteninglay attentivelyay, atchingcay anday earingfay eachay oundsay asay ifay
itay ereway otay announceay ethay approachay ofay ethay emoniacalday orpsecay otay ichwhay Iay
adhay osay iserablymay ivengay ifelay.

Ohay! Onay ortalmay ouldcay upportsay ethay orrorhay ofay atthay ountenancecay. Aay ummymay
againay endueday ithway animationay ouldcay otnay ebay osay ideoushay asay atthay etchwray. Iay
adhay azedgay onay imhay ilewhay unfinisheday; ehay asway uglyay enthay, utbay enwhay osethay
usclesmay anday ointsjay ereway enderedray apablecay ofay otionmay, itay ecamebay aay ingthay
uchsay asay evenay Anteday ouldcay otnay avehay onceivedcay.

Iay assedpay ethay ightnay etchedlywray. Ometimessay myay ulsepay eatbay osay uicklyqay anday
ardlyhay atthay Iay eltfay ethay alpitationpay ofay everyay arteryay; atay othersay, Iay earlynay
anksay otay ethay oundgray oughthray anguorlay anday extremeay eaknessway. Ingledmay ithway
isthay orrorhay, Iay eltfay ethay itternessbay ofay isappointmentday; eamsdray atthay adhay
eenbay myay oodfay anday easantplay estray orfay osay onglay aay acespay ereway ownay ecomebay aay
ellhay otay emay; anday ethay angechay asway osay apidray, ethay overthroway osay ompletecay!

Orningmay, ismalday anday etway, atay engthlay awnedday anday iscoveredday otay myay
eeplessslay anday achingay eyesay ethay urchchay ofay Ingolstadtay, itsay itewhay eeplestay
anday ockclay, ichwhay indicateday ethay ixthsay ourhay. Ethay orterpay openeday ethay atesgay
ofay ethay ourtcay, ichwhay adhay atthay ightnay eenbay myay asylumay, anday Iay issueday intoay
ethay eetsstray, acingpay emthay ithway uickqay epsstay, asay ifay Iay oughtsay otay avoiday ethay
etchwray omwhay Iay earedfay everyay urningtay ofay ethay eetstray ouldway esentpray otay myay
iewvay. Iay idday otnay areday eturnray otay ethay apartmentay ichwhay Iay inhabiteday, utbay
eltfay impelleday otay urryhay onay, althoughay encheddray byay ethay ainray ichwhay ouredpay
omfray aay ackblay anday omfortlesscay skyay.

Iay ontinuedcay alkingway inay isthay annermay orfay omesay imetay, endeavouringay byay
odilybay exerciseay otay easeay ethay oadlay atthay eighedway uponay myay indmay. Iay
aversedtray ethay eetsstray ithoutway anyay earclay onceptioncay ofay erewhay Iay asway oray
atwhay Iay asway oingday. Myay earthay alpitatedpay inay ethay icknesssay ofay earfay, anday Iay
urriedhay onay ithway irregularay epsstay, otnay aringday otay ooklay aboutay emay:

Ikelay oneay owhay, onay aay onelylay oadray,
Othday alkway inay earfay anday eaddray,
Anday, avinghay onceay urnedtay oundray, alksway onay,
Anday urnstay onay oremay ishay eadhay;
Ecausebay ehay owsknay aay ightfulfray iendfay
Othday oseclay ehindbay imhay eadtray.

oleridge’s[cay Ancient“ay Arinermay.”]



Ontinuingcay usthay, Iay amecay atay engthlay oppositeay otay ethay innay atay ichwhay ethay ariousvay
iligencesday anday arriagescay usuallyay oppedstay. Erehay Iay ausedpay, Iay ewknay otnay whyay;
utbay Iay emainedray omesay inutesmay ithway myay eyesay ixedfay onay aay oachcay atthay asway omingcay
owardstay emay omfray ethay otheray enday ofay ethay eetstray. Asay itay ewdray earernay Iay observeday
atthay itay asway ethay Isssway iligenceday; itay oppedstay ustjay erewhay Iay asway andingstay, anday
onay ethay oorday eingbay openeday, Iay erceivedpay Enryhay Ervalclay, owhay, onay eeingsay emay,
instantlyay ungspray outay. “myay earday Ankensteinfray,” exclaimeday ehay,
ow“hay adglay Iay amay otay eesay ouyay! Owhay ortunatefay atthay ouyay ouldshay ebay erehay atay
ethay eryvay omentmay ofay myay alightingay!”

Othingnay ouldcay equalay myay elightday onay eeingsay Ervalclay; ishay esencepray oughtbray ackbay
otay myay oughtsthay myay atherfay, Elizabethay, anday allay osethay enesscay ofay omehay osay earday
otay myay ecollectionray. Iay aspedgray ishay andhay, anday inay aay omentmay orgotfay myay orrorhay
anday isfortunemay; Iay eltfay uddenlysay, anday orfay ethay irstfay imetay uringday anymay onthsmay,
almcay anday erenesay oyjay. Iay elcomedway myay iendfray, ereforethay, inay ethay ostmay ordialcay
annermay, anday eway alkedway owardstay myay ollegecay. Ervalclay ontinuedcay alkingtay orfay
omesay imetay aboutay ouray utualmay iendsfray anday ishay ownay oodgay ortunefay inay eingbay
ermittedpay otay omecay otay Ingolstadtay. ou“yay aymay easilyay elievebay,” aidsay
ehay, ow“hay eatgray asway ethay ifficultyday otay ersuadepay myay atherfay atthay allay
ecessarynay owledgeknay asway otnay omprisedcay inay ethay oblenay artay ofay ook-keepingclay;
anday, indeeday, Iay elievebay Iay eftlay imhay incredulousay otay ethay astlay, orfay ishay onstantcay
answeray otay myay unwearieday entreatiesay asway ethay amesay asay atthay ofay ethay Utchday
oolmasterschay inay Ethay Icarvay ofay Akefieldway: I‘ay avehay entay ousandthay orinsflay
aay earyay ithoutway Eekgray, Iay eatay eartilyhay ithoutway Eekgray.’ Utbay ishay
affectionay orfay emay atay engthlay overcameay ishay islikeday ofay earninglay, anday ehay ashay
ermittedpay emay otay undertakeay aay oyagevay ofay iscoveryday otay ethay andlay ofay
owledgeknay.”

It“ay ivesgay emay ethay eatestgray elightday otay eesay ouyay; utbay elltay emay owhay ouyay eftlay
myay atherfay, othersbray, anday Elizabethay.”

ery“vay ellway, anday eryvay appyhay, onlyay aay ittlelay uneasyay atthay eythay earhay omfray
ouyay osay eldomsay. Byay ethay byay, Iay eanmay otay ecturelay ouyay aay ittlelay uponay eirthay
accountay elfmysay. Utbay, myay earday Ankensteinfray,” ontinuedcay ehay, oppingstay
ortshay anday azinggay ullfay inay myay acefay, I“ay idday otnay eforebay emarkray owhay eryvay illay
ouyay appearay; osay inthay anday alepay; ouyay ooklay asay ifay ouyay adhay eenbay atchingway orfay
everalsay ightsnay.”

ou“yay avehay uessedgay ightray; Iay avehay atelylay eenbay osay eeplyday engageday inay oneay
occupationay atthay Iay avehay otnay alloweday elfmysay ufficientsay estray, asay ouyay eesay;
utbay Iay opehay, Iay incerelysay opehay, atthay allay esethay employmentsay areay ownay atay anay
enday anday atthay Iay amay atay engthlay eefray.”

Iay embledtray excessivelyay; Iay ouldcay otnay endureay otay inkthay ofay, anday arfay esslay otay
alludeay otay, ethay occurrencesay ofay ethay ecedingpray ightnay. Iay alkedway ithway aay
uickqay acepay, anday eway oonsay arriveday atay myay ollegecay. Iay enthay eflectedray, anday
ethay oughtthay ademay emay ivershay, atthay ethay eaturecray omwhay Iay adhay eftlay inay myay
apartmentay ightmay illstay ebay erethay, aliveay anday alkingway aboutay. Iay eadeddray otay
eholdbay isthay onstermay, utbay Iay earedfay illstay oremay atthay Enryhay ouldshay eesay imhay.
Entreatingay imhay, ereforethay, otay emainray aay ewfay inutesmay atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay
airsstay, Iay artedday upay owardstay myay ownay oomray. Myay andhay asway alreadyay onay ethay
ocklay ofay ethay oorday eforebay Iay ecollectedray elfmysay. Iay enthay ausedpay, anday aay
oldcay iveringshay amecay overay emay. Iay ewthray ethay oorday orciblyfay openay, asay
ildrenchay areay accustomeday otay oday enwhay eythay expectay aay ectrespay otay andstay inay
aitingway orfay emthay onay ethay otheray idesay; utbay othingnay appeareday. Iay eppedstay
earfullyfay inay: ethay apartmentay asway emptyay, anday myay edroombay asway alsoay eedfray
omfray itsay ideoushay uestgay. Iay ouldcay ardlyhay elievebay atthay osay eatgray aay oodgay
ortunefay ouldcay avehay efallenbay emay, utbay enwhay Iay ecamebay assureday atthay myay enemyay
adhay indeeday edflay, Iay appedclay myay andshay orfay oyjay anday anray ownday otay Ervalclay.

Eway ascendeday intoay myay oomray, anday ethay ervantsay esentlypray oughtbray eakfastbray;
utbay Iay asway unableay otay ontaincay elfmysay. Itay asway otnay oyjay onlyay atthay ossessedpay
emay; Iay eltfay myay eshflay ingletay ithway excessay ofay ensitivenesssay, anday myay ulsepay
eatbay apidlyray. Iay asway unableay otay emainray orfay aay inglesay instantay inay ethay amesay
aceplay; Iay umpedjay overay ethay airschay, appedclay myay andshay, anday aughedlay alouday.
Ervalclay atay irstfay attributeday myay unusualay iritsspay otay oyjay onay ishay arrivalay,
utbay enwhay ehay observeday emay oremay attentivelyay, ehay awsay aay ildnessway inay myay eyesay
orfay ichwhay ehay ouldcay otnay accountay, anday myay oudlay, unrestraineday, eartlesshay
aughterlay ightenedfray anday astonisheday imhay.

“myay earday Ictorvay,” iedcray ehay, at“whay, orfay Od’sgay akesay,
isay ethay attermay? Oday otnay aughlay inay atthay annermay. Owhay illay ouyay areay! Atwhay isay ethay
ausecay ofay allay isthay?”

o“day otnay askay emay,” iedcray Iay, uttingpay myay andshay eforebay myay eyesay, orfay Iay
oughtthay Iay awsay ethay eadeddray ectrespay ideglay intoay ethay oomray; e“_hay_ ancay
elltay. Ohay, avesay emay! Avesay emay!” Iay imagineday atthay ethay onstermay eizedsay emay;
Iay uggledstray uriouslyfay anday ellfay ownday inay aay itfay.

Oorpay Ervalclay! Atwhay ustmay avehay eenbay ishay eelingsfay? Aay eetingmay, ichwhay ehay
anticipateday ithway uchsay oyjay, osay angelystray urnedtay otay itternessbay. Utbay Iay
asway otnay ethay itnessway ofay ishay iefgray, orfay Iay asway ifelesslay anday idday otnay
ecoverray myay ensessay orfay aay onglay, onglay imetay.

Isthay asway ethay ommencementcay ofay aay ervousnay everfay ichwhay onfinedcay emay orfay
everalsay onthsmay. Uringday allay atthay imetay Enryhay asway myay onlyay ursenay. Iay
afterwardsay earnedlay atthay, owingknay myay ather’sfay advanceday ageay anday unfitnessay
orfay osay onglay aay ourneyjay, anday owhay etchedwray myay icknesssay ouldway akemay
Elizabethay, ehay aredspay emthay isthay iefgray byay oncealingcay ethay extentay ofay myay
isorderday. Ehay ewknay atthay Iay ouldcay otnay avehay aay oremay indkay anday attentiveay
ursenay anthay imselfhay; anday, irmfay inay ethay opehay ehay eltfay ofay myay ecoveryray, ehay
idday otnay oubtday atthay, insteaday ofay oingday armhay, ehay erformedpay ethay indestkay
actionay atthay ehay ouldcay owardstay emthay.

Utbay Iay asway inay ealityray eryvay illay, anday urelysay othingnay utbay ethay unboundeday anday
unremittingay attentionsay ofay myay iendfray ouldcay avehay estoredray emay otay ifelay.
Ethay ormfay ofay ethay onstermay onay omwhay Iay adhay estowedbay existenceay asway orfay everay
eforebay myay eyesay, anday Iay avedray incessantlyay oncerningcay imhay. Oubtlessday myay
ordsway urprisedsay Enryhay; ehay atay irstfay elievedbay emthay otay ebay ethay anderingsway
ofay myay isturbedday imaginationay, utbay ethay ertinacitypay ithway ichwhay Iay
ontinuallycay ecurredray otay ethay amesay ubjectsay ersuadedpay imhay atthay myay isorderday
indeeday oweday itsay originay otay omesay uncommonay anday erribletay eventay.

Byay eryvay owslay egreesday, anday ithway equentfray elapsesray atthay alarmeday anday
ievedgray myay iendfray, Iay ecoveredray. Iay ememberray ethay irstfay imetay Iay ecamebay
apablecay ofay observingay outwarday objectsay ithway anyay indkay ofay easureplay, Iay
erceivedpay atthay ethay allenfay eaveslay adhay isappearedday anday atthay ethay oungyay
udsbay ereway ootingshay orthfay omfray ethay eestray atthay adedshay myay indowway. Itay asway
aay ivineday ingspray, anday ethay easonsay ontributedcay eatlygray otay myay
onvalescencecay. Iay eltfay alsoay entimentssay ofay oyjay anday affectionay eviveray inay
myay osombay; myay oomglay isappearedday, anday inay aay ortshay imetay Iay ecamebay asay
eerfulchay asay eforebay Iay asway attackeday byay ethay atalfay assionpay.

earest“day Ervalclay,” exclaimeday Iay, ow“hay indkay, owhay eryvay oodgay
ouyay areay otay emay. Isthay olewhay interway, insteaday ofay eingbay entspay inay udystay, asay ouyay
omisedpray ourselfyay, ashay eenbay onsumedcay inay myay icksay oomray. Owhay allshay Iay everay
epayray ouyay? Iay eelfay ethay eatestgray emorseray orfay ethay isappointmentday ofay ichwhay Iay
avehay eenbay ethay occasionay, utbay ouyay illway orgivefay emay.”

ou“yay illway epayray emay entirelyay ifay ouyay oday otnay iscomposeday ourselfyay, utbay etgay
ellway asay astfay asay ouyay ancay; anday incesay ouyay appearay inay uchsay oodgay iritsspay, Iay
aymay eakspay otay ouyay onay oneay ubjectsay, aymay Iay otnay?”

Iay embledtray. Oneay ubjectsay! Atwhay ouldcay itay ebay? Ouldcay ehay alludeay otay anay objectay onay
omwhay Iay aredday otnay evenay inkthay?

ompose“cay ourselfyay,” aidsay Ervalclay, owhay observeday myay angechay ofay
olourcay, I“ay illway otnay entionmay itay ifay itay agitatesay ouyay; utbay ouryay atherfay
anday ousincay ouldway ebay eryvay appyhay ifay eythay eceivedray aay etterlay omfray ouyay inay ouryay
ownay andwritinghay. Eythay ardlyhay owknay owhay illay ouyay avehay eenbay anday areay uneasyay atay
ouryay onglay ilencesay.”

Is“ay atthay allay, myay earday Enryhay? Owhay ouldcay ouyay upposesay atthay myay irstfay
oughtthay ouldway otnay flyay owardstay osethay earday, earday iendsfray omwhay Iay ovelay anday
owhay areay osay eservingday ofay myay ovelay?”

If“ay isthay isay ouryay esentpray empertay, myay iendfray, ouyay illway erhapspay ebay adglay
otay eesay aay etterlay atthay ashay eenbay inglyay erehay omesay aysday orfay ouyay; itay isay omfray
ouryay ousincay, Iay elievebay.”




Apterchay 6ay


Ervalclay enthay utpay ethay ollowingfay etterlay intoay myay andshay. Itay asway omfray myay
ownay Elizabethay:

“myay earestday Ousincay,

ou“yay avehay eenbay illay, eryvay illay, anday evenay ethay onstantcay etterslay ofay earday
indkay Enryhay areay otnay ufficientsay otay eassureray emay onay ouryay accountay. Ouyay areay
orbiddenfay otay ite—towray oldhay aay enpay; etyay oneay ordway omfray ouyay, earday Ictorvay,
isay ecessarynay otay almcay ouray apprehensionsay. Orfay aay onglay imetay Iay avehay oughtthay
atthay eachay ostpay ouldway ingbray isthay inelay, anday myay ersuasionspay avehay
estrainedray myay uncleay omfray undertakingay aay ourneyjay otay Ingolstadtay. Iay avehay
eventedpray ishay encounteringay ethay inconveniencesay anday erhapspay angersday ofay osay
onglay aay ourneyjay, etyay owhay oftenay avehay Iay egrettedray otnay eingbay ableay otay
erformpay itay elfmysay! Iay igurefay otay elfmysay atthay ethay asktay ofay attendingay onay
ouryay ickbedsay ashay evolvedday onay omesay ercenarymay olday ursenay, owhay ouldcay evernay
uessgay ouryay ishesway ornay inistermay otay emthay ithway ethay arecay anday affectionay ofay
ouryay oorpay ousincay. Etyay atthay isay overay ownay: Ervalclay iteswray atthay indeeday
ouyay areay ettinggay etterbay. Iay eagerlyay opehay atthay ouyay illway onfirmcay isthay
intelligenceay oonsay inay ouryay ownay andwritinghay.

et“gay ell—andway eturnray otay usay. Ouyay illway indfay aay appyhay, eerfulchay omehay anday
iendsfray owhay ovelay ouyay earlyday. Ouryay ather’sfay ealthhay isay igorousvay, anday ehay
asksay utbay otay eesay ouyay, utbay otay ebay assureday atthay ouyay areay ellway; anday otnay aay
arecay illway everay oudclay ishay enevolentbay ountenancecay. Owhay easedplay ouyay ouldway
ebay otay emarkray ethay improvementay ofay ouray Ernestay! Ehay isay ownay ixteensay anday ullfay
ofay activityay anday iritspay. Ehay isay esirousday otay ebay aay uetray Isssway anday otay enteray
intoay oreignfay ervicesay, utbay eway annotcay artpay ithway imhay, atay eastlay untilay ishay
elderay otherbray eturnsray otay usay. Myay uncleay isay otnay easedplay ithway ethay ideaay ofay
aay ilitarymay areercay inay aay istantday ountrycay, utbay Ernestay evernay adhay ouryay
owerspay ofay applicationay. Ehay ookslay uponay udystay asay anay odiousay etterfay; ishay
imetay isay entspay inay ethay openay airay, imbingclay ethay illshay oray owingray onay ethay
akelay. Iay earfay atthay ehay illway ecomebay anay idleray unlessay eway ieldyay ethay ointpay
anday ermitpay imhay otay enteray onay ethay ofessionpray ichwhay ehay ashay electedsay.

ittle“lay alterationay, exceptay ethay owthgray ofay ouray earday ildrenchay, ashay akentay
aceplay incesay ouyay eftlay usay. Ethay ueblay akelay anday ow-cladclay ountains—theymay
evernay angechay; anday Iay inkthay ouray acidplay omehay anday ouray ontentedcay eartshay areay
egulatedray byay ethay amesay immutableay awslay. Myay iflingtray occupationsay aketay upay
myay imetay anday amuseay emay, anday Iay amay ewardedray orfay anyay exertionsay byay eeingsay
onenay utbay appyhay, indkay acesfay arounday emay. Incesay ouyay eftlay usay, utbay oneay
angechay ashay akentay aceplay inay ouray ittlelay ouseholdhay. Oday ouyay ememberray onay
atwhay occasionay Ustinejay Oritzmay entereday ouray amilyfay? Obablypray ouyay oday otnay;
Iay illway elateray erhay istoryhay, ereforethay inay aay ewfay ordsway. Adamemay Oritzmay,
erhay othermay, asway aay idowway ithway ourfay ildrenchay, ofay omwhay Ustinejay asway ethay
irdthay. Isthay irlgay adhay alwaysay eenbay ethay avouritefay ofay erhay atherfay, utbay
oughthray aay angestray erversitypay, erhay othermay ouldcay otnay endureay erhay, anday
afteray ethay eathday ofay May. Oritzmay, eatedtray erhay eryvay illay. Myay auntay observeday
isthay, anday enwhay Ustinejay asway elvetway earsyay ofay ageay, evailedpray onay erhay othermay
otay alloway erhay otay ivelay atay ouray ousehay. Ethay epublicanray institutionsay ofay ouray
ountrycay avehay oducedpray implersay anday appierhay annersmay anthay osethay ichwhay
evailpray inay ethay eatgray onarchiesmay atthay urroundsay itay. Encehay erethay isay esslay
istinctionday etweenbay ethay everalsay assesclay ofay itsay inhabitantsay; anday ethay
owerlay ordersay, eingbay eithernay osay oorpay ornay osay espisedday, eirthay annersmay areay
oremay efinedray anday oralmay. Aay ervantsay inay Enevagay oesday otnay eanmay ethay amesay
ingthay asay aay ervantsay inay Ancefray anday Englanday. Ustinejay, usthay eceivedray inay
ouray amilyfay, earnedlay ethay utiesday ofay aay ervantsay, aay onditioncay ichwhay, inay ouray
ortunatefay ountrycay, oesday otnay includeay ethay ideaay ofay ignoranceay anday aay
acrificesay ofay ethay ignityday ofay aay umanhay eingbay.

ustine“jay, ouyay aymay ememberray, asway aay eatgray avouritefay ofay oursyay; anday Iay
ecollectray ouyay onceay emarkedray atthay ifay ouyay ereway inay anay illay umourhay, oneay
anceglay omfray Ustinejay ouldcay issipateday itay, orfay ethay amesay easonray atthay
Ariostoay ivesgay oncerningcay ethay eautybay ofay Angelica—sheay ookedlay osay
ank-heartedclay anday appyhay. Myay auntay onceivedcay aay eatgray attachmentay orfay erhay,
byay ichwhay eshay asway induceday otay ivegay erhay anay educationay uperiorsay otay atthay
ichwhay eshay adhay atay irstfay intendeday. Isthay enefitbay asway ullyfay epaidray;
Ustinejay asway ethay ostmay atefulgray ittlelay eaturecray inay ethay orldway: Iay oday otnay
eanmay atthay eshay ademay anyay ofessionspray Iay evernay eardhay oneay asspay erhay ipslay, utbay
ouyay ouldcay eesay byay erhay eyesay atthay eshay almostay adoreday erhay otectresspray.
Althoughay erhay ispositionday asway aygay anday inay anymay espectsray inconsiderateay,
etyay eshay aidpay ethay eatestgray attentionay otay everyay esturegay ofay myay auntay. Eshay
oughtthay erhay ethay odelmay ofay allay excellenceay anday endeavoureday otay imitateay erhay
aseologyphray anday annersmay, osay atthay evenay ownay eshay oftenay emindsray emay ofay erhay.

en“whay myay earestday auntay iedday everyay oneay asway ootay uchmay occupieday inay eirthay ownay
iefgray otay oticenay oorpay Ustinejay, owhay adhay attendeday erhay uringday erhay illnessay
ithway ethay ostmay anxiousay affectionay. Oorpay Ustinejay asway eryvay illay; utbay otheray
ialstray ereway eservedray orfay erhay.

One“ay byay oneay, erhay othersbray anday istersay iedday; anday erhay othermay, ithway ethay
exceptionay ofay erhay eglectednay aughterday, asway eftlay ildlesschay. Ethay
onsciencecay ofay ethay omanway asway oubledtray; eshay eganbay otay inkthay atthay ethay
eathsday ofay erhay avouritesfay asway aay udgementjay omfray eavenhay otay astisechay erhay
artialitypay. Eshay asway aay Omanray Atholiccay; anday Iay elievebay erhay onfessorcay
onfirmedcay ethay ideaay ichwhay eshay adhay onceivedcay. Accordinglyay, aay ewfay onthsmay
afteray ouryay epartureday orfay Ingolstadtay, Ustinejay asway alledcay omehay byay erhay
epentantray othermay. Oorpay irlgay! Eshay eptway enwhay eshay uittedqay ouray ousehay; eshay
asway uchmay altereday incesay ethay eathday ofay myay auntay; iefgray adhay ivengay oftnesssay
anday aay inningway ildnessmay otay erhay annersmay, ichwhay adhay eforebay eenbay emarkableray
orfay ivacityvay. Ornay asway erhay esidenceray atay erhay other’smay ousehay ofay aay aturenay
otay estoreray erhay aietygay. Ethay oorpay omanway asway eryvay acillatingvay inay erhay
epentanceray. Eshay ometimessay eggedbay Ustinejay otay orgivefay erhay unkindnessay,
utbay uchmay ofteneray accuseday erhay ofay avinghay ausedcay ethay eathsday ofay erhay
othersbray anday istersay. Erpetualpay ettingfray atay engthlay ewthray Adamemay Oritzmay
intoay aay eclineday, ichwhay atay irstfay increaseday erhay irritabilityay, utbay eshay isay
ownay atay eacepay orfay everay. Eshay iedday onay ethay irstfay approachay ofay oldcay eatherway,
atay ethay eginningbay ofay isthay astlay interway. Ustinejay ashay ustjay eturnedray otay usay;
anday Iay assureay ouyay Iay ovelay erhay enderlytay. Eshay isay eryvay everclay anday entlegay,
anday extremelyay ettypray; asay Iay entionedmay eforebay, erhay ienmay anday erhay
expressionay ontinuallycay emindray emay ofay myay earday auntay.

I“ay ustmay aysay alsoay aay ewfay ordsway otay ouyay, myay earday ousincay, ofay ittlelay arlingday
Illiamway. Iay ishway ouyay ouldcay eesay imhay; ehay isay eryvay alltay ofay ishay ageay, ithway
eetsway aughinglay ueblay eyesay, arkday eyelashesay, anday urlingcay airhay. Enwhay ehay
ilessmay, otway ittlelay implesday appearay onay eachay eekchay, ichwhay areay osyray ithway
ealthhay. Ehay ashay alreadyay adhay oneay oray otway ittlelay ives_way,_ utbay Ouisalay Ironbay
isay ishay avouritefay, aay ettypray ittlelay irlgay ofay ivefay earsyay ofay ageay.

ow“nay, earday Ictorvay, Iay areday aysay ouyay ishway otay ebay indulgeday inay aay ittlelay
ossipgay oncerningcay ethay oodgay eoplepay ofay Enevagay. Ethay ettypray Issmay Ansfieldmay
ashay alreadyay eceivedray ethay ongratulatorycay isitsvay onay erhay approachingay
arriagemay ithway aay oungyay Englishmanay, Ohnjay Elbournemay, Esqay. Erhay uglyay
istersay, Anonmay, arriedmay May. Uvillardday, ethay ichray ankerbay, astlay autumnay. Ouryay
avouritefay oolfellowschay, Ouislay Anoirmay, ashay ufferedsay everalsay isfortunesmay
incesay ethay epartureday ofay Ervalclay omfray Enevagay. Utbay ehay ashay alreadyay
ecoveredray ishay iritsspay, anday isay eportedray otay ebay onay ethay ointpay ofay arryingmay aay
ivelylay ettypray Enchwomanfray, Adamemay Averniertay. Eshay isay aay idowway, anday uchmay
olderay anthay Anoirmay; utbay eshay isay eryvay uchmay admireday, anday aay avouritefay ithway
everybodyay.

I“ay avehay ittenwray elfmysay intoay etterbay iritsspay, earday ousincay; utbay myay anxietyay
eturnsray uponay emay asay Iay oncludecay. Itewray, earestday Ictor,—onevay ine—onelay
ordway illway ebay aay essingblay otay usay. Entay ousandthay anksthay otay Enryhay orfay ishay
indnesskay, ishay affectionay, anday ishay anymay etterslay; eway areay incerelysay
atefulgray. Adieuay! myay ousincay; aketay arecay ofay ourselfyay; anday, Iay entreatay
ouyay, itewray!

Elizabeth“ay Avenzalay.


eneva“gay, Archmay 18thay, 17ay—.”



ear“day, earday Elizabethay!” Iay exclaimeday, enwhay Iay adhay eadray erhay
etterlay: I“ay illway itewray instantlyay anday elieveray emthay omfray ethay anxietyay
eythay ustmay eelfay.” Iay otewray, anday isthay exertionay eatlygray atiguedfay emay; utbay
myay onvalescencecay adhay ommencedcay, anday oceededpray egularlyray. Inay anotheray
ortnightfay Iay asway ableay otay eavelay myay amberchay.

Oneay ofay myay irstfay utiesday onay myay ecoveryray asway otay introduceay Ervalclay otay ethay
everalsay ofessorspray ofay ethay universityay. Inay oingday isthay, Iay underwentay aay
indkay ofay oughray usageay, illay efittingbay ethay oundsway atthay myay indmay adhay
ustainedsay. Everay incesay ethay atalfay ightnay, ethay enday ofay myay abourslay, anday ethay
eginningbay ofay myay isfortunesmay, Iay adhay onceivedcay aay iolentvay antipathyay evenay
otay ethay amenay ofay aturalnay ilosophyphay. Enwhay Iay asway otherwiseay uiteqay estoredray
otay ealthhay, ethay ightsay ofay aay emicalchay instrumentay ouldway enewray allay ethay agonyay
ofay myay ervousnay omssymptay. Enryhay awsay isthay, anday adhay emovedray allay myay
apparatusay omfray myay iewvay. Ehay adhay alsoay angedchay myay apartmentay; orfay ehay
erceivedpay atthay Iay adhay acquireday aay islikeday orfay ethay oomray ichwhay adhay
eviouslypray eenbay myay aboratorylay. Utbay esethay arescay ofay Ervalclay ereway ademay ofay
onay availay enwhay Iay isitedvay ethay ofessorspray. May. Aldmanway inflicteday orturetay
enwhay ehay aisedpray, ithway indnesskay anday armthway, ethay astonishingay ogresspray Iay
adhay ademay inay ethay iencesscay. Ehay oonsay erceivedpay atthay Iay islikedday ethay
ubjectsay; utbay otnay uessinggay ethay ealray ausecay, ehay attributeday myay eelingsfay otay
odestymay, anday angedchay ethay ubjectsay omfray myay improvementay, otay ethay iencescay
itselfay, ithway aay esireday, asay Iay evidentlyay awsay, ofay awingdray emay outay. Atwhay
ouldcay Iay oday? Ehay eantmay otay easeplay, anday ehay ormentedtay emay. Iay eltfay asay ifay ehay
adhay acedplay arefullycay, oneay byay oneay, inay myay iewvay osethay instrumentsay ichwhay
ereway otay ebay afterwardsay useday inay uttingpay emay otay aay owslay anday uelcray eathday. Iay
ithedwray underay ishay ordsway, etyay aredday otnay exhibitay ethay ainpay Iay eltfay.
Ervalclay, osewhay eyesay anday eelingsfay ereway alwaysay uickqay inay iscerningday ethay
ensationssay ofay othersay, eclinedday ethay ubjectsay, allegingay, inay excuseay, ishay
otaltay ignoranceay; anday ethay onversationcay ooktay aay oremay eneralgay urntay. Iay
ankedthay myay iendfray omfray myay earthay, utbay Iay idday otnay eakspay. Iay awsay ainlyplay
atthay ehay asway urprisedsay, utbay ehay evernay attempteday otay awdray myay ecretsay omfray
emay; anday althoughay Iay ovedlay imhay ithway aay ixturemay ofay affectionay anday everenceray
atthay ewknay onay oundsbay, etyay Iay ouldcay evernay ersuadepay elfmysay otay onfidecay inay
imhay atthay eventay ichwhay asway osay oftenay esentpray otay myay ecollectionray, utbay ichwhay
Iay earedfay ethay etailday otay anotheray ouldway onlyay impressay oremay eeplyday.

May. Empekray asway otnay equallyay ocileday; anday inay myay onditioncay atay atthay imetay, ofay
almostay insupportableay ensitivenesssay, ishay arshhay untblay encomiumsay avegay emay evenay
oremay ainpay anthay ethay enevolentbay approbationay ofay May. Aldmanway. “d—nay
ethay ellowfay!” iedcray ehay; “whyay, May. Ervalclay, Iay assureay ouyay ehay ashay
outstriptay usay allay. Ayay, arestay ifay ouyay easeplay; utbay itay isay everthelessnay uetray. Aay
oungsteryay owhay, utbay aay ewfay earsyay agoay, elievedbay inay Orneliuscay Agrippaay asay irmlyfay
asay inay ethay ospelgay, ashay ownay etsay imselfhay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay universityay; anday ifay
ehay isay otnay oonsay ulledpay ownday, eway allshay allay ebay outay ofay ountenance.—Aycay,
ayay,” ontinuedcay ehay, observingay myay acefay expressiveay ofay ufferingsay,
“may. Ankensteinfray isay odestmay; anay excellentay ualityqay inay aay oungyay anmay.
Oungyay enmay ouldshay ebay iffidentday ofay emselvesthay, ouyay owknay, May. Ervalclay: Iay asway
elfmysay enwhay oungyay; utbay atthay earsway outay inay aay eryvay ortshay imetay.”

May. Empekray adhay ownay ommencedcay anay eulogyay onay imselfhay, ichwhay appilyhay urnedtay
ethay onversationcay omfray aay ubjectsay atthay asway osay annoyingay otay emay.

Ervalclay adhay evernay athisedsympay inay myay astestay orfay aturalnay iencescay; anday ishay
iterarylay ursuitspay ifferedday ollywhay omfray osethay ichwhay adhay occupieday emay. Ehay
amecay otay ethay universityay ithway ethay esignday ofay akingmay imselfhay ompletecay
astermay ofay ethay orientalay anguageslay, anday usthay ehay ouldshay openay aay ieldfay orfay
ethay anplay ofay ifelay ehay adhay arkedmay outay orfay imselfhay. Esolvedray otay ursuepay onay
ingloriousay areercay, ehay urnedtay ishay eyesay owardtay ethay Eastay, asay affordingay
opescay orfay ishay iritspay ofay enterpriseay. Ethay Ersianpay, Arabicay, anday Anskritsay
anguageslay engageday ishay attentionay, anday Iay asway easilyay induceday otay enteray onay
ethay amesay udiesstay. Idlenessay adhay everay eenbay irksomeay otay emay, anday ownay atthay Iay
ishedway otay flyay omfray eflectionray, anday atedhay myay ormerfay udiesstay, Iay eltfay
eatgray eliefray inay eingbay ethay ellow-pupilclay ithway myay iendfray, anday oundfay otnay
onlyay instructionay utbay onsolationcay inay ethay orksway ofay ethay orientalistsay. Iay
idday otnay, ikelay imhay, attemptay aay iticalcray owledgeknay ofay eirthay ialectsday, orfay
Iay idday otnay ontemplatecay akingmay anyay otheray useay ofay emthay anthay emporarytay
amusementay. Iay eadray erelymay otay understanday eirthay eaningmay, anday eythay ellway
epaidray myay abourslay. Eirthay elancholymay isay oothingsay, anday eirthay oyjay
elevatingay, otay aay egreeday Iay evernay experienceday inay udyingstay ethay authorsay ofay
anyay otheray ountrycay. Enwhay ouyay eadray eirthay itingswray, ifelay appearsay otay
onsistcay inay aay armway unsay anday aay ardengay ofay oses,—inray ethay ilessmay anday ownsfray
ofay aay airfay enemyay, anday ethay irefay atthay onsumescay ouryay ownay earthay. Owhay
ifferentday omfray ethay anlymay anday eroicalhay oetrypay ofay Eecegray anday Omeray!

Ummersay assedpay awayay inay esethay occupationsay, anday myay eturnray otay Enevagay asway
ixedfay orfay ethay atterlay enday ofay autumnay; utbay eingbay elayedday byay everalsay
accidentsay, interway anday owsnay arriveday, ethay oadsray ereway eemedday impassableay,
anday myay ourneyjay asway etardedray untilay ethay ensuingay ingspray. Iay eltfay isthay
elayday eryvay itterlybay; orfay Iay ongedlay otay eesay myay ativenay owntay anday myay elovedbay
iendsfray. Myay eturnray adhay onlyay eenbay elayedday osay onglay, omfray anay
unwillingnessay otay eavelay Ervalclay inay aay angestray aceplay, eforebay ehay adhay ecomebay
acquainteday ithway anyay ofay itsay inhabitantsay. Ethay interway, oweverhay, asway entspay
eerfullychay; anday althoughay ethay ingspray asway uncommonlyay atelay, enwhay itay amecay
itsay eautybay ompensatedcay orfay itsay ilatorinessday.

Ethay onthmay ofay Aymay adhay alreadyay ommencedcay, anday Iay expecteday ethay etterlay ailyday
ichwhay asway otay ixfay ethay ateday ofay myay epartureday, enwhay Enryhay oposedpray aay
edestrianpay ourtay inay ethay environsay ofay Ingolstadtay, atthay Iay ightmay idbay aay
ersonalpay arewellfay otay ethay ountrycay Iay adhay osay onglay inhabiteday. Iay accededay
ithway easureplay otay isthay opositionpray: Iay asway ondfay ofay exerciseay, anday Ervalclay
adhay alwaysay eenbay myay avouritefay ompanioncay inay ethay ambleray ofay isthay aturenay
atthay Iay adhay akentay amongay ethay enesscay ofay myay ativenay ountrycay.

Eway assedpay aay ortnightfay inay esethay erambulationspay: myay ealthhay anday iritsspay
adhay onglay eenbay estoredray, anday eythay ainedgay additionalay engthstray omfray ethay
alubrioussay airay Iay eathedbray, ethay aturalnay incidentsay ofay ouray ogresspray, anday
ethay onversationcay ofay myay iendfray. Udystay adhay eforebay ecludedsay emay omfray ethay
intercourseay ofay myay ellow-creaturesclay, anday enderedray emay unsocialay; utbay
Ervalclay alledcay orthfay ethay etterbay eelingsfay ofay myay earthay; ehay againay aughttay
emay otay ovelay ethay aspectay ofay aturenay, anday ethay eerfulchay acesfay ofay ildrenchay.
Excellentay iendfray! owhay incerelysay ouyay idday ovelay emay, anday endeavouray otay
elevateay myay indmay untilay itay asway onay aay evellay ithway ouryay ownay. Aay elfishsay
ursuitpay adhay ampedcray anday arrowednay emay, untilay ouryay entlenessgay anday
affectionay armedway anday openeday myay ensessay; Iay ecamebay ethay amesay appyhay eaturecray
owhay, aay ewfay earsyay agoay, ovedlay anday elovedbay byay allay, adhay onay orrowsay oray arecay.
Enwhay appyhay, inanimateay aturenay adhay ethay owerpay ofay estowingbay onay emay ethay ostmay
elightfulday ensationssay. Aay erenesay skyay anday erdantvay ieldsfay illedfay emay ithway
ecstasyay. Ethay esentpray easonsay asway indeeday ivineday; ethay owersflay ofay ingspray
oomedblay inay ethay edgeshay, ilewhay osethay ofay ummersay ereway alreadyay inay udbay. Iay
asway undisturbeday byay oughtsthay ichwhay uringday ethay ecedingpray earyay adhay essedpray
uponay emay, otwithstandingnay myay endeavoursay otay owthray emthay offay, ithway anay
invincibleay urdenbay.

Enryhay ejoicedray inay myay aietygay, anday incerelysay athisedsympay inay myay eelingsfay: ehay
exerteday imselfhay otay amuseay emay, ilewhay ehay expresseday ethay ensationssay atthay illedfay
ishay oulsay. Ethay esourcesray ofay ishay indmay onay isthay occasionay ereway ulytray
astonishingay: ishay onversationcay asway ullfay ofay imaginationay; anday eryvay oftenay, inay
imitationay ofay ethay Ersianpay anday Arabicay iterswray, ehay inventeday alestay ofay onderfulway
ancyfay anday assionpay. Atay otheray imestay ehay epeatedray myay avouritefay oemspay, oray ewdray
emay outay intoay argumentsay, ichwhay ehay upportedsay ithway eatgray ingenuityay.

Eway eturnedray otay ouray ollegecay onay aay Undaysay afternoonay: ethay easantspay ereway
ancingday, anday everyay oneay eway etmay appeareday aygay anday appyhay. Myay ownay iritsspay ereway
ighhay, anday Iay oundedbay alongay ithway eelingsfay ofay unbridleday oyjay anday ilarityhay.




Apterchay 7ay


Onay myay eturnray, Iay oundfay ethay ollowingfay etterlay omfray myay atherfay:—

“myay earday Ictorvay,

ou“yay avehay obablypray aitedway impatientlyay orfay aay etterlay otay ixfay ethay ateday ofay
ouryay eturnray otay usay; anday Iay asway atay irstfay emptedtay otay itewray onlyay aay ewfay
ineslay, erelymay entioningmay ethay ayday onay ichwhay Iay ouldshay expectay ouyay. Utbay
atthay ouldway ebay aay uelcray indnesskay, anday Iay areday otnay oday itay. Atwhay ouldway ebay
ouryay urprisesay, myay onsay, enwhay ouyay expecteday aay appyhay anday adglay elcomeway, otay
eholdbay, onay ethay ontrarycay, earstay anday etchednesswray? Anday owhay, Ictorvay, ancay
Iay elateray ouray isfortunemay? Absenceay annotcay avehay enderedray ouyay allouscay otay
ouray oysjay anday iefsgray; anday owhay allshay Iay inflictay ainpay onay myay onglay absentay
onsay? Iay ishway otay eparepray ouyay orfay ethay oefulway ewsnay, utbay Iay owknay itay isay
impossibleay; evenay ownay ouryay eyeay imsskay overay ethay agepay otay eeksay ethay ordsway
ichwhay areay otay onveycay otay ouyay ethay orriblehay idingstay.

illiam“way isay ead!—thatday eetsway ildchay, osewhay ilessmay elightedday anday armedway
myay earthay, owhay asway osay entlegay, etyay osay aygay! Ictorvay, ehay isay urderedmay!

I“ay illway otnay attemptay otay onsolecay ouyay; utbay illway implysay elateray ethay
ircumstancescay ofay ethay ansactiontray.

ast“lay Ursdaythay ay(may 7thay), Iay, myay iecenay, anday ouryay otway othersbray, entway otay
alkway inay Ainpalaisplay. Ethay eveningay asway armway anday erenesay, anday eway olongedpray
ouray alkway artherfay anthay usualay. Itay asway alreadyay uskday eforebay eway oughtthay ofay
eturningray; anday enthay eway iscoveredday atthay Illiamway anday Ernestay, owhay adhay onegay
onay eforebay, ereway otnay otay ebay oundfay. Eway accordinglyay estedray onay aay eatsay untilay
eythay ouldshay eturnray. Esentlypray Ernestay amecay, anday enquireday ifay eway adhay eensay
ishay otherbray; ehay aidsay, atthay ehay adhay eenbay ayingplay ithway imhay, atthay Illiamway
adhay unray awayay otay idehay imselfhay, anday atthay ehay ainlyvay oughtsay orfay imhay, anday
afterwardsay aitedway orfay aay onglay imetay, utbay atthay ehay idday otnay eturnray.

is“thay accountay atherray alarmeday usay, anday eway ontinuedcay otay earchsay orfay imhay
untilay ightnay ellfay, enwhay Elizabethay onjecturedcay atthay ehay ightmay avehay
eturnedray otay ethay ousehay. Ehay asway otnay erethay. Eway eturnedray againay, ithway
orchestay; orfay Iay ouldcay otnay estray, enwhay Iay oughtthay atthay myay eetsway oybay adhay
ostlay imselfhay, anday asway exposeday otay allay ethay ampsday anday ewsday ofay ightnay;
Elizabethay alsoay ufferedsay extremeay anguishay. Aboutay ivefay inay ethay orningmay Iay
iscoveredday myay ovelylay oybay, omwhay ethay ightnay eforebay Iay adhay eensay oomingblay anday
activeay inay ealthhay, etchedstray onay ethay assgray ividlay anday otionlessmay; ethay
intpray ofay ethay urder’smay ingerfay asway onay ishay ecknay.

e“hay asway onveyedcay omehay, anday ethay anguishay atthay asway isiblevay inay myay
ountenancecay etrayedbay ethay ecretsay otay Elizabethay. Eshay asway eryvay earnestay otay
eesay ethay orpsecay. Atay irstfay Iay attempteday otay eventpray erhay utbay eshay ersistedpay,
anday enteringay ethay oomray erewhay itay aylay, astilyhay examineday ethay ecknay ofay ethay
ictimvay, anday aspingclay erhay andshay exclaimeday, O‘ay Odgay! Iay avehay urderedmay myay
arlingday ildchay!’

e“shay aintedfay, anday asway estoredray ithway extremeay ifficultyday. Enwhay eshay againay
ivedlay, itay asway onlyay otay eepway anday ighsay. Eshay oldtay emay, atthay atthay amesay
eveningay Illiamway adhay easedtay erhay otay etlay imhay earway aay eryvay aluablevay
iniaturemay atthay eshay ossessedpay ofay ouryay othermay. Isthay icturepay isay onegay, anday
asway oubtlessday ethay emptationtay ichwhay urgeday ethay urderermay otay ethay eedday. Eway
avehay onay acetray ofay imhay atay esentpray, althoughay ouray exertionsay otay iscoverday imhay
areay unremitteday; utbay eythay illway otnay estoreray myay elovedbay Illiamway!

ome“cay, earestday Ictorvay; ouyay aloneay ancay onsolecay Elizabethay. Eshay eepsway
ontinuallycay, anday accusesay erselfhay unjustlyay asay ethay ausecay ofay ishay eathday;
erhay ordsway iercepay myay earthay. Eway areay allay unhappyay; utbay illway otnay atthay ebay anay
additionalay otivemay orfay ouyay, myay onsay, otay eturnray anday ebay ouray omfortercay?
Ouryay earday othermay! Alasay, Ictorvay! Iay ownay aysay, Ankthay Odgay eshay idday otnay ivelay
otay itnessway ethay uelcray, iserablemay eathday ofay erhay oungestyay arlingday!

ome“cay, Ictorvay; otnay oodingbray oughtsthay ofay engeancevay againstay ethay assassinay,
utbay ithway eelingsfay ofay eacepay anday entlenessgay, atthay illway ealhay, insteaday ofay
esteringfay, ethay oundsway ofay ouray indsmay. Enteray ethay ousehay ofay ourningmay, myay
iendfray, utbay ithway indnesskay anday affectionay orfay osethay owhay ovelay ouyay, anday otnay
ithway atredhay orfay ouryay enemiesay.

our“yay affectionateay anday afflicteday atherfay,

Alphonse“ay Ankensteinfray.



eneva“gay, Aymay 12thay, 17ay—.”



Ervalclay, owhay adhay atchedway myay ountenancecay asay Iay eadray isthay etterlay, asway
urprisedsay otay observeay ethay espairday atthay ucceededsay ethay oyjay Iay atay irstfay
expresseday onay eceivingray ewsnay omfray myay iendsfray. Iay ewthray ethay etterlay onay ethay
abletay, anday overedcay myay acefay ithway myay andshay.

“myay earday Ankensteinfray,” exclaimeday Enryhay, enwhay ehay erceivedpay emay
eepway ithway itternessbay, are“ay ouyay alwaysay otay ebay unhappyay? Myay earday iendfray,
atwhay ashay appenedhay?”

Iay otionedmay imhay otay aketay upay ethay etterlay, ilewhay Iay alkedway upay anday ownday ethay
oomray inay ethay extremestay agitationay. Earstay alsoay ushedgay omfray ethay eyesay ofay
Ervalclay, asay ehay eadray ethay accountay ofay myay isfortunemay.

I“ay ancay offeray ouyay onay onsolationcay, myay iendfray,” aidsay ehay;
our“yay isasterday isay irreparableay. Atwhay oday ouyay intenday otay oday?”

o“tay ogay instantlyay otay Enevagay: omecay ithway emay, Enryhay, otay orderay ethay orseshay.”

Uringday ouray alkway, Ervalclay endeavoureday otay aysay aay ewfay ordsway ofay onsolationcay;
ehay ouldcay onlyay expressay ishay eartfelthay athysympay. oor“pay Illiamway!” aidsay ehay,
ear“day ovelylay ildchay, ehay ownay eepsslay ithway ishay angelay othermay! Owhay atthay adhay
eensay imhay ightbray anday oyousjay inay ishay oungyay eautybay, utbay ustmay eepway overay ishay
untimelyay osslay! Otay ieday osay iserablymay; otay eelfay ethay urderer’smay aspgray! Owhay
uchmay oremay aay urderedmay atthay ouldcay estroyday adiantray innocenceay! Oorpay ittlelay
ellowfay! oneay onlyay onsolationcay avehay eway; ishay iendsfray ournmay anday eepway, utbay
ehay isay atay estray. Ethay angpay isay overay, ishay ufferingssay areay atay anay enday orfay everay.
Aay odsay overscay ishay entlegay ormfay, anday ehay owsknay onay ainpay. Ehay ancay onay ongerlay
ebay aay ubjectsay orfay itypay; eway ustmay eserveray atthay orfay ishay iserablemay
urvivorssay.”

Ervalclay okespay usthay asay eway urriedhay oughthray ethay eetsstray; ethay ordsway
impresseday emselvesthay onay myay indmay anday Iay ememberedray emthay afterwardsay inay
olitudesay. Utbay ownay, asay oonsay asay ethay orseshay arriveday, Iay urriedhay intoay aay
abrioletcay, anday adebay arewellfay otay myay iendfray.

Myay ourneyjay asway eryvay elancholymay. Atay irstfay Iay ishedway otay urryhay onay, orfay Iay ongedlay
otay onsolecay anday athisesympay ithway myay ovedlay anday orrowingsay iendsfray; utbay enwhay Iay
ewdray earnay myay ativenay owntay, Iay ackenedslay myay ogresspray. Iay ouldcay ardlyhay ustainsay
ethay ultitudemay ofay eelingsfay atthay owdedcray intoay myay indmay. Iay assedpay oughthray
