enesscay amiliarfay otay myay outhyay, utbay ichwhay Iay adhay otnay eensay orfay earlynay ixsay earsyay.
Owhay altereday everyay ingthay ightmay ebay uringday atthay imetay! Oneay uddensay anday
esolatingday angechay adhay akentay aceplay; utbay aay ousandthay ittlelay ircumstancescay
ightmay avehay byay egreesday orkedway otheray alterationsay, ichwhay, althoughay eythay ereway
oneday oremay anquillytray, ightmay otnay ebay ethay esslay ecisiveday. Earfay overcameay emay; Iay
aredday onay advanceay, eadingdray aay ousandthay amelessnay evilsay atthay ademay emay embletray,
althoughay Iay asway unableay otay efineday emthay.

Iay emainedray otway aysday atay Ausannelay, inay isthay ainfulpay atestay ofay indmay. Iay
ontemplatedcay ethay akelay: ethay atersway ereway acidplay; allay arounday asway almcay; anday ethay
owysnay ountainsmay, e“thay alacespay ofay aturenay,” ereway otnay angedchay. Byay
egreesday ethay almcay anday eavenlyhay enescay estoredray emay, anday Iay ontinuedcay myay ourneyjay
owardstay Enevagay.

Ethay oadray anray byay ethay idesay ofay ethay akelay, ichwhay ecamebay arrowernay asay Iay
approacheday myay ativenay owntay. Iay iscoveredday oremay istinctlyday ethay ackblay
idessay ofay Urajay, anday ethay ightbray ummitsay ofay Ontmay Ancblay. Iay eptway ikelay aay
ildchay. ear“day ountainsmay! myay ownay eautifulbay akelay! owhay oday ouyay elcomeway ouryay
andererway? Ouryay ummitssay areay earclay; ethay skyay anday akelay areay ueblay anday
acidplay. Isay isthay otay ognosticatepray eacepay, oray otay ockmay atay myay unhappinessay?”

Iay earfay, myay iendfray, atthay Iay allshay enderray elfmysay edioustay byay ellingdway onay
esethay eliminarypray ircumstancescay; utbay eythay ereway aysday ofay omparativecay
appinesshay, anday Iay inkthay ofay emthay ithway easureplay. Myay ountrycay, myay elovedbay
ountrycay! owhay utbay aay ativenay ancay elltay ethay elightday Iay ooktay inay againay
eholdingbay thyay eamsstray, thyay ountainsmay, anday, oremay anthay allay, thyay ovelylay
akelay!

Etyay, asay Iay ewdray earernay omehay, iefgray anday earfay againay overcameay emay. Ightnay alsoay
osedclay arounday; anday enwhay Iay ouldcay ardlyhay eesay ethay arkday ountainsmay, Iay eltfay illstay
oremay oomilyglay. Ethay icturepay appeareday aay astvay anday imday enescay ofay evilay, anday Iay
oresawfay obscurelyay atthay Iay asway estinedday otay ecomebay ethay ostmay etchedwray ofay umanhay
eingsbay. Alasay! Iay ophesiedpray ulytray, anday ailedfay onlyay inay oneay inglesay
ircumstancecay, atthay inay allay ethay iserymay Iay imagineday anday eadeddray, Iay idday otnay
onceivecay ethay undredthhay artpay ofay ethay anguishay Iay asway estinedday otay endureay.

Itay asway ompletelycay arkday enwhay Iay arriveday inay ethay environsay ofay Enevagay; ethay atesgay
ofay ethay owntay ereway alreadyay utshay; anday Iay asway obligeday otay asspay ethay ightnay atay
Echeronsay, aay illagevay atay ethay istanceday ofay alfhay aay eaguelay omfray ethay itycay. Ethay skyay
asway erenesay; anday, asay Iay asway unableay otay estray, Iay esolvedray otay isitvay ethay otspay
erewhay myay oorpay Illiamway adhay eenbay urderedmay. Asay Iay ouldcay otnay asspay oughthray ethay
owntay, Iay asway obligeday otay osscray ethay akelay inay aay oatbay otay arriveay atay Ainpalaisplay.
Uringday isthay ortshay oyagevay Iay awsay ethay ightninglay ayingplay onay ethay ummitsay ofay Ontmay
Ancblay inay ethay ostmay eautifulbay iguresfay. Ethay ormstay appeareday otay approachay
apidlyray, anday, onay andinglay, Iay ascendeday aay owlay illhay, atthay Iay ightmay observeay itsay
ogresspray. Itay advanceday; ethay eavenshay ereway oudedclay, anday Iay oonsay eltfay ethay ainray
omingcay owlyslay inay argelay opsdray, utbay itsay iolencevay uicklyqay increaseday.

Iay uittedqay myay eatsay, anday alkedway onay, althoughay ethay arknessday anday ormstay
increaseday everyay inutemay, anday ethay underthay urstbay ithway aay errifictay ashcray
overay myay eadhay. Itay asway echoeday omfray Alêvesay, ethay Urasjay, anday ethay Alpsay ofay
Avoysay; ividvay ashesflay ofay ightninglay azzledday myay eyesay, illuminatingay ethay
akelay, akingmay itay appearay ikelay aay astvay eetshay ofay irefay; enthay orfay anay instantay
everyay ingthay eemedsay ofay aay itchypay arknessday, untilay ethay eyeay ecoveredray itselfay
omfray ethay ecedingpray ashflay. Ethay ormstay, asay isay oftenay ethay asecay inay
Itzerlandsway, appeareday atay onceay inay ariousvay artspay ofay ethay eavenshay. Ethay
ostmay iolentvay ormstay unghay exactlyay orthnay ofay ethay owntay, overay ethay artpay ofay ethay
akelay ichwhay ieslay etweenbay ethay omontorypray ofay Elrivebay anday ethay illagevay ofay
Opêtcay. Anotheray ormstay enlighteneday Urajay ithway aintfay ashesflay; anday anotheray
arkenedday anday ometimessay isclosedday ethay Emôlay, aay eakedpay ountainmay otay ethay
eastay ofay ethay akelay.

Ilewhay Iay atchedway ethay empesttay, osay eautifulbay etyay errifictay, Iay anderedway onay ithway
aay astyhay epstay. Isthay oblenay arway inay ethay skyay elevateday myay iritsspay; Iay aspedclay myay
andshay, anday exclaimeday alouday, illiam“way, earday angelay! isthay isay thyay
uneralfay, isthay thyay irgeday!” Asay Iay aidsay esethay ordsway, Iay erceivedpay inay ethay
oomglay aay igurefay ichwhay olestay omfray ehindbay aay umpclay ofay eestray earnay emay; Iay oodstay
ixedfay, azinggay intentlyay: Iay ouldcay otnay ebay istakenmay. Aay ashflay ofay ightninglay
illuminateday ethay objectay, anday iscoveredday itsay apeshay ainlyplay otay emay; itsay
iganticgay aturestay, anday ethay eformityday ofay itsay aspectay oremay ideoushay anthay elongsbay
otay umanityhay, instantlyay informeday emay atthay itay asway ethay etchwray, ethay ilthyfay
ondæmay, otay omwhay Iay adhay ivengay ifelay. Atwhay idday ehay erethay? Ouldcay ehay ebay I(ay
udderedshay atay ethay onceptioncay) ethay urderermay ofay myay otherbray? Onay oonersay idday atthay
ideaay osscray myay imaginationay, anthay Iay ecamebay onvincedcay ofay itsay uthtray; myay eethtay
atteredchay, anday Iay asway orcedfay otay eanlay againstay aay eetray orfay upportsay. Ethay igurefay
assedpay emay uicklyqay, anday Iay ostlay itay inay ethay oomglay. Othingnay inay umanhay apeshay ouldcay
avehay estroyedday ethay airfay ildchay. e_hay_ asway ethay urderermay! Iay ouldcay otnay
oubtday itay. Ethay eremay esencepray ofay ethay ideaay asway anay irresistibleay oofpray ofay ethay
actfay. Iay oughtthay ofay ursuingpay ethay evilday; utbay itay ouldway avehay eenbay inay ainvay, orfay
anotheray ashflay iscoveredday imhay otay emay anginghay amongay ethay ocksray ofay ethay earlynay
erpendicularpay ascentay ofay Ontmay Alêvesay, aay illhay atthay oundsbay Ainpalaisplay onay ethay
outhsay. Ehay oonsay eachedray ethay ummitsay, anday isappearedday.

Iay emainedray otionlessmay. Ethay underthay easedcay; utbay ethay ainray illstay
ontinuedcay, anday ethay enescay asway envelopeday inay anay impenetrableay arknessday. Iay
evolvedray inay myay indmay ethay eventsay ichwhay Iay adhay untilay ownay oughtsay otay orgetfay:
ethay olewhay aintray ofay myay ogresspray owardtay ethay eationcray; ethay appearanceay ofay
ethay orksway ofay myay ownay andshay atay myay edsidebay; itsay epartureday. Otway earsyay adhay
ownay earlynay elapseday incesay ethay ightnay onay ichwhay ehay irstfay eceivedray ifelay; anday
asway isthay ishay irstfay imecray? Alasay! Iay adhay urnedtay ooselay intoay ethay orldway aay
epravedday etchwray, osewhay elightday asway inay arnagecay anday iserymay; adhay ehay otnay
urderedmay myay otherbray?

Onay oneay ancay onceivecay ethay anguishay Iay ufferedsay uringday ethay emainderray ofay ethay
ightnay, ichwhay Iay entspay, oldcay anday etway, inay ethay openay airay. Utbay Iay idday otnay
eelfay ethay inconvenienceay ofay ethay eatherway; myay imaginationay asway usybay inay
enesscay ofay evilay anday espairday. Iay onsideredcay ethay eingbay omwhay Iay adhay astcay
amongay ankindmay, anday endoweday ithway ethay illway anday owerpay otay effectay urposespay
ofay orrorhay, uchsay asay ethay eedday ichwhay ehay adhay ownay oneday, earlynay inay ethay ightlay
ofay myay ownay ampirevay, myay ownay iritspay etlay ooselay omfray ethay avegray, anday orcedfay
otay estroyday allay atthay asway earday otay emay.

Ayday awnedday; anday Iay irectedday myay epsstay owardstay ethay owntay. Ethay atesgay ereway
openay, anday Iay astenedhay otay myay ather’sfay ousehay. Myay irstfay oughtthay asway otay
iscoverday atwhay Iay ewknay ofay ethay urderermay, anday ausecay instantay ursuitpay otay ebay
ademay. Utbay Iay ausedpay enwhay Iay eflectedray onay ethay orystay atthay Iay adhay otay elltay. Aay
eingbay omwhay Iay elfmysay adhay ormedfay, anday endueday ithway ifelay, adhay etmay emay atay
idnightmay amongay ethay ecipicespray ofay anay inaccessibleay ountainmay. Iay
ememberedray alsoay ethay ervousnay everfay ithway ichwhay Iay adhay eenbay eizedsay ustjay atay
ethay imetay atthay Iay atedday myay eationcray, anday ichwhay ouldway ivegay anay airay ofay
eliriumday otay aay aletay otherwiseay osay utterlyay improbableay. Iay ellway ewknay atthay
ifay anyay otheray adhay ommunicatedcay uchsay aay elationray otay emay, Iay ouldshay avehay
ookedlay uponay itay asay ethay avingsray ofay insanityay. Esidesbay, ethay angestray aturenay
ofay ethay animalay ouldway eludeay allay ursuitpay, evenay ifay Iay ereway osay arfay editedcray
asay otay ersuadepay myay elativesray otay ommencecay itay. Anday enthay ofay atwhay useay ouldway
ebay ursuitpay? Owhay ouldcay arrestay aay eaturecray apablecay ofay alingscay ethay
overhangingay idessay ofay Ontmay Alêvesay? Esethay eflectionsray eterminedday emay, anday
Iay esolvedray otay emainray ilentsay.

Itay asway aboutay ivefay inay ethay orningmay enwhay Iay entereday myay ather’sfay ousehay. Iay
oldtay ethay ervantssay otnay otay isturbday ethay amilyfay, anday entway intoay ethay ibrarylay
otay attenday eirthay usualay ourhay ofay isingray.

Ixsay earsyay adhay elapseday, assedpay inay aay eamdray utbay orfay oneay indelibleay acetray, anday Iay
oodstay inay ethay amesay aceplay erewhay Iay adhay astlay embraceday myay atherfay eforebay myay
epartureday orfay Ingolstadtay. Elovedbay anday enerablevay arentpay! Ehay illstay emainedray
otay emay. Iay azedgay onay ethay icturepay ofay myay othermay, ichwhay oodstay overay ethay
antel-piececlay. Itay asway anay istoricalhay ubjectsay, aintedpay atay myay ather’sfay
esireday, anday epresentedray Arolinecay Eaufortbay inay anay agonyay ofay espairday, eelingknay
byay ethay offincay ofay erhay eadday atherfay. Erhay arbgay asway usticray, anday erhay eekchay alepay;
utbay erethay asway anay airay ofay ignityday anday eautybay, atthay ardlyhay ermittedpay ethay
entimentsay ofay itypay. Elowbay isthay icturepay asway aay iniaturemay ofay Illiamway; anday myay
earstay owedflay enwhay Iay ookedlay uponay itay. Ilewhay Iay asway usthay engageday, Ernestay
entereday: ehay adhay eardhay emay arriveay, anday astenedhay otay elcomeway emay:
elcome“way, myay earestday Ictorvay,” aidsay ehay. Ah“ay! Iay ishway ouyay
adhay omecay eethray onthsmay agoay, anday enthay ouyay ouldway avehay oundfay usay allay oyousjay anday
elightedday. Ouyay omecay otay usay ownay otay areshay aay iserymay ichwhay othingnay ancay
alleviateay; etyay ouryay esencepray illway, Iay opehay, eviveray ouray atherfay, owhay eemssay
inkingsay underay ishay isfortunemay; anday ouryay ersuasionspay illway induceay oorpay
Elizabethay otay easecay erhay ainvay anday ormentingtay elf-accusations.—Poorclay
Illiamway! ehay asway ouray arlingday anday ouray idepray!”

Earstay, unrestraineday, ellfay omfray myay other’sbray eyesay; aay ensesay ofay ortalmay
agonyay eptcray overay myay amefray. Eforebay, Iay adhay onlyay imagineday ethay
etchednesswray ofay myay esolatedday omehay; ethay ealityray amecay onay emay asay aay ewnay, anday
aay otnay esslay erribletay, isasterday. Iay iedtray otay almcay Ernestay; Iay enquireday oremay
inutelymay oncerningcay myay atherfay, anday erehay Iay amednay myay ousincay.

e“shay ostmay ofay allay,” aidsay Ernestay, equires“ray onsolationcay; eshay accuseday
erselfhay ofay avinghay ausedcay ethay eathday ofay myay otherbray, anday atthay ademay erhay
eryvay etchedwray. Utbay incesay ethay urderermay ashay eenbay iscoveredday—”

e“thay urderermay iscoveredday! Oodgay Odgay! owhay ancay atthay ebay? owhay ouldcay attemptay
otay ursuepay imhay? Itay isay impossibleay; oneay ightmay asay ellway tryay otay overtakeay ethay
indsway, oray onfinecay aay ountain-streamclay ithway aay awstray. Iay awsay imhay ootay; ehay
asway eefray astlay ightnay!”

I“ay oday otnay owknay atwhay ouyay eanmay,” epliedray myay otherbray, inay accentsay ofay
onderway, ut“bay otay usay ethay iscoveryday eway avehay ademay ompletescay ouray iserymay. Onay
oneay ouldway elievebay itay atay irstfay; anday evenay ownay Elizabethay illway otnay ebay
onvincedcay, otwithstandingnay allay ethay evidenceay. Indeeday, owhay ouldway editcray
atthay Ustinejay Oritzmay, owhay asway osay amiableay, anday ondfay ofay allay ethay amilyfay,
ouldcay uddenlysay ecomebay osay apablecay ofay osay ightfulfray, osay appallingay aay imecray?”

ustine“jay Oritzmay! Oorpay, oorpay irlgay, isay eshay ethay accuseday? Utbay itay isay
ongfullywray; everyay oneay owsknay atthay; onay oneay elievesbay itay, urelysay, Ernestay?”

o“nay oneay idday atay irstfay; utbay everalsay ircumstancescay amecay outay, atthay avehay
almostay orcedfay onvictioncay uponay usay; anday erhay ownay ehaviourbay ashay eenbay osay
onfusedcay, asay otay adday otay ethay evidenceay ofay actsfay aay eightway atthay, Iay earfay,
eaveslay onay opehay orfay oubtday. Utbay eshay illway ebay iedtray odaytay, anday ouyay illway
enthay earhay allay.”

Ehay enthay elatedray atthay, ethay orningmay onay ichwhay ethay urdermay ofay oorpay Illiamway
adhay eenbay iscoveredday, Ustinejay adhay eenbay akentay illay, anday onfinedcay otay erhay
edbay orfay everalsay aysday. Uringday isthay intervalay, oneay ofay ethay ervantssay,
appeninghay otay examineay ethay apparelay eshay adhay ornway onay ethay ightnay ofay ethay
urdermay, adhay iscoveredday inay erhay ocketpay ethay icturepay ofay myay othermay, ichwhay
adhay eenbay udgedjay otay ebay ethay emptationtay ofay ethay urderermay. Ethay ervantsay
instantlyay owedshay itay otay oneay ofay ethay othersay, owhay, ithoutway ayingsay aay ordway otay
anyay ofay ethay amilyfay, entway otay aay agistratemay; anday, uponay eirthay epositionday,
Ustinejay asway apprehendeday. Onay eingbay argedchay ithway ethay actfay, ethay oorpay irlgay
onfirmedcay ethay uspicionsay inay aay eatgray easuremay byay erhay extremeay onfusioncay ofay
annermay.

Isthay asway aay angestray aletay, utbay itay idday otnay akeshay myay aithfay; anday Iay epliedray
earnestlyay, ou“yay areay allay istakenmay; Iay owknay ethay urderermay. Ustinejay, oorpay,
oodgay Ustinejay, isay innocentay.”

Atay atthay instantay myay atherfay entereday. Iay awsay unhappinessay eeplyday impresseday
onay ishay ountenancecay, utbay ehay endeavoureday otay elcomeway emay eerfullychay; anday,
afteray eway adhay exchangeday ouray ournfulmay eetinggray, ouldway avehay introduceday
omesay otheray opictay anthay atthay ofay ouray isasterday, adhay otnay Ernestay exclaimeday,
ood“gay Odgay, apapay! Ictorvay ayssay atthay ehay owsknay owhay asway ethay urderermay ofay
oorpay Illiamway.”

e“way oday alsoay, unfortunatelyay,” epliedray myay atherfay, or“fay indeeday Iay adhay
atherray avehay eenbay orfay everay ignorantay anthay avehay iscoveredday osay uchmay
epravityday anday ungratitudeay inay oneay Iay aluedvay osay ighlyhay.”

“myay earday atherfay, ouyay areay istakenmay; Ustinejay isay innocentay.”

If“ay eshay isay, Odgay orbidfay atthay eshay ouldshay uffersay asay uiltygay. Eshay isay otay ebay
iedtray odaytay, anday Iay opehay, Iay incerelysay opehay, atthay eshay illway ebay acquitteday.”

Isthay eechspay almedcay emay. Iay asway irmlyfay onvincedcay inay myay ownay indmay atthay
Ustinejay, anday indeeday everyay umanhay eingbay, asway uiltlessgay ofay isthay urdermay. Iay
adhay onay earfay, ereforethay, atthay anyay ircumstantialcay evidenceay ouldcay ebay
oughtbray orwardfay ongstray enoughay otay onvictcay erhay. Myay aletay asway otnay oneay otay
announceay ubliclypay; itsay astoundingay orrorhay ouldway ebay ookedlay uponay asay
adnessmay byay ethay ulgarvay. Idday anyay oneay indeeday existay, exceptay Iay, ethay
eatorcray, owhay ouldway elievebay, unlessay ishay ensessay onvincedcay imhay, inay ethay
existenceay ofay ethay ivinglay onumentmay ofay esumptionpray anday ashray ignoranceay
ichwhay Iay adhay etlay ooselay uponay ethay orldway?

Eway ereway oonsay oinedjay byay Elizabethay. Imetay adhay altereday erhay incesay Iay astlay
eheldbay erhay; itay adhay endoweday erhay ithway ovelinesslay urpassingsay ethay eautybay ofay
erhay ildishchay earsyay. Erethay asway ethay amesay andourcay, ethay amesay ivacityvay, utbay
itay asway allieday otay anay expressionay oremay ullfay ofay ensibilitysay anday intellectay.
Eshay elcomedway emay ithway ethay eatestgray affectionay. our“yay arrivalay, myay earday
ousincay,” aidsay eshay, ills“fay emay ithway opehay. Ouyay erhapspay illway indfay omesay
eansmay otay ustifyjay myay oorpay uiltlessgay Ustinejay. Alasay! owhay isay afesay, ifay eshay
ebay onvictedcay ofay imecray? Iay elyray onay erhay innocenceay asay ertainlycay asay Iay oday
uponay myay ownay. Ouray isfortunemay isay oublyday ardhay otay usay; eway avehay otnay onlyay
ostlay atthay ovelylay arlingday oybay, utbay isthay oorpay irlgay, omwhay Iay incerelysay
ovelay, isay otay ebay orntay awayay byay evenay aay orseway atefay. Ifay eshay isay ondemnedcay, Iay
evernay allshay owknay oyjay oremay. Utbay eshay illway otnay, Iay amay uresay eshay illway otnay;
anday enthay Iay allshay ebay appyhay againay, evenay afteray ethay adsay eathday ofay myay ittlelay
Illiamway.”

e“shay isay innocentay, myay Elizabethay,” aidsay Iay, and“ay atthay allshay
ebay ovedpray; earfay othingnay, utbay etlay ouryay iritsspay ebay eeredchay byay ethay assuranceay
ofay erhay acquittalay.”

ow“hay indkay anday enerousgay ouyay areay! everyay oneay elseay elievesbay inay erhay uiltgay,
anday atthay ademay emay etchedwray, orfay Iay ewknay atthay itay asway impossibleay: anday otay
eesay everyay oneay elseay ejudicedpray inay osay eadlyday aay annermay enderedray emay
opelesshay anday espairingday.” Eshay eptway.

earest“day iecenay,” aidsay myay atherfay, “dryay ouryay earstay. Ifay eshay
isay, asay ouyay elievebay, innocentay, elyray onay ethay usticejay ofay ouray awslay, anday ethay
activityay ithway ichwhay Iay allshay eventpray ethay ightestslay adowshay ofay
artialitypay.”




Apterchay 8ay


Eway assedpay aay ewfay adsay ourshay untilay elevenay o’clockay, enwhay ethay ialtray asway otay
ommencecay. Myay atherfay anday ethay estray ofay ethay amilyfay eingbay obligeday otay attenday
asay itnessesway, Iay accompanieday emthay otay ethay ourtcay. Uringday ethay olewhay ofay
isthay etchedwray ockerymay ofay usticejay Iay ufferedsay ivinglay orturetay. Itay asway otay
ebay ecidedday etherwhay ethay esultray ofay myay uriositycay anday awlesslay evicesday ouldway
ausecay ethay eathday ofay otway ofay myay ellowfay eingsbay: oneay aay ilingsmay abebay ullfay ofay
innocenceay anday oyjay, ethay otheray arfay oremay eadfullydray urderedmay, ithway everyay
aggravationay ofay infamyay atthay ouldcay akemay ethay urdermay emorablemay inay orrorhay.
Ustinejay alsoay asway aay irlgay ofay eritmay anday ossessedpay ualitiesqay ichwhay omisedpray
otay enderray erhay ifelay appyhay; ownay allay asway otay ebay obliterateday inay anay
ignominiousay avegray, anday Iay ethay ausecay! Aay ousandthay imestay atherray ouldway Iay
avehay onfessedcay elfmysay uiltygay ofay ethay imecray ascribeday otay Ustinejay, utbay Iay
asway absentay enwhay itay asway ommittedcay, anday uchsay aay eclarationday ouldway avehay
eenbay onsideredcay asay ethay avingsray ofay aay admanmay anday ouldway otnay avehay
exculpateday erhay owhay ufferedsay oughthray emay.

Ethay appearanceay ofay Ustinejay asway almcay. Eshay asway esseddray inay ourningmay, anday
erhay ountenancecay, alwaysay engagingay, asway enderedray, byay ethay olemnitysay ofay erhay
eelingsfay, exquisitelyay eautifulbay. Etyay eshay appeareday onfidentcay inay
innocenceay anday idday otnay embletray, althoughay azedgay onay anday execrateday byay
ousandsthay, orfay allay ethay indnesskay ichwhay erhay eautybay ightmay otherwiseay avehay
exciteday asway obliterateday inay ethay indsmay ofay ethay ectatorsspay byay ethay
imaginationay ofay ethay enormityay eshay asway upposedsay otay avehay ommittedcay. Eshay
asway anquiltray, etyay erhay anquillitytray asway evidentlyay onstrainedcay; anday asay
erhay onfusioncay adhay eforebay eenbay adduceday asay aay oofpray ofay erhay uiltgay, eshay
orkedway upay erhay indmay otay anay appearanceay ofay ouragecay. Enwhay eshay entereday ethay
ourtcay eshay ewthray erhay eyesay oundray itay anday uicklyqay iscoveredday erewhay eway ereway
eatedsay. Aay eartay eemedsay otay imday erhay eyeay enwhay eshay awsay usay, utbay eshay uicklyqay
ecoveredray erselfhay, anday aay ooklay ofay orrowfulsay affectionay eemedsay otay attestay
erhay utteray uiltlessnessgay.

Ethay ialtray eganbay, anday afteray ethay advocateay againstay erhay adhay atedstay ethay
argechay, everalsay itnessesway ereway alledcay. Everalsay angestray actsfay ombinedcay
againstay erhay, ichwhay ightmay avehay aggeredstay anyoneay owhay adhay otnay uchsay oofpray
ofay erhay innocenceay asay Iay adhay. Eshay adhay eenbay outay ethay olewhay ofay ethay ightnay onay
ichwhay ethay urdermay adhay eenbay ommittedcay anday owardstay orningmay adhay eenbay
erceivedpay byay aay arket-womanclay otnay arfay omfray ethay otspay erewhay ethay odybay ofay ethay
urderedmay ildchay adhay eenbay afterwardsay oundfay. Ethay omanway askeday erhay atwhay eshay
idday erethay, utbay eshay ookedlay eryvay angelystray anday onlyay eturnedray aay onfusedcay
anday unintelligibleay answeray. Eshay eturnedray otay ethay ousehay aboutay eightay
o’clockay, anday enwhay oneay inquireday erewhay eshay adhay assedpay ethay ightnay, eshay
epliedray atthay eshay adhay eenbay ookinglay orfay ethay ildchay anday emandedday earnestlyay
ifay anythingay adhay eenbay eardhay oncerningcay imhay. Enwhay ownshay ethay odybay, eshay
ellfay intoay iolentvay ericshystay anday eptkay erhay edbay orfay everalsay aysday. Ethay
icturepay asway enthay oducedpray ichwhay ethay ervantsay adhay oundfay inay erhay ocketpay;
anday enwhay Elizabethay, inay aay alteringfay oicevay, ovedpray atthay itay asway ethay amesay
ichwhay, anay ourhay eforebay ethay ildchay adhay eenbay issedmay, eshay adhay acedplay oundray
ishay ecknay, aay urmurmay ofay orrorhay anday indignationay illedfay ethay ourtcay.

Ustinejay asway alledcay onay orfay erhay efenceday. Asay ethay ialtray adhay oceededpray, erhay
ountenancecay adhay altereday. Urprisesay, orrorhay, anday iserymay ereway onglystray
expresseday. Ometimessay eshay uggledstray ithway erhay earstay, utbay enwhay eshay asway
esiredday otay eadplay, eshay ollectedcay erhay owerspay anday okespay inay anay audibleay
althoughay ariablevay oicevay.

od“gay owsknay,” eshay aidsay, ow“hay entirelyay Iay amay innocentay. Utbay Iay
oday otnay etendpray atthay myay otestationspray ouldshay acquitay emay; Iay estray myay innocenceay
onay aay ainplay anday implesay explanationay ofay ethay actsfay ichwhay avehay eenbay adduceday
againstay emay, anday Iay opehay ethay aracterchay Iay avehay alwaysay ornebay illway inclineay myay
udgesjay otay aay avourablefay interpretationay erewhay anyay ircumstancecay appearsay
oubtfulday oray uspicioussay.”

Eshay enthay elatedray atthay, byay ethay ermissionpay ofay Elizabethay, eshay adhay assedpay
ethay eveningay ofay ethay ightnay onay ichwhay ethay urdermay adhay eenbay ommittedcay atay ethay
ousehay ofay anay auntay atay Echênay, aay illagevay ituatedsay atay aboutay aay eaguelay omfray
Enevagay. Onay erhay eturnray, atay aboutay inenay o’clockay, eshay etmay aay anmay owhay askeday
erhay ifay eshay adhay eensay anythingay ofay ethay ildchay owhay asway ostlay. Eshay asway
alarmeday byay isthay accountay anday assedpay everalsay ourshay inay ookinglay orfay imhay,
enwhay ethay atesgay ofay Enevagay ereway utshay, anday eshay asway orcedfay otay emainray
everalsay ourshay ofay ethay ightnay inay aay arnbay elongingbay otay aay ottagecay, eingbay
unwillingay otay allcay upay ethay inhabitantsay, otay omwhay eshay asway ellway ownknay. Ostmay
ofay ethay ightnay eshay entspay erehay atchingway; owardstay orningmay eshay elievedbay atthay
eshay eptslay orfay aay ewfay inutesmay; omesay epsstay isturbedday erhay, anday eshay awokeay.
Itay asway awnday, anday eshay uittedqay erhay asylumay, atthay eshay ightmay againay endeavouray
otay indfay myay otherbray. Ifay eshay adhay onegay earnay ethay otspay erewhay ishay odybay aylay,
itay asway ithoutway erhay owledgeknay. Atthay eshay adhay eenbay ewilderedbay enwhay
uestionedqay byay ethay arket-womanclay asway otnay urprisingsay, incesay eshay adhay assedpay
aay eeplessslay ightnay anday ethay atefay ofay oorpay Illiamway asway etyay uncertainay.
Oncerningcay ethay icturepay eshay ouldcay ivegay onay accountay.

I“ay owknay,” ontinuedcay ethay unhappyay ictimvay, ow“hay eavilyhay anday
atallyfay isthay oneay ircumstancecay eighsway againstay emay, utbay Iay avehay onay owerpay ofay
explainingay itay; anday enwhay Iay avehay expresseday myay utteray ignoranceay, Iay amay onlyay eftlay
otay onjecturecay oncerningcay ethay obabilitiespray byay ichwhay itay ightmay avehay eenbay
acedplay inay myay ocketpay. Utbay erehay alsoay Iay amay eckedchay. Iay elievebay atthay Iay avehay onay
enemyay onay earthay, anday onenay urelysay ouldway avehay eenbay osay ickedway asay otay estroyday emay
antonlyway. Idday ethay urderermay aceplay itay erethay? Iay owknay ofay onay opportunityay
affordeday imhay orfay osay oingday; oray, ifay Iay adhay, whyay ouldshay ehay avehay olenstay ethay
eweljay, otay artpay ithway itay againay osay oonsay?

I“ay ommitcay myay ausecay otay ethay usticejay ofay myay udgesjay, etyay Iay eesay onay oomray orfay
opehay. Iay egbay ermissionpay otay avehay aay ewfay itnessesway examineday oncerningcay myay
aracterchay, anday ifay eirthay estimonytay allshay otnay overweighay myay upposedsay
uiltgay, Iay ustmay ebay ondemnedcay, althoughay Iay ouldway edgeplay myay alvationsay onay myay
innocenceay.”

Everalsay itnessesway ereway alledcay owhay adhay ownknay erhay orfay anymay earsyay, anday
eythay okespay ellway ofay erhay; utbay earfay anday atredhay ofay ethay imecray ofay ichwhay eythay
upposedsay erhay uiltygay enderedray emthay imoroustay anday unwillingay otay omecay
orwardfay. Elizabethay awsay evenay isthay astlay esourceray, erhay excellentay
ispositionsday anday irreproachableay onductcay, aboutay otay ailfay ethay accuseday,
enwhay, althoughay iolentlyvay agitateday, eshay esiredday ermissionpay otay addressay
ethay ourtcay.

I“ay amay,” aidsay eshay, e“thay ousincay ofay ethay unhappyay ildchay owhay
asway urderedmay, oray atherray ishay istersay, orfay Iay asway educateday byay anday avehay ivedlay
ithway ishay arentspay everay incesay anday evenay onglay eforebay ishay irthbay. Itay aymay
ereforethay ebay udgedjay indecentay inay emay otay omecay orwardfay onay isthay occasionay, utbay
enwhay Iay eesay aay ellowfay eaturecray aboutay otay erishpay oughthray ethay owardicecay ofay erhay
etendedpray iendsfray, Iay ishway otay ebay alloweday otay eakspay, atthay Iay aymay aysay atwhay Iay
owknay ofay erhay aracterchay. Iay amay ellway acquainteday ithway ethay accuseday. Iay avehay ivedlay
inay ethay amesay ousehay ithway erhay, atay oneay imetay orfay ivefay anday atay anotheray orfay earlynay
otway earsyay. Uringday allay atthay eriodpay eshay appeareday otay emay ethay ostmay amiableay anday
enevolentbay ofay umanhay eaturescray. Eshay ursednay Adamemay Ankensteinfray, myay auntay, inay
erhay astlay illnessay, ithway ethay eatestgray affectionay anday arecay anday afterwardsay
attendeday erhay ownay othermay uringday aay edioustay illnessay, inay aay annermay atthay exciteday
ethay admirationay ofay allay owhay ewknay erhay, afteray ichwhay eshay againay ivedlay inay myay
uncle’say ousehay, erewhay eshay asway elovedbay byay allay ethay amilyfay. Eshay asway
armlyway attacheday otay ethay ildchay owhay isay ownay eadday anday acteday owardstay imhay ikelay aay
ostmay affectionateay othermay. Orfay myay ownay artpay, Iay oday otnay esitatehay otay aysay atthay,
otwithstandingnay allay ethay evidenceay oducedpray againstay erhay, Iay elievebay anday elyray
onay erhay erfectpay innocenceay. Eshay adhay onay emptationtay orfay uchsay anay actionay; asay otay
ethay aublebay onay ichwhay ethay iefchay oofpray estsray, ifay eshay adhay earnestlyay esiredday itay,
Iay ouldshay avehay illinglyway ivengay itay otay erhay, osay uchmay oday Iay esteemay anday aluevay
erhay.”

Aay urmurmay ofay approbationay ollowedfay Elizabeth’say implesay anday owerfulpay
appealay, utbay itay asway exciteday byay erhay enerousgay interferenceay, anday otnay inay
avourfay ofay oorpay Ustinejay, onay omwhay ethay ublicpay indignationay asway urnedtay ithway
enewedray iolencevay, argingchay erhay ithway ethay ackestblay ingratitudeay. Eshay
erselfhay eptway asay Elizabethay okespay, utbay eshay idday otnay answeray. Myay ownay
agitationay anday anguishay asway extremeay uringday ethay olewhay ialtray. Iay elievedbay
inay erhay innocenceay; Iay ewknay itay. Ouldcay ethay ondæmay owhay adhay I(ay idday otnay orfay aay
inutemay oubtday) urderedmay myay otherbray alsoay inay ishay ellishhay ortspay avehay
etrayedbay ethay innocentay otay eathday anday ignominyay? Iay ouldcay otnay ustainsay ethay
orrorhay ofay myay ituationsay, anday enwhay Iay erceivedpay atthay ethay opularpay oicevay anday
ethay ountenancescay ofay ethay udgesjay adhay alreadyay ondemnedcay myay unhappyay ictimvay,
Iay ushedray outay ofay ethay ourtcay inay agonyay. Ethay orturestay ofay ethay accuseday idday
otnay equalay inemay; eshay asway ustainedsay byay innocenceay, utbay ethay angsfay ofay
emorseray oretay myay osombay anday ouldway otnay orgofay eirthay oldhay.

Iay assedpay aay ightnay ofay unmingleday etchednesswray. Inay ethay orningmay Iay entway otay
ethay ourtcay; myay ipslay anday oatthray ereway archedpay. Iay aredday otnay askay ethay atalfay
uestionqay, utbay Iay asway ownknay, anday ethay officeray uessedgay ethay ausecay ofay myay
isitvay. Ethay allotsbay adhay eenbay ownthray; eythay ereway allay ackblay, anday Ustinejay
asway ondemnedcay.

Iay annotcay etendpray otay escribeday atwhay Iay enthay eltfay. Iay adhay eforebay
experienceday ensationssay ofay orrorhay, anday Iay avehay endeavoureday otay estowbay uponay
emthay adequateay expressionsay, utbay ordsway annotcay onveycay anay ideaay ofay ethay
eart-sickeningclay espairday atthay Iay enthay endureday. Ethay ersonpay otay omwhay Iay
addresseday elfmysay addeday atthay Ustinejay adhay alreadyay onfessedcay erhay uiltgay.
at“thay evidenceay,” ehay observeday, as“way ardlyhay equiredray inay osay aringglay aay
asecay, utbay Iay amay adglay ofay itay, anday, indeeday, onenay ofay ouray udgesjay ikelay otay
ondemncay aay iminalcray uponay ircumstantialcay evidenceay, ebay itay everay osay
ecisiveday.”

Isthay asway angestray anday unexpecteday intelligenceay; atwhay ouldcay itay eanmay? Adhay
myay eyesay eceivedday emay? Anday asway Iay eallyray asay admay asay ethay olewhay orldway ouldway
elievebay emay otay ebay ifay Iay isclosedday ethay objectay ofay myay uspicionssay? Iay
astenedhay otay eturnray omehay, anday Elizabethay eagerlyay emandedday ethay esultray.

“myay ousincay,” epliedray Iay, it“ay isay ecidedday asay ouyay aymay avehay expecteday; allay
udgesjay adhay atherray atthay entay innocentay ouldshay uffersay anthay atthay oneay uiltygay
ouldshay escapeay. Utbay eshay ashay onfessedcay.”

Isthay asway aay ireday owblay otay oorpay Elizabethay, owhay adhay eliedray ithway irmnessfay uponay
Ustine’sjay innocenceay. Alas“ay!” aidsay eshay. ow“hay allshay Iay
everay againay elievebay inay umanhay oodnessgay? Ustinejay, omwhay Iay ovedlay anday esteemeday asay
myay istersay, owhay ouldcay eshay utpay onay osethay ilessmay ofay innocenceay onlyay otay etraybay?
Erhay ildmay eyesay eemedsay incapableay ofay anyay everitysay oray uilegay, anday etyay eshay ashay
ommittedcay aay urdermay.”

Oonsay afteray eway eardhay atthay ethay oorpay ictimvay adhay expresseday aay esireday otay eesay myay
ousincay. Myay atherfay ishedway erhay otnay otay ogay utbay aidsay atthay ehay eftlay itay otay erhay ownay
udgmentjay anday eelingsfay otay ecideday. es“yay,” aidsay Elizabethay,
I“ay illway ogay, althoughay eshay isay uiltygay; anday ouyay, Ictorvay, allshay accompanyay
emay; Iay annotcay ogay aloneay.” Ethay ideaay ofay isthay isitvay asway orturetay otay emay, etyay
Iay ouldcay otnay efuseray.

Eway entereday ethay oomyglay isonpray amberchay anday eheldbay Ustinejay ittingsay onay omesay
awstray atay ethay artherfay enday; erhay andshay ereway anacledmay, anday erhay eadhay estedray onay
erhay eesknay. Eshay oseray onay eeingsay usay enteray, anday enwhay eway ereway eftlay aloneay ithway
erhay, eshay ewthray erselfhay atay ethay eetfay ofay Elizabethay, eepingway itterlybay. Myay
ousincay eptway alsoay.

Oh“ay, Ustinejay!” aidsay eshay. “whyay idday ouyay obray emay ofay myay astlay onsolationcay?
Iay eliedray onay ouryay innocenceay, anday althoughay Iay asway enthay eryvay etchedwray, Iay
asway otnay osay iserablemay asay Iay amay ownay.”

And“ay oday ouyay alsoay elievebay atthay Iay amay osay eryvay, eryvay ickedway? Oday ouyay alsoay
oinjay ithway myay enemiesay otay ushcray emay, otay ondemncay emay asay aay urderermay?” Erhay
oicevay asway uffocatedsay ithway obssay.

ise“ray, myay oorpay irlgay,” aidsay Elizabethay; “whyay oday ouyay eelknay,
ifay ouyay areay innocentay? Iay amay otnay oneay ofay ouryay enemiesay, Iay elievedbay ouyay
uiltlessgay, otwithstandingnay everyay evidenceay, untilay Iay eardhay atthay ouyay adhay
ourselfyay eclaredday ouryay uiltgay. Atthay eportray, ouyay aysay, isay alsefay; anday ebay
assureday, earday Ustinejay, atthay othingnay ancay akeshay myay onfidencecay inay ouyay orfay aay
omentmay, utbay ouryay ownay onfessioncay.”

I“ay idday onfesscay, utbay Iay onfessedcay aay ielay. Iay onfessedcay, atthay Iay ightmay
obtainay absolutionay; utbay ownay atthay alsehoodfay ieslay eavierhay atay myay earthay anthay
allay myay otheray inssay. Ethay Odgay ofay eavenhay orgivefay emay! Everay incesay Iay asway
ondemnedcay, myay onfessorcay ashay esiegedbay emay; ehay eatenedthray anday enacedmay,
untilay Iay almostay eganbay otay inkthay atthay Iay asway ethay onstermay atthay ehay aidsay Iay
asway. Ehay eatenedthray excommunicationay anday ellhay irefay inay myay astlay omentsmay ifay
Iay ontinuedcay obdurateay. Earday adylay, Iay adhay onenay otay upportsay emay; allay ookedlay
onay emay asay aay etchwray oomedday otay ignominyay anday erditionpay. Atwhay ouldcay Iay oday?
Inay anay evilay ourhay Iay ubscribedsay otay aay ielay; anday ownay onlyay amay Iay ulytray
iserablemay.”

Eshay ausedpay, eepingway, anday enthay ontinuedcay, I“ay oughtthay ithway orrorhay, myay
eetsway adylay, atthay ouyay ouldshay elievebay ouryay Ustinejay, omwhay ouryay essedblay
auntay adhay osay ighlyhay onouredhay, anday omwhay ouyay ovedlay, asway aay eaturecray apablecay
ofay aay imecray ichwhay onenay utbay ethay evilday imselfhay ouldcay avehay erpetratedpay.
Earday Illiamway! earestday essedblay ildchay! Iay oonsay allshay eesay ouyay againay inay
eavenhay, erewhay eway allshay allay ebay appyhay; anday atthay onsolescay emay, oinggay asay Iay
amay otay uffersay ignominyay anday eathday.”

Oh“ay, Ustinejay! Orgivefay emay orfay avinghay orfay oneay omentmay istrustedday ouyay.
Whyay idday ouyay onfesscay? Utbay oday otnay ournmay, earday irlgay. Oday otnay earfay. Iay
illway oclaimpray, Iay illway ovepray ouryay innocenceay. Iay illway eltmay ethay onystay
eartshay ofay ouryay enemiesay byay myay earstay anday ayerspray. Ouyay allshay otnay ieday!
Ouyay, myay ayfellowplay, myay ompanioncay, myay istersay, erishpay onay ethay affoldscay!
Onay! Onay! Iay evernay ouldcay urvivesay osay orriblehay aay isfortunemay.”

Ustinejay ookshay erhay eadhay ournfullymay. I“ay oday otnay earfay otay ieday,” eshay aidsay;
at“thay angpay isay astpay. Odgay aisesray myay eaknessway anday ivesgay emay ouragecay otay
endureay ethay orstway. Iay eavelay aay adsay anday itterbay orldway; anday ifay ouyay ememberray
emay anday inkthay ofay emay asay ofay oneay unjustlyay ondemnedcay, Iay amay esignedray otay ethay
atefay awaitingay emay. Earnlay omfray emay, earday adylay, otay ubmitsay inay atiencepay otay
ethay illway ofay eavenhay!”

Uringday isthay onversationcay Iay adhay etiredray otay aay ornercay ofay ethay isonpray oomray,
erewhay Iay ouldcay oncealcay ethay orridhay anguishay atthay ossessedpay emay. Espairday!
Owhay aredday alktay ofay atthay? Ethay oorpay ictimvay, owhay onay ethay orrowmay asway otay asspay
ethay awfulay oundarybay etweenbay ifelay anday eathday, eltfay otnay, asay Iay idday, uchsay
eepday anday itterbay agonyay. Iay ashedgnay myay eethtay anday oundgray emthay ogethertay,
utteringay aay oangray atthay amecay omfray myay inmostay oulsay. Ustinejay artedstay. Enwhay
eshay awsay owhay itay asway, eshay approacheday emay anday aidsay, ear“day irsay, ouyay areay eryvay
indkay otay isitvay emay; ouyay, Iay opehay, oday otnay elievebay atthay Iay amay uiltygay?”

Iay ouldcay otnay answeray. o“nay, Ustinejay,” aidsay Elizabethay; e“hay isay oremay
onvincedcay ofay ouryay innocenceay anthay Iay asway, orfay evenay enwhay ehay eardhay atthay ouyay
adhay onfessedcay, ehay idday otnay editcray itay.”

I“ay ulytray ankthay imhay. Inay esethay astlay omentsmay Iay eelfay ethay incerestsay
atitudegray owardstay osethay owhay inkthay ofay emay ithway indnesskay. Owhay eetsway isay
ethay affectionay ofay othersay otay uchsay aay etchwray asay Iay amay! Itay emovesray oremay anthay
alfhay myay isfortunemay, anday Iay eelfay asay ifay Iay ouldcay ieday inay eacepay ownay atthay myay
innocenceay isay acknowledgeday byay ouyay, earday adylay, anday ouryay ousincay.”

Usthay ethay oorpay ufferersay iedtray otay omfortcay othersay anday erselfhay. Eshay indeeday
ainedgay ethay esignationray eshay esiredday. Utbay Iay, ethay uetray urderermay, eltfay ethay
ever-dyingclay ormway aliveay inay myay osombay, ichwhay alloweday ofay onay opehay oray
onsolationcay. Elizabethay alsoay eptway anday asway unhappyay, utbay ershay alsoay asway
ethay iserymay ofay innocenceay, ichwhay, ikelay aay oudclay atthay assespay overay ethay airfay
oonmay, orfay aay ilewhay ideshay utbay annotcay arnishtay itsay ightnessbray. Anguishay anday
espairday adhay enetratedpay intoay ethay orecay ofay myay earthay; Iay orebay aay ellhay ithinway
emay ichwhay othingnay ouldcay extinguishay. Eway ayedstay everalsay ourshay ithway
Ustinejay, anday itay asway ithway eatgray ifficultyday atthay Elizabethay ouldcay eartay
erselfhay awayay. I“ay ishway,” iedcray eshay, at“thay Iay ereway otay ieday ithway ouyay; Iay
annotcay ivelay inay isthay orldway ofay iserymay.”

Ustinejay assumeday anay airay ofay eerfulnesschay, ilewhay eshay ithway ifficultyday
epressedray erhay itterbay earstay. Eshay embraceday Elizabethay anday aidsay inay aay oicevay
ofay alf-suppressedclay emotionay, arewell“fay, eetsway adylay, earestday Elizabethay,
myay elovedbay anday onlyay iendfray; aymay eavenhay, inay itsay ountybay, essblay anday
eservepray ouyay; aymay isthay ebay ethay astlay isfortunemay atthay ouyay illway everay
uffersay! Ivelay, anday ebay appyhay, anday akemay othersay osay.”

Anday onay ethay orrowmay Ustinejay iedday. Elizabeth’say eart-rendingclay eloquenceay
ailedfay otay ovemay ethay udgesjay omfray eirthay ettledsay onvictioncay inay ethay
iminalitycray ofay ethay aintlysay ufferersay. Myay assionatepay anday indignantay
appealsay ereway ostlay uponay emthay. Anday enwhay Iay eceivedray eirthay oldcay answersay
anday eardhay ethay arshhay, unfeelingay easoningray ofay esethay enmay, myay urposedpay
avowalay iedday awayay onay myay ipslay. Usthay Iay ightmay oclaimpray elfmysay aay admanmay,
utbay otnay evokeray ethay entencesay assedpay uponay myay etchedwray ictimvay. Eshay
erishedpay onay ethay affoldscay asay aay urderessmay!

Omfray ethay orturestay ofay myay ownay earthay, Iay urnedtay otay ontemplatecay ethay eepday anday
oicelessvay iefgray ofay myay Elizabethay. Isthay alsoay asway myay oingday! Anday myay
ather’sfay oeway, anday ethay esolationday ofay atthay atelay osay ilingsmay omehay allay asway
ethay orkway ofay myay ice-accursedclay andshay! Eyay eepway, unhappyay onesay, utbay esethay
areay otnay ouryay astlay earstay! Againay allshay ouyay aiseray ethay uneralfay ailway, anday
ethay oundsay ofay ouryay amentationslay allshay againay anday againay ebay eardhay!
Ankensteinfray, ouryay onsay, ouryay insmankay, ouryay earlyay, uch-lovedclay iendfray; ehay
owhay ouldway endspay eachay italvay opdray ofay oodblay orfay ouryay akessay, owhay ashay onay
oughtthay ornay ensesay ofay oyjay exceptay asay itay isay irroredmay alsoay inay ouryay earday
ountenancescay, owhay ouldway illfay ethay airay ithway essingsblay anday endspay ishay ifelay
inay ervingsay ou—heyay idsbay ouyay eepway, otay edshay ountlesscay earstay; appyhay eyondbay
ishay opeshay, ifay usthay inexorableay atefay ebay atisfiedsay, anday ifay ethay estructionday
ausepay eforebay ethay eacepay ofay ethay avegray avehay ucceededsay otay ouryay adsay ormentstay!

Usthay okespay myay opheticpray oulsay, asay, orntay byay emorseray, orrorhay, anday espairday,
Iay eheldbay osethay Iay ovedlay endspay ainvay orrowsay uponay ethay avesgray ofay Illiamway anday
Ustinejay, ethay irstfay aplesshay ictimsvay otay myay unhalloweday artsay.




Apterchay 9ay


Othingnay isay oremay ainfulpay otay ethay umanhay indmay anthay, afteray ethay eelingsfay avehay
eenbay orkedway upay byay aay uickqay uccessionsay ofay eventsay, ethay eadday almnesscay ofay
inactionay anday ertaintycay ichwhay ollowsfay anday eprivesday ethay oulsay othbay ofay opehay
anday earfay. Ustinejay iedday, eshay estedray, anday Iay asway aliveay. Ethay oodblay owedflay
eelyfray inay myay einsvay, utbay aay eightway ofay espairday anday emorseray essedpray onay myay
earthay ichwhay othingnay ouldcay emoveray. Eepslay edflay omfray myay eyesay; Iay anderedway
ikelay anay evilay iritspay, orfay Iay adhay ommittedcay eedsday ofay ischiefmay eyondbay
escriptionday orriblehay, anday oremay, uchmay oremay I(ay ersuadedpay elfmysay) asway etyay
ehindbay. Etyay myay earthay overfloweday ithway indnesskay anday ethay ovelay ofay irtuevay.
Iay adhay egunbay ifelay ithway enevolentbay intentionsay anday irstedthay orfay ethay omentmay
enwhay Iay ouldshay utpay emthay inay acticepray anday akemay elfmysay usefulay otay myay ellowfay
eingsbay. Ownay allay asway astedblay; insteaday ofay atthay erenitysay ofay onsciencecay
ichwhay alloweday emay otay ooklay ackbay uponay ethay astpay ithway elf-satisfactionclay, anday
omfray encethay otay athergay omisepray ofay ewnay opeshay, Iay asway eizedsay byay emorseray anday
ethay ensesay ofay uiltgay, ichwhay urriedhay emay awayay otay aay ellhay ofay intenseay orturestay
uchsay asay onay anguagelay ancay escribeday.

Isthay atestay ofay indmay eyedpray uponay myay ealthhay, ichwhay adhay erhapspay evernay
entirelyay ecoveredray omfray ethay irstfay ockshay itay adhay ustainedsay. Iay unnedshay
ethay acefay ofay anmay; allay oundsay ofay oyjay oray omplacencycay asway orturetay otay emay;
olitudesay asway myay onlyay onsolation—deepcay, arkday, eathlikeday olitudesay.

Myay atherfay observeday ithway ainpay ethay alterationay erceptiblepay inay myay ispositionday
anday abitshay anday endeavoureday byay argumentsay educedday omfray ethay eelingsfay ofay ishay
erenesay onsciencecay anday uiltlessgay ifelay otay inspireay emay ithway ortitudefay anday
awakenay inay emay ethay ouragecay otay ispelday ethay arkday oudclay ichwhay oodedbray overay emay.
o“day ouyay inkthay, Ictorvay,” aidsay ehay, at“thay Iay oday otnay uffersay
alsoay? Onay oneay ouldcay ovelay aay ildchay oremay anthay Iay ovedlay ouryay
other”—tearsbray amecay intoay ishay eyesay asay ehay oke—“butspay
isay itay otnay aay utyday otay ethay urvivorssay atthay eway ouldshay efrainray omfray augmentingay
eirthay unhappinessay byay anay appearanceay ofay immoderateay iefgray? Itay isay alsoay aay utyday
oweday otay ourselfyay, orfay excessiveay orrowsay eventspray improvementay oray enjoymentay,
oray evenay ethay ischargeday ofay ailyday usefulnessay, ithoutway ichwhay onay anmay isay itfay orfay
ocietysay.”

Isthay adviceay, althoughay oodgay, asway otallytay inapplicableay otay myay asecay; Iay
ouldshay avehay eenbay ethay irstfay otay idehay myay iefgray anday onsolecay myay iendsfray ifay
emorseray adhay otnay ingledmay itsay itternessbay, anday errortay itsay alarmay, ithway myay
otheray ensationssay. Ownay Iay ouldcay onlyay answeray myay atherfay ithway aay ooklay ofay
espairday anday endeavouray otay idehay elfmysay omfray ishay iewvay.

Aboutay isthay imetay eway etiredray otay ouray ousehay atay Elrivebay. Isthay angechay asway
articularlypay agreeableay otay emay. Ethay uttingshay ofay ethay atesgay egularlyray atay
entay o’clockay anday ethay impossibilityay ofay emainingray onay ethay akelay afteray atthay
ourhay adhay enderedray ouray esidenceray ithinway ethay allsway ofay Enevagay eryvay irksomeay
otay emay. Iay asway ownay eefray. Oftenay, afteray ethay estray ofay ethay amilyfay adhay
etiredray orfay ethay ightnay, Iay ooktay ethay oatbay anday assedpay anymay ourshay uponay ethay
aterway. Ometimessay, ithway myay ailssay etsay, Iay asway arriedcay byay ethay indway; anday
ometimessay, afteray owingray intoay ethay iddlemay ofay ethay akelay, Iay eftlay ethay oatbay otay
ursuepay itsay ownay oursecay anday avegay ayway otay myay ownay iserablemay eflectionsray. Iay
asway oftenay emptedtay, enwhay allay asway atay eacepay arounday emay, anday Iay ethay onlyay
unquietay ingthay atthay anderedway estlessray inay aay enescay osay eautifulbay anday
eavenly—ifhay Iay exceptay omesay atbay, oray ethay ogsfray, osewhay arshhay anday
interrupteday oakingcray asway eardhay onlyay enwhay Iay approacheday ethay ore—oftenshay,
Iay aysay, Iay asway emptedtay otay ungeplay intoay ethay ilentsay akelay, atthay ethay atersway
ightmay oseclay overay emay anday myay alamitiescay orfay everay. Utbay Iay asway estrainedray,
enwhay Iay oughtthay ofay ethay eroichay anday ufferingsay Elizabethay, omwhay Iay enderlytay
ovedlay, anday osewhay existenceay asway oundbay upay inay inemay. Iay oughtthay alsoay ofay myay
atherfay anday urvivingsay otherbray; ouldshay Iay byay myay asebay esertionday eavelay emthay
exposeday anday unprotecteday otay ethay alicemay ofay ethay iendfay omwhay Iay adhay etlay ooselay
amongay emthay?

Atay esethay omentsmay Iay eptway itterlybay anday ishedway atthay eacepay ouldway evisitray myay
indmay onlyay atthay Iay ightmay afforday emthay onsolationcay anday appinesshay. Utbay atthay
ouldcay otnay ebay. Emorseray extinguisheday everyay opehay. Iay adhay eenbay ethay authoray ofay
unalterableay evilsay, anday Iay ivedlay inay ailyday earfay estlay ethay onstermay omwhay Iay adhay
eatedcray ouldshay erpetratepay omesay ewnay ickednessway. Iay adhay anay obscureay eelingfay
atthay allay asway otnay overay anday atthay ehay ouldway illstay ommitcay omesay ignalsay imecray,
ichwhay byay itsay enormityay ouldshay almostay effaceay ethay ecollectionray ofay ethay astpay.
Erethay asway alwaysay opescay orfay earfay osay onglay asay anythingay Iay ovedlay emainedray
ehindbay. Myay abhorrenceay ofay isthay iendfay annotcay ebay onceivedcay. Enwhay Iay oughtthay ofay
imhay Iay ashedgnay myay eethtay, myay eyesay ecamebay inflameday, anday Iay ardentlyay ishedway otay
extinguishay atthay ifelay ichwhay Iay adhay osay oughtlesslythay estowedbay. Enwhay Iay
eflectedray onay ishay imescray anday alicemay, myay atredhay anday evengeray urstbay allay oundsbay
ofay oderationmay. Iay ouldway avehay ademay aay ilgrimagepay otay ethay ighesthay eakpay ofay ethay
Andesay, ouldcay Iay, enwhay erethay, avehay ecipitatedpray imhay otay eirthay asebay. Iay ishedway
otay eesay imhay againay, atthay Iay ightmay eakwray ethay utmostay extentay ofay abhorrenceay onay ishay
eadhay anday avengeay ethay eathsday ofay Illiamway anday Ustinejay.

Ouray ousehay asway ethay ousehay ofay ourningmay. Myay ather’sfay ealthhay asway eeplyday
akenshay byay ethay orrorhay ofay ethay ecentray eventsay. Elizabethay asway adsay anday
espondingday; eshay onay ongerlay ooktay elightday inay erhay ordinaryay occupationsay; allay
easureplay eemedsay otay erhay acrilegesay owardtay ethay eadday; eternalay oeway anday earstay eshay
enthay oughtthay asway ethay ustjay ibutetray eshay ouldshay aypay otay innocenceay osay astedblay
anday estroyedday. Eshay asway onay ongerlay atthay appyhay eaturecray owhay inay earlieray outhyay
anderedway ithway emay onay ethay anksbay ofay ethay akelay anday alkedtay ithway ecstasyay ofay ouray
uturefay ospectspray. Ethay irstfay ofay osethay orrowssay ichwhay areay entsay otay eanway usay omfray
ethay earthay adhay isitedvay erhay, anday itsay immingday influenceay uenchedqay erhay earestday
ilessmay.

en“whay Iay eflectray, myay earday ousincay,” aidsay eshay, on“ay ethay iserablemay eathday ofay
Ustinejay Oritzmay, Iay onay ongerlay eesay ethay orldway anday itsay orksway asay eythay eforebay
appeareday otay emay. Eforebay, Iay ookedlay uponay ethay accountsay ofay icevay anday
injusticeay atthay Iay eadray inay ooksbay oray eardhay omfray othersay asay alestay ofay ancientay
aysday oray imaginaryay evilsay; atay eastlay eythay ereway emoteray anday oremay amiliarfay otay
easonray anthay otay ethay imaginationay; utbay ownay iserymay ashay omecay omehay, anday enmay
appearay otay emay asay onstersmay irstingthay orfay eachay other’say oodblay. Etyay Iay amay
ertainlycay unjustay. Everybodyay elievedbay atthay oorpay irlgay otay ebay uiltygay; anday
ifay eshay ouldcay avehay ommittedcay ethay imecray orfay ichwhay eshay ufferedsay, assuredlyay
eshay ouldway avehay eenbay ethay ostmay epravedday ofay umanhay eaturescray. Orfay ethay akesay
ofay aay ewfay ewelsjay, otay avehay urderedmay ethay onsay ofay erhay enefactorbay anday iendfray,
aay ildchay omwhay eshay adhay ursednay omfray itsay irthbay, anday appeareday otay ovelay asay ifay
itay adhay eenbay erhay ownay! Iay ouldcay otnay onsentcay otay ethay eathday ofay anyay umanhay
eingbay, utbay ertainlycay Iay ouldshay avehay oughtthay uchsay aay eaturecray unfitay otay
emainray inay ethay ocietysay ofay enmay. Utbay eshay asway innocentay. Iay owknay, Iay eelfay
eshay asway innocentay; ouyay areay ofay ethay amesay opinionay, anday atthay onfirmscay emay.
Alasay! Ictorvay, enwhay alsehoodfay ancay ooklay osay ikelay ethay uthtray, owhay ancay
assureay emselvesthay ofay ertaincay appinesshay? Iay eelfay asay ifay Iay ereway alkingway onay
ethay edgeay ofay aay ecipicepray, owardstay ichwhay ousandsthay areay owdingcray anday
endeavouringay otay ungeplay emay intoay ethay abyssay. Illiamway anday Ustinejay ereway
assassinateday, anday ethay urderermay escapesay; ehay alksway aboutay ethay orldway eefray,
anday erhapspay espectedray. Utbay evenay ifay Iay ereway ondemnedcay otay uffersay onay ethay
affoldscay orfay ethay amesay imescray, Iay ouldway otnay angechay acesplay ithway uchsay aay
etchwray.”

Iay istenedlay otay isthay iscourseday ithway ethay extremestay agonyay. Iay, otnay inay eedday,
utbay inay effectay, asway ethay uetray urderermay. Elizabethay eadray myay anguishay inay myay
ountenancecay, anday indlykay akingtay myay andhay, aidsay, “myay earestday iendfray, ouyay
ustmay almcay ourselfyay. Esethay eventsay avehay affecteday emay, Odgay owsknay owhay
eeplyday; utbay Iay amay otnay osay etchedwray asay ouyay areay. Erethay isay anay expressionay ofay
espairday, anday ometimessay ofay evengeray, inay ouryay ountenancecay atthay akesmay emay
embletray. Earday Ictorvay, anishbay esethay arkday assionspay. Ememberray ethay
iendsfray arounday ouyay, owhay entrecay allay eirthay opeshay inay ouyay. Avehay eway ostlay
ethay owerpay ofay enderingray ouyay appyhay? Ahay! Ilewhay eway ovelay, ilewhay eway areay
uetray otay eachay otheray, erehay inay isthay andlay ofay eacepay anday eautybay, ouryay ativenay
ountrycay, eway aymay eapray everyay anquiltray essing—whatblay ancay isturbday ouray
eacepay?”

Anday ouldcay otnay uchsay ordsway omfray erhay omwhay Iay ondlyfay izedpray eforebay everyay
otheray iftgay ofay ortunefay ufficesay otay asechay awayay ethay iendfay atthay urkedlay inay myay
earthay? Evenay asay eshay okespay Iay ewdray earnay otay erhay, asay ifay inay errortay, estlay atay
atthay eryvay omentmay ethay estroyerday adhay eenbay earnay otay obray emay ofay erhay.

Usthay otnay ethay endernesstay ofay iendshipfray, ornay ethay eautybay ofay earthay, ornay ofay
eavenhay, ouldcay edeemray myay oulsay omfray oeway; ethay eryvay accentsay ofay ovelay ereway
ineffectualay. Iay asway encompasseday byay aay oudclay ichwhay onay eneficialbay
influenceay ouldcay enetratepay. Ethay oundedway eerday aggingdray itsay aintingfay
imbslay otay omesay untroddenay akebray, erethay otay azegay uponay ethay arroway ichwhay adhay
iercedpay itay, anday otay ieday, asway utbay aay etypay ofay emay.

Ometimessay Iay ouldcay opecay ithway ethay ullensay espairday atthay overwhelmeday emay, utbay
ometimessay ethay irlwindwhay assionspay ofay myay oulsay ovedray emay otay eeksay, byay odilybay
exerciseay anday byay angechay ofay aceplay, omesay eliefray omfray myay intolerableay
ensationssay. Itay asway uringday anay accessay ofay isthay indkay atthay Iay uddenlysay eftlay
myay omehay, anday endingbay myay epsstay owardstay ethay earnay Alpineay alleysvay, oughtsay
inay ethay agnificencemay, ethay eternityay ofay uchsay enesscay, otay orgetfay elfmysay anday
myay ephemeralay, ecausebay umanhay, orrowssay. Myay anderingsway ereway irectedday
owardstay ethay alleyvay ofay Amounixchay. Iay adhay isitedvay itay equentlyfray uringday myay
oyhoodbay. Ixsay earsyay adhay assedpay incesay enthay: I_ay_ asway aay eckwray, utbay oughtnay
adhay angedchay inay osethay avagesay anday enduringay enesscay.

Iay erformedpay ethay irstfay artpay ofay myay ourneyjay onay orsebackhay. Iay afterwardsay
iredhay aay ulemay, asay ethay oremay ure-footedclay anday eastlay iablelay otay eceiveray
injuryay onay esethay uggedray oadsray. Ethay eatherway asway inefay; itay asway aboutay ethay
iddlemay ofay ethay onthmay ofay Augustay, earlynay otway onthsmay afteray ethay eathday ofay
Ustinejay, atthay iserablemay epochay omfray ichwhay Iay atedday allay myay oeway. Ethay
eightway uponay myay iritspay asway ensiblysay ightenedlay asay Iay ungedplay etyay eeperday inay
ethay avineray ofay Arveay. Ethay immenseay ountainsmay anday ecipicespray atthay overhungay
emay onay everyay idesay, ethay oundsay ofay ethay iverray agingray amongay ethay ocksray, anday
ethay ashingday ofay ethay aterfallsway arounday okespay ofay aay owerpay ightymay asay
Omnipotence—anday Iay easedcay otay earfay oray otay endbay eforebay anyay eingbay esslay
almightyay anthay atthay ichwhay adhay eatedcray anday uledray ethay elementsay, erehay
isplayedday inay eirthay ostmay errifictay uisegay. Illstay, asay Iay ascendeday igherhay,
ethay alleyvay assumeday aay oremay agnificentmay anday astonishingay aracterchay.
Uinedray astlescay anginghay onay ethay ecipicespray ofay inypay ountainsmay, ethay
impetuousay Arveay, anday ottagescay everyay erehay anday erethay eepingpay orthfay omfray
amongay ethay eestray ormedfay aay enescay ofay ingularsay eautybay. Utbay itay asway
augmenteday anday enderedray ublimesay byay ethay ightymay Alpsay, osewhay itewhay anday
iningshay amidspyray anday omesday oweredtay aboveay allay, asay elongingbay otay anotheray
earthay, ethay abitationshay ofay anotheray aceray ofay eingsbay.

Iay assedpay ethay idgebray ofay Issierpélay, erewhay ethay avineray, ichwhay ethay iverray
ormsfay, openeday eforebay emay, anday Iay eganbay otay ascenday ethay ountainmay atthay
overhangsay itay. Oonsay afteray, Iay entereday ethay alleyvay ofay Amounixchay. Isthay
alleyvay isay oremay onderfulway anday ublimesay, utbay otnay osay eautifulbay anday
icturesquepay asay atthay ofay Ervoxsay, oughthray ichwhay Iay adhay ustjay assedpay. Ethay
ighhay anday owysnay ountainsmay ereway itsay immediateay oundariesbay, utbay Iay awsay onay
oremay uinedray astlescay anday ertilefay ieldsfay. Immenseay aciersglay approacheday
ethay oadray; Iay eardhay ethay umblingray underthay ofay ethay allingfay avalancheay anday
arkedmay ethay okesmay ofay itsay assagepay. Ontmay Ancblay, ethay upremesay anday
agnificentmay Ontmay Ancblay, aisedray itselfay omfray ethay urroundingsay aiguilles_ay_,
anday itsay emendoustray e_dômay_ overlookeday ethay alleyvay.

Aay inglingtay ong-lostclay ensesay ofay easureplay oftenay amecay acrossay emay uringday isthay
ourneyjay. Omesay urntay inay ethay oadray, omesay ewnay objectay uddenlysay erceivedpay anday
ecognisedray, emindedray emay ofay aysday onegay byay, anday ereway associateday ithway ethay
ightheartedlay aietygay ofay oyhoodbay. Ethay eryvay indsway isperedwhay inay oothingsay
accentsay, anday aternalmay Aturenay adebay emay eepway onay oremay. Enthay againay ethay
indlykay influenceay easedcay otay act—Iay oundfay elfmysay etteredfay againay otay iefgray
anday indulgingay inay allay ethay iserymay ofay eflectionray. Enthay Iay urredspay onay myay
animalay, ivingstray osay otay orgetfay ethay orldway, myay earsfay, anday oremay anthay allay,
elf—ormysay, inay aay oremay esperateday ashionfay, Iay alighteday anday ewthray elfmysay onay
ethay assgray, eighedway ownday byay orrorhay anday espairday.

Atay engthlay Iay arriveday atay ethay illagevay ofay Amounixchay. Exhaustionay ucceededsay
otay ethay extremeay atiguefay othbay ofay odybay anday ofay indmay ichwhay Iay adhay endureday.
Orfay aay ortshay acespay ofay imetay Iay emainedray atay ethay indowway atchingway ethay allidpay
ightningslay atthay ayedplay aboveay Ontmay Ancblay anday isteninglay otay ethay ushingray ofay
ethay Arveay, ichwhay ursuedpay itsay oisynay ayway eneathbay. Ethay amesay ullinglay oundssay
acteday asay aay ullabylay otay myay ootay eenkay ensationssay; enwhay Iay acedplay myay eadhay
uponay myay illowpay, eepslay eptcray overay emay; Iay eltfay itay asay itay amecay anday essedblay
ethay ivergay ofay oblivionay.




Apterchay 10ay


Iay entspay ethay ollowingfay ayday oamingray oughthray ethay alleyvay. Iay oodstay esidebay
ethay ourcessay ofay ethay Arveironay, ichwhay aketay eirthay iseray inay aay acierglay, atthay
ithway owslay acepay isay advancingay ownday omfray ethay ummitsay ofay ethay illshay otay
arricadebay ethay alleyvay. Ethay abruptay idessay ofay astvay ountainsmay ereway eforebay
emay; ethay icyay allway ofay ethay acierglay overhungay emay; aay ewfay atteredshay inespay ereway
atteredscay arounday; anday ethay olemnsay ilencesay ofay isthay oriousglay
esence-chamberclay ofay imperialay Aturenay asway okenbray onlyay byay ethay awlingbray
avesway oray ethay allfay ofay omesay astvay agmentfray, ethay underthay oundsay ofay ethay
avalancheay oray ethay ackingcray, everberatedray alongay ethay ountainsmay, ofay ethay
accumulateday iceay, ichwhay, oughthray ethay ilentsay orkingway ofay immutableay awslay,
asway everay anday anonay entray anday orntay, asay ifay itay adhay eenbay utbay aay aythingplay inay
eirthay andshay. Esethay ublimesay anday agnificentmay enesscay affordeday emay ethay
eatestgray onsolationcay atthay Iay asway apablecay ofay eceivingray. Eythay elevateday emay
omfray allay ittlenesslay ofay eelingfay, anday althoughay eythay idday otnay emoveray myay
iefgray, eythay ubduedsay anday anquillisedtray itay. Inay omesay egreeday, alsoay, eythay
ivertedday myay indmay omfray ethay oughtsthay overay ichwhay itay adhay oodedbray orfay ethay
astlay onthmay. Iay etiredray otay estray atay ightnay; myay umbersslay, asay itay ereway,
aitedway onay anday inisteredmay otay byay ethay assemblanceay ofay andgray apesshay ichwhay Iay
adhay ontemplatedcay uringday ethay ayday. Eythay ongregatedcay oundray emay; ethay
unstaineday owysnay ountain-topclay, ethay itteringglay innaclepay, ethay inepay oodsway,
anday aggedray arebay avineray, ethay eagleay, oaringsay amidstay ethay ouds—theyclay allay
atheredgay oundray emay anday adebay emay ebay atay eacepay.

Erewhay adhay eythay edflay enwhay ethay extnay orningmay Iay awokeay? Allay ofay
oul-inspiritingclay edflay ithway eepslay, anday arkday elancholymay oudedclay everyay
oughtthay. Ethay ainray asway ouringpay inay orrentstay, anday ickthay istsmay idhay ethay
ummitssay ofay ethay ountainsmay, osay atthay Iay evenay awsay otnay ethay acesfay ofay osethay
ightymay iendsfray. Illstay Iay ouldway enetratepay eirthay istymay eilvay anday eeksay emthay
inay eirthay oudyclay etreatsray. Atwhay ereway ainray anday ormstay otay emay? Myay ulemay asway
oughtbray otay ethay oorday, anday Iay esolvedray otay ascenday otay ethay ummitsay ofay
Ontanvertmay. Iay ememberedray ethay effectay atthay ethay iewvay ofay ethay emendoustray
anday ever-movingclay acierglay adhay oducedpray uponay myay indmay enwhay Iay irstfay awsay itay.
Itay adhay enthay illedfay emay ithway aay ublimesay ecstasyay atthay avegay ingsway otay ethay
oulsay anday alloweday itay otay oarsay omfray ethay obscureay orldway otay ightlay anday oyjay.
Ethay ightsay ofay ethay awfulay anday ajesticmay inay aturenay adhay indeeday alwaysay ethay
effectay ofay olemnisingsay myay indmay anday ausingcay emay otay orgetfay ethay assingpay
arescay ofay ifelay. Iay eterminedday otay ogay ithoutway aay uidegay, orfay Iay asway ellway
acquainteday ithway ethay athpay, anday ethay esencepray ofay anotheray ouldway estroyday ethay
olitarysay andeurgray ofay ethay enescay.

Ethay ascentay isay ecipitouspray, utbay ethay athpay isay utcay intoay ontinualcay anday ortshay
indingsway, ichwhay enableay ouyay otay urmountsay ethay erpendicularitypay ofay ethay
ountainmay. Itay isay aay enescay errificallytay esolateday. Inay aay ousandthay otsspay
ethay acestray ofay ethay interway avalancheay aymay ebay erceivedpay, erewhay eestray ielay
okenbray anday ewedstray onay ethay oundgray, omesay entirelyay estroyedday, othersay entbay,
eaninglay uponay ethay uttingjay ocksray ofay ethay ountainmay oray ansverselytray uponay
otheray eestray. Ethay athpay, asay ouyay ascenday igherhay, isay intersecteday byay avinesray
ofay owsnay, ownday ichwhay onesstay ontinuallycay ollray omfray aboveay; oneay ofay emthay isay
articularlypay angerousday, asay ethay ightestslay oundsay, uchsay asay evenay eakingspay
inay aay oudlay oicevay, oducespray aay oncussioncay ofay airay ufficientsay otay awdray
estructionday uponay ethay eadhay ofay ethay eakerspay. Ethay inespay areay otnay alltay oray
uxuriantlay, utbay eythay areay ombresay anday adday anay airay ofay everitysay otay ethay enescay.
Iay ookedlay onay ethay alleyvay eneathbay; astvay istsmay ereway isingray omfray ethay iversray
ichwhay anray oughthray itay anday urlingcay inay ickthay eathswray arounday ethay oppositeay
ountainsmay, osewhay ummitssay ereway idhay inay ethay uniformay oudsclay, ilewhay ainray
ouredpay omfray ethay arkday skyay anday addeday otay ethay elancholymay impressionay Iay
eceivedray omfray ethay objectsay arounday emay. Alasay! Whyay oesday anmay oastbay ofay
ensibilitiessay uperiorsay otay osethay apparentay inay ethay utebray; itay onlyay endersray
emthay oremay ecessarynay eingsbay. Ifay ouray impulsesay ereway onfinedcay otay ungerhay,
irstthay, anday esireday, eway ightmay ebay earlynay eefray; utbay ownay eway areay ovedmay byay
everyay indway atthay owsblay anday aay ancechay ordway oray enescay atthay atthay ordway aymay
onveycay otay usay.

Eway estray; aay eamdray ashay owerpay otay oisonpay eepslay.
Eway iseray; oneay and’ringway oughtthay ollutespay ethay ayday.
Eway eelfay, onceivecay, oray easonray; aughlay oray eepway,
Embraceay ondfay oeway, oray astcay ouray arescay awayay;
Itay isay ethay amesay: orfay, ebay itay oyjay oray orrowsay,
Ethay athpay ofay itsay epartureday illstay isay eefray.
An’smay esterdayyay aymay e’ernay ebay ikelay ishay orrowmay;
Oughtnay aymay endureay utbay utabilitymay!


Itay asway earlynay oonnay enwhay Iay arriveday atay ethay optay ofay ethay ascentay. Orfay omesay
imetay Iay atsay uponay ethay ockray atthay overlooksay ethay easay ofay iceay. Aay istmay overedcay
othbay atthay anday ethay urroundingsay ountainsmay. Esentlypray aay eezebray issipatedday
ethay oudclay, anday Iay escendedday uponay ethay acierglay. Ethay urfacesay isay eryvay
unevenay, isingray ikelay ethay avesway ofay aay oubledtray easay, escendingday owlay, anday
intersperseday byay iftsray atthay inksay eepday. Ethay ieldfay ofay iceay isay almostay aay
eaguelay inay idthway, utbay Iay entspay earlynay otway ourshay inay ossingcray itay. Ethay
oppositeay ountainmay isay aay arebay erpendicularpay ockray. Omfray ethay idesay erewhay Iay
ownay oodstay Ontanvertmay asway exactlyay oppositeay, atay ethay istanceday ofay aay eaguelay;
anday aboveay itay oseray Ontmay Ancblay, inay awfulay ajestymay. Iay emainedray inay aay ecessray
ofay ethay ockray, azinggay onay isthay onderfulway anday upendousstay enescay. Ethay easay,
oray atherray ethay astvay iverray ofay iceay, oundway amongay itsay ependentday ountainsmay,
osewhay aerialay ummitssay unghay overay itsay ecessesray. Eirthay icyay anday itteringglay
eakspay oneshay inay ethay unlightsay overay ethay oudsclay. Myay earthay, ichwhay asway
eforebay orrowfulsay, ownay elledsway ithway omethingsay ikelay oyjay; Iay exclaimeday,
andering“way iritsspay, ifay indeeday eyay anderway, anday oday otnay estray inay ouryay arrownay
edsbay, alloway emay isthay aintfay appinesshay, oray aketay emay, asay ouryay ompanioncay,
awayay omfray ethay oysjay ofay ifelay.”

Asay Iay aidsay isthay Iay uddenlysay eheldbay ethay igurefay ofay aay anmay, atay omesay istanceday,
advancingay owardstay emay ithway uperhumansay eedspay. Ehay oundedbay overay ethay
evicescray inay ethay iceay, amongay ichwhay Iay adhay alkedway ithway autioncay; ishay
aturestay, alsoay, asay ehay approacheday, eemedsay otay exceeday atthay ofay anmay. Iay asway
oubledtray; aay istmay amecay overay myay eyesay, anday Iay eltfay aay aintnessfay eizesay emay,
utbay Iay asway uicklyqay estoredray byay ethay oldcay alegay ofay ethay ountainsmay. Iay
erceivedpay, asay ethay apeshay amecay earernay ight(say emendoustray anday abhorreday!)
atthay itay asway ethay etchwray omwhay Iay adhay eatedcray. Iay embledtray ithway ageray anday
orrorhay, esolvingray otay aitway ishay approachay anday enthay oseclay ithway imhay inay
ortalmay ombatcay. Ehay approacheday; ishay ountenancecay espokebay itterbay anguishay,
ombinedcay ithway isdainday anday alignitymay, ilewhay itsay unearthlyay uglinessay
enderedray itay almostay ootay orriblehay orfay umanhay eyesay. Utbay Iay arcelyscay
observeday isthay; ageray anday atredhay adhay atay irstfay eprivedday emay ofay utteranceay,
anday Iay ecoveredray onlyay otay overwhelmay imhay ithway ordsway expressiveay ofay uriousfay
etestationday anday ontemptcay.

evil“day,” Iay exclaimeday, o“day ouyay areday approachay emay? Anday oday
otnay ouyay earfay ethay iercefay engeancevay ofay myay armay eakedwray onay ouryay iserablemay eadhay?
Egonebay, ilevay insectay! Oray atherray, aystay, atthay Iay aymay ampletray ouyay otay ustday! Anday,
ohay! Atthay Iay ouldcay, ithway ethay extinctionay ofay ouryay iserablemay existenceay, estoreray
osethay ictimsvay omwhay ouyay avehay osay iabolicallyday urderedmay!”

I“ay expecteday isthay eceptionray,” aidsay ethay ondæmay. All“ay enmay atehay ethay
etchedwray; owhay, enthay, ustmay Iay ebay atedhay, owhay amay iserablemay eyondbay allay
ivinglay ingsthay! Etyay ouyay, myay eatorcray, etestday anday urnspay emay, thyay eaturecray,
otay omwhay outhay artay oundbay byay iestay onlyay issolubleday byay ethay annihilationay ofay
oneay ofay usay. Ouyay urposepay otay illkay emay. Owhay areday ouyay ortspay usthay ithway ifelay?
Oday ouryay utyday owardstay emay, anday Iay illway oday inemay owardstay ouyay anday ethay estray ofay
ankindmay. Ifay ouyay illway omplycay ithway myay onditionscay, Iay illway eavelay emthay anday
ouyay atay eacepay; utbay ifay ouyay efuseray, Iay illway utglay ethay awmay ofay eathday, untilay itay
ebay atiatedsay ithway ethay oodblay ofay ouryay emainingray iendsfray.”

Abhorred“ay onstermay! Iendfay atthay outhay artay! Ethay orturestay ofay ellhay areay ootay
ildmay aay engeancevay orfay thyay imescray. Etchedwray evilday! Ouyay eproachray emay ithway
ouryay eationcray, omecay onay, enthay, atthay Iay aymay extinguishay ethay arkspay ichwhay Iay
osay egligentlynay estowedbay.”

Myay ageray asway ithoutway oundsbay; Iay angspray onay imhay, impelleday byay allay ethay
eelingsfay ichwhay ancay armay oneay eingbay againstay ethay existenceay ofay anotheray.

Ehay easilyay eludeday emay anday aidsay,

e“bay almcay! Iay entreatay ouyay otay earhay emay eforebay ouyay ivegay entvay otay ouryay atredhay
onay myay evotedday eadhay. Avehay Iay otnay ufferedsay enoughay, atthay ouyay eeksay otay
increaseay myay iserymay? Ifelay, althoughay itay aymay onlyay ebay anay accumulationay ofay
anguishay, isay earday otay emay, anday Iay illway efendday itay. Ememberray, outhay asthay ademay
emay oremay owerfulpay anthay elfthysay; myay eighthay isay uperiorsay otay inethay, myay
ointsjay oremay upplesay. Utbay Iay illway otnay ebay emptedtay otay etsay elfmysay inay
oppositionay otay eethay. Iay amay thyay eaturecray, anday Iay illway ebay evenay ildmay anday
ocileday otay myay aturalnay ordlay anday ingkay ifay outhay iltway alsoay erformpay thyay artpay,
ethay ichwhay outhay owestay emay. Ohay, Ankensteinfray, ebay otnay equitableay otay everyay
otheray anday ampletray uponay emay aloneay, otay omwhay thyay usticejay, anday evenay thyay
emencyclay anday affectionay, isay ostmay ueday. Ememberray atthay Iay amay thyay eaturecray;
Iay oughtay otay ebay thyay Adamay, utbay Iay amay atherray ethay allenfay angelay, omwhay outhay
ivestdray omfray oyjay orfay onay isdeedmay. Everywhereay Iay eesay issblay, omfray ichwhay Iay
aloneay amay irrevocablyay excludeday. Iay asway enevolentbay anday oodgay; iserymay ademay
emay aay iendfay. Akemay emay appyhay, anday Iay allshay againay ebay irtuousvay.”

egone“bay! Iay illway otnay earhay ouyay. Erethay ancay ebay onay ommunitycay etweenbay ouyay
anday emay; eway areay enemiesay. Egonebay, oray etlay usay tryay ouray engthstray inay aay ightfay,
inay ichwhay oneay ustmay allfay.”

ow“hay ancay Iay ovemay eethay? Illway onay entreatiesay ausecay eethay otay urntay aay
avourablefay eyeay uponay thyay eaturecray, owhay imploresay thyay oodnessgay anday
ompassioncay? Elievebay emay, Ankensteinfray, Iay asway enevolentbay; myay oulsay owedglay
ithway ovelay anday umanityhay; utbay amay Iay otnay aloneay, iserablymay aloneay? Ouyay, myay
eatorcray, abhoray emay; atwhay opehay ancay Iay athergay omfray ouryay ellowfay eaturescray,
owhay oweay emay othingnay? Eythay urnspay anday atehay emay. Ethay esertday ountainsmay anday
earydray aciersglay areay myay efugeray. Iay avehay anderedway erehay anymay aysday; ethay
avescay ofay iceay, ichwhay Iay onlyay oday otnay earfay, areay aay ellingdway otay emay, anday ethay
onlyay oneay ichwhay anmay oesday otnay udgegray. Esethay eakblay iesskay Iay ailhay, orfay eythay
areay inderkay otay emay anthay ouryay ellowfay eingsbay. Ifay ethay ultitudemay ofay ankindmay
ewknay ofay myay existenceay, eythay ouldway oday asay ouyay oday, anday armay emselvesthay orfay
myay estructionday. Allshay Iay otnay enthay atehay emthay owhay abhoray emay? Iay illway eepkay
onay ermstay ithway myay enemiesay. Iay amay iserablemay, anday eythay allshay areshay myay
etchednesswray. Etyay itay isay inay ouryay owerpay otay ecompenseray emay, anday eliverday
emthay omfray anay evilay ichwhay itay onlyay emainsray orfay ouyay otay akemay osay eatgray, atthay
otnay onlyay ouyay anday ouryay amilyfay, utbay ousandsthay ofay othersay, allshay ebay
allowedsway upay inay ethay irlwindswhay ofay itsay ageray. Etlay ouryay ompassioncay ebay
ovedmay, anday oday otnay isdainday emay. Istenlay otay myay aletay; enwhay ouyay avehay eardhay
atthay, abandonay oray ommiseratecay emay, asay ouyay allshay udgejay atthay Iay eserveday.
Utbay earhay emay. Ethay uiltygay areay alloweday, byay umanhay awslay, oodyblay asay eythay
areay, otay eakspay inay eirthay ownay efenceday eforebay eythay areay ondemnedcay. Istenlay
otay emay, Ankensteinfray. Ouyay accuseay emay ofay urdermay, anday etyay ouyay ouldway, ithway
aay atisfiedsay onsciencecay, estroyday ouryay ownay eaturecray. Ohay, aisepray ethay
eternalay usticejay ofay anmay! Etyay Iay askay ouyay otnay otay arespay emay; istenlay otay emay,
anday enthay, ifay ouyay ancay, anday ifay ouyay illway, estroyday ethay orkway ofay ouryay andshay.”

“whyay oday ouyay allcay otay myay emembranceray,” Iay ejoinedray, ircumstances“cay ofay
ichwhay Iay uddershay otay eflectray, atthay Iay avehay eenbay ethay iserablemay originay anday
authoray? Ursedcay ebay ethay ayday, abhorreday evilday, inay ichwhay ouyay irstfay awsay
ightlay! Ursedcay although(ay Iay ursecay elfmysay) ebay ethay andshay atthay ormedfay ouyay!
Ouyay avehay ademay emay etchedwray eyondbay expressionay. Ouyay avehay eftlay emay onay owerpay
otay onsidercay etherwhay Iay amay ustjay otay ouyay oray otnay. Egonebay! Elieveray emay omfray
ethay ightsay ofay ouryay etestedday ormfay.”

us“thay Iay elieveray eethay, myay eatorcray,” ehay aidsay, anday acedplay ishay atedhay andshay
eforebay myay eyesay, ichwhay Iay ungflay omfray emay ithway iolencevay; us“thay Iay aketay omfray
eethay aay ightsay ichwhay ouyay abhoray. Illstay outhay anstcay istenlay otay emay anday antgray
emay thyay ompassioncay. Byay ethay irtuesvay atthay Iay onceay ossessedpay, Iay emandday isthay
omfray ouyay. Earhay myay aletay; itay isay onglay anday angestray, anday ethay emperaturetay ofay
isthay aceplay isay otnay ittingfay otay ouryay inefay ensationssay; omecay otay ethay uthay uponay
ethay ountainmay. Ethay unsay isay etyay ighhay inay ethay eavenshay; eforebay itay escendsday
otay idehay itselfay ehindbay ouryay owysnay ecipicespray anday illuminateay anotheray
orldway, ouyay illway avehay eardhay myay orystay anday ancay ecideday. Onay ouyay itay estsray,
etherwhay Iay uitqay orfay everay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofay anmay anday eadlay aay armlesshay
ifelay, oray ecomebay ethay ourgescay ofay ouryay ellowfay eaturescray anday ethay authoray ofay
ouryay ownay eedyspay uinray.”

Asay ehay aidsay isthay ehay edlay ethay ayway acrossay ethay iceay; Iay ollowedfay. Myay earthay
asway ullfay, anday Iay idday otnay answeray imhay, utbay asay Iay oceededpray, Iay eighedway ethay
ariousvay argumentsay atthay ehay adhay useday anday eterminedday atay eastlay otay istenlay otay
ishay aletay. Iay asway artlypay urgeday byay uriositycay, anday ompassioncay onfirmedcay myay
esolutionray. Iay adhay ithertohay upposedsay imhay otay ebay ethay urderermay ofay myay
otherbray, anday Iay eagerlyay oughtsay aay onfirmationcay oray enialday ofay isthay opinionay.
Orfay ethay irstfay imetay, alsoay, Iay eltfay atwhay ethay utiesday ofay aay eatorcray owardstay
ishay eaturecray ereway, anday atthay Iay oughtay otay enderray imhay appyhay eforebay Iay
omplainedcay ofay ishay ickednessway. Esethay otivesmay urgeday emay otay omplycay ithway
ishay emandday. Eway ossedcray ethay iceay, ereforethay, anday ascendeday ethay oppositeay
ockray. Ethay airay asway oldcay, anday ethay ainray againay eganbay otay escendday; eway
entereday ethay uthay, ethay iendfay ithway anay airay ofay exultationay, Iay ithway aay eavyhay
earthay anday epressedday iritsspay. Utbay Iay onsentedcay otay istenlay, anday eatingsay
elfmysay byay ethay irefay ichwhay myay odiousay ompanioncay adhay ightedlay, ehay usthay eganbay
ishay aletay.




Apterchay 11ay


It“ay isay ithway onsiderablecay ifficultyday atthay Iay ememberray ethay originalay eraay ofay
myay eingbay; allay ethay eventsay ofay atthay eriodpay appearay onfusedcay anday indistinctay.
Aay angestray ultiplicitymay ofay ensationssay eizedsay emay, anday Iay awsay, eltfay, eardhay,
anday eltsmay atay ethay amesay imetay; anday itay asway, indeeday, aay onglay imetay eforebay Iay
earnedlay otay istinguishday etweenbay ethay operationsay ofay myay ariousvay ensessay. Byay
egreesday, Iay ememberray, aay ongerstray ightlay essedpray uponay myay ervesnay, osay atthay Iay
asway obligeday otay utshay myay eyesay. Arknessday enthay amecay overay emay anday oubledtray
emay, utbay ardlyhay adhay Iay eltfay isthay enwhay, byay openingay myay eyesay, asay Iay ownay
upposesay, ethay ightlay ouredpay inay uponay emay againay. Iay alkedway anday, Iay elievebay,
escendedday, utbay Iay esentlypray oundfay aay eatgray alterationay inay myay ensationssay.
Eforebay, arkday anday opaqueay odiesbay adhay urroundedsay emay, imperviousay otay myay
ouchtay oray ightsay; utbay Iay ownay oundfay atthay Iay ouldcay anderway onay atay ibertylay, ithway
onay obstaclesay ichwhay Iay ouldcay otnay eitheray urmountsay oray avoiday. Ethay ightlay
ecamebay oremay anday oremay oppressiveay otay emay, anday ethay eathay earyingway emay asay Iay
alkedway, Iay oughtsay aay aceplay erewhay Iay ouldcay eceiveray adeshay. Isthay asway ethay
orestfay earnay Ingolstadtay; anday erehay Iay aylay byay ethay idesay ofay aay ookbray estingray
omfray myay atiguefay, untilay Iay eltfay ormentedtay byay ungerhay anday irstthay. Isthay
ousedray emay omfray myay earlynay ormantday atestay, anday Iay ateay omesay erriesbay ichwhay Iay
oundfay anginghay onay ethay eestray oray inglyay onay ethay oundgray. Iay akedslay myay irstthay
atay ethay ookbray, anday enthay inglyay ownday, asway overcomeay byay eepslay.

It“ay asway arkday enwhay Iay awokeay; Iay eltfay oldcay alsoay, anday alfhay ightenedfray, asay itay
ereway, instinctivelyay, indingfay elfmysay osay esolateday. Eforebay Iay adhay uittedqay
ouryay apartmentay, onay aay ensationsay ofay oldcay, Iay adhay overedcay elfmysay ithway omesay
othesclay, utbay esethay ereway insufficientay otay ecuresay emay omfray ethay ewsday ofay
ightnay. Iay asway aay oorpay, elplesshay, iserablemay etchwray; Iay ewknay, anday ouldcay
istinguishday, othingnay; utbay eelingfay ainpay invadeay emay onay allay idessay, Iay atsay
ownday anday eptway.

oon“say aay entlegay ightlay olestay overay ethay eavenshay anday avegay emay aay ensationsay ofay
easureplay. Iay artedstay upay anday eheldbay aay adiantray ormfay iseray omfray amongay ethay
eestray. e[thay oonmay] Iay azedgay ithway aay indkay ofay onderway. Itay ovedmay owlyslay,
utbay itay enlighteneday myay athpay, anday Iay againay entway outay inay earchsay ofay erriesbay.
Iay asway illstay oldcay enwhay underay oneay ofay ethay eestray Iay oundfay aay ugehay oakclay, ithway
