ichwhay Iay overedcay elfmysay, anday atsay ownday uponay ethay oundgray. Onay istinctday
ideasay occupieday myay indmay; allay asway onfusedcay. Iay eltfay ightlay, anday ungerhay,
anday irstthay, anday arknessday; innumerableay oundssay angray inay myay earsay, anday onay
allay idessay ariousvay entsscay alutedsay emay; ethay onlyay objectay atthay Iay ouldcay
istinguishday asway ethay ightbray oonmay, anday Iay ixedfay myay eyesay onay atthay ithway
easureplay.

everal“say angeschay ofay ayday anday ightnay assedpay, anday ethay orbay ofay ightnay adhay
eatlygray essenedlay, enwhay Iay eganbay otay istinguishday myay ensationssay omfray eachay
otheray. Iay aduallygray awsay ainlyplay ethay earclay eamstray atthay uppliedsay emay ithway
inkdray anday ethay eestray atthay adedshay emay ithway eirthay oliagefay. Iay asway elightedday
enwhay Iay irstfay iscoveredday atthay aay easantplay oundsay, ichwhay oftenay alutedsay myay
earsay, oceededpray omfray ethay oatsthray ofay ethay ittlelay ingedway animalsay owhay adhay
oftenay intercepteday ethay ightlay omfray myay eyesay. Iay eganbay alsoay otay observeay,
ithway eatergray accuracyay, ethay ormsfay atthay urroundedsay emay anday otay erceivepay ethay
oundariesbay ofay ethay adiantray oofray ofay ightlay ichwhay anopiedcay emay. Ometimessay Iay
iedtray otay imitateay ethay easantplay ongssay ofay ethay irdsbay utbay asway unableay.
Ometimessay Iay ishedway otay expressay myay ensationssay inay myay ownay odemay, utbay ethay
uncouthay anday inarticulateay oundssay ichwhay okebray omfray emay ightenedfray emay intoay
ilencesay againay.

e“thay oonmay adhay isappearedday omfray ethay ightnay, anday againay, ithway aay essenedlay
ormfay, owedshay itselfay, ilewhay Iay illstay emainedray inay ethay orestfay. Myay
ensationssay adhay byay isthay imetay ecomebay istinctday, anday myay indmay eceivedray everyay
ayday additionalay ideasay. Myay eyesay ecamebay accustomeday otay ethay ightlay anday otay
erceivepay objectsay inay eirthay ightray ormsfay; Iay istinguishedday ethay insectay omfray
ethay erbhay, anday byay egreesday, oneay erbhay omfray anotheray. Iay oundfay atthay ethay
arrowspay uttereday onenay utbay arshhay otesnay, ilstwhay osethay ofay ethay ackbirdblay anday
ushthray ereway eetsway anday enticingay.

One“ay ayday, enwhay Iay asway oppresseday byay oldcay, Iay oundfay aay irefay ichwhay adhay eenbay
eftlay byay omesay anderingway eggarsbay, anday asway overcomeay ithway elightday atay ethay
armthway Iay experienceday omfray itay. Inay myay oyjay Iay ustthray myay andhay intoay ethay ivelay
embersay, utbay uicklyqay ewdray itay outay againay ithway aay cryay ofay ainpay. Owhay angestray,
Iay oughtthay, atthay ethay amesay ausecay ouldshay oducepray uchsay oppositeay effectsay! Iay
examineday ethay aterialsmay ofay ethay irefay, anday otay myay oyjay oundfay itay otay ebay
omposedcay ofay oodway. Iay uicklyqay ollectedcay omesay anchesbray, utbay eythay ereway etway
anday ouldway otnay urnbay. Iay asway ainedpay atay isthay anday atsay illstay atchingway ethay
operationay ofay ethay irefay. Ethay etway oodway ichwhay Iay adhay acedplay earnay ethay eathay
ieddray anday itselfay ecamebay inflameday. Iay eflectedray onay isthay, anday byay ouchingtay
ethay ariousvay anchesbray, Iay iscoveredday ethay ausecay anday usiedbay elfmysay inay
ollectingcay aay eatgray uantityqay ofay oodway, atthay Iay ightmay dryay itay anday avehay aay
entifulplay upplysay ofay irefay. Enwhay ightnay amecay onay anday oughtbray eepslay ithway
itay, Iay asway inay ethay eatestgray earfay estlay myay irefay ouldshay ebay extinguisheday. Iay
overedcay itay arefullycay ithway dryay oodway anday eaveslay anday acedplay etway anchesbray
uponay itay; anday enthay, eadingspray myay oakclay, Iay aylay onay ethay oundgray anday anksay
intoay eepslay.

It“ay asway orningmay enwhay Iay awokeay, anday myay irstfay arecay asway otay isitvay ethay irefay.
Iay uncovereday itay, anday aay entlegay eezebray uicklyqay annedfay itay intoay aay ameflay. Iay
observeday isthay alsoay anday ontrivedcay aay anfay ofay anchesbray, ichwhay ousedray ethay
embersay enwhay eythay ereway earlynay extinguisheday. Enwhay ightnay amecay againay Iay
oundfay, ithway easureplay, atthay ethay irefay avegay ightlay asay ellway asay eathay anday atthay
ethay iscoveryday ofay isthay elementay asway usefulay otay emay inay myay oodfay, orfay Iay oundfay
omesay ofay ethay offalsay atthay ethay avellerstray adhay eftlay adhay eenbay oastedray, anday
astedtay uchmay oremay avourysay anthay ethay erriesbay Iay atheredgay omfray ethay eestray. Iay
iedtray, ereforethay, otay essdray myay oodfay inay ethay amesay annermay, acingplay itay onay
ethay ivelay embersay. Iay oundfay atthay ethay erriesbay ereway oiledspay byay isthay
operationay, anday ethay utsnay anday ootsray uchmay improveday.

ood“fay, oweverhay, ecamebay arcescay, anday Iay oftenay entspay ethay olewhay ayday
earchingsay inay ainvay orfay aay ewfay acornsay otay assuageay ethay angspay ofay ungerhay. Enwhay
Iay oundfay isthay, Iay esolvedray otay uitqay ethay aceplay atthay Iay adhay ithertohay
inhabiteday, otay eeksay orfay oneay erewhay ethay ewfay antsway Iay experienceday ouldway ebay
oremay easilyay atisfiedsay. Inay isthay emigrationay Iay exceedinglyay amentedlay ethay
osslay ofay ethay irefay ichwhay Iay adhay obtaineday oughthray accidentay anday ewknay otnay owhay
otay eproduceray itay. Iay avegay everalsay ourshay otay ethay erioussay onsiderationcay ofay
isthay ifficultyday, utbay Iay asway obligeday otay elinquishray allay attemptay otay upplysay
itay, anday appingwray elfmysay upay inay myay oakclay, Iay uckstray acrossay ethay oodway
owardstay ethay ettingsay unsay. Iay assedpay eethray aysday inay esethay amblesray anday atay
engthlay iscoveredday ethay openay ountrycay. Aay eatgray allfay ofay owsnay adhay akentay
aceplay ethay ightnay eforebay, anday ethay ieldsfay ereway ofay oneay uniformay itewhay; ethay
appearanceay asway isconsolateday, anday Iay oundfay myay eetfay illedchay byay ethay oldcay
ampday ubstancesay atthay overedcay ethay oundgray.

It“ay asway aboutay evensay inay ethay orningmay, anday Iay ongedlay otay obtainay oodfay anday
eltershay; atay engthlay Iay erceivedpay aay allsmay uthay, onay aay isingray oundgray, ichwhay
adhay oubtlessday eenbay uiltbay orfay ethay onveniencecay ofay omesay epherdshay. Isthay
asway aay ewnay ightsay otay emay, anday Iay examineday ethay ucturestray ithway eatgray
uriositycay. Indingfay ethay oorday openay, Iay entereday. Anay olday anmay atsay inay itay,
earnay aay irefay, overay ichwhay ehay asway eparingpray ishay eakfastbray. Ehay urnedtay onay
earinghay aay oisenay, anday erceivingpay emay, iekedshray oudlylay, anday uittingqay ethay
uthay, anray acrossay ethay ieldsfay ithway aay eedspay ofay ichwhay ishay ebilitatedday ormfay
ardlyhay appeareday apablecay. Ishay appearanceay, ifferentday omfray anyay Iay adhay everay
eforebay eensay, anday ishay ightflay omewhatsay urprisedsay emay. Utbay Iay asway enchanteday
byay ethay appearanceay ofay ethay uthay; erehay ethay owsnay anday ainray ouldcay otnay
enetratepay; ethay oundgray asway dryay; anday itay esentedpray otay emay enthay asay exquisiteay
anday ivineday aay etreatray asay Andæmoniumpay appeareday otay ethay onsdæmay ofay ellhay
afteray eirthay ufferingssay inay ethay akelay ofay irefay. Iay eedilygray evouredday ethay
emnantsray ofay ethay epherd’sshay eakfastbray, ichwhay onsistedcay ofay eadbray, eesechay,
ilkmay, anday ineway; ethay atterlay, oweverhay, Iay idday otnay ikelay. Enthay, overcomeay byay
atiguefay, Iay aylay ownday amongay omesay awstray anday ellfay asleepay.

It“ay asway oonnay enwhay Iay awokeay, anday allureday byay ethay armthway ofay ethay unsay, ichwhay
oneshay ightlybray onay ethay itewhay oundgray, Iay eterminedday otay ecommenceray myay
avelstray; anday, epositingday ethay emainsray ofay ethay easant’spay eakfastbray inay aay
alletway Iay oundfay, Iay oceededpray acrossay ethay ieldsfay orfay everalsay ourshay, untilay
atay unsetsay Iay arriveday atay aay illagevay. Owhay iraculousmay idday isthay appearay! Ethay
utshay, ethay eaternay ottagescay, anday atelystay ouseshay engageday myay admirationay byay
urnstay. Ethay egetablesvay inay ethay ardensgay, ethay ilkmay anday eesechay atthay Iay awsay
acedplay atay ethay indowsway ofay omesay ofay ethay ottagescay, allureday myay appetiteay. Oneay
ofay ethay estbay ofay esethay Iay entereday, utbay Iay adhay ardlyhay acedplay myay ootfay ithinway
ethay oorday eforebay ethay ildrenchay iekedshray, anday oneay ofay ethay omenway aintedfay.
Ethay olewhay illagevay asway ousedray; omesay edflay, omesay attackeday emay, untilay,
ievouslygray uisedbray byay onesstay anday anymay otheray indskay ofay issilemay eaponsway, Iay
escapeday otay ethay openay ountrycay anday earfullyfay ooktay efugeray inay aay owlay ovelhay,
uiteqay arebay, anday akingmay aay etchedwray appearanceay afteray ethay alacespay Iay adhay
eheldbay inay ethay illagevay. Isthay ovelhay oweverhay, oinedjay aay ottagecay ofay aay eatnay
anday easantplay appearanceay, utbay afteray myay atelay earlyday oughtbay experienceay, Iay
aredday otnay enteray itay. Myay aceplay ofay efugeray asway onstructedcay ofay oodway, utbay osay
owlay atthay Iay ouldcay ithway ifficultyday itsay uprightay inay itay. Onay oodway, oweverhay,
asway acedplay onay ethay earthay, ichwhay ormedfay ethay oorflay, utbay itay asway dryay; anday
althoughay ethay indway entereday itay byay innumerableay inkschay, Iay oundfay itay anay
agreeableay asylumay omfray ethay owsnay anday ainray.

ere“hay, enthay, Iay etreatedray anday aylay ownday appyhay otay avehay oundfay aay eltershay,
oweverhay iserablemay, omfray ethay inclemencyay ofay ethay easonsay, anday illstay oremay
omfray ethay arbaritybay ofay anmay. Asay oonsay asay orningmay awnedday Iay eptcray omfray myay
ennelkay, atthay Iay ightmay iewvay ethay adjacentay ottagecay anday iscoverday ifay Iay ouldcay
emainray inay ethay abitationhay Iay adhay oundfay. Itay asway ituatedsay againstay ethay ackbay
ofay ethay ottagecay anday urroundedsay onay ethay idessay ichwhay ereway exposeday byay aay igpay
styay anday aay earclay oolpay ofay aterway. Oneay artpay asway openay, anday byay atthay Iay adhay
eptcray inay; utbay ownay Iay overedcay everyay evicecray byay ichwhay Iay ightmay ebay erceivedpay
ithway onesstay anday oodway, etyay inay uchsay aay annermay atthay Iay ightmay ovemay emthay onay
occasionay otay asspay outay; allay ethay ightlay Iay enjoyeday amecay oughthray ethay styay, anday
atthay asway ufficientsay orfay emay.

aving“hay usthay arrangeday myay ellingdway anday arpetedcay itay ithway eanclay awstray, Iay
etiredray, orfay Iay awsay ethay igurefay ofay aay anmay atay aay istanceday, anday Iay ememberedray
ootay ellway myay eatmenttray ethay ightnay eforebay otay usttray elfmysay inay ishay owerpay. Iay
adhay irstfay, oweverhay, ovidedpray orfay myay ustenancesay orfay atthay ayday byay aay oaflay
ofay oarsecay eadbray, ichwhay Iay urloinedpay, anday aay upcay ithway ichwhay Iay ouldcay inkdray
oremay onvenientlycay anthay omfray myay andhay ofay ethay urepay aterway ichwhay owedflay byay
myay etreatray. Ethay oorflay asway aay ittlelay aisedray, osay atthay itay asway eptkay
erfectlypay dryay, anday byay itsay icinityvay otay ethay imneychay ofay ethay ottagecay itay asway
olerablytay armway.

eing“bay usthay ovidedpray, Iay esolvedray otay esideray inay isthay ovelhay untilay
omethingsay ouldshay occuray ichwhay ightmay alteray myay eterminationday. Itay asway
indeeday aay aradisepay omparedcay otay ethay eakblay orestfay, myay ormerfay esidenceray,
ethay ain-droppingclay anchesbray, anday ankday earthay. Iay ateay myay eakfastbray ithway
easureplay anday asway aboutay otay emoveray aay ankplay otay ocurepray elfmysay aay ittlelay
aterway enwhay Iay eardhay aay epstay, anday ookinglay oughthray aay allsmay inkchay, Iay eheldbay
aay oungyay eaturecray, ithway aay ailpay onay erhay eadhay, assingpay eforebay myay ovelhay. Ethay
irlgay asway oungyay anday ofay entlegay emeanourday, unlikeay atwhay Iay avehay incesay oundfay
ottagerscay anday armhousefay ervantssay otay ebay. Etyay eshay asway eanlymay esseddray, aay
oarsecay ueblay etticoatpay anday aay inenlay acketjay eingbay erhay onlyay arbgay; erhay airfay
airhay asway aitedplay utbay otnay adorneday: eshay ookedlay atientpay etyay adsay. Iay ostlay
ightsay ofay erhay, anday inay aboutay aay uarterqay ofay anay ourhay eshay eturnedray earingbay
ethay ailpay, ichwhay asway ownay artlypay illedfay ithway ilkmay. Asay eshay alkedway alongay,
eeminglysay incommodeday byay ethay urdenbay, aay oungyay anmay etmay erhay, osewhay
ountenancecay expresseday aay eeperday espondenceday. Utteringay aay ewfay oundssay ithway
anay airay ofay elancholymay, ehay ooktay ethay ailpay omfray erhay eadhay anday orebay itay otay ethay
ottagecay imselfhay. Eshay ollowedfay, anday eythay isappearedday. Esentlypray Iay awsay
ethay oungyay anmay againay, ithway omesay oolstay inay ishay andhay, osscray ethay ieldfay
ehindbay ethay ottagecay; anday ethay irlgay asway alsoay usiedbay, ometimessay inay ethay
ousehay anday ometimessay inay ethay ardyay.

On“ay examiningay myay ellingdway, Iay oundfay atthay oneay ofay ethay indowsway ofay ethay
ottagecay adhay ormerlyfay occupieday aay artpay ofay itay, utbay ethay anespay adhay eenbay
illedfay upay ithway oodway. Inay oneay ofay esethay asway aay allsmay anday almostay
imperceptibleay inkchay oughthray ichwhay ethay eyeay ouldcay ustjay enetratepay.
Oughthray isthay evicecray aay allsmay oomray asway isiblevay, itewashedwhay anday eanclay
utbay eryvay arebay ofay urniturefay. Inay oneay ornercay, earnay aay allsmay irefay, atsay anay
olday anmay, eaninglay ishay eadhay onay ishay andshay inay aay isconsolateday attitudeay. Ethay
oungyay irlgay asway occupieday inay arrangingay ethay ottagecay; utbay esentlypray eshay
ooktay omethingsay outay ofay aay awerdray, ichwhay employeday erhay andshay, anday eshay atsay
ownday esidebay ethay olday anmay, owhay, akingtay upay anay instrumentay, eganbay otay ayplay
anday otay oducepray oundssay eetersway anthay ethay oicevay ofay ethay ushthray oray ethay
ightingalenay. Itay asway aay ovelylay ightsay, evenay otay emay, oorpay etchwray owhay adhay
evernay eheldbay aughtay eautifulbay eforebay. Ethay ilversay airhay anday enevolentbay
ountenancecay ofay ethay ageday ottagercay onway myay everenceray, ilewhay ethay entlegay
annersmay ofay ethay irlgay enticeday myay ovelay. Ehay ayedplay aay eetsway ournfulmay airay
ichwhay Iay erceivedpay ewdray earstay omfray ethay eyesay ofay ishay amiableay ompanioncay, ofay
ichwhay ethay olday anmay ooktay onay oticenay, untilay eshay obbedsay audiblyay; ehay enthay
onouncedpray aay ewfay oundssay, anday ethay airfay eaturecray, eavinglay erhay orkway, eltknay
atay ishay eetfay. Ehay aisedray erhay anday iledsmay ithway uchsay indnesskay anday affectionay
atthay Iay eltfay ensationssay ofay aay eculiarpay anday overpoweringay aturenay; eythay ereway
aay ixturemay ofay ainpay anday easureplay, uchsay asay Iay adhay evernay eforebay experienceday,
eitheray omfray ungerhay oray oldcay, armthway oray oodfay; anday Iay ithdrewway omfray ethay
indowway, unableay otay earbay esethay emotionsay.

oon“say afteray isthay ethay oungyay anmay eturnedray, earingbay onay ishay ouldersshay aay
oadlay ofay oodway. Ethay irlgay etmay imhay atay ethay oorday, elpedhay otay elieveray imhay ofay
ishay urdenbay, anday akingtay omesay ofay ethay uelfay intoay ethay ottagecay, acedplay itay onay
ethay irefay; enthay eshay anday ethay outhyay entway apartay intoay aay ooknay ofay ethay ottagecay,
anday ehay owedshay erhay aay argelay oaflay anday aay iecepay ofay eesechay. Eshay eemedsay
easedplay anday entway intoay ethay ardengay orfay omesay ootsray anday antsplay, ichwhay eshay
acedplay inay aterway, anday enthay uponay ethay irefay. Eshay afterwardsay ontinuedcay erhay
orkway, ilstwhay ethay oungyay anmay entway intoay ethay ardengay anday appeareday usilybay
employeday inay iggingday anday ullingpay upay ootsray. Afteray ehay adhay eenbay employeday
usthay aboutay anay ourhay, ethay oungyay omanway oinedjay imhay anday eythay entereday ethay
ottagecay ogethertay.

e“thay olday anmay adhay, inay ethay eantimemay, eenbay ensivepay, utbay onay ethay appearanceay
ofay ishay ompanionscay ehay assumeday aay oremay eerfulchay airay, anday eythay atsay ownday otay
eatay. Ethay ealmay asway uicklyqay ispatchedday. Ethay oungyay omanway asway againay
occupieday inay arrangingay ethay ottagecay, ethay olday anmay alkedway eforebay ethay
ottagecay inay ethay unsay orfay aay ewfay inutesmay, eaninglay onay ethay armay ofay ethay outhyay.
Othingnay ouldcay exceeday inay eautybay ethay ontrastcay etweenbay esethay otway excellentay
eaturescray. Oneay asway olday, ithway ilversay airshay anday aay ountenancecay eamingbay
ithway enevolencebay anday ovelay; ethay oungeryay asway ightslay anday acefulgray inay ishay
igurefay, anday ishay eaturesfay ereway ouldedmay ithway ethay inestfay etrysymmay, etyay ishay
eyesay anday attitudeay expresseday ethay utmostay adnesssay anday espondencyday. Ethay
olday anmay eturnedray otay ethay ottagecay, anday ethay outhyay, ithway oolstay ifferentday
omfray osethay ehay adhay useday inay ethay orningmay, irectedday ishay epsstay acrossay ethay
ieldsfay.

ight“nay uicklyqay utshay inay, utbay otay myay extremeay onderway, Iay oundfay atthay ethay
ottagerscay adhay aay eansmay ofay olongingpray ightlay byay ethay useay ofay aperstay, anday asway
elightedday otay indfay atthay ethay ettingsay ofay ethay unsay idday otnay utpay anay enday otay ethay
easureplay Iay experienceday inay atchingway myay umanhay eighboursnay. Inay ethay eveningay
ethay oungyay irlgay anday erhay ompanioncay ereway employeday inay ariousvay occupationsay
ichwhay Iay idday otnay understanday; anday ethay olday anmay againay ooktay upay ethay
instrumentay ichwhay oducedpray ethay ivineday oundssay atthay adhay enchanteday emay inay
ethay orningmay. Osay oonsay asay ehay adhay inishedfay, ethay outhyay eganbay, otnay otay ayplay,
utbay otay utteray oundssay atthay ereway onotonousmay, anday eithernay esemblingray ethay
armonyhay ofay ethay olday an’smay instrumentay ornay ethay ongssay ofay ethay irdsbay; Iay incesay
oundfay atthay ehay eadray alouday, utbay atay atthay imetay Iay ewknay othingnay ofay ethay
iencescay ofay ordsway oray etterslay.

e“thay amilyfay, afteray avinghay eenbay usthay occupieday orfay aay ortshay imetay,
extinguisheday eirthay ightslay anday etiredray, asay Iay onjecturedcay, otay estray.”




Apterchay 12ay


I“ay aylay onay myay awstray, utbay Iay ouldcay otnay eepslay. Iay oughtthay ofay ethay
occurrencesay ofay ethay ayday. Atwhay ieflychay uckstray emay asway ethay entlegay annersmay
ofay esethay eoplepay, anday Iay ongedlay otay oinjay emthay, utbay aredday otnay. Iay
ememberedray ootay ellway ethay eatmenttray Iay adhay ufferedsay ethay ightnay eforebay omfray
ethay arbarousbay illagersvay, anday esolvedray, ateverwhay oursecay ofay onductcay Iay
ightmay ereafterhay inkthay itay ightray otay ursuepay, atthay orfay ethay esentpray Iay ouldway
emainray uietlyqay inay myay ovelhay, atchingway anday endeavouringay otay iscoverday ethay
otivesmay ichwhay influenceday eirthay actionsay.

e“thay ottagerscay aroseay ethay extnay orningmay eforebay ethay unsay. Ethay oungyay omanway
arrangeday ethay ottagecay anday eparedpray ethay oodfay, anday ethay outhyay epartedday
afteray ethay irstfay ealmay.

is“thay ayday asway assedpay inay ethay amesay outineray asay atthay ichwhay ecededpray itay.
Ethay oungyay anmay asway onstantlycay employeday outay ofay oorsday, anday ethay irlgay inay
ariousvay aboriouslay occupationsay ithinway. Ethay olday anmay, omwhay Iay oonsay
erceivedpay otay ebay indblay, employeday ishay eisurelay ourshay onay ishay instrumentay oray
inay ontemplationcay. Othingnay ouldcay exceeday ethay ovelay anday espectray ichwhay ethay
oungeryay ottagerscay exhibiteday owardstay eirthay enerablevay ompanioncay. Eythay
erformedpay owardstay imhay everyay ittlelay officeay ofay affectionay anday utyday ithway
entlenessgay, anday ehay ewardedray emthay byay ishay enevolentbay ilessmay.

ey“thay ereway otnay entirelyay appyhay. Ethay oungyay anmay anday ishay ompanioncay oftenay
entway apartay anday appeareday otay eepway. Iay awsay onay ausecay orfay eirthay unhappinessay,
utbay Iay asway eeplyday affecteday byay itay. Ifay uchsay ovelylay eaturescray ereway
iserablemay, itay asway esslay angestray atthay Iay, anay imperfectay anday olitarysay eingbay,
ouldshay ebay etchedwray. Etyay whyay ereway esethay entlegay eingsbay unhappyay? Eythay
ossessedpay aay elightfulday ousehay or(fay uchsay itay asway inay myay eyesay) anday everyay
uxurylay; eythay adhay aay irefay otay armway emthay enwhay illchay anday eliciousday iandsvay
enwhay ungryhay; eythay ereway esseddray inay excellentay othesclay; anday, illstay oremay,
eythay enjoyeday oneay another’say ompanycay anday eechspay, interchangingay eachay ayday
ookslay ofay affectionay anday indnesskay. Atwhay idday eirthay earstay implyay? Idday eythay
eallyray expressay ainpay? Iay asway atay irstfay unableay otay olvesay esethay uestionsqay,
utbay erpetualpay attentionay anday imetay explaineday otay emay anymay appearancesay ichwhay
ereway atay irstfay enigmaticay.

A“ay onsiderablecay eriodpay elapseday eforebay Iay iscoveredday oneay ofay ethay ausescay ofay
ethay uneasinessay ofay isthay amiableay amilyfay: itay asway overtypay, anday eythay
ufferedsay atthay evilay inay aay eryvay istressingday egreeday. Eirthay ourishmentnay
onsistedcay entirelyay ofay ethay egetablesvay ofay eirthay ardengay anday ethay ilkmay ofay
oneay owcay, ichwhay avegay eryvay ittlelay uringday ethay interway, enwhay itsay astersmay
ouldcay arcelyscay ocurepray oodfay otay upportsay itay. Eythay oftenay, Iay elievebay,
ufferedsay ethay angspay ofay ungerhay eryvay oignantlypay, especiallyay ethay otway
oungeryay ottagerscay, orfay everalsay imestay eythay acedplay oodfay eforebay ethay olday
anmay enwhay eythay eservedray onenay orfay emselvesthay.

is“thay aittray ofay indnesskay ovedmay emay ensiblysay. Iay adhay eenbay accustomeday,
uringday ethay ightnay, otay ealstay aay artpay ofay eirthay orestay orfay myay ownay
onsumptioncay, utbay enwhay Iay oundfay atthay inay oingday isthay Iay inflicteday ainpay onay
ethay ottagerscay, Iay abstaineday anday atisfiedsay elfmysay ithway erriesbay, utsnay, anday
ootsray ichwhay Iay atheredgay omfray aay eighbouringnay oodway.

I“ay iscoveredday alsoay anotheray eansmay oughthray ichwhay Iay asway enableday otay assistay
eirthay abourslay. Iay oundfay atthay ethay outhyay entspay aay eatgray artpay ofay eachay ayday
inay ollectingcay oodway orfay ethay amilyfay irefay, anday uringday ethay ightnay Iay oftenay
ooktay ishay oolstay, ethay useay ofay ichwhay Iay uicklyqay iscoveredday, anday oughtbray omehay
iringfay ufficientsay orfay ethay onsumptioncay ofay everalsay aysday.

I“ay ememberray, ethay irstfay imetay atthay Iay idday isthay, ethay oungyay omanway, enwhay eshay
openeday ethay oorday inay ethay orningmay, appeareday eatlygray astonisheday onay eeingsay aay eatgray
ilepay ofay oodway onay ethay outsideay. Eshay uttereday omesay ordsway inay aay oudlay oicevay, anday ethay
outhyay oinedjay erhay, owhay alsoay expresseday urprisesay. Iay observeday, ithway easureplay,
atthay ehay idday otnay ogay otay ethay orestfay atthay ayday, utbay entspay itay inay epairingray ethay
ottagecay anday ultivatingcay ethay ardengay.

“byay egreesday Iay ademay aay iscoveryday ofay illstay eatergray omentmay. Iay oundfay atthay
esethay eoplepay ossessedpay aay ethodmay ofay ommunicatingcay eirthay experienceay anday
eelingsfay otay oneay anotheray byay articulateay oundssay. Iay erceivedpay atthay ethay ordsway
eythay okespay ometimessay oducedpray easureplay oray ainpay, ilessmay oray adnesssay, inay ethay
indsmay anday ountenancescay ofay ethay earershay. Isthay asway indeeday aay odlikegay iencescay,
anday Iay ardentlyay esiredday otay ecomebay acquainteday ithway itay. Utbay Iay asway affledbay inay
everyay attemptay Iay ademay orfay isthay urposepay. Eirthay onunciationpray asway uickqay, anday
ethay ordsway eythay uttereday, otnay avinghay anyay apparentay onnectioncay ithway isiblevay
objectsay, Iay asway unableay otay iscoverday anyay ueclay byay ichwhay Iay ouldcay unravelay ethay
erymystay ofay eirthay eferenceray. Byay eatgray applicationay, oweverhay, anday afteray avinghay
emainedray uringday ethay acespay ofay everalsay evolutionsray ofay ethay oonmay inay myay ovelhay, Iay
iscoveredday ethay amesnay atthay ereway ivengay otay omesay ofay ethay ostmay amiliarfay objectsay ofay
iscourseday; Iay earnedlay anday applieday ethay ordsway, ire_fay, ilkmay, eadbray,_ anday
ood_way._ Iay earnedlay alsoay ethay amesnay ofay ethay ottagerscay emselvesthay. Ethay outhyay
anday ishay ompanioncay adhay eachay ofay emthay everalsay amesnay, utbay ethay olday anmay adhay onlyay
oneay, ichwhay asway ather_fay._ Ethay irlgay asway alledcay ister_say_ oray
Agatha_ay,_ anday ethay outhyay elix_fay, otherbray,_ oray on_say_. Iay annotcay
escribeday ethay elightday Iay eltfay enwhay Iay earnedlay ethay ideasay appropriateday otay eachay ofay
esethay oundssay anday asway ableay otay onouncepray emthay. Iay istinguishedday everalsay otheray
ordsway ithoutway eingbay ableay asay etyay otay understanday oray applyay emthay, uchsay asay ood_gay,
earestday, unhappyay._

I“ay entspay ethay interway inay isthay annermay. Ethay entlegay annersmay anday eautybay ofay
ethay ottagerscay eatlygray endeareday emthay otay emay; enwhay eythay ereway unhappyay, Iay
eltfay epressedday; enwhay eythay ejoicedray, Iay athisedsympay inay eirthay oysjay. Iay awsay
ewfay umanhay eingsbay esidesbay emthay, anday ifay anyay otheray appenedhay otay enteray ethay
ottagecay, eirthay arshhay annersmay anday uderay aitgay onlyay enhanceday otay emay ethay
uperiorsay accomplishmentsay ofay myay iendsfray. Ethay olday anmay, Iay ouldcay erceivepay,
oftenay endeavoureday otay encourageay ishay ildrenchay, asay ometimessay Iay oundfay atthay
ehay alledcay emthay, otay astcay offay eirthay elancholymay. Ehay ouldway alktay inay aay
eerfulchay accentay, ithway anay expressionay ofay oodnessgay atthay estowedbay easureplay
evenay uponay emay. Agathaay istenedlay ithway espectray, erhay eyesay ometimessay illedfay
ithway earstay, ichwhay eshay endeavoureday otay ipeway awayay unperceiveday; utbay Iay
enerallygay oundfay atthay erhay ountenancecay anday onetay ereway oremay eerfulchay afteray
avinghay istenedlay otay ethay exhortationsay ofay erhay atherfay. Itay asway otnay usthay
ithway Elixfay. Ehay asway alwaysay ethay addestsay ofay ethay oupgray, anday evenay otay myay
unpractiseday ensessay, ehay appeareday otay avehay ufferedsay oremay eeplyday anthay ishay
iendsfray. Utbay ifay ishay ountenancecay asway oremay orrowfulsay, ishay oicevay asway oremay
eerfulchay anthay atthay ofay ishay istersay, especiallyay enwhay ehay addresseday ethay olday
anmay.

I“ay ouldcay entionmay innumerableay instancesay ichwhay, althoughay ightslay, arkedmay
ethay ispositionsday ofay esethay amiableay ottagerscay. Inay ethay idstmay ofay overtypay
anday antway, Elixfay arriedcay ithway easureplay otay ishay istersay ethay irstfay ittlelay
itewhay owerflay atthay eepedpay outay omfray eneathbay ethay owysnay oundgray. Earlyay inay
ethay orningmay, eforebay eshay adhay isenray, ehay earedclay awayay ethay owsnay atthay
obstructeday erhay athpay otay ethay ilk-houseclay, ewdray aterway omfray ethay ellway, anday
oughtbray ethay oodway omfray ethay outhouseay, erewhay, otay ishay erpetualpay
astonishmentay, ehay oundfay ishay orestay alwaysay eplenishedray byay anay invisibleay
andhay. Inay ethay ayday, Iay elievebay, ehay orkedway ometimessay orfay aay eighbouringnay
armerfay, ecausebay ehay oftenay entway orthfay anday idday otnay eturnray untilay innerday,
etyay oughtbray onay oodway ithway imhay. Atay otheray imestay ehay orkedway inay ethay ardengay,
utbay asay erethay asway ittlelay otay oday inay ethay ostyfray easonsay, ehay eadray otay ethay olday
anmay anday Agathaay.

is“thay eadingray adhay uzzledpay emay extremelyay atay irstfay, utbay byay egreesday Iay
iscoveredday atthay ehay uttereday anymay ofay ethay amesay oundssay enwhay ehay eadray asay enwhay
ehay alkedtay. Iay onjecturedcay, ereforethay, atthay ehay oundfay onay ethay aperpay ignssay
orfay eechspay ichwhay ehay understooday, anday Iay ardentlyay ongedlay otay omprehendcay
esethay alsoay; utbay owhay asway atthay ossiblepay enwhay Iay idday otnay evenay understanday
ethay oundssay orfay ichwhay eythay oodstay asay ignssay? Iay improveday, oweverhay,
ensiblysay inay isthay iencescay, utbay otnay ufficientlysay otay ollowfay upay anyay indkay ofay
onversationcay, althoughay Iay applieday myay olewhay indmay otay ethay endeavouray, orfay Iay
easilyay erceivedpay atthay, althoughay Iay eagerlyay ongedlay otay iscoverday elfmysay otay
ethay ottagerscay, Iay oughtay otnay otay akemay ethay attemptay untilay Iay adhay irstfay ecomebay
astermay ofay eirthay anguagelay, ichwhay owledgeknay ightmay enableay emay otay akemay emthay
overlookay ethay eformityday ofay myay igurefay, orfay ithway isthay alsoay ethay ontrastcay
erpetuallypay esentedpray otay myay eyesay adhay ademay emay acquainteday.

I“ay adhay admireday ethay erfectpay ormsfay ofay myay ottagers—theircay acegray, eautybay,
anday elicateday omplexionscay; utbay owhay asway Iay errifiedtay enwhay Iay iewedvay elfmysay
inay aay ansparenttray oolpay! Atay irstfay Iay artedstay ackbay, unableay otay elievebay atthay
itay asway indeeday Iay owhay asway eflectedray inay ethay irrormay; anday enwhay Iay ecamebay
ullyfay onvincedcay atthay Iay asway inay ealityray ethay onstermay atthay Iay amay, Iay asway
illedfay ithway ethay itterestbay ensationssay ofay espondenceday anday ortificationmay.
Alasay! Iay idday otnay etyay entirelyay owknay ethay atalfay effectsay ofay isthay iserablemay
eformityday.

As“ay ethay unsay ecamebay armerway anday ethay ightlay ofay ayday ongerlay, ethay owsnay
anishedvay, anday Iay eheldbay ethay arebay eestray anday ethay ackblay earthay. Omfray isthay
imetay Elixfay asway oremay employeday, anday ethay eart-movingclay indicationsay ofay
impendingay aminefay isappearedday. Eirthay oodfay, asay Iay afterwardsay oundfay, asway
oarsecay, utbay itay asway olesomewhay; anday eythay ocuredpray aay ufficiencysay ofay itay.
Everalsay ewnay indskay ofay antsplay angspray upay inay ethay ardengay, ichwhay eythay
esseddray; anday esethay ignssay ofay omfortcay increaseday ailyday asay ethay easonsay
advanceday.

e“thay olday anmay, eaninglay onay ishay onsay, alkedway eachay ayday atay oonnay, enwhay itay idday
otnay ainray, asay Iay oundfay itay asway alledcay enwhay ethay eavenshay ouredpay orthfay itsay
atersway. Isthay equentlyfray ooktay aceplay, utbay aay ighhay indway uicklyqay ieddray ethay
earthay, anday ethay easonsay ecamebay arfay oremay easantplay anthay itay adhay eenbay.

“myay odemay ofay ifelay inay myay ovelhay asway uniformay. Uringday ethay orningmay Iay
attendeday ethay otionsmay ofay ethay ottagerscay, anday enwhay eythay ereway ispersedday inay
ariousvay occupationsay, Iay eptslay; ethay emainderray ofay ethay ayday asway entspay inay
observingay myay iendsfray. Enwhay eythay adhay etiredray otay estray, ifay erethay asway anyay
oonmay oray ethay ightnay asway ar-lightclay, Iay entway intoay ethay oodsway anday ollectedcay
myay ownay oodfay anday uelfay orfay ethay ottagecay. Enwhay Iay eturnedray, asay oftenay asay itay
asway ecessarynay, Iay earedclay eirthay athpay omfray ethay owsnay anday erformedpay osethay
officesay atthay Iay adhay eensay oneday byay Elixfay. Iay afterwardsay oundfay atthay esethay
abourslay, erformedpay byay anay invisibleay andhay, eatlygray astonisheday emthay; anday
onceay oray icetway Iay eardhay emthay, onay esethay occasionsay, utteray ethay ordsway ood_gay
iritspay, onderfulway_; utbay Iay idday otnay enthay understanday ethay ignificationsay
ofay esethay ermstay.

“myay oughtsthay ownay ecamebay oremay activeay, anday Iay ongedlay otay iscoverday ethay
otivesmay anday eelingsfay ofay esethay ovelylay eaturescray; Iay asway inquisitiveay otay
owknay whyay Elixfay appeareday osay iserablemay anday Agathaay osay adsay. Iay oughtthay
oolish(fay etchwray!) atthay itay ightmay ebay inay myay owerpay otay estoreray appinesshay otay
esethay eservingday eoplepay. Enwhay Iay eptslay oray asway absentay, ethay ormsfay ofay ethay
enerablevay indblay atherfay, ethay entlegay Agathaay, anday ethay excellentay Elixfay
ittedflay eforebay emay. Iay ookedlay uponay emthay asay uperiorsay eingsbay owhay ouldway ebay
ethay arbitersay ofay myay uturefay estinyday. Iay ormedfay inay myay imaginationay aay
ousandthay icturespay ofay esentingpray elfmysay otay emthay, anday eirthay eceptionray ofay
emay. Iay imagineday atthay eythay ouldway ebay isgustedday, untilay, byay myay entlegay
emeanourday anday onciliatingcay ordsway, Iay ouldshay irstfay inway eirthay avourfay anday
afterwardsay eirthay ovelay.

ese“thay oughtsthay exhilarateday emay anday edlay emay otay applyay ithway eshfray ardouray otay
ethay acquiringay ethay artay ofay anguagelay. Myay organsay ereway indeeday arshhay, utbay
upplesay; anday althoughay myay oicevay asway eryvay unlikeay ethay oftsay usicmay ofay eirthay
onestay, etyay Iay onouncedpray uchsay ordsway asay Iay understooday ithway olerabletay easeay.
Itay asway asay ethay assay anday ethay ap-dogclay; etyay urelysay ethay entlegay assay osewhay
intentionsay ereway affectionateay, althoughay ishay annersmay ereway uderay, eservedday
etterbay eatmenttray anthay owsblay anday execrationay.

e“thay easantplay owersshay anday enialgay armthway ofay ingspray eatlygray altereday ethay
aspectay ofay ethay earthay. Enmay owhay eforebay isthay angechay eemedsay otay avehay eenbay
idhay inay avescay ispersedday emselvesthay anday ereway employeday inay ariousvay artsay ofay
ultivationcay. Ethay irdsbay angsay inay oremay eerfulchay otesnay, anday ethay eaveslay
eganbay otay udbay orthfay onay ethay eestray. Appyhay, appyhay earthay! Itfay abitationhay
orfay odsgay, ichwhay, osay ortshay aay imetay eforebay, asway eakblay, ampday, anday
unwholesomeay. Myay iritsspay ereway elevateday byay ethay enchantingay appearanceay ofay
aturenay; ethay astpay asway ottedblay omfray myay emorymay, ethay esentpray asway anquiltray,
anday ethay uturefay ildedgay byay ightbray aysray ofay opehay anday anticipationsay ofay oyjay.”




Apterchay 13ay


I“ay ownay astenhay otay ethay oremay ovingmay artpay ofay myay orystay. Iay allshay elateray
eventsay atthay impresseday emay ithway eelingsfay ichwhay, omfray atwhay Iay adhay eenbay,
avehay ademay emay atwhay Iay amay.

ing“spray advanceday apidlyray; ethay eatherway ecamebay inefay anday ethay iesskay
oudlessclay. Itay urprisedsay emay atthay atwhay eforebay asway esertday anday oomyglay
ouldshay ownay oomblay ithway ethay ostmay eautifulbay owersflay anday erdurevay. Myay
ensessay ereway atifiedgray anday efreshedray byay aay ousandthay entsscay ofay elightday anday
aay ousandthay ightssay ofay eautybay.

It“ay asway onay oneay ofay esethay aysday, enwhay myay ottagerscay eriodicallypay estedray
omfray abour—thelay olday anmay ayedplay onay ishay uitargay, anday ethay ildrenchay
istenedlay otay im—thathay Iay observeday ethay ountenancecay ofay Elixfay asway
elancholymay eyondbay expressionay; ehay ighedsay equentlyfray, anday onceay ishay atherfay
ausedpay inay ishay usicmay, anday Iay onjecturedcay byay ishay annermay atthay ehay inquireday
ethay ausecay ofay ishay on’ssay orrowsay. Elixfay epliedray inay aay eerfulchay accentay, anday
ethay olday anmay asway ecommencingray ishay usicmay enwhay omeonesay appedtay atay ethay oorday.

It“ay asway aay adylay onay orsebackhay, accompanieday byay aay ountry-manclay asay aay uidegay.
Ethay adylay asway esseddray inay aay arkday uitsay anday overedcay ithway aay ickthay ackblay
eilvay. Agathaay askeday aay uestionqay, otay ichwhay ethay angerstray onlyay epliedray byay
onouncingpray, inay aay eetsway accentay, ethay amenay ofay Elixfay. Erhay oicevay asway
usicalmay utbay unlikeay atthay ofay eitheray ofay myay iendsfray. Onay earinghay isthay ordway,
Elixfay amecay upay astilyhay otay ethay adylay, owhay, enwhay eshay awsay imhay, ewthray upay erhay
eilvay, anday Iay eheldbay aay ountenancecay ofay angelicay eautybay anday expressionay. Erhay
airhay ofay aay iningshay avenray ackblay, anday uriouslycay aidedbray; erhay eyesay ereway
arkday, utbay entlegay, althoughay animateday; erhay eaturesfay ofay aay egularray
oportionpray, anday erhay omplexioncay ondrouslyway airfay, eachay eekchay ingedtay ithway
aay ovelylay inkpay.

elix“fay eemedsay avishedray ithway elightday enwhay ehay awsay erhay, everyay aittray ofay
orrowsay anishedvay omfray ishay acefay, anday itay instantlyay expresseday aay egreeday ofay
ecstaticay oyjay, ofay ichwhay Iay ouldcay ardlyhay avehay elievedbay itay apablecay; ishay
eyesay arkledspay, asay ishay eekchay ushedflay ithway easureplay; anday atay atthay omentmay Iay
oughtthay imhay asay eautifulbay asay ethay angerstray. Eshay appeareday affecteday byay
ifferentday eelingsfay; ipingway aay ewfay earstay omfray erhay ovelylay eyesay, eshay eldhay
outay erhay andhay otay Elixfay, owhay issedkay itay apturouslyray anday alledcay erhay, asay
ellway asay Iay ouldcay istinguishday, ishay eetsway Arabianay. Eshay idday otnay appearay otay
understanday imhay, utbay iledsmay. Ehay assisteday erhay otay ismountday, anday
ismissingday erhay uidegay, onductedcay erhay intoay ethay ottagecay. Omesay
onversationcay ooktay aceplay etweenbay imhay anday ishay atherfay, anday ethay oungyay
angerstray eltknay atay ethay olday an’smay eetfay anday ouldway avehay issedkay ishay andhay,
utbay ehay aisedray erhay anday embraceday erhay affectionatelyay.

I“ay oonsay erceivedpay atthay althoughay ethay angerstray uttereday articulateay oundssay
anday appeareday otay avehay aay anguagelay ofay erhay ownay, eshay asway eithernay understooday
byay ornay erselfhay understooday ethay ottagerscay. Eythay ademay anymay ignssay ichwhay Iay
idday otnay omprehendcay, utbay Iay awsay atthay erhay esencepray iffusedday adnessglay
oughthray ethay ottagecay, ispellingday eirthay orrowsay asay ethay unsay issipatesday ethay
orningmay istsmay. Elixfay eemedsay eculiarlypay appyhay anday ithway ilessmay ofay
elightday elcomedway ishay Arabianay. Agathaay, ethay ever-gentleclay Agathaay, issedkay
ethay andshay ofay ethay ovelylay angerstray, anday ointingpay otay erhay otherbray, ademay
ignssay ichwhay appeareday otay emay otay eanmay atthay ehay adhay eenbay orrowfulsay untilay eshay
amecay. Omesay ourshay assedpay usthay, ilewhay eythay, byay eirthay ountenancescay,
expresseday oyjay, ethay ausecay ofay ichwhay Iay idday otnay omprehendcay. Esentlypray Iay
oundfay, byay ethay equentfray ecurrenceray ofay omesay oundsay ichwhay ethay angerstray
epeatedray afteray emthay, atthay eshay asway endeavouringay otay earnlay eirthay anguagelay;
anday ethay ideaay instantlyay occurreday otay emay atthay Iay ouldshay akemay useay ofay ethay
amesay instructionsay otay ethay amesay enday. Ethay angerstray earnedlay aboutay entytway
ordsway atay ethay irstfay essonlay; ostmay ofay emthay, indeeday, ereway osethay ichwhay Iay adhay
eforebay understooday, utbay Iay ofitedpray byay ethay othersay.

As“ay ightnay amecay onay, Agathaay anday ethay Arabianay etiredray earlyay. Enwhay eythay
eparatedsay Elixfay issedkay ethay andhay ofay ethay angerstray anday aidsay, ood‘gay ightnay
eetsway Afiesay.’ Ehay atsay upay uchmay ongerlay, onversingcay ithway ishay atherfay, anday
byay ethay equentfray epetitionray ofay erhay amenay Iay onjecturedcay atthay eirthay ovelylay
uestgay asway ethay ubjectsay ofay eirthay onversationcay. Iay ardentlyay esiredday otay
understanday emthay, anday entbay everyay acultyfay owardstay atthay urposepay, utbay oundfay
itay utterlyay impossibleay.

e“thay extnay orningmay Elixfay entway outay otay ishay orkway, anday afteray ethay usualay
occupationsay ofay Agathaay ereway inishedfay, ethay Arabianay atsay atay ethay eetfay ofay ethay
olday anmay, anday akingtay ishay uitargay, ayedplay omesay airsay osay entrancinglyay
eautifulbay atthay eythay atay onceay ewdray earstay ofay orrowsay anday elightday omfray myay
eyesay. Eshay angsay, anday erhay oicevay owedflay inay aay ichray adencecay, ellingsway oray
ingdyay awayay ikelay aay ightingalenay ofay ethay oodsway.

en“whay eshay adhay inishedfay, eshay avegay ethay uitargay otay Agathaay, owhay atay irstfay
eclinedday itay. Eshay ayedplay aay implesay airay, anday erhay oicevay accompanieday itay inay
eetsway accentsay, utbay unlikeay ethay ondrousway ainstray ofay ethay angerstray. Ethay olday
anmay appeareday enraptureday anday aidsay omesay ordsway ichwhay Agathaay endeavoureday otay
explainay otay Afiesay, anday byay ichwhay ehay appeareday otay ishway otay expressay atthay eshay
estowedbay onay imhay ethay eatestgray elightday byay erhay usicmay.

e“thay aysday ownay assedpay asay eaceablypay asay eforebay, ithway ethay olesay alterationay
atthay oyjay adhay akentay aceplay ofay adnesssay inay ethay ountenancescay ofay myay iendsfray.
Afiesay asway alwaysay aygay anday appyhay; eshay anday Iay improveday apidlyray inay ethay
owledgeknay ofay anguagelay, osay atthay inay otway onthsmay Iay eganbay otay omprehendcay ostmay
ofay ethay ordsway uttereday byay myay otectorspray.

In“ay ethay eanwhilemay alsoay ethay ackblay oundgray asway overedcay ithway erbagehay, anday
ethay eengray anksbay intersperseday ithway innumerableay owersflay, eetsway otay ethay
entscay anday ethay eyesay, arsstay ofay alepay adianceray amongay ethay oonlightmay oodsway;
ethay unsay ecamebay armerway, ethay ightsnay earclay anday almybay; anday myay octurnalnay
amblesray ereway anay extremeay easureplay otay emay, althoughay eythay ereway onsiderablycay
ortenedshay byay ethay atelay ettingsay anday earlyay isingray ofay ethay unsay, orfay Iay evernay
enturedvay abroaday uringday aylightday, earfulfay ofay eetingmay ithway ethay amesay
eatmenttray Iay adhay ormerlyfay endureday inay ethay irstfay illagevay ichwhay Iay entereday.

“myay aysday ereway entspay inay oseclay attentionay, atthay Iay ightmay oremay eedilyspay
astermay ethay anguagelay; anday Iay aymay oastbay atthay Iay improveday oremay apidlyray anthay
ethay Arabianay, owhay understooday eryvay ittlelay anday onversedcay inay okenbray
accentsay, ilstwhay Iay omprehendedcay anday ouldcay imitateay almostay everyay ordway atthay
asway okenspay.

ile“whay Iay improveday inay eechspay, Iay alsoay earnedlay ethay iencescay ofay etterslay asay
itay asway aughttay otay ethay angerstray, anday isthay openeday eforebay emay aay ideway ieldfay
orfay onderway anday elightday.

e“thay ookbay omfray ichwhay Elixfay instructeday Afiesay asway Olney’svay uins_ray
ofay Empiresay_. Iay ouldshay otnay avehay understooday ethay urportpay ofay isthay ookbay adhay otnay
Elixfay, inay eadingray itay, ivengay eryvay inutemay explanationsay. Ehay adhay osenchay isthay
orkway, ehay aidsay, ecausebay ethay eclamatoryday estylay asway amedfray inay imitationay ofay ethay
Easternay authorsay. Oughthray isthay orkway Iay obtaineday aay ursorycay owledgeknay ofay istoryhay
anday aay iewvay ofay ethay everalsay empiresay atay esentpray existingay inay ethay orldway; itay avegay
emay anay insightay intoay ethay annersmay, overnmentsgay, anday eligionsray ofay ethay ifferentday
ationsnay ofay ethay earthay. Iay eardhay ofay ethay othfulslay Asiaticsay, ofay ethay upendousstay
eniusgay anday entalmay activityay ofay ethay Eciansgray, ofay ethay arsway anday onderfulway irtuevay
ofay ethay earlyay Omans—ofray eirthay ubsequentsay egenerating—ofday ethay
eclineday ofay atthay ightymay empireay, ofay ivalrychay, Istianitychray, anday ingskay. Iay eardhay
ofay ethay iscoveryday ofay ethay Americanay emispherehay anday eptway ithway Afiesay overay ethay
aplesshay atefay ofay itsay originalay inhabitantsay.

ese“thay onderfulway arrationsnay inspireday emay ithway angestray eelingsfay. Asway
anmay, indeeday, atay onceay osay owerfulpay, osay irtuousvay anday agnificentmay, etyay osay
iciousvay anday asebay? Ehay appeareday atay oneay imetay aay eremay ionscay ofay ethay evilay
inciplepray anday atay anotheray asay allay atthay ancay ebay onceivedcay ofay oblenay anday
odlikegay. Otay ebay aay eatgray anday irtuousvay anmay appeareday ethay ighesthay onourhay
atthay ancay efallbay aay ensitivesay eingbay; otay ebay asebay anday iciousvay, asay anymay onay
ecordray avehay eenbay, appeareday ethay owestlay egradationday, aay onditioncay oremay
abjectay anthay atthay ofay ethay indblay olemay oray armlesshay ormway. Orfay aay onglay imetay Iay
ouldcay otnay onceivecay owhay oneay anmay ouldcay ogay orthfay otay urdermay ishay ellowfay, oray
evenay whyay erethay ereway awslay anday overnmentsgay; utbay enwhay Iay eardhay etailsday ofay
icevay anday oodshedblay, myay onderway easedcay anday Iay urnedtay awayay ithway isgustday anday
oathinglay.

Every“ay onversationcay ofay ethay ottagerscay ownay openeday ewnay ondersway otay emay.
Ilewhay Iay istenedlay otay ethay instructionsay ichwhay Elixfay estowedbay uponay ethay
Arabianay, ethay angestray emsystay ofay umanhay ocietysay asway explaineday otay emay. Iay
eardhay ofay ethay ivisionday ofay opertypray, ofay immenseay ealthway anday ualidsqay
overtypay, ofay ankray, escentday, anday oblenay oodblay.

e“thay ordsway induceday emay otay urntay owardstay elfmysay. Iay earnedlay atthay ethay
ossessionspay ostmay esteemeday byay ouryay ellowfay eaturescray ereway ighhay anday
unsullieday escentday uniteday ithway ichesray. Aay anmay ightmay ebay espectedray ithway
onlyay oneay ofay esethay advantagesay, utbay ithoutway eitheray ehay asway onsideredcay,
exceptay inay eryvay areray instancesay, asay aay agabondvay anday aay aveslay, oomedday otay
asteway ishay owerspay orfay ethay ofitspray ofay ethay osenchay ewfay! Anday atwhay asway Iay? Ofay
myay eationcray anday eatorcray Iay asway absolutelyay ignorantay, utbay Iay ewknay atthay Iay
ossessedpay onay oneymay, onay iendsfray, onay indkay ofay opertypray. Iay asway, esidesbay,
endueday ithway aay igurefay ideouslyhay eformedday anday oathsomelay; Iay asway otnay evenay
ofay ethay amesay aturenay asay anmay. Iay asway oremay agileay anthay eythay anday ouldcay
ubsistsay uponay oarsercay ietday; Iay orebay ethay extremesay ofay eathay anday oldcay ithway
esslay injuryay otay myay amefray; myay aturestay arfay exceededay eirsthay. Enwhay Iay ookedlay
arounday Iay awsay anday eardhay ofay onenay ikelay emay. Asway Iay, enthay, aay onstermay, aay otblay
uponay ethay earthay, omfray ichwhay allay enmay edflay anday omwhay allay enmay isownedday?

I“ay annotcay escribeday otay ouyay ethay agonyay atthay esethay eflectionsray inflicteday
uponay emay; Iay iedtray otay ispelday emthay, utbay orrowsay onlyay increaseday ithway
owledgeknay. Ohay, atthay Iay adhay orfay everay emainedray inay myay ativenay oodway, ornay
ownknay ornay eltfay eyondbay ethay ensationssay ofay ungerhay, irstthay, anday eathay!

Of“ay atwhay aay angestray aturenay isay owledgeknay! Itay ingsclay otay ethay indmay enwhay itay
ashay onceay eizedsay onay itay ikelay aay ichenlay onay ethay ockray. Iay ishedway ometimessay otay
akeshay offay allay oughtthay anday eelingfay, utbay Iay earnedlay atthay erethay asway utbay oneay
eansmay otay overcomeay ethay ensationsay ofay ainpay, anday atthay asway eath—aday atestay
ichwhay Iay earedfay etyay idday otnay understanday. Iay admireday irtuevay anday oodgay
eelingsfay anday ovedlay ethay entlegay annersmay anday amiableay ualitiesqay ofay myay
ottagerscay, utbay Iay asway utshay outay omfray intercourseay ithway emthay, exceptay
oughthray eansmay ichwhay Iay obtaineday byay ealthstay, enwhay Iay asway unseenay anday
unknownay, anday ichwhay atherray increaseday anthay atisfiedsay ethay esireday Iay adhay ofay
ecomingbay oneay amongay myay ellowsfay. Ethay entlegay ordsway ofay Agathaay anday ethay
animateday ilessmay ofay ethay armingchay Arabianay ereway otnay orfay emay. Ethay ildmay
exhortationsay ofay ethay olday anmay anday ethay ivelylay onversationcay ofay ethay ovedlay
Elixfay ereway otnay orfay emay. Iserablemay, unhappyay etchwray!

Other“ay essonslay ereway impresseday uponay emay evenay oremay eeplyday. Iay eardhay ofay ethay
ifferenceday ofay exessay, anday ethay irthbay anday owthgray ofay ildrenchay, owhay ethay
atherfay otedday onay ethay ilessmay ofay ethay infantay, anday ethay ivelylay alliessay ofay ethay
olderay ildchay, owhay allay ethay ifelay anday arescay ofay ethay othermay ereway appedwray upay
inay ethay eciouspray argechay, owhay ethay indmay ofay outhyay expandeday anday ainedgay
owledgeknay, ofay otherbray, istersay, anday allay ethay ariousvay elationshipsray ichwhay
indbay oneay umanhay eingbay otay anotheray inay utualmay ondsbay.

ut“bay erewhay ereway myay iendsfray anday elationsray? Onay atherfay adhay atchedway myay
infantay aysday, onay othermay adhay essedblay emay ithway ilessmay anday aressescay; oray ifay
eythay adhay, allay myay astpay ifelay asway ownay aay otblay, aay indblay acancyvay inay ichwhay Iay
istinguishedday othingnay. Omfray myay earliestay emembranceray Iay adhay eenbay asay Iay
enthay asway inay eighthay anday oportionpray. Iay adhay evernay etyay eensay aay eingbay
esemblingray emay oray owhay aimedclay anyay intercourseay ithway emay. Atwhay asway Iay? Ethay
uestionqay againay ecurredray, otay ebay answereday onlyay ithway oansgray.

I“ay illway oonsay explainay otay atwhay esethay eelingsfay endedtay, utbay alloway emay ownay otay
eturnray otay ethay ottagerscay, osewhay orystay exciteday inay emay uchsay ariousvay
eelingsfay ofay indignationay, elightday, anday onderway, utbay ichwhay allay erminatedtay
inay additionalay ovelay anday everenceray orfay myay otectorspray or(fay osay Iay ovedlay, inay
anay innocentay, alf-painfulclay elf-deceitclay, otay allcay emthay).”




Apterchay 14ay


ome“say imetay elapseday eforebay Iay earnedlay ethay istoryhay ofay myay iendsfray. Itay asway
oneay ichwhay ouldcay otnay ailfay otay impressay itselfay eeplyday onay myay indmay, unfoldingay
asay itay idday aay umbernay ofay ircumstancescay, eachay interestingay anday onderfulway otay
oneay osay utterlyay inexperienceday asay Iay asway.

e“thay amenay ofay ethay olday anmay asway Eday Aceylay. Ehay asway escendedday omfray aay oodgay
amilyfay inay Ancefray, erewhay ehay adhay ivedlay orfay anymay earsyay inay affluenceay,
espectedray byay ishay uperiorssay anday elovedbay byay ishay equalsay. Ishay onsay asway edbray
inay ethay ervicesay ofay ishay ountrycay, anday Agathaay adhay ankedray ithway adieslay ofay ethay
ighesthay istinctionday. Aay ewfay onthsmay eforebay myay arrivalay eythay adhay ivedlay inay
aay argelay anday uxuriouslay itycay alledcay Arispay, urroundedsay byay iendsfray anday
ossessedpay ofay everyay enjoymentay ichwhay irtuevay, efinementray ofay intellectay, oray
astetay, accompanieday byay aay oderatemay ortunefay, ouldcay afforday.

e“thay atherfay ofay Afiesay adhay eenbay ethay ausecay ofay eirthay uinray. Ehay asway aay
Urkishtay erchantmay anday adhay inhabiteday Arispay orfay anymay earsyay, enwhay, orfay omesay
easonray ichwhay Iay ouldcay otnay earnlay, ehay ecamebay obnoxiousay otay ethay overnmentgay.
Ehay asway eizedsay anday astcay intoay isonpray ethay eryvay ayday atthay Afiesay arriveday omfray
Onstantinoplecay otay oinjay imhay. Ehay asway iedtray anday ondemnedcay otay eathday. Ethay
injusticeay ofay ishay entencesay asway eryvay agrantflay; allay Arispay asway indignantay;
anday itay asway udgedjay atthay ishay eligionray anday ealthway atherray anthay ethay imecray
allegeday againstay imhay adhay eenbay ethay ausecay ofay ishay ondemnationcay.

elix“fay adhay accidentallyay eenbay esentpray atay ethay ialtray; ishay orrorhay anday
indignationay ereway uncontrollableay enwhay ehay eardhay ethay ecisionday ofay ethay
ourtcay. Ehay ademay, atay atthay omentmay, aay olemnsay owvay otay eliverday imhay anday enthay
ookedlay arounday orfay ethay eansmay. Afteray anymay uitlessfray attemptsay otay aingay
admittanceay otay ethay isonpray, ehay oundfay aay onglystray atedgray indowway inay anay
unguardeday artpay ofay ethay uildingbay, ichwhay ightedlay ethay ungeonday ofay ethay
unfortunateay Uhammadanmay, owhay, oadedlay ithway ainschay, aitedway inay espairday ethay
executionay ofay ethay arbarousbay entencesay. Elixfay isitedvay ethay ategray atay ightnay
anday ademay ownknay otay ethay isonerpray ishay intentionsay inay ishay avourfay. Ethay Urktay,
amazeday anday elightedday, endeavoureday otay indlekay ethay ealzay ofay ishay elivererday
byay omisespray ofay ewardray anday ealthway. Elixfay ejectedray ishay offersay ithway
ontemptcay, etyay enwhay ehay awsay ethay ovelylay Afiesay, owhay asway alloweday otay isitvay
erhay atherfay anday owhay byay erhay esturesgay expresseday erhay ivelylay atitudegray, ethay
outhyay ouldcay otnay elphay owningay otay ishay ownay indmay atthay ethay aptivecay ossessedpay
aay easuretray ichwhay ouldway ullyfay ewardray ishay oiltay anday azardhay.

e“thay Urktay uicklyqay erceivedpay ethay impressionay atthay ishay aughterday adhay ademay
onay ethay earthay ofay Elixfay anday endeavoureday otay ecuresay imhay oremay entirelyay inay
ishay interestsay byay ethay omisepray ofay erhay andhay inay arriagemay osay oonsay asay ehay
ouldshay ebay onveyedcay otay aay aceplay ofay afetysay. Elixfay asway ootay elicateday otay
acceptay isthay offeray, etyay ehay ookedlay orwardfay otay ethay obabilitypray ofay ethay
eventay asay otay ethay onsummationcay ofay ishay appinesshay.

uring“day ethay ensuingay aysday, ilewhay ethay eparationspray ereway oinggay orwardfay orfay
ethay escapeay ofay ethay erchantmay, ethay ealzay ofay Elixfay asway armedway byay everalsay
etterslay atthay ehay eceivedray omfray isthay ovelylay irlgay, owhay oundfay eansmay otay
expressay erhay oughtsthay inay ethay anguagelay ofay erhay overlay byay ethay aiday ofay anay olday
anmay, aay ervantsay ofay erhay atherfay owhay understooday Enchfray. Eshay ankedthay imhay inay
ethay ostmay ardentay ermstay orfay ishay intendeday ervicessay owardstay erhay arentpay, anday
atay ethay amesay imetay eshay entlygay eploredday erhay ownay atefay.

I“ay avehay opiescay ofay esethay etterslay, orfay Iay oundfay eansmay, uringday myay esidenceray
inay ethay ovelhay, otay ocurepray ethay implementsay ofay itingwray; anday ethay etterslay
ereway oftenay inay ethay andshay ofay Elixfay oray Agathaay. Eforebay Iay epartday Iay illway
ivegay emthay otay ouyay; eythay illway ovepray ethay uthtray ofay myay aletay; utbay atay esentpray,
asay ethay unsay isay alreadyay arfay eclinedday, Iay allshay onlyay avehay imetay otay epeatray
ethay ubstancesay ofay emthay otay ouyay.

afie“say elatedray atthay erhay othermay asway aay Istianchray Arabay, eizedsay anday ademay aay
aveslay byay ethay Urkstay; ecommendedray byay erhay eautybay, eshay adhay onway ethay earthay ofay
ethay atherfay ofay Afiesay, owhay arriedmay erhay. Ethay oungyay irlgay okespay inay ighhay anday
enthusiasticay ermstay ofay erhay othermay, owhay, ornbay inay eedomfray, urnedspay ethay
ondagebay otay ichwhay eshay asway ownay educedray. Eshay instructeday erhay aughterday inay
ethay enetstay ofay erhay eligionray anday aughttay erhay otay aspireay otay igherhay owerspay ofay
intellectay anday anay independenceay ofay iritspay orbiddenfay otay ethay emalefay
ollowersfay ofay Uhammadmay. Isthay adylay iedday, utbay erhay essonslay ereway indeliblyay
impresseday onay ethay indmay ofay Afiesay, owhay ickenedsay atay ethay ospectpray ofay againay
eturningray otay Asiaay anday eingbay immureday ithinway ethay allsway ofay aay aremhay,
alloweday onlyay otay occupyay erselfhay ithway infantileay amusementsay, ill-suitedclay otay
ethay empertay ofay erhay oulsay, ownay accustomeday otay andgray ideasay anday aay oblenay
emulationay orfay irtuevay. Ethay ospectpray ofay arryingmay aay Istianchray anday
emainingray inay aay ountrycay erewhay omenway ereway alloweday otay aketay aay ankray inay
ocietysay asway enchantingay otay erhay.

e“thay ayday orfay ethay executionay ofay ethay Urktay asway ixedfay, utbay onay ethay ightnay
eviouspray otay itay ehay uittedqay ishay isonpray anday eforebay orningmay asway istantday
anymay eagueslay omfray Arispay. Elixfay adhay ocuredpray assportspay inay ethay amenay ofay
ishay atherfay, istersay, anday imselfhay. Ehay adhay eviouslypray ommunicatedcay ishay
anplay otay ethay ormerfay, owhay aideday ethay eceitday byay uittingqay ishay ousehay, underay
ethay etencepray ofay aay ourneyjay anday oncealedcay imselfhay, ithway ishay aughterday, inay
anay obscureay artpay ofay Arispay.

elix“fay onductedcay ethay ugitivesfay oughthray Ancefray otay Onslyay anday acrossay Ontmay
Eniscay otay Eghornlay, erewhay ethay erchantmay adhay ecidedday otay aitway aay avourablefay
opportunityay ofay assingpay intoay omesay artpay ofay ethay Urkishtay ominionsday.

afie“say esolvedray otay emainray ithway erhay atherfay untilay ethay omentmay ofay ishay
epartureday, eforebay ichwhay imetay ethay Urktay enewedray ishay omisepray atthay eshay
ouldshay ebay uniteday otay ishay elivererday; anday Elixfay emainedray ithway emthay inay
expectationay ofay atthay eventay; anday inay ethay eantimemay ehay enjoyeday ethay ocietysay
ofay ethay Arabianay, owhay exhibiteday owardstay imhay ethay implestsay anday enderesttay
affectionay. Eythay onversedcay ithway oneay anotheray oughthray ethay eansmay ofay anay
interpreteray, anday ometimessay ithway ethay interpretationay ofay ookslay; anday Afiesay
angsay otay imhay ethay ivineday airsay ofay erhay ativenay ountrycay.

e“thay Urktay alloweday isthay intimacyay otay aketay aceplay anday encourageday ethay opeshay
ofay ethay outhfulyay overslay, ilewhay inay ishay earthay ehay adhay ormedfay arfay otheray
ansplay. Ehay oathedlay ethay ideaay atthay ishay aughterday ouldshay ebay uniteday otay aay
Istianchray, utbay ehay earedfay ethay esentmentray ofay Elixfay ifay ehay ouldshay appearay
ukewarmlay, orfay ehay ewknay atthay ehay asway illstay inay ethay owerpay ofay ishay elivererday
ifay ehay ouldshay oosechay otay etraybay imhay otay ethay Italianay atestay ichwhay eythay
inhabiteday. Ehay evolvedray aay ousandthay ansplay byay ichwhay ehay ouldshay ebay enableday
otay olongpray ethay eceitday untilay itay ightmay ebay onay ongerlay ecessarynay, anday
ecretlysay otay aketay ishay aughterday ithway imhay enwhay ehay epartedday. Ishay ansplay
ereway acilitatedfay byay ethay ewsnay ichwhay arriveday omfray Arispay.

e“thay overnmentgay ofay Ancefray ereway eatlygray enrageday atay ethay escapeay ofay eirthay
ictimvay anday aredspay onay ainspay otay etectday anday unishpay ishay elivererday. Ethay
otplay ofay Elixfay asway uicklyqay iscoveredday, anday Eday Aceylay anday Agathaay ereway
ownthray intoay isonpray. Ethay ewsnay eachedray Elixfay anday ousedray imhay omfray ishay
eamdray ofay easureplay. Ishay indblay anday ageday atherfay anday ishay entlegay istersay aylay
inay aay oisomenay ungeonday ilewhay ehay enjoyeday ethay eefray airay anday ethay ocietysay ofay
erhay omwhay ehay ovedlay. Isthay ideaay asway orturetay otay imhay. Ehay uicklyqay arrangeday
ithway ethay Urktay atthay ifay ethay atterlay ouldshay indfay aay avourablefay opportunityay
orfay escapeay eforebay Elixfay ouldcay eturnray otay Italyay, Afiesay ouldshay emainray asay aay
oarderbay atay aay onventcay atay Eghornlay; anday enthay, uittingqay ethay ovelylay Arabianay,
ehay astenedhay otay Arispay anday eliveredday imselfhay upay otay ethay engeancevay ofay ethay
awlay, opinghay otay eefray Eday Aceylay anday Agathaay byay isthay oceedingpray.

e“hay idday otnay ucceedsay. Eythay emainedray onfinedcay orfay ivefay onthsmay eforebay ethay
ialtray ooktay aceplay, ethay esultray ofay ichwhay eprivedday emthay ofay eirthay ortunefay
anday ondemnedcay emthay otay aay erpetualpay exileay omfray eirthay ativenay ountrycay.

ey“thay oundfay aay iserablemay asylumay inay ethay ottagecay inay Ermanygay, erewhay Iay
iscoveredday emthay. Elixfay oonsay earnedlay atthay ethay eacheroustray Urktay, orfay
omwhay ehay anday ishay amilyfay endureday uchsay unheard-ofclay oppressionay, onay
iscoveringday atthay ishay elivererday asway usthay educedray otay overtypay anday uinray,
ecamebay aay aitortray otay oodgay eelingfay anday onourhay anday adhay uittedqay Italyay ithway
ishay aughterday, insultinglyay endingsay Elixfay aay ittancepay ofay oneymay otay aiday imhay,
asay ehay aidsay, inay omesay anplay ofay uturefay aintenancemay.

uch“say ereway ethay eventsay atthay eyedpray onay ethay earthay ofay Elixfay anday enderedray
imhay, enwhay Iay irstfay awsay imhay, ethay ostmay iserablemay ofay ishay amilyfay. Ehay ouldcay
avehay endureday overtypay, anday ilewhay isthay istressday adhay eenbay ethay eedmay ofay ishay
irtuevay, ehay oriedglay inay itay; utbay ethay ingratitudeay ofay ethay Urktay anday ethay osslay
ofay ishay elovedbay Afiesay ereway isfortunesmay oremay itterbay anday irreparableay. Ethay
arrivalay ofay ethay Arabianay ownay infuseday ewnay ifelay intoay ishay oulsay.

en“whay ethay ewsnay eachedray Eghornlay atthay Elixfay asway eprivedday ofay ishay ealthway
anday ankray, ethay erchantmay ommandedcay ishay aughterday otay inkthay onay oremay ofay erhay
overlay, utbay otay eparepray otay eturnray otay erhay ativenay ountrycay. Ethay enerousgay
aturenay ofay Afiesay asway outrageday byay isthay ommandcay; eshay attempteday otay
expostulateay ithway erhay atherfay, utbay ehay eftlay erhay angrilyay, eiteratingray ishay
annicaltyray andatemay.

A“ay ewfay aysday afteray, ethay Urktay entereday ishay aughter’sday apartmentay anday oldtay
erhay astilyhay atthay ehay adhay easonray otay elievebay atthay ishay esidenceray atay Eghornlay
adhay eenbay ivulgedday anday atthay ehay ouldshay eedilyspay ebay eliveredday upay otay ethay
Enchfray overnmentgay; ehay adhay onsequentlycay iredhay aay esselvay otay onveycay imhay otay
Onstantinoplecay, orfay ichwhay itycay ehay ouldshay ailsay inay aay ewfay ourshay. Ehay
intendeday otay eavelay ishay aughterday underay ethay arecay ofay aay onfidentialcay
ervantsay, otay ollowfay atay erhay eisurelay ithway ethay eatergray artpay ofay ishay
opertypray, ichwhay adhay otnay etyay arriveday atay Eghornlay.

en“whay aloneay, Afiesay esolvedray inay erhay ownay indmay ethay anplay ofay onductcay atthay itay
ouldway ecomebay erhay otay ursuepay inay isthay emergencyay. Aay esidenceray inay Urkeytay
asway abhorrentay otay erhay; erhay eligionray anday erhay eelingsfay ereway alikeay averseay
otay itay. Byay omesay aperspay ofay erhay atherfay ichwhay ellfay intoay erhay andshay eshay
eardhay ofay ethay exileay ofay erhay overlay anday earntlay ethay amenay ofay ethay otspay erewhay
ehay enthay esidedray. Eshay esitatedhay omesay imetay, utbay atay engthlay eshay ormedfay erhay
eterminationday. Akingtay ithway erhay omesay ewelsjay atthay elongedbay otay erhay anday aay
umsay ofay oneymay, eshay uittedqay Italyay ithway anay attendantay, aay ativenay ofay Eghornlay,
utbay owhay understooday ethay ommoncay anguagelay ofay Urkeytay, anday epartedday orfay
Ermanygay.

e“shay arriveday inay afetysay atay aay owntay aboutay entytway eagueslay omfray ethay ottagecay
ofay Eday Aceylay, enwhay erhay attendantay ellfay angerouslyday illay. Afiesay ursednay erhay
ithway ethay ostmay evotedday affectionay, utbay ethay oorpay irlgay iedday, anday ethay
Arabianay asway eftlay aloneay, unacquainteday ithway ethay anguagelay ofay ethay ountrycay
anday utterlyay ignorantay ofay ethay ustomscay ofay ethay orldway. Eshay ellfay, oweverhay,
intoay oodgay andshay. Ethay Italianay adhay entionedmay ethay amenay ofay ethay otspay orfay
ichwhay eythay ereway oundbay, anday afteray erhay eathday ethay omanway ofay ethay ousehay inay
ichwhay eythay adhay ivedlay ooktay arecay atthay Afiesay ouldshay arriveay inay afetysay atay
ethay ottagecay ofay erhay overlay.”




Apterchay 15ay


uch“say asway ethay istoryhay ofay myay elovedbay ottagerscay. Itay impresseday emay eeplyday.
Iay earnedlay, omfray ethay iewsvay ofay ocialsay ifelay ichwhay itay evelopedday, otay admireay
eirthay irtuesvay anday otay eprecateday ethay icesvay ofay ankindmay.

As“ay etyay Iay ookedlay uponay imecray asay aay istantday evilay, enevolencebay anday
enerositygay ereway everay esentpray eforebay emay, incitingay ithinway emay aay esireday otay
ecomebay anay actoray inay ethay usybay enescay erewhay osay anymay admirableay ualitiesqay
ereway alledcay orthfay anday isplayedday. Utbay inay ivinggay anay accountay ofay ethay
ogresspray ofay myay intellectay, Iay ustmay otnay omitay aay ircumstancecay ichwhay occurreday
inay ethay eginningbay ofay ethay onthmay ofay Augustay ofay ethay amesay earyay.

One“ay ightnay uringday myay accustomeday isitvay otay ethay eighbouringnay oodway erewhay Iay
ollectedcay myay ownay oodfay anday oughtbray omehay iringfay orfay myay otectorspray, Iay oundfay onay
ethay oundgray aay eathernlay ortmanteaupay ontainingcay everalsay articlesay ofay essdray anday
omesay ooksbay. Iay eagerlyay eizedsay ethay izepray anday eturnedray ithway itay otay myay ovelhay.
Ortunatelyfay ethay ooksbay ereway ittenwray inay ethay anguagelay, ethay elementsay ofay ichwhay Iay
adhay acquireday atay ethay ottagecay; eythay onsistedcay ofay aradise_pay Ostlay_, aay olumevay
ofay utarch’s_play Iveslay_, anday ethay orrows_say ofay Erterway_. Ethay
ossessionpay ofay esethay easurestray avegay emay extremeay elightday; Iay ownay ontinuallycay
udiedstay anday exerciseday myay indmay uponay esethay istorieshay, ilstwhay myay iendsfray ereway
employeday inay eirthay ordinaryay occupationsay.

I“ay ancay ardlyhay escribeday otay ouyay ethay effectay ofay esethay ooksbay. Eythay oducedpray
inay emay anay infinityay ofay ewnay imagesay anday eelingsfay, atthay ometimessay aisedray emay
otay ecstasyay, utbay oremay equentlyfray unksay emay intoay ethay owestlay ejectionday. Inay
ethay orrows_say ofay Erterway_, esidesbay ethay interestay ofay itsay implesay anday affectingay
orystay, osay anymay opinionsay areay anvassedcay anday osay anymay ightslay ownthray uponay
atwhay adhay ithertohay eenbay otay emay obscureay ubjectssay atthay Iay oundfay inay itay aay
ever-endingclay ourcesay ofay eculationspay anday astonishmentay. Ethay entlegay anday
omesticday annersmay itay escribedday, ombinedcay ithway oftylay entimentssay anday
eelingsfay, ichwhay adhay orfay eirthay objectay omethingsay outay ofay elfsay, accordeday
ellway ithway myay experienceay amongay myay otectorspray anday ithway ethay antsway ichwhay
ereway orfay everay aliveay inay myay ownay osombay. Utbay Iay oughtthay Erterway imselfhay aay
oremay ivineday eingbay anthay Iay adhay everay eheldbay oray imagineday; ishay aracterchay
ontainedcay onay etensionpray, utbay itay anksay eepday. Ethay isquisitionsday uponay
eathday anday uicidesay ereway alculatedcay otay illfay emay ithway onderway. Iay idday otnay
etendpray otay enteray intoay ethay eritsmay ofay ethay asecay, etyay Iay inclineday owardstay
ethay opinionsay ofay ethay erohay, osewhay extinctionay Iay eptway, ithoutway eciselypray
understandingay itay.

As“ay Iay eadray, oweverhay, Iay applieday uchmay ersonallypay otay myay ownay eelingsfay anday
onditioncay. Iay oundfay elfmysay imilarsay etyay atay ethay amesay imetay angelystray
unlikeay otay ethay eingsbay oncerningcay omwhay Iay eadray anday otay osewhay onversationcay Iay
asway aay istenerlay. Iay athisedsympay ithway anday artlypay understooday emthay, utbay Iay
asway unformeday inay indmay; Iay asway ependentday onay onenay anday elatedray otay onenay.
e‘thay athpay ofay myay epartureday asway eefray,’ anday erethay asway onenay otay amentlay myay
annihilationay. Myay ersonpay asway ideoushay anday myay aturestay iganticgay. Atwhay idday
isthay eanmay? Owhay asway Iay? Atwhay asway Iay? Encewhay idday Iay omecay? Atwhay asway myay
estinationday? Esethay uestionsqay ontinuallycay ecurredray, utbay Iay asway unableay otay
olvesay emthay.

e“thay olumevay ofay utarch’s_play Iveslay_ ichwhay Iay ossessedpay ontainedcay ethay
istorieshay ofay ethay irstfay oundersfay ofay ethay ancientay epublicsray. Isthay ookbay
adhay aay arfay ifferentday effectay uponay emay omfray ethay orrows_say ofay Erterway_. Iay
earnedlay omfray Erter’sway imaginationsay espondencyday anday oomglay, utbay Utarchplay
aughttay emay ighhay oughtsthay; ehay elevateday emay aboveay ethay etchedwray eresphay ofay myay
ownay eflectionsray, otay admireay anday ovelay ethay eroeshay ofay astpay agesay. Anymay
ingsthay Iay eadray urpassedsay myay understandingay anday experienceay. Iay adhay aay eryvay
onfusedcay owledgeknay ofay ingdomskay, ideway extentsay ofay ountrycay, ightymay iversray,
anday oundlessbay eassay. Utbay Iay asway erfectlypay unacquainteday ithway ownstay anday
argelay assemblagesay ofay enmay. Ethay ottagecay ofay myay otectorspray adhay eenbay ethay
onlyay oolschay inay ichwhay Iay adhay udiedstay umanhay aturenay, utbay isthay ookbay
evelopedday ewnay anday ightiermay enesscay ofay actionay. Iay eadray ofay enmay oncernedcay
inay ublicpay affairsay, overninggay oray assacringmay eirthay eciesspay. Iay eltfay ethay
eatestgray ardouray orfay irtuevay iseray ithinway emay, anday abhorrenceay orfay icevay, asay
arfay asay Iay understooday ethay ignificationsay ofay osethay ermstay, elativeray asay eythay
ereway, asay Iay applieday emthay, otay easureplay anday ainpay aloneay. Induceday byay esethay
eelingsfay, Iay asway ofay oursecay edlay otay admireay eaceablepay awgiverslay, Umanay,
Olonsay, anday Urguslycay, inay eferencepray otay Omulusray anday Eseusthay. Ethay
atriarchalpay iveslay ofay myay otectorspray ausedcay esethay impressionsay otay aketay aay
irmfay oldhay onay myay indmay; erhapspay, ifay myay irstfay introductionay otay umanityhay adhay
eenbay ademay byay aay oungyay oldiersay, urningbay orfay oryglay anday aughterslay, Iay ouldshay
avehay eenbay imbueday ithway ifferentday ensationssay.

ut“bay aradise_pay Ostlay_ exciteday ifferentday anday arfay eeperday emotionsay. Iay eadray
itay, asay Iay adhay eadray ethay otheray olumesvay ichwhay adhay allenfay intoay myay andshay, asay
aay uetray istoryhay. Itay ovedmay everyay eelingfay ofay onderway anday aweay atthay ethay
icturepay ofay anay omnipotentay Odgay arringway ithway ishay eaturescray asway apablecay ofay
excitingay. Iay oftenay eferredray ethay everalsay ituationssay, asay eirthay imilaritysay
uckstray emay, otay myay ownay. Ikelay Adamay, Iay asway apparentlyay uniteday byay onay inklay otay
anyay otheray eingbay inay existenceay; utbay ishay atestay asway arfay ifferentday omfray inemay
inay everyay otheray espectray. Ehay adhay omecay orthfay omfray ethay andshay ofay Odgay aay
erfectpay eaturecray, appyhay anday osperouspray, uardedgay byay ethay especialay arecay ofay
ishay Eatorcray; ehay asway alloweday otay onversecay ithway anday acquireay owledgeknay omfray
eingsbay ofay aay uperiorsay aturenay, utbay Iay asway etchedwray, elplesshay, anday aloneay.
Anymay imestay Iay onsideredcay Atansay asay ethay itterfay emblemay ofay myay onditioncay, orfay
oftenay, ikelay imhay, enwhay Iay iewedvay ethay issblay ofay myay otectorspray, ethay itterbay
allgay ofay envyay oseray ithinway emay.

Another“ay ircumstancecay engthenedstray anday onfirmedcay esethay eelingsfay. Oonsay
afteray myay arrivalay inay ethay ovelhay Iay iscoveredday omesay aperspay inay ethay ocketpay ofay
ethay essdray ichwhay Iay adhay akentay omfray ouryay aboratorylay. Atay irstfay Iay adhay
eglectednay emthay, utbay ownay atthay Iay asway ableay otay ecipherday ethay aracterschay inay
ichwhay eythay ereway ittenwray, Iay eganbay otay udystay emthay ithway iligenceday. Itay asway
ouryay ournaljay ofay ethay ourfay onthsmay atthay ecededpray myay eationcray. Ouyay
inutelymay escribedday inay esethay aperspay everyay epstay ouyay ooktay inay ethay ogresspray
ofay ouryay orkway; isthay istoryhay asway ingledmay ithway accountsay ofay omesticday
occurrencesay. Ouyay oubtlessday ecollectray esethay aperspay. Erehay eythay areay.
Everythingay isay elatedray inay emthay ichwhay earsbay eferenceray otay myay accurseday
originay; ethay olewhay etailday ofay atthay eriessay ofay isgustingday ircumstancescay
ichwhay oducedpray itay isay etsay inay iewvay; ethay inutestmay escriptionday ofay myay odiousay
anday oathsomelay ersonpay isay ivengay, inay anguagelay ichwhay aintedpay ouryay ownay
orrorshay anday enderedray inemay indelibleay. Iay ickenedsay asay Iay eadray. ateful‘hay
ayday enwhay Iay eceivedray ifelay!’ Iay exclaimeday inay agonyay. Accursed‘ay eatorcray!
Whyay idday ouyay ormfay aay onstermay osay ideoushay atthay evenay ou_yay_ urnedtay omfray emay inay
isgustday? Odgay, inay itypay, ademay anmay eautifulbay anday alluringay, afteray ishay ownay
imageay; utbay myay ormfay isay aay ilthyfay etypay ofay oursyay, oremay orridhay evenay omfray ethay
eryvay esemblanceray. Atansay adhay ishay ompanionscay, ellowfay evilsday, otay admireay
anday encourageay imhay, utbay Iay amay olitarysay anday abhorreday.’

ese“thay ereway ethay eflectionsray ofay myay ourshay ofay espondencyday anday olitudesay;
utbay enwhay Iay ontemplatedcay ethay irtuesvay ofay ethay ottagerscay, eirthay amiableay anday
enevolentbay ispositionsday, Iay ersuadedpay elfmysay atthay enwhay eythay ouldshay
ecomebay acquainteday ithway myay admirationay ofay eirthay irtuesvay eythay ouldway
ompassionatecay emay anday overlookay myay ersonalpay eformityday. Ouldcay eythay urntay
omfray eirthay oorday oneay, oweverhay onstrousmay, owhay olicitedsay eirthay ompassioncay
anday iendshipfray? Iay esolvedray, atay eastlay, otnay otay espairday, utbay inay everyay ayway
otay itfay elfmysay orfay anay intervieway ithway emthay ichwhay ouldway ecideday myay atefay. Iay
ostponedpay isthay attemptay orfay omesay onthsmay ongerlay, orfay ethay importanceay
attacheday otay itsay uccesssay inspireday emay ithway aay eaddray estlay Iay ouldshay ailfay.
Esidesbay, Iay oundfay atthay myay understandingay improveday osay uchmay ithway everyay
ay’sday experienceay atthay Iay asway unwillingay otay ommencecay isthay undertakingay
untilay aay ewfay oremay onthsmay ouldshay avehay addeday otay myay agacitysay.

everal“say angeschay, inay ethay eantimemay, ooktay aceplay inay ethay ottagecay. Ethay
esencepray ofay Afiesay iffusedday appinesshay amongay itsay inhabitantsay, anday Iay alsoay
oundfay atthay aay eatergray egreeday ofay entyplay eignedray erethay. Elixfay anday Agathaay
entspay oremay imetay inay amusementay anday onversationcay, anday ereway assisteday inay
eirthay abourslay byay ervantssay. Eythay idday otnay appearay ichray, utbay eythay ereway
ontentedcay anday appyhay; eirthay eelingsfay ereway erenesay anday eacefulpay, ilewhay
inemay ecamebay everyay ayday oremay umultuoustay. Increaseay ofay owledgeknay onlyay
iscoveredday otay emay oremay earlyclay atwhay aay etchedwray outcastay Iay asway. Iay
erishedchay opehay, itay isay uetray, utbay itay anishedvay enwhay Iay eheldbay myay ersonpay
eflectedray inay aterway oray myay adowshay inay ethay oonshinemay, evenay asay atthay ailfray
imageay anday atthay inconstantay adeshay.

I“ay endeavoureday otay ushcray esethay earsfay anday otay ortifyfay elfmysay orfay ethay ialtray
ichwhay inay aay ewfay onthsmay Iay esolvedray otay undergoay; anday ometimessay Iay alloweday myay
oughtsthay, uncheckeday byay easonray, otay ambleray inay ethay ieldsfay ofay Aradisepay, anday
aredday otay ancyfay amiableay anday ovelylay eaturescray athisingsympay ithway myay
eelingsfay anday eeringchay myay oomglay; eirthay angelicay ountenancescay eathedbray
ilessmay ofay onsolationcay. Utbay itay asway allay aay eamdray; onay Eveay oothedsay myay
orrowssay ornay aredshay myay oughtsthay; Iay asway aloneay. Iay ememberedray Adam’say
upplicationsay otay ishay Eatorcray. Utbay erewhay asway inemay? Ehay adhay abandoneday emay,
anday inay ethay itternessbay ofay myay earthay Iay ursedcay imhay.

Autumn“ay assedpay usthay. Iay awsay, ithway urprisesay anday iefgray, ethay eaveslay ecayday
anday allfay, anday aturenay againay assumeay ethay arrenbay anday eakblay appearanceay itay
adhay ornway enwhay Iay irstfay eheldbay ethay oodsway anday ethay ovelylay oonmay. Etyay Iay idday
otnay eedhay ethay eaknessblay ofay ethay eatherway; Iay asway etterbay ittedfay byay myay
onformationcay orfay ethay enduranceay ofay oldcay anthay eathay. Utbay myay iefchay
elightsday ereway ethay ightsay ofay ethay owersflay, ethay irdsbay, anday allay ethay aygay
apparelay ofay ummersay; enwhay osethay esertedday emay, Iay urnedtay ithway oremay attentionay
owardstay ethay ottagerscay. Eirthay appinesshay asway otnay ecreasedday byay ethay
absenceay ofay ummersay. Eythay ovedlay anday athisedsympay ithway oneay anotheray; anday
eirthay oysjay, ependingday onay eachay otheray, ereway otnay interrupteday byay ethay
asualtiescay atthay ooktay aceplay arounday emthay. Ethay oremay Iay awsay ofay emthay, ethay
eatergray ecamebay myay esireday otay aimclay eirthay otectionpray anday indnesskay; myay
earthay earnedyay otay ebay ownknay anday ovedlay byay esethay amiableay eaturescray; otay eesay
eirthay eetsway ookslay irectedday owardstay emay ithway affectionay asway ethay utmostay
imitlay ofay myay ambitionay. Iay aredday otnay inkthay atthay eythay ouldway urntay emthay omfray
emay ithway isdainday anday orrorhay. Ethay oorpay atthay oppedstay atay eirthay oorday ereway
evernay ivendray awayay. Iay askeday, itay isay uetray, orfay eatergray easurestray anthay aay
ittlelay oodfay oray estray: Iay equiredray indnesskay anday athysympay; utbay Iay idday otnay
elievebay elfmysay utterlyay unworthyay ofay itay.

e“thay interway advanceday, anday anay entireay evolutionray ofay ethay easonssay adhay akentay
aceplay incesay Iay awokeay intoay ifelay. Myay attentionay atay isthay imetay asway olelysay
irectedday owardstay myay anplay ofay introducingay elfmysay intoay ethay ottagecay ofay myay
otectorspray. Iay evolvedray anymay ojectspray, utbay atthay onay ichwhay Iay inallyfay
ixedfay asway otay enteray ethay ellingdway enwhay ethay indblay olday anmay ouldshay ebay aloneay.
Iay adhay agacitysay enoughay otay iscoverday atthay ethay unnaturalay ideousnesshay ofay myay
ersonpay asway ethay iefchay objectay ofay orrorhay ithway osethay owhay adhay ormerlyfay
eheldbay emay. Myay oicevay, althoughay arshhay, adhay othingnay erribletay inay itay; Iay
oughtthay, ereforethay, atthay ifay inay ethay absenceay ofay ishay ildrenchay Iay ouldcay aingay
ethay oodgay illway anday ediationmay ofay ethay olday Eday Aceylay, Iay ightmay byay ishay eansmay
ebay oleratedtay byay myay oungeryay otectorspray.

One“ay ayday, enwhay ethay unsay oneshay onay ethay edray eaveslay atthay ewedstray ethay oundgray
anday iffusedday eerfulnesschay, althoughay itay eniedday armthway, Afiesay, Agathaay,
anday Elixfay epartedday onay aay onglay ountrycay alkway, anday ethay olday anmay, atay ishay ownay
esireday, asway eftlay aloneay inay ethay ottagecay. Enwhay ishay ildrenchay adhay epartedday,
