ehay ooktay upay ishay uitargay anday ayedplay everalsay ournfulmay utbay eetsway airsay, oremay
eetsway anday ournfulmay anthay Iay adhay everay eardhay imhay ayplay eforebay. Atay irstfay ishay
ountenancecay asway illuminateday ithway easureplay, utbay asay ehay ontinuedcay,
oughtfulnessthay anday adnesssay ucceededsay; atay engthlay, ayinglay asideay ethay
instrumentay, ehay atsay absorbeday inay eflectionray.

“myay earthay eatbay uickqay; isthay asway ethay ourhay anday omentmay ofay ialtray, ichwhay
ouldway ecideday myay opeshay oray ealiseray myay earsfay. Ethay ervantssay ereway onegay otay aay
eighbouringnay airfay. Allay asway ilentsay inay anday arounday ethay ottagecay; itay asway anay
excellentay opportunityay; etyay, enwhay Iay oceededpray otay executeay myay anplay, myay
imbslay ailedfay emay anday Iay anksay otay ethay oundgray. Againay Iay oseray, anday exertingay
allay ethay irmnessfay ofay ichwhay Iay asway astermay, emovedray ethay anksplay ichwhay Iay adhay
acedplay eforebay myay ovelhay otay oncealcay myay etreatray. Ethay eshfray airay evivedray
emay, anday ithway enewedray eterminationday Iay approacheday ethay oorday ofay eirthay
ottagecay.

I“ay ockedknay. o‘whay isay erethay?’ aidsay ethay olday anmay. ome‘cay inay.’

I“ay entereday. ardon‘pay isthay intrusionay,’ aidsay Iay; I‘ay amay
aay avellertray inay antway ofay aay ittlelay estray; ouyay ouldway eatlygray obligeay emay ifay ouyay
ouldway alloway emay otay emainray aay ewfay inutesmay eforebay ethay irefay.’

Enter“‘ay,’ aidsay Eday Aceylay, and‘ay Iay illway tryay inay atwhay
annermay Iay ancay otay elieveray ouryay antsway; utbay, unfortunatelyay, myay ildrenchay areay
omfray omehay, anday asay Iay amay indblay, Iay amay afraiday Iay allshay indfay itay ifficultday otay
ocurepray oodfay orfay ouyay.’

o“‘day otnay oubletray ourselfyay, myay indkay osthay; Iay avehay oodfay; itay isay
armthway anday estray onlyay atthay Iay eednay.’

I“ay atsay ownday, anday aay ilencesay ensueday. Iay ewknay atthay everyay inutemay asway
eciouspray otay emay, etyay Iay emainedray irresoluteay inay atwhay annermay otay ommencecay
ethay intervieway, enwhay ethay olday anmay addresseday emay.

‘byay ouryay anguagelay, angerstray, Iay upposesay ouyay areay myay ountrymancay; areay ouyay
Enchfray?’

o“‘nay; utbay Iay asway educateday byay aay Enchfray amilyfay anday understanday atthay
anguagelay onlyay. Iay amay ownay oinggay otay aimclay ethay otectionpray ofay omesay iendsfray,
omwhay Iay incerelysay ovelay, anday ofay osewhay avourfay Iay avehay omesay opeshay.’

Are“‘ay eythay Ermansgay?’

o“‘nay, eythay areay Enchfray. Utbay etlay usay angechay ethay ubjectsay. Iay amay anay
unfortunateay anday esertedday eaturecray, Iay ooklay arounday anday Iay avehay onay elationray
oray iendfray uponay earthay. Esethay amiableay eoplepay otay omwhay Iay ogay avehay evernay
eensay emay anday owknay ittlelay ofay emay. Iay amay ullfay ofay earsfay, orfay ifay Iay ailfay
erethay, Iay amay anay outcastay inay ethay orldway orfay everay.’

o“‘day otnay espairday. Otay ebay iendlessfray isay indeeday otay ebay unfortunateay, utbay
ethay eartshay ofay enmay, enwhay unprejudiceday byay anyay obviousay elf-interestclay, areay
ullfay ofay otherlybray ovelay anday aritychay. Elyray, ereforethay, onay ouryay opeshay;
anday ifay esethay iendsfray areay oodgay anday amiableay, oday otnay espairday.’

ey“‘thay areay ind—theykay areay ethay ostmay excellentay eaturescray inay ethay orldway;
utbay, unfortunatelyay, eythay areay ejudicedpray againstay emay. Iay avehay oodgay
ispositionsday; myay ifelay ashay eenbay ithertohay armlesshay anday inay omesay egreeday
eneficialbay; utbay aay atalfay ejudicepray oudsclay eirthay eyesay, anday erewhay eythay
oughtay otay eesay aay eelingfay anday indkay iendfray, eythay eholdbay onlyay aay etestableday
onstermay.’

at“‘thay isay indeeday unfortunateay; utbay ifay ouyay areay eallyray amelessblay, annotcay
ouyay undeceiveay emthay?’

I“‘ay amay aboutay otay undertakeay atthay asktay; anday itay isay onay atthay accountay atthay Iay
eelfay osay anymay overwhelmingay errorstay. Iay enderlytay ovelay esethay iendsfray; Iay
avehay, unknownay otay emthay, eenbay orfay anymay onthsmay inay ethay abitshay ofay ailyday
indnesskay owardstay emthay; utbay eythay elievebay atthay Iay ishway otay injureay emthay, anday
itay isay atthay ejudicepray ichwhay Iay ishway otay overcomeay.’

ere“‘whay oday esethay iendsfray esideray?’

ear“‘nay isthay otspay.’

e“thay olday anmay ausedpay anday enthay ontinuedcay, If‘ay ouyay illway unreservedlyay
onfidecay otay emay ethay articularspay ofay ouryay aletay, Iay erhapspay aymay ebay ofay useay inay
undeceivingay emthay. Iay amay indblay anday annotcay udgejay ofay ouryay ountenancecay, utbay
erethay isay omethingsay inay ouryay ordsway ichwhay ersuadespay emay atthay ouyay areay
inceresay. Iay amay oorpay anday anay exileay, utbay itay illway afforday emay uetray easureplay
otay ebay inay anyay ayway erviceablesay otay aay umanhay eaturecray.’

Excellent“‘ay anmay! Iay ankthay ouyay anday acceptay ouryay enerousgay offeray. Ouyay
aiseray emay omfray ethay ustday byay isthay indnesskay; anday Iay usttray atthay, byay ouryay aiday,
Iay allshay otnay ebay ivendray omfray ethay ocietysay anday athysympay ofay ouryay ellowfay
eaturescray.’

eaven“‘hay orbidfay! Evenay ifay ouyay ereway eallyray iminalcray, orfay atthay ancay onlyay
ivedray ouyay otay esperationday, anday otnay instigateay ouyay otay irtuevay. Iay alsoay amay
unfortunateay; Iay anday myay amilyfay avehay eenbay ondemnedcay, althoughay innocentay;
udgejay, ereforethay, ifay Iay oday otnay eelfay orfay ouryay isfortunesmay.’

ow“‘hay ancay Iay ankthay ouyay, myay estbay anday onlyay enefactorbay? Omfray ouryay ipslay
irstfay avehay Iay eardhay ethay oicevay ofay indnesskay irectedday owardstay emay; Iay allshay
ebay orfay everay atefulgray; anday ouryay esentpray umanityhay assuresay emay ofay uccesssay
ithway osethay iendsfray omwhay Iay amay onay ethay ointpay ofay eetingmay.’

ay“‘may Iay owknay ethay amesnay anday esidenceray ofay osethay iendsfray?’

I“ay ausedpay. Isthay, Iay oughtthay, asway ethay omentmay ofay ecisionday, ichwhay asway otay
obray emay ofay oray estowbay appinesshay onay emay orfay everay. Iay uggledstray ainlyvay orfay
irmnessfay ufficientsay otay answeray imhay, utbay ethay effortay estroyedday allay myay
emainingray engthstray; Iay anksay onay ethay airchay anday obbedsay alouday. Atay atthay
omentmay Iay eardhay ethay epsstay ofay myay oungeryay otectorspray. Iay adhay otnay aay omentmay
otay oselay, utbay eizingsay ethay andhay ofay ethay olday anmay, Iay iedcray, ow‘nay isay ethay
imetay! Avesay anday otectpray emay! Ouyay anday ouryay amilyfay areay ethay iendsfray omwhay Iay
eeksay. Oday otnay ouyay esertday emay inay ethay ourhay ofay ialtray!’

eat“‘gray Odgay!’ exclaimeday ethay olday anmay. o‘whay areay ouyay?’

At“ay atthay instantay ethay ottagecay oorday asway openeday, anday Elixfay, Afiesay, anday
Agathaay entereday. Owhay ancay escribeday eirthay orrorhay anday onsternationcay onay
eholdingbay emay? Agathaay aintedfay, anday Afiesay, unableay otay attenday otay erhay
iendfray, ushedray outay ofay ethay ottagecay. Elixfay artedday orwardfay, anday ithway
upernaturalsay orcefay oretay emay omfray ishay atherfay, otay osewhay eesknay Iay ungclay, inay
aay ansporttray ofay uryfay, ehay ashedday emay otay ethay oundgray anday uckstray emay iolentlyvay
ithway aay ickstay. Iay ouldcay avehay orntay imhay imblay omfray imblay, asay ethay ionlay endsray
ethay antelopeay. Utbay myay earthay anksay ithinway emay asay ithway itterbay icknesssay, anday
Iay efrainedray. Iay awsay imhay onay ethay ointpay ofay epeatingray ishay owblay, enwhay,
overcomeay byay ainpay anday anguishay, Iay uittedqay ethay ottagecay, anday inay ethay eneralgay
umulttay escapeday unperceiveday otay myay ovelhay.”




Apterchay 16ay


ursed“cay, ursedcay eatorcray! Whyay idday Iay ivelay? Whyay, inay atthay instantay, idday Iay
otnay extinguishay ethay arkspay ofay existenceay ichwhay ouyay adhay osay antonlyway
estowedbay? Iay owknay otnay; espairday adhay otnay etyay akentay ossessionpay ofay emay; myay
eelingsfay ereway osethay ofay ageray anday evengeray. Iay ouldcay ithway easureplay avehay
estroyedday ethay ottagecay anday itsay inhabitantsay anday avehay uttedglay elfmysay ithway
eirthay ieksshray anday iserymay.

en“whay ightnay amecay Iay uittedqay myay etreatray anday anderedway inay ethay oodway; anday
ownay, onay ongerlay estrainedray byay ethay earfay ofay iscoveryday, Iay avegay entvay otay myay
anguishay inay earfulfay owlingshay. Iay asway ikelay aay ildway eastbay atthay adhay okenbray
ethay oilstay, estroyingday ethay objectsay atthay obstructeday emay anday angingray
oughthray ethay oodway ithway aay ag-likeclay iftnesssway. Ohay! Atwhay aay iserablemay
ightnay Iay assedpay! Ethay oldcay arsstay oneshay inay ockerymay, anday ethay arebay eestray
avedway eirthay anchesbray aboveay emay; ownay anday enthay ethay eetsway oicevay ofay aay irdbay
urstbay orthfay amidstay ethay universalay illnessstay. Allay, avesay Iay, ereway atay estray
oray inay enjoymentay; Iay, ikelay ethay arch-fiendclay, orebay aay ellhay ithinway emay, anday
indingfay elfmysay unsympathiseday ithway, ishedway otay eartay upay ethay eestray, eadspray
avochay anday estructionday arounday emay, anday enthay otay avehay atsay ownday anday enjoyeday
ethay uinray.

ut“bay isthay asway aay uxurylay ofay ensationsay atthay ouldcay otnay endureay; Iay ecamebay
atiguedfay ithway excessay ofay odilybay exertionay anday anksay onay ethay ampday assgray inay
ethay icksay impotenceay ofay espairday. Erethay asway onenay amongay ethay iadsmyray ofay enmay
atthay existeday owhay ouldway itypay oray assistay emay; anday ouldshay Iay eelfay indnesskay
owardstay myay enemiesay? Onay; omfray atthay omentmay Iay eclaredday everlastingay arway
againstay ethay eciesspay, anday oremay anthay allay, againstay imhay owhay adhay ormedfay emay
anday entsay emay orthfay otay isthay insupportableay iserymay.

e“thay unsay oseray; Iay eardhay ethay oicesvay ofay enmay anday ewknay atthay itay asway
impossibleay otay eturnray otay myay etreatray uringday atthay ayday. Accordinglyay Iay idhay
elfmysay inay omesay ickthay underwooday, eterminingday otay evoteday ethay ensuingay ourshay
otay eflectionray onay myay ituationsay.

e“thay easantplay unshinesay anday ethay urepay airay ofay ayday estoredray emay otay omesay
egreeday ofay anquillitytray; anday enwhay Iay onsideredcay atwhay adhay assedpay atay ethay
ottagecay, Iay ouldcay otnay elphay elievingbay atthay Iay adhay eenbay ootay astyhay inay myay
onclusionscay. Iay adhay ertainlycay acteday imprudentlyay. Itay asway apparentay atthay
myay onversationcay adhay interesteday ethay atherfay inay myay ehalfbay, anday Iay asway aay
oolfay inay avinghay exposeday myay ersonpay otay ethay orrorhay ofay ishay ildrenchay. Iay
oughtay otay avehay amiliarisedfay ethay olday Eday Aceylay otay emay, anday byay egreesday otay
avehay iscoveredday elfmysay otay ethay estray ofay ishay amilyfay, enwhay eythay ouldshay avehay
eenbay eparedpray orfay myay approachay. Utbay Iay idday otnay elievebay myay errorsay otay ebay
irretrievableay, anday afteray uchmay onsiderationcay Iay esolvedray otay eturnray otay ethay
ottagecay, eeksay ethay olday anmay, anday byay myay epresentationsray inway imhay otay myay
artypay.

ese“thay oughtsthay almedcay emay, anday inay ethay afternoonay Iay anksay intoay aay ofoundpray
eepslay; utbay ethay everfay ofay myay oodblay idday otnay alloway emay otay ebay isitedvay byay
eacefulpay eamsdray. Ethay orriblehay enescay ofay ethay ecedingpray ayday asway orfay everay
actingay eforebay myay eyesay; ethay emalesfay ereway ingflyay anday ethay enrageday Elixfay
earingtay emay omfray ishay ather’sfay eetfay. Iay awokeay exhausteday, anday indingfay atthay
itay asway alreadyay ightnay, Iay eptcray orthfay omfray myay iding-placeclay, anday entway inay
earchsay ofay oodfay.

en“whay myay ungerhay asway appeaseday, Iay irectedday myay epsstay owardstay ethay
ell-knownclay athpay atthay onductedcay otay ethay ottagecay. Allay erethay asway atay eacepay.
Iay eptcray intoay myay ovelhay anday emainedray inay ilentsay expectationay ofay ethay
accustomeday ourhay enwhay ethay amilyfay aroseay. Atthay ourhay assedpay, ethay unsay
ountedmay ighhay inay ethay eavenshay, utbay ethay ottagerscay idday otnay appearay. Iay
embledtray iolentlyvay, apprehendingay omesay eadfuldray isfortunemay. Ethay insideay
ofay ethay ottagecay asway arkday, anday Iay eardhay onay otionmay; Iay annotcay escribeday ethay
agonyay ofay isthay uspensesay.

esently“pray otway ountrymencay assedpay byay, utbay ausingpay earnay ethay ottagecay, eythay
entereday intoay onversationcay, usingay iolentvay esticulationsgay; utbay Iay idday otnay
understanday atwhay eythay aidsay, asay eythay okespay ethay anguagelay ofay ethay ountrycay,
ichwhay ifferedday omfray atthay ofay myay otectorspray. Oonsay afteray, oweverhay, Elixfay
approacheday ithway anotheray anmay; Iay asway urprisedsay, asay Iay ewknay atthay ehay adhay otnay
uittedqay ethay ottagecay atthay orningmay, anday aitedway anxiouslyay otay iscoverday omfray
ishay iscourseday ethay eaningmay ofay esethay unusualay appearancesay.

o“‘day ouyay onsidercay,’ aidsay ishay ompanioncay otay imhay,
at‘thay ouyay illway ebay obligeday otay aypay eethray onthsmay’ entray anday otay oselay
ethay oducepray ofay ouryay ardengay? Iay oday otnay ishway otay aketay anyay unfairay advantageay, anday
Iay egbay ereforethay atthay ouyay illway aketay omesay aysday otay onsidercay ofay ouryay
eterminationday.’

It“‘ay isay utterlyay uselessay,’ epliedray Elixfay; e‘way ancay
evernay againay inhabitay ouryay ottagecay. Ethay ifelay ofay myay atherfay isay inay ethay eatestgray
angerday, owingay otay ethay eadfuldray ircumstancecay atthay Iay avehay elatedray. Myay ifeway anday
myay istersay illway evernay ecoverray omfray eirthay orrorhay. Iay entreatay ouyay otnay otay easonray
ithway emay anyay oremay. Aketay ossessionpay ofay ouryay enementtay anday etlay emay flyay omfray isthay
aceplay.’

elix“fay embledtray iolentlyvay asay ehay aidsay isthay. Ehay anday ishay ompanioncay
entereday ethay ottagecay, inay ichwhay eythay emainedray orfay aay ewfay inutesmay, anday enthay
epartedday. Iay evernay awsay anyay ofay ethay amilyfay ofay Eday Aceylay oremay.

I“ay ontinuedcay orfay ethay emainderray ofay ethay ayday inay myay ovelhay inay aay atestay ofay
utteray anday upidstay espairday. Myay otectorspray adhay epartedday anday adhay okenbray
ethay onlyay inklay atthay eldhay emay otay ethay orldway. Orfay ethay irstfay imetay ethay
eelingsfay ofay evengeray anday atredhay illedfay myay osombay, anday Iay idday otnay ivestray otay
ontrolcay emthay, utbay allowingay elfmysay otay ebay ornebay awayay byay ethay eamstray, Iay
entbay myay indmay owardstay injuryay anday eathday. Enwhay Iay oughtthay ofay myay iendsfray,
ofay ethay ildmay oicevay ofay Eday Aceylay, ethay entlegay eyesay ofay Agathaay, anday ethay
exquisiteay eautybay ofay ethay Arabianay, esethay oughtsthay anishedvay anday aay ushgay ofay
earstay omewhatsay oothedsay emay. Utbay againay enwhay Iay eflectedray atthay eythay adhay
urnedspay anday esertedday emay, angeray eturnedray, aay ageray ofay angeray, anday unableay otay
injureay anythingay umanhay, Iay urnedtay myay uryfay owardstay inanimateay objectsay. Asay
ightnay advanceday, Iay acedplay aay arietyvay ofay ombustiblescay arounday ethay ottagecay,
anday afteray avinghay estroyedday everyay estigevay ofay ultivationcay inay ethay ardengay,
Iay aitedway ithway orcedfay impatienceay untilay ethay oonmay adhay unksay otay ommencecay myay
operationsay.

As“ay ethay ightnay advanceday, aay iercefay indway aroseay omfray ethay oodsway anday uicklyqay
ispersedday ethay oudsclay atthay adhay oiteredlay inay ethay eavenshay; ethay astblay oretay
alongay ikelay aay ightymay avalancheay anday oducedpray aay indkay ofay insanityay inay myay
iritsspay atthay urstbay allay oundsbay ofay easonray anday eflectionray. Iay ightedlay ethay
dryay anchbray ofay aay eetray anday ancedday ithway uryfay arounday ethay evotedday ottagecay,
myay eyesay illstay ixedfay onay ethay esternway orizonhay, ethay edgeay ofay ichwhay ethay oonmay
earlynay ouchedtay. Aay artpay ofay itsay orbay asway atay engthlay idhay, anday Iay avedway myay
andbray; itay anksay, anday ithway aay oudlay eamscray Iay iredfay ethay awstray, anday eathhay,
anday ushesbay, ichwhay Iay adhay ollectedcay. Ethay indway annedfay ethay irefay, anday ethay
ottagecay asway uicklyqay envelopeday byay ethay amesflay, ichwhay ungclay otay itay anday
ickedlay itay ithway eirthay orkedfay anday estroyingday onguestay.

As“ay oonsay asay Iay asway onvincedcay atthay onay assistanceay ouldcay avesay anyay artpay ofay
ethay abitationhay, Iay uittedqay ethay enescay anday oughtsay orfay efugeray inay ethay oodsway.

And“ay ownay, ithway ethay orldway eforebay emay, itherwhay ouldshay Iay endbay myay epsstay? Iay
esolvedray otay flyay arfay omfray ethay enescay ofay myay isfortunesmay; utbay otay emay, atedhay
anday espisedday, everyay ountrycay ustmay ebay equallyay orriblehay. Atay engthlay ethay
oughtthay ofay ouyay ossedcray myay indmay. Iay earnedlay omfray ouryay aperspay atthay ouyay
ereway myay atherfay, myay eatorcray; anday otay omwhay ouldcay Iay applyay ithway oremay itnessfay
anthay otay imhay owhay adhay ivengay emay ifelay? Amongay ethay essonslay atthay Elixfay adhay
estowedbay uponay Afiesay, eographygay adhay otnay eenbay omitteday; Iay adhay earnedlay omfray
esethay ethay elativeray ituationssay ofay ethay ifferentday ountriescay ofay ethay earthay.
Ouyay adhay entionedmay Enevagay asay ethay amenay ofay ouryay ativenay owntay, anday owardstay
isthay aceplay Iay esolvedray otay oceedpray.

ut“bay owhay asway Iay otay irectday elfmysay? Iay ewknay atthay Iay ustmay aveltray inay aay
outhwesterlysay irectionday otay eachray myay estinationday, utbay ethay unsay asway myay
onlyay uidegay. Iay idday otnay owknay ethay amesnay ofay ethay ownstay atthay Iay asway otay asspay
oughthray, ornay ouldcay Iay askay informationay omfray aay inglesay umanhay eingbay; utbay Iay
idday otnay espairday. Omfray ouyay onlyay ouldcay Iay opehay orfay uccoursay, althoughay
owardstay ouyay Iay eltfay onay entimentsay utbay atthay ofay atredhay. Unfeelingay,
eartlesshay eatorcray! Ouyay adhay endoweday emay ithway erceptionspay anday assionspay
anday enthay astcay emay abroaday anay objectay orfay ethay ornscay anday orrorhay ofay ankindmay.
Utbay onay ouyay onlyay adhay Iay anyay aimclay orfay itypay anday edressray, anday omfray ouyay Iay
eterminedday otay eeksay atthay usticejay ichwhay Iay ainlyvay attempteday otay aingay omfray
anyay otheray eingbay atthay oreway ethay umanhay ormfay.

“myay avelstray ereway onglay anday ethay ufferingssay Iay endureday intenseay. Itay asway
atelay inay autumnay enwhay Iay uittedqay ethay istrictday erewhay Iay adhay osay onglay esidedray.
Iay avelledtray onlyay atay ightnay, earfulfay ofay encounteringay ethay isagevay ofay aay
umanhay eingbay. Aturenay ecayedday arounday emay, anday ethay unsay ecamebay eatlesshay;
ainray anday owsnay ouredpay arounday emay; ightymay iversray ereway ozenfray; ethay urfacesay
ofay ethay earthay asway ardhay anday illchay, anday arebay, anday Iay oundfay onay eltershay. Ohay,
earthay! Owhay oftenay idday Iay imprecateay ursescay onay ethay ausecay ofay myay eingbay! Ethay
ildnessmay ofay myay aturenay adhay edflay, anday allay ithinway emay asway urnedtay otay allgay
anday itternessbay. Ethay earernay Iay approacheday otay ouryay abitationhay, ethay oremay
eeplyday idday Iay eelfay ethay iritspay ofay evengeray enkindleday inay myay earthay. Owsnay
ellfay, anday ethay atersway ereway ardenedhay, utbay Iay estedray otnay. Aay ewfay incidentsay
ownay anday enthay irectedday emay, anday Iay ossessedpay aay apmay ofay ethay ountrycay; utbay Iay
oftenay anderedway ideway omfray myay athpay. Ethay agonyay ofay myay eelingsfay alloweday emay
onay espiteray; onay incidentay occurreday omfray ichwhay myay ageray anday iserymay ouldcay
otnay extractay itsay oodfay; utbay aay ircumstancecay atthay appenedhay enwhay Iay arriveday
onay ethay onfinescay ofay Itzerlandsway, enwhay ethay unsay adhay ecoveredray itsay armthway
anday ethay earthay againay eganbay otay ooklay eengray, onfirmedcay inay anay especialay
annermay ethay itternessbay anday orrorhay ofay myay eelingsfay.

I“ay enerallygay estedray uringday ethay ayday anday avelledtray onlyay enwhay Iay asway
ecuredsay byay ightnay omfray ethay iewvay ofay anmay. Oneay orningmay, oweverhay, indingfay
atthay myay athpay aylay oughthray aay eepday oodway, Iay enturedvay otay ontinuecay myay ourneyjay
afteray ethay unsay adhay isenray; ethay ayday, ichwhay asway oneay ofay ethay irstfay ofay ingspray,
eeredchay evenay emay byay ethay ovelinesslay ofay itsay unshinesay anday ethay alminessbay ofay
ethay airay. Iay eltfay emotionsay ofay entlenessgay anday easureplay, atthay adhay onglay
appeareday eadday, eviveray ithinway emay. Alfhay urprisedsay byay ethay oveltynay ofay
esethay ensationssay, Iay alloweday elfmysay otay ebay ornebay awayay byay emthay, anday
orgettingfay myay olitudesay anday eformityday, aredday otay ebay appyhay. Oftsay earstay
againay edewedbay myay eekschay, anday Iay evenay aisedray myay umidhay eyesay ithway
ankfulnessthay owardstay ethay essedblay unsay, ichwhay estowedbay uchsay oyjay uponay emay.

I“ay ontinuedcay otay indway amongay ethay athspay ofay ethay oodway, untilay Iay amecay otay itsay
oundarybay, ichwhay asway irtedskay byay aay eepday anday apidray iverray, intoay ichwhay anymay
ofay ethay eestray entbay eirthay anchesbray, ownay uddingbay ithway ethay eshfray ingspray.
Erehay Iay ausedpay, otnay exactlyay owingknay atwhay athpay otay ursuepay, enwhay Iay eardhay
ethay oundsay ofay oicesvay, atthay induceday emay otay oncealcay elfmysay underay ethay adeshay
ofay aay esscypray. Iay asway arcelyscay idhay enwhay aay oungyay irlgay amecay unningray
owardstay ethay otspay erewhay Iay asway oncealedcay, aughinglay, asay ifay eshay anray omfray
omeonesay inay ortspay. Eshay ontinuedcay erhay oursecay alongay ethay ecipitouspray idessay
ofay ethay iverray, enwhay uddenlysay erhay ootfay ippedslay, anday eshay ellfay intoay ethay
apidray eamstray. Iay ushedray omfray myay iding-placeclay anday ithway extremeay abourlay,
omfray ethay orcefay ofay ethay urrentcay, avedsay erhay anday aggeddray erhay otay oreshay. Eshay
asway enselesssay, anday Iay endeavoureday byay everyay eansmay inay myay owerpay otay estoreray
animationay, enwhay Iay asway uddenlysay interrupteday byay ethay approachay ofay aay usticray,
owhay asway obablypray ethay ersonpay omfray omwhay eshay adhay ayfullyplay edflay. Onay
eeingsay emay, ehay artedday owardstay emay, anday earingtay ethay irlgay omfray myay armsay,
astenedhay owardstay ethay eeperday artspay ofay ethay oodway. Iay ollowedfay eedilyspay, Iay
ardlyhay ewknay whyay; utbay enwhay ethay anmay awsay emay awdray earnay, ehay aimeday aay ungay,
ichwhay ehay arriedcay, atay myay odybay anday iredfay. Iay anksay otay ethay oundgray, anday myay
injureray, ithway increaseday iftnesssway, escapeday intoay ethay oodway.

is“thay asway enthay ethay ewardray ofay myay enevolencebay! Iay adhay avedsay aay umanhay eingbay
omfray estructionday, anday asay aay ecompenseray Iay ownay ithedwray underay ethay iserablemay
ainpay ofay aay oundway ichwhay atteredshay ethay eshflay anday onebay. Ethay eelingsfay ofay
indnesskay anday entlenessgay ichwhay Iay adhay entertaineday utbay aay ewfay omentsmay
eforebay avegay aceplay otay ellishhay ageray anday ashinggnay ofay eethtay. Inflameday byay
ainpay, Iay owedvay eternalay atredhay anday engeancevay otay allay ankindmay. Utbay ethay
agonyay ofay myay oundway overcameay emay; myay ulsespay ausedpay, anday Iay aintedfay.

or“fay omesay eeksway Iay edlay aay iserablemay ifelay inay ethay oodsway, endeavouringay otay
urecay ethay oundway ichwhay Iay adhay eceivedray. Ethay allbay adhay entereday myay ouldershay,
anday Iay ewknay otnay etherwhay itay adhay emainedray erethay oray assedpay oughthray; atay anyay
ateray Iay adhay onay eansmay ofay extractingay itay. Myay ufferingssay ereway augmenteday
alsoay byay ethay oppressiveay ensesay ofay ethay injusticeay anday ingratitudeay ofay eirthay
inflictionay. Myay ailyday owsvay oseray orfay evenge—aray eepday anday eadlyday evengeray,
uchsay asay ouldway aloneay ompensatecay orfay ethay outragesay anday anguishay Iay adhay
endureday.

After“ay omesay eeksway myay oundway ealedhay, anday Iay ontinuedcay myay ourneyjay. Ethay
abourslay Iay endureday ereway onay ongerlay otay ebay alleviateday byay ethay ightbray unsay oray
entlegay eezesbray ofay ingspray; allay oyjay asway utbay aay ockerymay ichwhay insulteday myay
esolateday atestay anday ademay emay eelfay oremay ainfullypay atthay Iay asway otnay ademay orfay
ethay enjoymentay ofay easureplay.

ut“bay myay oilstay ownay ewdray earnay aay oseclay, anday inay otway onthsmay omfray isthay imetay Iay
eachedray ethay environsay ofay Enevagay.

It“ay asway eveningay enwhay Iay arriveday, anday Iay etiredray otay aay iding-placeclay amongay
ethay ieldsfay atthay urroundsay itay otay editatemay inay atwhay annermay Iay ouldshay applyay
otay ouyay. Iay asway oppresseday byay atiguefay anday ungerhay anday arfay ootay unhappyay otay
enjoyay ethay entlegay eezesbray ofay eveningay oray ethay ospectpray ofay ethay unsay ettingsay
ehindbay ethay upendousstay ountainsmay ofay Urajay.

At“ay isthay imetay aay ightslay eepslay elievedray emay omfray ethay ainpay ofay eflectionray,
ichwhay asway isturbedday byay ethay approachay ofay aay eautifulbay ildchay, owhay amecay
unningray intoay ethay ecessray Iay adhay osenchay, ithway allay ethay ortivenessspay ofay
infancyay. Uddenlysay, asay Iay azedgay onay imhay, anay ideaay eizedsay emay atthay isthay
ittlelay eaturecray asway unprejudiceday anday adhay ivedlay ootay ortshay aay imetay otay avehay
imbibeday aay orrorhay ofay eformityday. Ifay, ereforethay, Iay ouldcay eizesay imhay anday
educateay imhay asay myay ompanioncay anday iendfray, Iay ouldshay otnay ebay osay esolateday inay
isthay eopledpay earthay.

Urged“ay byay isthay impulseay, Iay eizedsay onay ethay oybay asay ehay assedpay anday ewdray imhay
owardstay emay. Asay oonsay asay ehay eheldbay myay ormfay, ehay acedplay ishay andshay eforebay
ishay eyesay anday uttereday aay illshray eamscray; Iay ewdray ishay andhay orciblyfay omfray ishay
acefay anday aidsay, ild‘chay, atwhay isay ethay eaningmay ofay isthay? Iay oday otnay intenday otay
urthay ouyay; istenlay otay emay.’

e“hay uggledstray iolentlyvay. et‘lay emay ogay,’ ehay iedcray;
onster‘may! Uglyay etchwray! Ouyay ishway otay eatay emay anday eartay emay otay iecespay. Ouyay
areay anay ogreay. Etlay emay ogay, oray Iay illway elltay myay apapay.’

oy“‘bay, ouyay illway evernay eesay ouryay atherfay againay; ouyay ustmay omecay ithway emay.’

ideous“‘hay onstermay! Etlay emay ogay. Myay apapay isay aay ic—hesynday isay May.
Ankenstein—hefray illway unishpay ouyay. Ouyay areday otnay eepkay emay.’

ankenstein“‘fray! ouyay elongbay enthay otay myay enemy—toay imhay owardstay omwhay Iay avehay
ornsway eternalay evengeray; ouyay allshay ebay myay irstfay ictimvay.’

e“thay ildchay illstay uggledstray anday oadedlay emay ithway epithetsay ichwhay arriedcay
espairday otay myay earthay; Iay aspedgray ishay oatthray otay ilencesay imhay, anday inay aay
omentmay ehay aylay eadday atay myay eetfay.

I“ay azedgay onay myay ictimvay, anday myay earthay elledsway ithway exultationay anday ellishhay
iumphtray; appingclay myay andshay, Iay exclaimeday, I‘ay ootay ancay eatecray esolationday;
myay enemyay isay otnay invulnerableay; isthay eathday illway arrycay espairday otay imhay, anday
aay ousandthay otheray iseriesmay allshay ormenttay anday estroyday imhay.’

As“ay Iay ixedfay myay eyesay onay ethay ildchay, Iay awsay omethingsay itteringglay onay ishay
eastbray. Iay ooktay itay; itay asway aay ortraitpay ofay aay ostmay ovelylay omanway. Inay itespay
ofay myay alignitymay, itay oftenedsay anday attracteday emay. Orfay aay ewfay omentsmay Iay
azedgay ithway elightday onay erhay arkday eyesay, ingedfray byay eepday asheslay, anday erhay
ovelylay ipslay; utbay esentlypray myay ageray eturnedray; Iay ememberedray atthay Iay asway
orfay everay eprivedday ofay ethay elightsday atthay uchsay eautifulbay eaturescray ouldcay
estowbay anday atthay eshay osewhay esemblanceray Iay ontemplatedcay ouldway, inay
egardingray emay, avehay angedchay atthay airay ofay ivineday enignitybay otay oneay
expressiveay ofay isgustday anday affrightay.

an“cay ouyay onderway atthay uchsay oughtsthay ansportedtray emay ithway ageray? Iay onlyay
onderway atthay atay atthay omentmay, insteaday ofay entingvay myay ensationssay inay
exclamationsay anday agonyay, Iay idday otnay ushray amongay ankindmay anday erishpay inay ethay
attemptay otay estroyday emthay.

ile“whay Iay asway overcomeay byay esethay eelingsfay, Iay eftlay ethay otspay erewhay Iay adhay
ommittedcay ethay urdermay, anday eekingsay aay oremay ecludedsay iding-placeclay, Iay
entereday aay arnbay ichwhay adhay appeareday otay emay otay ebay emptyay. Aay omanway asway
eepingslay onay omesay awstray; eshay asway oungyay, otnay indeeday osay eautifulbay asay erhay
osewhay ortraitpay Iay eldhay, utbay ofay anay agreeableay aspectay anday oomingblay inay ethay
ovelinesslay ofay outhyay anday ealthhay. Erehay, Iay oughtthay, isay oneay ofay osethay osewhay
oy-impartingclay ilessmay areay estowedbay onay allay utbay emay. Anday enthay Iay entbay overay
erhay anday isperedwhay, Awake‘ay, airestfay, thyay overlay isay ear—henay owhay ouldway
ivegay ishay ifelay utbay otay obtainay oneay ooklay ofay affectionay omfray inethay eyesay; myay
elovedbay, awakeay!’

e“thay eeperslay irredstay; aay illthray ofay errortay anray oughthray emay. Ouldshay eshay
indeeday awakeay, anday eesay emay, anday ursecay emay, anday enounceday ethay urderermay? Usthay
ouldway eshay assuredlyay actay ifay erhay arkenedday eyesay openeday anday eshay eheldbay emay.
Ethay oughtthay asway adnessmay; itay irredstay ethay iendfay ithinway e—notmay Iay, utbay
eshay, allshay uffersay; ethay urdermay Iay avehay ommittedcay ecausebay Iay amay orfay everay
obbedray ofay allay atthay eshay ouldcay ivegay emay, eshay allshay atoneay. Ethay imecray adhay
itsay ourcesay inay erhay; ebay ershay ethay unishmentpay! Anksthay otay ethay essonslay ofay
Elixfay anday ethay anguinarysay awslay ofay anmay, Iay adhay earnedlay ownay otay orkway
ischiefmay. Iay entbay overay erhay anday acedplay ethay ortraitpay ecurelysay inay oneay ofay
ethay oldsfay ofay erhay essdray. Eshay ovedmay againay, anday Iay edflay.

or“fay omesay aysday Iay auntedhay ethay otspay erewhay esethay enesscay adhay akentay aceplay,
ometimessay ishingway otay eesay ouyay, ometimessay esolvedray otay uitqay ethay orldway anday
itsay iseriesmay orfay everay. Atay engthlay Iay anderedway owardstay esethay ountainsmay,
anday avehay angedray oughthray eirthay immenseay ecessesray, onsumedcay byay aay urningbay
assionpay ichwhay ouyay aloneay ancay atifygray. Eway aymay otnay artpay untilay ouyay avehay
omisedpray otay omplycay ithway myay equisitionray. Iay amay aloneay anday iserablemay; anmay
illway otnay associateay ithway emay; utbay oneay asay eformedday anday orriblehay asay elfmysay
ouldway otnay enyday erselfhay otay emay. Myay ompanioncay ustmay ebay ofay ethay amesay eciesspay
anday avehay ethay amesay efectsday. Isthay eingbay ouyay ustmay eatecray.”




Apterchay 17ay


Ethay eingbay inishedfay eakingspay anday ixedfay ishay ookslay uponay emay inay ethay
expectationay ofay aay eplyray. Utbay Iay asway ewilderedbay, erplexedpay, anday unableay otay
arrangeay myay ideasay ufficientlysay otay understanday ethay ullfay extentay ofay ishay
opositionpray. Ehay ontinuedcay,

ou“yay ustmay eatecray aay emalefay orfay emay ithway omwhay Iay ancay ivelay inay ethay
interchangeay ofay osethay athiessympay ecessarynay orfay myay eingbay. Isthay ouyay aloneay
ancay oday, anday Iay emandday itay ofay ouyay asay aay ightray ichwhay ouyay ustmay otnay efuseray otay
oncedecay.”

Ethay atterlay artpay ofay ishay aletay adhay indledkay aneway inay emay ethay angeray atthay adhay
iedday awayay ilewhay ehay arratednay ishay eacefulpay ifelay amongay ethay ottagerscay, anday
asay ehay aidsay isthay Iay ouldcay onay ongerlay uppresssay ethay ageray atthay urnedbay ithinway
emay.

I“ay oday efuseray itay,” Iay epliedray; and“ay onay orturetay allshay everay extortay aay
onsentcay omfray emay. Ouyay aymay enderray emay ethay ostmay iserablemay ofay enmay, utbay ouyay
allshay evernay akemay emay asebay inay myay ownay eyesay. Allshay Iay eatecray anotheray ikelay
ourselfyay, osewhay ointjay ickednessway ightmay esolateday ethay orldway. Egonebay! Iay
avehay answereday ouyay; ouyay aymay orturetay emay, utbay Iay illway evernay onsentcay.”

ou“yay areay inay ethay ongwray,” epliedray ethay iendfay; and“ay insteaday
ofay eateningthray, Iay amay ontentcay otay easonray ithway ouyay. Iay amay aliciousmay ecausebay Iay
amay iserablemay. Amay Iay otnay unnedshay anday atedhay byay allay ankindmay? Ouyay, myay eatorcray,
ouldway eartay emay otay iecespay anday iumphtray; ememberray atthay, anday elltay emay whyay Iay
ouldshay itypay anmay oremay anthay ehay itiespay emay? Ouyay ouldway otnay allcay itay urdermay ifay ouyay
ouldcay ecipitatepray emay intoay oneay ofay osethay ice-riftsclay anday estroyday myay amefray, ethay
orkway ofay ouryay ownay andshay. Allshay Iay espectray anmay enwhay ehay ondemnscay emay? Etlay imhay
ivelay ithway emay inay ethay interchangeay ofay indnesskay, anday insteaday ofay injuryay Iay ouldway
estowbay everyay enefitbay uponay imhay ithway earstay ofay atitudegray atay ishay acceptanceay.
Utbay atthay annotcay ebay; ethay umanhay ensessay areay insurmountableay arriersbay otay ouray
unionay. Etyay inemay allshay otnay ebay ethay ubmissionsay ofay abjectay averyslay. Iay illway
evengeray myay injuriesay; ifay Iay annotcay inspireay ovelay, Iay illway ausecay earfay, anday
ieflychay owardstay ouyay myay arch-enemyclay, ecausebay myay eatorcray, oday Iay earsway
inextinguishableay atredhay. Avehay aay arecay; Iay illway orkway atay ouryay estructionday, ornay
inishfay untilay Iay esolateday ouryay earthay, osay atthay ouyay allshay ursecay ethay ourhay ofay
ouryay irthbay.”

Aay iendishfay ageray animateday imhay asay ehay aidsay isthay; ishay acefay asway inkledwray
intoay ontortionscay ootay orriblehay orfay umanhay eyesay otay eholdbay; utbay esentlypray
ehay almedcay imselfhay anday oceededpray—

I“ay intendeday otay easonray. Isthay assionpay isay etrimentalday otay emay, orfay ouyay oday
otnay eflectray atthay ou_yay_ areay ethay ausecay ofay itsay excessay. Ifay anyay eingbay eltfay
emotionsay ofay enevolencebay owardstay emay, Iay ouldshay eturnray emthay aay undredhay anday aay
undredfoldhay; orfay atthay oneay eature’scray akesay Iay ouldway akemay eacepay ithway ethay
olewhay indkay! Utbay Iay ownay indulgeay inay eamsdray ofay issblay atthay annotcay ebay ealisedray.
Atwhay Iay askay ofay ouyay isay easonableray anday oderatemay; Iay emandday aay eaturecray ofay
anotheray exsay, utbay asay ideoushay asay elfmysay; ethay atificationgray isay allsmay, utbay itay
isay allay atthay Iay ancay eceiveray, anday itay allshay ontentcay emay. Itay isay uetray, eway allshay ebay
onstersmay, utcay offay omfray allay ethay orldway; utbay onay atthay accountay eway allshay ebay oremay
attacheday otay oneay anotheray. Ouray iveslay illway otnay ebay appyhay, utbay eythay illway ebay
armlesshay anday eefray omfray ethay iserymay Iay ownay eelfay. Ohay! Myay eatorcray, akemay emay
appyhay; etlay emay eelfay atitudegray owardstay ouyay orfay oneay enefitbay! Etlay emay eesay atthay Iay
exciteay ethay athysympay ofay omesay existingay ingthay; oday otnay enyday emay myay
equestray!”

Iay asway ovedmay. Iay udderedshay enwhay Iay oughtthay ofay ethay ossiblepay onsequencescay
ofay myay onsentcay, utbay Iay eltfay atthay erethay asway omesay usticejay inay ishay argumentay.
Ishay aletay anday ethay eelingsfay ehay ownay expresseday ovedpray imhay otay ebay aay eaturecray
ofay inefay ensationssay, anday idday Iay otnay asay ishay akermay oweay imhay allay ethay ortionpay
ofay appinesshay atthay itay asway inay myay owerpay otay estowbay? Ehay awsay myay angechay ofay
eelingfay anday ontinuedcay,

If“ay ouyay onsentcay, eithernay ouyay ornay anyay otheray umanhay eingbay allshay everay eesay
usay againay; Iay illway ogay otay ethay astvay ildsway ofay Outhsay Americaay. Myay oodfay isay otnay
atthay ofay anmay; Iay oday otnay estroyday ethay amblay anday ethay idkay otay utglay myay appetiteay;
acornsay anday erriesbay afforday emay ufficientsay ourishmentnay. Myay ompanioncay illway
ebay ofay ethay amesay aturenay asay elfmysay anday illway ebay ontentcay ithway ethay amesay arefay.
Eway allshay akemay ouray edbay ofay ieddray eaveslay; ethay unsay illway ineshay onay usay asay onay
anmay anday illway ipenray ouray oodfay. Ethay icturepay Iay esentpray otay ouyay isay eacefulpay
anday umanhay, anday ouyay ustmay eelfay atthay ouyay ouldcay enyday itay onlyay inay ethay
antonnessway ofay owerpay anday ueltycray. Itilesspay asay ouyay avehay eenbay owardstay emay,
Iay ownay eesay ompassioncay inay ouryay eyesay; etlay emay eizesay ethay avourablefay omentmay
anday ersuadepay ouyay otay omisepray atwhay Iay osay ardentlyay esireday.”

ou“yay oposepray,” epliedray Iay, o“tay flyay omfray ethay abitationshay ofay
anmay, otay elldway inay osethay ildsway erewhay ethay eastsbay ofay ethay ieldfay illway ebay ouryay
onlyay ompanionscay. Owhay ancay ouyay, owhay onglay orfay ethay ovelay anday athysympay ofay anmay,
erseverepay inay isthay exileay? Ouyay illway eturnray anday againay eeksay eirthay indnesskay, anday
ouyay illway eetmay ithway eirthay etestationday; ouryay evilay assionspay illway ebay enewedray,
anday ouyay illway enthay avehay aay ompanioncay otay aiday ouyay inay ethay asktay ofay estructionday.
Isthay aymay otnay ebay; easecay otay argueay ethay ointpay, orfay Iay annotcay onsentcay.”

ow“hay inconstantay areay ouryay eelingsfay! Utbay aay omentmay agoay ouyay ereway ovedmay byay
myay epresentationsray, anday whyay oday ouyay againay ardenhay ourselfyay otay myay omplaintscay?
Iay earsway otay ouyay, byay ethay earthay ichwhay Iay inhabitay, anday byay ouyay atthay ademay emay, atthay
ithway ethay ompanioncay ouyay estowbay, Iay illway uitqay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofay anmay anday
elldway, asay itay aymay ancechay, inay ethay ostmay avagesay ofay acesplay. Myay evilay assionspay
illway avehay edflay, orfay Iay allshay eetmay ithway athysympay! Myay ifelay illway owflay uietlyqay
awayay, anday inay myay ingdyay omentsmay Iay allshay otnay ursecay myay akermay.”

Ishay ordsway adhay aay angestray effectay uponay emay. Iay ompassionatedcay imhay anday
ometimessay eltfay aay ishway otay onsolecay imhay, utbay enwhay Iay ookedlay uponay imhay, enwhay
Iay awsay ethay ilthyfay assmay atthay ovedmay anday alkedtay, myay earthay ickenedsay anday myay
eelingsfay ereway altereday otay osethay ofay orrorhay anday atredhay. Iay iedtray otay iflestay
esethay ensationssay; Iay oughtthay atthay asay Iay ouldcay otnay athisesympay ithway imhay, Iay
adhay onay ightray otay ithholdway omfray imhay ethay allsmay ortionpay ofay appinesshay ichwhay
asway etyay inay myay owerpay otay estowbay.

ou“yay earsway,” Iay aidsay, o“tay ebay armlesshay; utbay avehay ouyay otnay
alreadyay ownshay aay egreeday ofay alicemay atthay ouldshay easonablyray akemay emay istrustday
ouyay? Aymay otnay evenay isthay ebay aay eintfay atthay illway increaseay ouryay iumphtray byay
affordingay aay iderway opescay orfay ouryay evengeray?”

ow“hay isay isthay? Iay ustmay otnay ebay ifledtray ithway, anday Iay emandday anay answeray. Ifay
Iay avehay onay iestay anday onay affectionsay, atredhay anday icevay ustmay ebay myay ortionpay;
ethay ovelay ofay anotheray illway estroyday ethay ausecay ofay myay imescray, anday Iay allshay
ecomebay aay ingthay ofay osewhay existenceay everyoneay illway ebay ignorantay. Myay icesvay
areay ethay ildrenchay ofay aay orcedfay olitudesay atthay Iay abhoray, anday myay irtuesvay illway
ecessarilynay ariseay enwhay Iay ivelay inay ommunioncay ithway anay equalay. Iay allshay eelfay
ethay affectionsay ofay aay ensitivesay eingbay anday ecomebay inkedlay otay ethay ainchay ofay
existenceay anday eventsay omfray ichwhay Iay amay ownay excludeday.”

Iay ausedpay omesay imetay otay eflectray onay allay ehay adhay elatedray anday ethay ariousvay
argumentsay ichwhay ehay adhay employeday. Iay oughtthay ofay ethay omisepray ofay irtuesvay ichwhay
ehay adhay isplayedday onay ethay openingay ofay ishay existenceay anday ethay ubsequentsay ightblay
ofay allay indlykay eelingfay byay ethay oathinglay anday ornscay ichwhay ishay otectorspray adhay
anifestedmay owardstay imhay. Ishay owerpay anday eatsthray ereway otnay omitteday inay myay
alculationscay; aay eaturecray owhay ouldcay existay inay ethay ice-cavesclay ofay ethay aciersglay
anday idehay imselfhay omfray ursuitpay amongay ethay idgesray ofay inaccessibleay ecipicespray
asway aay eingbay ossessingpay acultiesfay itay ouldway ebay ainvay otay opecay ithway. Afteray aay
onglay ausepay ofay eflectionray Iay oncludedcay atthay ethay usticejay ueday othbay otay imhay anday
myay ellowfay eaturescray emandedday ofay emay atthay Iay ouldshay omplycay ithway ishay equestray.
Urningtay otay imhay, ereforethay, Iay aidsay,

I“ay onsentcay otay ouryay emandday, onay ouryay olemnsay oathay otay uitqay Europeay orfay everay,
anday everyay otheray aceplay inay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofay anmay, asay oonsay asay Iay allshay
eliverday intoay ouryay andshay aay emalefay owhay illway accompanyay ouyay inay ouryay exileay.”

I“ay earsway,” ehay iedcray, “byay ethay unsay, anday byay ethay ueblay skyay ofay
eavenhay, anday byay ethay irefay ofay ovelay atthay urnsbay myay earthay, atthay ifay ouyay antgray myay
ayerpray, ilewhay eythay existay ouyay allshay evernay eholdbay emay againay. Epartday otay ouryay
omehay anday ommencecay ouryay abourslay; Iay allshay atchway eirthay ogresspray ithway
unutterableay anxietyay; anday earfay otnay utbay atthay enwhay ouyay areay eadyray Iay allshay
appearay.”

Ayingsay isthay, ehay uddenlysay uittedqay emay, earfulfay, erhapspay, ofay anyay angechay inay
myay entimentssay. Iay awsay imhay escendday ethay ountainmay ithway eatergray eedspay anthay
ethay ightflay ofay anay eagleay, anday uicklyqay ostlay amongay ethay undulationsay ofay ethay
easay ofay iceay.

Ishay aletay adhay occupieday ethay olewhay ayday, anday ethay unsay asway uponay ethay ergevay ofay
ethay orizonhay enwhay ehay epartedday. Iay ewknay atthay Iay oughtay otay astenhay myay escentday
owardstay ethay alleyvay, asay Iay ouldshay oonsay ebay encompasseday inay arknessday; utbay myay
earthay asway eavyhay, anday myay epsstay owslay. Ethay abourlay ofay indingway amongay ethay
ittlelay athspay ofay ethay ountainmay anday ixingfay myay eetfay irmlyfay asay Iay advanceday
erplexedpay emay, occupieday asay Iay asway byay ethay emotionsay ichwhay ethay occurrencesay
ofay ethay ayday adhay oducedpray. Ightnay asway arfay advanceday enwhay Iay amecay otay ethay
alfwayhay esting-placeclay anday eatedsay elfmysay esidebay ethay ountainfay. Ethay arsstay
oneshay atay intervalsay asay ethay oudsclay assedpay omfray overay emthay; ethay arkday inespay
oseray eforebay emay, anday everyay erehay anday erethay aay okenbray eetray aylay onay ethay
oundgray; itay asway aay enescay ofay onderfulway olemnitysay anday irredstay angestray
oughtsthay ithinway emay. Iay eptway itterlybay, anday aspingclay myay andshay inay agonyay, Iay
exclaimeday, Oh“ay! arsstay anday oudsclay anday indsway, eyay areay allay aboutay otay ockmay
emay; ifay eyay eallyray itypay emay, ushcray ensationsay anday emorymay; etlay emay ecomebay asay
oughtnay; utbay ifay otnay, epartday, epartday, anday eavelay emay inay arknessday.”

Esethay ereway ildway anday iserablemay oughtsthay, utbay Iay annotcay escribeday otay ouyay
owhay ethay eternalay inklingtway ofay ethay arsstay eighedway uponay emay anday owhay Iay
istenedlay otay everyay astblay ofay indway asay ifay itay ereway aay ullday uglyay irocsay onay itsay
ayway otay onsumecay emay.

Orningmay awnedday eforebay Iay arriveday atay ethay illagevay ofay Amounixchay; Iay ooktay onay
estray, utbay eturnedray immediatelyay otay Enevagay. Evenay inay myay ownay earthay Iay ouldcay
ivegay onay expressionay otay myay ensations—theysay eighedway onay emay ithway aay
ountain’smay eightway anday eirthay excessay estroyedday myay agonyay eneathbay emthay.
Usthay Iay eturnedray omehay, anday enteringay ethay ousehay, esentedpray elfmysay otay ethay
amilyfay. Myay aggardhay anday ildway appearanceay awokeay intenseay alarmay, utbay Iay
answereday onay uestionqay, arcelyscay idday Iay eakspay. Iay eltfay asay ifay Iay ereway acedplay
underay aay an—asbay ifay Iay adhay onay ightray otay aimclay eirthay athies—assympay ifay
evernay oremay ightmay Iay enjoyay ompanionshipcay ithway emthay. Etyay evenay usthay Iay
ovedlay emthay otay adorationay; anday otay avesay emthay, Iay esolvedray otay edicateday
elfmysay otay myay ostmay abhorreday asktay. Ethay ospectpray ofay uchsay anay occupationay
ademay everyay otheray ircumstancecay ofay existenceay asspay eforebay emay ikelay aay eamdray,
anday atthay oughtthay onlyay adhay otay emay ethay ealityray ofay ifelay.




Apterchay 18ay


Ayday afteray ayday, eekway afteray eekway, assedpay awayay onay myay eturnray otay Enevagay; anday
Iay ouldcay otnay ollectcay ethay ouragecay otay ecommenceray myay orkway. Iay earedfay ethay
engeancevay ofay ethay isappointedday iendfay, etyay Iay asway unableay otay overcomeay myay
epugnanceray otay ethay asktay ichwhay asway enjoineday emay. Iay oundfay atthay Iay ouldcay otnay
omposecay aay emalefay ithoutway againay evotingday everalsay onthsmay otay ofoundpray
udystay anday aboriouslay isquisitionday. Iay adhay eardhay ofay omesay iscoveriesday
avinghay eenbay ademay byay anay Englishay ilosopherphay, ethay owledgeknay ofay ichwhay asway
aterialmay otay myay uccesssay, anday Iay ometimessay oughtthay ofay obtainingay myay
ather’sfay onsentcay otay isitvay Englanday orfay isthay urposepay; utbay Iay ungclay otay
everyay etencepray ofay elayday anday ankshray omfray akingtay ethay irstfay epstay inay anay
undertakingay osewhay immediateay ecessitynay eganbay otay appearay esslay absoluteay otay
emay. Aay angechay indeeday adhay akentay aceplay inay emay; myay ealthhay, ichwhay adhay
ithertohay eclinedday, asway ownay uchmay estoredray; anday myay iritsspay, enwhay
uncheckeday byay ethay emorymay ofay myay unhappyay omisepray, oseray oportionablypray. Myay
atherfay awsay isthay angechay ithway easureplay, anday ehay urnedtay ishay oughtsthay
owardstay ethay estbay ethodmay ofay eradicatingay ethay emainsray ofay myay elancholymay,
ichwhay everyay ownay anday enthay ouldway eturnray byay itsfay, anday ithway aay evouringday
acknessblay overcastay ethay approachingay unshinesay. Atay esethay omentsmay Iay ooktay
efugeray inay ethay ostmay erfectpay olitudesay. Iay assedpay olewhay aysday onay ethay akelay
aloneay inay aay ittlelay oatbay, atchingway ethay oudsclay anday isteninglay otay ethay
ipplingray ofay ethay avesway, ilentsay anday istlesslay. Utbay ethay eshfray airay anday
ightbray unsay eldomsay ailedfay otay estoreray emay otay omesay egreeday ofay omposurecay, anday
onay myay eturnray Iay etmay ethay alutationssay ofay myay iendsfray ithway aay eadierray ilesmay
anday aay oremay eerfulchay earthay.

Itay asway afteray myay eturnray omfray oneay ofay esethay amblesray atthay myay atherfay,
allingcay emay asideay, usthay addresseday emay,

I“ay amay appyhay otay emarkray, myay earday onsay, atthay ouyay avehay esumedray ouryay ormerfay
easuresplay anday eemsay otay ebay eturningray otay ourselfyay. Anday etyay ouyay areay illstay
unhappyay anday illstay avoiday ouray ocietysay. Orfay omesay imetay Iay asway ostlay inay
onjecturecay asay otay ethay ausecay ofay isthay, utbay esterdayyay anay ideaay uckstray emay,
anday ifay itay isay ellway oundedfay, Iay onjurecay ouyay otay avoway itay. Eserveray onay uchsay aay
ointpay ouldway ebay otnay onlyay uselessay, utbay awdray ownday ebletray iserymay onay usay allay.”

Iay embledtray iolentlyvay atay ishay exordiumay, anday myay atherfay ontinuedcay—

I“ay onfesscay, myay onsay, atthay Iay avehay alwaysay ookedlay orwardfay otay ouryay
arriagemay ithway ouray earday Elizabethay asay ethay ietay ofay ouray omesticday omfortcay anday ethay
aystay ofay myay ecliningday earsyay. Ouyay ereway attacheday otay eachay otheray omfray ouryay
earliestay infancyay; ouyay udiedstay ogethertay, anday appeareday, inay ispositionsday anday
astestay, entirelyay uitedsay otay oneay anotheray. Utbay osay indblay isay ethay experienceay ofay
anmay atthay atwhay Iay onceivedcay otay ebay ethay estbay assistantsay otay myay anplay aymay avehay
entirelyay estroyedday itay. Ouyay, erhapspay, egardray erhay asay ouryay istersay, ithoutway anyay
ishway atthay eshay ightmay ecomebay ouryay ifeway. Aynay, ouyay aymay avehay etmay ithway anotheray
omwhay ouyay aymay ovelay; anday onsideringcay ourselfyay asay oundbay inay onourhay otay
Elizabethay, isthay ugglestray aymay occasionay ethay oignantpay iserymay ichwhay ouyay appearay
otay eelfay.”

“myay earday atherfay, eassureray ourselfyay. Iay ovelay myay ousincay enderlytay anday
incerelysay. Iay evernay awsay anyay omanway owhay exciteday, asay Elizabethay oesday, myay
armestway admirationay anday affectionay. Myay uturefay opeshay anday ospectspray areay
entirelyay oundbay upay inay ethay expectationay ofay ouray unionay.”

e“thay expressionay ofay ouryay entimentssay ofay isthay ubjectsay, myay earday Ictorvay,
ivesgay emay oremay easureplay anthay Iay avehay orfay omesay imetay experienceday. Ifay ouyay
eelfay usthay, eway allshay assuredlyay ebay appyhay, oweverhay esentpray eventsay aymay astcay
aay oomglay overay usay. Utbay itay isay isthay oomglay ichwhay appearsay otay avehay akentay osay
ongstray aay oldhay ofay ouryay indmay atthay Iay ishway otay issipateday. Elltay emay,
ereforethay, etherwhay ouyay objectay otay anay immediateay olemnisationsay ofay ethay
arriagemay. Eway avehay eenbay unfortunateay, anday ecentray eventsay avehay awndray usay
omfray atthay everydayay anquillitytray efittingbay myay earsyay anday infirmitiesay. Ouyay
areay oungeryay; etyay Iay oday otnay upposesay, ossessedpay asay ouyay areay ofay aay ompetentcay
ortunefay, atthay anay earlyay arriagemay ouldway atay allay interfereay ithway anyay uturefay
ansplay ofay onourhay anday utilityay atthay ouyay aymay avehay ormedfay. Oday otnay upposesay,
oweverhay, atthay Iay ishway otay ictateday appinesshay otay ouyay oray atthay aay elayday onay
ouryay artpay ouldway ausecay emay anyay erioussay uneasinessay. Interpretay myay ordsway
ithway andourcay anday answeray emay, Iay onjurecay ouyay, ithway onfidencecay anday
inceritysay.”

Iay istenedlay otay myay atherfay inay ilencesay anday emainedray orfay omesay imetay incapableay
ofay offeringay anyay eplyray. Iay evolvedray apidlyray inay myay indmay aay ultitudemay ofay
oughtsthay anday endeavoureday otay arriveay atay omesay onclusioncay. Alasay! Otay emay
ethay ideaay ofay anay immediateay unionay ithway myay Elizabethay asway oneay ofay orrorhay anday
ismayday. Iay asway oundbay byay aay olemnsay omisepray ichwhay Iay adhay otnay etyay ulfilledfay
anday aredday otnay eakbray, oray ifay Iay idday, atwhay anifoldmay iseriesmay ightmay otnay
impenday overay emay anday myay evotedday amilyfay! Ouldcay Iay enteray intoay aay estivalfay
ithway isthay eadlyday eightway etyay anginghay oundray myay ecknay anday owingbay emay otay ethay
oundgray? Iay ustmay erformpay myay engagementay anday etlay ethay onstermay epartday ithway
ishay atemay eforebay Iay alloweday elfmysay otay enjoyay ethay elightday ofay aay unionay omfray
ichwhay Iay expecteday eacepay.

Iay ememberedray alsoay ethay ecessitynay imposeday uponay emay ofay eitheray ourneyingjay otay
Englanday oray enteringay intoay aay onglay orrespondencecay ithway osethay ilosophersphay
ofay atthay ountrycay osewhay owledgeknay anday iscoveriesday ereway ofay indispensableay
useay otay emay inay myay esentpray undertakingay. Ethay atterlay ethodmay ofay obtainingay
ethay esiredday intelligenceay asway ilatoryday anday unsatisfactoryay; esidesbay, Iay
adhay anay insurmountableay aversionay otay ethay ideaay ofay engagingay elfmysay inay myay
oathsomelay asktay inay myay ather’sfay ousehay ilewhay inay abitshay ofay amiliarfay
intercourseay ithway osethay Iay ovedlay. Iay ewknay atthay aay ousandthay earfulfay
accidentsay ightmay occuray, ethay ightestslay ofay ichwhay ouldway iscloseday aay aletay otay
illthray allay onnectedcay ithway emay ithway orrorhay. Iay asway awareay alsoay atthay Iay
ouldshay oftenay oselay allay elf-commandclay, allay apacitycay ofay idinghay ethay
arrowinghay ensationssay atthay ouldway ossesspay emay uringday ethay ogresspray ofay myay
unearthlyay occupationay. Iay ustmay absentay elfmysay omfray allay Iay ovedlay ilewhay usthay
employeday. Onceay ommencedcay, itay ouldway uicklyqay ebay achieveday, anday Iay ightmay ebay
estoredray otay myay amilyfay inay eacepay anday appinesshay. Myay omisepray ulfilledfay,
ethay onstermay ouldway epartday orfay everay. Oray o(say myay ondfay ancyfay imageday) omesay
accidentay ightmay eanwhilemay occuray otay estroyday imhay anday utpay anay enday otay myay
averyslay orfay everay.

Esethay eelingsfay ictatedday myay answeray otay myay atherfay. Iay expresseday aay ishway otay
isitvay Englanday, utbay oncealingcay ethay uetray easonsray ofay isthay equestray, Iay
othedclay myay esiresday underay aay uisegay ichwhay exciteday onay uspicionsay, ilewhay Iay
urgeday myay esireday ithway anay earnestnessay atthay easilyay induceday myay atherfay otay
omplycay. Afteray osay onglay aay eriodpay ofay anay absorbingay elancholymay atthay
esembledray adnessmay inay itsay intensityay anday effectsay, ehay asway adglay otay indfay
atthay Iay asway apablecay ofay akingtay easureplay inay ethay ideaay ofay uchsay aay ourneyjay,
anday ehay opedhay atthay angechay ofay enescay anday ariedvay amusementay ouldway, eforebay myay
eturnray, avehay estoredray emay entirelyay otay elfmysay.

Ethay urationday ofay myay absenceay asway eftlay otay myay ownay oicechay; aay ewfay onthsmay, oray
atay ostmay aay earyay, asway ethay eriodpay ontemplatedcay. Oneay aternalpay indkay
ecautionpray ehay adhay akentay otay ensureay myay avinghay aay ompanioncay. Ithoutway
eviouslypray ommunicatingcay ithway emay, ehay adhay, inay oncertcay ithway Elizabethay,
arrangeday atthay Ervalclay ouldshay oinjay emay atay Asburghstray. Isthay interfereday
ithway ethay olitudesay Iay ovetedcay orfay ethay osecutionpray ofay myay asktay; etyay atay ethay
ommencementcay ofay myay ourneyjay ethay esencepray ofay myay iendfray ouldcay inay onay ayway ebay
anay impedimentay, anday ulytray Iay ejoicedray atthay usthay Iay ouldshay ebay avedsay anymay
ourshay ofay onelylay, addeningmay eflectionray. Aynay, Enryhay ightmay andstay etweenbay
emay anday ethay intrusionay ofay myay oefay. Ifay Iay ereway aloneay, ouldway ehay otnay atay imestay
orcefay ishay abhorreday esencepray onay emay otay emindray emay ofay myay asktay oray otay
ontemplatecay itsay ogresspray?

Otay Englanday, ereforethay, Iay asway oundbay, anday itay asway understooday atthay myay unionay
ithway Elizabethay ouldshay aketay aceplay immediatelyay onay myay eturnray. Myay ather’sfay
ageay enderedray imhay extremelyay averseay otay elayday. Orfay elfmysay, erethay asway oneay
ewardray Iay omisedpray elfmysay omfray myay etestedday oils—onetay onsolationcay orfay myay
unparalleleday ufferingssay; itay asway ethay ospectpray ofay atthay ayday enwhay,
enfranchiseday omfray myay iserablemay averyslay, Iay ightmay aimclay Elizabethay anday
orgetfay ethay astpay inay myay unionay ithway erhay.

Iay ownay ademay arrangementsay orfay myay ourneyjay, utbay oneay eelingfay auntedhay emay
ichwhay illedfay emay ithway earfay anday agitationay. Uringday myay absenceay Iay ouldshay
eavelay myay iendsfray unconsciousay ofay ethay existenceay ofay eirthay enemyay anday
unprotecteday omfray ishay attacksay, exasperateday asay ehay ightmay ebay byay myay
epartureday. Utbay ehay adhay omisedpray otay ollowfay emay ereverwhay Iay ightmay ogay, anday
ouldway ehay otnay accompanyay emay otay Englanday? Isthay imaginationay asway eadfuldray inay
itselfay, utbay oothingsay inasmuchay asay itay upposedsay ethay afetysay ofay myay iendsfray.
Iay asway agoniseday ithway ethay ideaay ofay ethay ossibilitypay atthay ethay everseray ofay
isthay ightmay appenhay. Utbay oughthray ethay olewhay eriodpay uringday ichwhay Iay asway ethay
aveslay ofay myay eaturecray Iay alloweday elfmysay otay ebay overnedgay byay ethay impulsesay ofay
ethay omentmay; anday myay esentpray ensationssay onglystray intimateday atthay ethay iendfay
ouldway ollowfay emay anday exemptay myay amilyfay omfray ethay angerday ofay ishay
achinationsmay.

Itay asway inay ethay atterlay enday ofay Eptembersay atthay Iay againay uittedqay myay ativenay
ountrycay. Myay ourneyjay adhay eenbay myay ownay uggestionsay, anday Elizabethay
ereforethay acquiesceday, utbay eshay asway illedfay ithway isquietday atay ethay ideaay ofay
myay ufferingsay, awayay omfray erhay, ethay inroadsay ofay iserymay anday iefgray. Itay adhay
eenbay erhay arecay ichwhay ovidedpray emay aay ompanioncay inay Erval—andclay etyay aay anmay
isay indblay otay aay ousandthay inutemay ircumstancescay ichwhay allcay orthfay aay oman’sway
eduloussay attentionay. Eshay ongedlay otay idbay emay astenhay myay eturnray; aay ousandthay
onflictingcay emotionsay enderedray erhay utemay asay eshay adebay emay aay earfultay, ilentsay
arewellfay.

Iay ewthray elfmysay intoay ethay arriagecay atthay asway otay onveycay emay awayay, ardlyhay
owingknay itherwhay Iay asway oinggay, anday arelesscay ofay atwhay asway assingpay arounday.
Iay ememberedray onlyay, anday itay asway ithway aay itterbay anguishay atthay Iay eflectedray onay
itay, otay orderay atthay myay emicalchay instrumentsay ouldshay ebay ackedpay otay ogay ithway
emay. Illedfay ithway earydray imaginationsay, Iay assedpay oughthray anymay eautifulbay
anday ajesticmay enesscay, utbay myay eyesay ereway ixedfay anday unobservingay. Iay ouldcay
onlyay inkthay ofay ethay ournebay ofay myay avelstray anday ethay orkway ichwhay asway otay occupyay
emay ilstwhay eythay endureday.

Afteray omesay aysday entspay inay istlesslay indolenceay, uringday ichwhay Iay aversedtray
anymay eagueslay, Iay arriveday atay Asburghstray, erewhay Iay aitedway otway aysday orfay
Ervalclay. Ehay amecay. Alasay, owhay eatgray asway ethay ontrastcay etweenbay usay! Ehay
asway aliveay otay everyay ewnay enescay, oyfuljay enwhay ehay awsay ethay eautiesbay ofay ethay
ettingsay unsay, anday oremay appyhay enwhay ehay eheldbay itay iseray anday ecommenceray aay ewnay
ayday. Ehay ointedpay outay otay emay ethay iftingshay olourscay ofay ethay andscapelay anday
ethay appearancesay ofay ethay skyay. is“thay isay atwhay itay isay otay ivelay,” ehay iedcray;
ow“nay Iay enjoyay existenceay! Utbay ouyay, myay earday Ankensteinfray, ereforewhay areay
ouyay espondingday anday orrowfulsay!” Inay uthtray, Iay asway occupieday byay oomyglay
oughtsthay anday eithernay awsay ethay escentday ofay ethay eveningay arstay ornay ethay oldengay
unrisesay eflectedray inay ethay Inerhay. Anday ouyay, myay iendfray, ouldway ebay arfay oremay
amuseday ithway ethay ournaljay ofay Ervalclay, owhay observeday ethay eneryscay ithway anay
eyeay ofay eelingfay anday elightday, anthay inay isteninglay otay myay eflectionsray. Iay, aay
iserablemay etchwray, auntedhay byay aay ursecay atthay utshay upay everyay avenueay otay
enjoymentay.

Eway adhay agreeday otay escendday ethay Inerhay inay aay oatbay omfray Asburghstray otay
Otterdamray, encewhay eway ightmay aketay ippingshay orfay Ondonlay. Uringday isthay
oyagevay eway assedpay anymay illowyway islandsay anday awsay everalsay eautifulbay ownstay.
Eway ayedstay aay ayday atay Annheimmay, anday onay ethay ifthfay omfray ouray epartureday omfray
Asburghstray, arriveday atay Ainzmay. Ethay oursecay ofay ethay Inerhay elowbay Ainzmay
ecomesbay uchmay oremay icturesquepay. Ethay iverray escendsday apidlyray anday indsway
etweenbay illshay, otnay ighhay, utbay eepstay, anday ofay eautifulbay ormsfay. Eway awsay
anymay uinedray astlescay andingstay onay ethay edgesay ofay ecipicespray, urroundedsay byay
ackblay oodsway, ighhay anday inaccessibleay. Isthay artpay ofay ethay Inerhay, indeeday,
esentspray aay ingularlysay ariegatedvay andscapelay. Inay oneay otspay ouyay iewvay
uggedray illshay, uinedray astlescay overlookingay emendoustray ecipicespray, ithway
ethay arkday Inerhay ushingray eneathbay; anday onay ethay uddensay urntay ofay aay omontorypray,
ourishingflay ineyardsvay ithway eengray opingslay anksbay anday aay eanderingmay iverray
anday opulouspay ownstay occupyay ethay enescay.

Eway avelledtray atay ethay imetay ofay ethay intagevay anday eardhay ethay ongsay ofay ethay abourerslay
asay eway idedglay ownday ethay eamstray. Evenay Iay, epressedday inay indmay, anday myay iritsspay
ontinuallycay agitateday byay oomyglay eelingsfay, evenay Iay asway easedplay. Iay aylay atay ethay
ottombay ofay ethay oatbay, anday asay Iay azedgay onay ethay oudlessclay ueblay skyay, Iay eemedsay otay
inkdray inay aay anquillitytray otay ichwhay Iay adhay onglay eenbay aay angerstray. Anday ifay esethay
ereway myay ensationssay, owhay ancay escribeday osethay ofay Enryhay? Ehay eltfay asay ifay ehay adhay
eenbay ansportedtray otay airy-landclay anday enjoyeday aay appinesshay eldomsay astedtay byay
anmay. I“ay avehay eensay,” ehay aidsay, e“thay ostmay eautifulbay enesscay
ofay myay ownay ountrycay; Iay avehay isitedvay ethay akeslay ofay Ucernelay anday Uriay, erewhay ethay
owysnay ountainsmay escendday almostay erpendicularlypay otay ethay aterway, astingcay ackblay
anday impenetrableay adesshay, ichwhay ouldway ausecay aay oomyglay anday ournfulmay appearanceay
ereway itay otnay orfay ethay ostmay erdantvay islandsay atthay elieveray ethay eyeay byay eirthay aygay
appearanceay; Iay avehay eensay isthay akelay agitateday byay aay empesttay, enwhay ethay indway oretay
upay irlwindswhay ofay aterway anday avegay ouyay anay ideaay ofay atwhay ethay ater-spoutclay ustmay ebay
onay ethay eatgray oceanay; anday ethay avesway ashday ithway uryfay ethay asebay ofay ethay ountainmay,
erewhay ethay iestpray anday ishay istressmay ereway overwhelmeday byay anay avalancheay anday
erewhay eirthay ingdyay oicesvay areay illstay aidsay otay ebay eardhay amiday ethay ausespay ofay ethay
ightlynay indway; Iay avehay eensay ethay ountainsmay ofay Alay Alaisvay, anday ethay Ayspay eday Audvay;
utbay isthay ountrycay, Ictorvay, easesplay emay oremay anthay allay osethay ondersway. Ethay
ountainsmay ofay Itzerlandsway areay oremay ajesticmay anday angestray, utbay erethay isay aay
armchay inay ethay anksbay ofay isthay ivineday iverray atthay Iay evernay eforebay awsay equalleday.
Ooklay atay atthay astlecay ichwhay overhangsay onyay ecipicepray; anday atthay alsoay onay ethay
islanday, almostay oncealedcay amongstay ethay oliagefay ofay osethay ovelylay eestray; anday ownay
atthay oupgray ofay abourerslay omingcay omfray amongay eirthay inesvay; anday atthay illagevay
alfhay idhay inay ethay ecessray ofay ethay ountainmay. Ohay, urelysay ethay iritspay atthay inhabitsay
anday uardsgay isthay aceplay ashay aay oulsay oremay inay armonyhay ithway anmay anthay osethay owhay
ilepay ethay acierglay oray etireray otay ethay inaccessibleay eakspay ofay ethay ountainsmay ofay
ouray ownay ountrycay.”

Ervalclay! Elovedbay iendfray! Evenay ownay itay elightsday emay otay ecordray ouryay ordsway anday
otay elldway onay ethay aisepray ofay ichwhay ouyay areay osay eminentlyay eservingday. Ehay asway aay
eingbay ormedfay inay ethay ery“vay oetrypay ofay aturenay.” Ishay ildway anday
enthusiasticay imaginationay asway astenedchay byay ethay ensibilitysay ofay ishay earthay. Ishay
oulsay overfloweday ithway ardentay affectionsay, anday ishay iendshipfray asway ofay atthay
evotedday anday ondrousway aturenay atthay ethay orldly-mindedclay eachtay usay otay ooklay orfay onlyay
inay ethay imaginationay. Utbay evenay umanhay athiessympay ereway otnay ufficientsay otay
atisfysay ishay eageray indmay. Ethay eneryscay ofay externalay aturenay, ichwhay othersay egardray
onlyay ithway admirationay, ehay ovedlay ithway ardouray:—

e——thay oundingsay ataractcay
Auntedhay imhay ikelay aay assionpay: ethay alltay ockray,
Ethay ountainmay, anday ethay eepday anday oomyglay oodway,
Eirthay olourscay anday eirthay ormsfay, ereway enthay otay imhay
Anay appetiteay; aay eelingfay, anday aay ovelay,
Atthay adhay onay eednay ofay aay emoterray armchay,
Byay oughtthay uppliedsay, oray anyay interestay
Unborrow’day omfray ethay eyeay.

ordsworth’s[way intern“tay Abbeyay”.]

Anday erewhay oesday ehay ownay existay? Isay isthay entlegay anday ovelylay eingbay ostlay
orfay everay? Ashay isthay indmay, osay epleteray ithway ideasay, imaginationsay ancifulfay
anday agnificentmay, ichwhay ormedfay aay orldway, osewhay existenceay ependedday onay ethay
ifelay ofay itsay eator;—hascray isthay indmay erishedpay? Oesday itay ownay onlyay existay
inay myay emorymay? Onay, itay isay otnay usthay; ouryay ormfay osay ivinelyday oughtwray, anday
eamingbay ithway eautybay, ashay ecayedday, utbay ouryay iritspay illstay isitsvay anday
onsolescay ouryay unhappyay iendfray.

Ardonpay isthay ushgay ofay orrowsay; esethay ineffectualay ordsway areay utbay aay ightslay
ibutetray otay ethay unexampleday orthway ofay Enryhay, utbay eythay oothesay myay earthay,
overflowingay ithway ethay anguishay ichwhay ishay emembranceray eatescray. Iay illway
oceedpray ithway myay aletay.

Eyondbay Olognecay eway escendedday otay ethay ainsplay ofay Ollandhay; anday eway esolvedray otay
ostpay ethay emainderray ofay ouray ayway, orfay ethay indway asway ontrarycay anday ethay eamstray ofay
ethay iverray asway ootay entlegay otay aiday usay.

Ouray ourneyjay erehay ostlay ethay interestay arisingay omfray eautifulbay eneryscay, utbay eway
arriveday inay aay ewfay aysday atay Otterdamray, encewhay eway oceededpray byay easay otay Englanday.
Itay asway onay aay earclay orningmay, inay ethay atterlay aysday ofay Ecemberday, atthay Iay irstfay awsay
ethay itewhay iffsclay ofay Itainbray. Ethay anksbay ofay ethay Amesthay esentedpray aay ewnay enescay;
eythay ereway atflay utbay ertilefay, anday almostay everyay owntay asway arkedmay byay ethay
emembranceray ofay omesay orystay. Eway awsay Ilburytay Ortfay anday ememberedray ethay Anishspay
Armadaay, Avesendgray, Oolwichway, anday Eenwich—placesgray ichwhay Iay adhay eardhay
ofay evenay inay myay ountrycay.

Atay engthlay eway awsay ethay umerousnay eeplesstay ofay Ondonlay, Stay. Aul’spay oweringtay
aboveay allay, anday ethay Owertay amedfay inay Englishay istoryhay.




Apterchay 19ay


Ondonlay asway ouray esentpray ointpay ofay estray; eway eterminedday otay emainray everalsay
onthsmay inay isthay onderfulway anday elebratedcay itycay. Ervalclay esiredday ethay
intercourseay ofay ethay enmay ofay eniusgay anday alenttay owhay ourishedflay atay isthay
imetay, utbay isthay asway ithway emay aay econdarysay objectay; Iay asway incipallypray
occupieday ithway ethay eansmay ofay obtainingay ethay informationay ecessarynay orfay ethay
ompletioncay ofay myay omisepray anday uicklyqay availeday elfmysay ofay ethay etterslay ofay
introductionay atthay Iay adhay oughtbray ithway emay, addresseday otay ethay ostmay
istinguishedday aturalnay ilosophersphay.

Ifay isthay ourneyjay adhay akentay aceplay uringday myay aysday ofay udystay anday appinesshay,
itay ouldway avehay affordeday emay inexpressibleay easureplay. Utbay aay ightblay adhay
omecay overay myay existenceay, anday Iay onlyay isitedvay esethay eoplepay orfay ethay akesay ofay
ethay informationay eythay ightmay ivegay emay onay ethay ubjectsay inay ichwhay myay interestay
asway osay erriblytay ofoundpray. Ompanycay asway irksomeay otay emay; enwhay aloneay, Iay
ouldcay illfay myay indmay ithway ethay ightssay ofay eavenhay anday earthay; ethay oicevay ofay
Enryhay oothedsay emay, anday Iay ouldcay usthay eatchay elfmysay intoay aay ansitorytray
eacepay. Utbay usybay, uninterestingay, oyousjay acesfay oughtbray ackbay espairday otay
myay earthay. Iay awsay anay insurmountableay arrierbay acedplay etweenbay emay anday myay
ellowfay enmay; isthay arrierbay asway ealedsay ithway ethay oodblay ofay Illiamway anday
Ustinejay, anday otay eflectray onay ethay eventsay onnectedcay ithway osethay amesnay illedfay
myay oulsay ithway anguishay.

Utbay inay Ervalclay Iay awsay ethay imageay ofay myay ormerfay elfsay; ehay asway inquisitiveay
anday anxiousay otay aingay experienceay anday instructionay. Ethay ifferenceday ofay
annersmay ichwhay ehay observeday asway otay imhay anay inexhaustibleay ourcesay ofay
instructionay anday amusementay. Ehay asway alsoay ursuingpay anay objectay ehay adhay onglay
adhay inay iewvay. Ishay esignday asway otay isitvay Indiaay, inay ethay eliefbay atthay ehay adhay
inay ishay owledgeknay ofay itsay ariousvay anguageslay, anday inay ethay iewsvay ehay adhay
akentay ofay itsay ocietysay, ethay eansmay ofay ateriallymay assistingay ethay ogresspray ofay
Europeanay olonizationcay anday adetray. Inay Itainbray onlyay ouldcay ehay urtherfay ethay
executionay ofay ishay anplay. Ehay asway orfay everay usybay, anday ethay onlyay eckchay otay ishay
enjoymentsay asway myay orrowfulsay anday ejectedday indmay. Iay iedtray otay oncealcay isthay
asay uchmay asay ossiblepay, atthay Iay ightmay otnay ebarday imhay omfray ethay easuresplay
aturalnay otay oneay owhay asway enteringay onay aay ewnay enescay ofay ifelay, undisturbeday byay
anyay arecay oray itterbay ecollectionray. Iay oftenay efusedray otay accompanyay imhay,
allegingay anotheray engagementay, atthay Iay ightmay emainray aloneay. Iay ownay alsoay
eganbay otay ollectcay ethay aterialsmay ecessarynay orfay myay ewnay eationcray, anday isthay
asway otay emay ikelay ethay orturetay ofay inglesay opsdray ofay aterway ontinuallycay allingfay
onay ethay eadhay. Everyay oughtthay atthay asway evotedday otay itay asway anay extremeay
anguishay, anday everyay ordway atthay Iay okespay inay allusionay otay itay ausedcay myay ipslay
otay uiverqay, anday myay earthay otay alpitatepay.

Afteray assingpay omesay onthsmay inay Ondonlay, eway eceivedray aay etterlay omfray aay ersonpay inay
Otlandscay owhay adhay ormerlyfay eenbay ouray isitorvay atay Enevagay. Ehay entionedmay ethay
eautiesbay ofay ishay ativenay ountrycay anday askeday usay ifay osethay ereway otnay ufficientsay
allurementsay otay induceay usay otay olongpray ouray ourneyjay asay arfay orthnay asay Erthpay,
erewhay ehay esidedray. Ervalclay eagerlyay esiredday otay acceptay isthay invitationay, anday Iay,
althoughay Iay abhorreday ocietysay, ishedway otay iewvay againay ountainsmay anday eamsstray anday
allay ethay ondrousway orksway ithway ichwhay Aturenay adornsay erhay osenchay elling-placesclay.

Eway adhay arriveday inay Englanday atay ethay eginningbay ofay Octoberay, anday itay asway ownay
Ebruaryfay. Eway accordinglyay eterminedday otay ommencecay ouray ourneyjay owardstay ethay
orthnay atay ethay expirationay ofay anotheray onthmay. Inay isthay expeditionay eway idday otnay
intenday otay ollowfay ethay eatgray oadray otay Edinburghay, utbay otay isitvay Indsorway, Oxforday,
Atlockmay, anday ethay Umberlandcay akeslay, esolvingray otay arriveay atay ethay ompletioncay ofay
isthay ourtay aboutay ethay enday ofay Ulyjay. Iay ackedpay upay myay emicalchay instrumentsay anday
ethay aterialsmay Iay adhay ollectedcay, esolvingray otay inishfay myay abourslay inay omesay
obscureay ooknay inay ethay orthernnay ighlandshay ofay Otlandscay.

Eway uittedqay Ondonlay onay ethay 27thay ofay Archmay anday emainedray aay ewfay aysday atay
Indsorway, amblingray inay itsay eautifulbay orestfay. Isthay asway aay ewnay enescay otay usay
ountaineersmay; ethay ajesticmay oaksay, ethay uantityqay ofay amegay, anday ethay erdshay ofay
atelystay eerday ereway allay oveltiesnay otay usay.

Omfray encethay eway oceededpray otay Oxforday. Asay eway entereday isthay itycay, ouray indsmay
ereway illedfay ithway ethay emembranceray ofay ethay eventsay atthay adhay eenbay ansactedtray
erethay oremay anthay aay enturycay anday aay alfhay eforebay. Itay asway erehay atthay Arleschay
Iay. adhay ollectedcay ishay orcesfay. Isthay itycay adhay emainedray aithfulfay otay imhay,
afteray ethay olewhay ationnay adhay orsakenfay ishay ausecay otay oinjay ethay andardstay ofay
Arliamentpay anday ibertylay. Ethay emorymay ofay atthay unfortunateay ingkay anday ishay
ompanionscay, ethay amiableay Alklandfay, ethay insolentay Oringgay, ishay ueenqay, anday
onsay, avegay aay eculiarpay interestay otay everyay artpay ofay ethay itycay ichwhay eythay
ightmay ebay upposedsay otay avehay inhabiteday. Ethay iritspay ofay elderay aysday oundfay aay
ellingdway erehay, anday eway elightedday otay acetray itsay ootstepsfay. Ifay esethay
eelingsfay adhay otnay oundfay anay imaginaryay atificationgray, ethay appearanceay ofay
ethay itycay adhay etyay inay itselfay ufficientsay eautybay otay obtainay ouray admirationay.
Ethay ollegescay areay ancientay anday icturesquepay; ethay eetsstray areay almostay
agnificentmay; anday ethay ovelylay Isisay, ichwhay owsflay esidebay itay oughthray eadowsmay
ofay exquisiteay erdurevay, isay eadspray orthfay intoay aay acidplay expanseay ofay atersway,
ichwhay eflectsray itsay ajesticmay assemblageay ofay owerstay, anday iresspay, anday
omesday, embosomeday amongay ageday eestray.

Iay enjoyeday isthay enescay, anday etyay myay enjoymentay asway embittereday othbay byay ethay
emorymay ofay ethay astpay anday ethay anticipationay ofay ethay uturefay. Iay asway ormedfay
orfay eacefulpay appinesshay. Uringday myay outhfulyay aysday iscontentday evernay
isitedvay myay indmay, anday ifay Iay asway everay overcomeay byay ennui_ay_, ethay ightsay ofay atwhay
isay eautifulbay inay aturenay oray ethay udystay ofay atwhay isay excellentay anday ublimesay inay
ethay oductionspray ofay anmay ouldcay alwaysay interestay myay earthay anday ommunicatecay
elasticityay otay myay iritsspay. Utbay Iay amay aay astedblay eetray; ethay oltbay ashay
entereday myay oulsay; anday Iay eltfay enthay atthay Iay ouldshay urvivesay otay exhibitay atwhay
Iay allshay oonsay easecay otay e—abay iserablemay ectaclespay ofay eckedwray umanityhay,
itiablepay otay othersay anday intolerableay otay elfmysay.

Eway assedpay aay onsiderablecay eriodpay atay Oxforday, amblingray amongay itsay environsay
anday endeavouringay otay identifyay everyay otspay ichwhay ightmay elateray otay ethay ostmay
animatingay epochay ofay Englishay istoryhay. Ouray ittlelay oyagesvay ofay iscoveryday
ereway oftenay olongedpray byay ethay uccessivesay objectsay atthay esentedpray
emselvesthay. Eway isitedvay ethay ombtay ofay ethay illustriousay Ampdenhay anday ethay
ieldfay onay ichwhay atthay atriotpay ellfay. Orfay aay omentmay myay oulsay asway elevateday
omfray itsay ebasingday anday iserablemay earsfay otay ontemplatecay ethay ivineday ideasay
ofay ibertylay anday elf-sacrificeclay ofay ichwhay esethay ightssay ereway ethay onumentsmay
anday ethay emembrancersray. Orfay anay instantay Iay aredday otay akeshay offay myay ainschay
anday ooklay arounday emay ithway aay eefray anday oftylay iritspay, utbay ethay ironay adhay eatenay
intoay myay eshflay, anday Iay anksay againay, emblingtray anday opelesshay, intoay myay
iserablemay elfsay.

Eway eftlay Oxforday ithway egretray anday oceededpray otay Atlockmay, ichwhay asway ouray extnay
aceplay ofay estray. Ethay ountrycay inay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofay isthay illagevay
esembledray, otay aay eatergray egreeday, ethay eneryscay ofay Itzerlandsway; utbay
everythingay isay onay aay owerlay alescay, anday ethay eengray illshay antway ethay owncray ofay
istantday itewhay Alpsay ichwhay alwaysay attenday onay ethay inypay ountainsmay ofay myay
ativenay ountrycay. Eway isitedvay ethay ondrousway avecay anday ethay ittlelay abinetscay
ofay aturalnay istoryhay, erewhay ethay uriositiescay areay isposedday inay ethay amesay
annermay asay inay ethay ollectionscay atay Ervoxsay anday Amounixchay. Ethay atterlay amenay
ademay emay embletray enwhay onouncedpray byay Enryhay, anday Iay astenedhay otay uitqay
Atlockmay, ithway ichwhay atthay erribletay enescay asway usthay associateday.

Omfray Erbyday, illstay ourneyingjay orthwardsnay, eway assedpay otway onthsmay inay
Umberlandcay anday Estmorlandway. Iay ouldcay ownay almostay ancyfay elfmysay amongay ethay
Isssway ountainsmay. Ethay ittlelay atchespay ofay owsnay ichwhay etyay ingeredlay onay ethay
orthernnay idessay ofay ethay ountainsmay, ethay akeslay, anday ethay ashingday ofay ethay
ockyray eamsstray ereway allay amiliarfay anday earday ightssay otay emay. Erehay alsoay eway
ademay omesay acquaintancesay, owhay almostay ontrivedcay otay eatchay emay intoay
appinesshay. Ethay elightday ofay Ervalclay asway oportionablypray eatergray anthay
inemay; ishay indmay expandeday inay ethay ompanycay ofay enmay ofay alenttay, anday ehay oundfay
inay ishay ownay aturenay eatergray apacitiescay anday esourcesray anthay ehay ouldcay avehay
imagineday imselfhay otay avehay ossessedpay ilewhay ehay associateday ithway ishay
inferiorsay. I“ay ouldcay asspay myay ifelay erehay,” aidsay ehay otay emay; and“ay amongay
esethay ountainsmay Iay ouldshay arcelyscay egretray Itzerlandsway anday ethay Inerhay.”

Utbay ehay oundfay atthay aay aveller’stray ifelay isay oneay atthay includesay uchmay ainpay
amidstay itsay enjoymentsay. Ishay eelingsfay areay orfay everay onay ethay etchstray; anday
enwhay ehay eginsbay otay inksay intoay eposeray, ehay indsfay imselfhay obligeday otay uitqay
atthay onay ichwhay ehay estsray inay easureplay orfay omethingsay ewnay, ichwhay againay
engagesay ishay attentionay, anday ichwhay alsoay ehay orsakesfay orfay otheray oveltiesnay.

Eway adhay arcelyscay isitedvay ethay ariousvay akeslay ofay Umberlandcay anday Estmorlandway
anday onceivedcay anay affectionay orfay omesay ofay ethay inhabitantsay enwhay ethay eriodpay
ofay ouray appointmentay ithway ouray Otchscay iendfray approacheday, anday eway eftlay emthay
otay aveltray onay. Orfay myay ownay artpay Iay asway otnay orrysay. Iay adhay ownay eglectednay myay
omisepray orfay omesay imetay, anday Iay earedfay ethay effectsay ofay ethay on’sdæmay
isappointmentday. Ehay ightmay emainray inay Itzerlandsway anday eakwray ishay engeancevay
onay myay elativesray. Isthay ideaay ursuedpay emay anday ormentedtay emay atay everyay omentmay
omfray ichwhay Iay ightmay otherwiseay avehay atchedsnay eposeray anday eacepay. Iay aitedway
orfay myay etterslay ithway everishfay impatienceay; ifay eythay ereway elayedday Iay asway
iserablemay anday overcomeay byay aay ousandthay earsfay; anday enwhay eythay arriveday anday Iay
