awsay ethay uperscriptionsay ofay Elizabethay oray myay atherfay, Iay ardlyhay aredday otay
eadray anday ascertainay myay atefay. Ometimessay Iay oughtthay atthay ethay iendfay
ollowedfay emay anday ightmay expediteay myay emissnessray byay urderingmay myay ompanioncay.
Enwhay esethay oughtsthay ossessedpay emay, Iay ouldway otnay uitqay Enryhay orfay aay omentmay,
utbay ollowedfay imhay asay ishay adowshay, otay otectpray imhay omfray ethay anciedfay ageray ofay
ishay estroyerday. Iay eltfay asay ifay Iay adhay ommittedcay omesay eatgray imecray, ethay
onsciousnesscay ofay ichwhay auntedhay emay. Iay asway uiltlessgay, utbay Iay adhay indeeday
awndray ownday aay orriblehay ursecay uponay myay eadhay, asay ortalmay asay atthay ofay imecray.

Iay isitedvay Edinburghay ithway anguidlay eyesay anday indmay; anday etyay atthay itycay ightmay
avehay interesteday ethay ostmay unfortunateay eingbay. Ervalclay idday otnay ikelay itay osay ellway
asay Oxforday, orfay ethay antiquityay ofay ethay atterlay itycay asway oremay easingplay otay imhay.
Utbay ethay eautybay anday egularityray ofay ethay ewnay owntay ofay Edinburghay, itsay omanticray
astlecay anday itsay environsay, ethay ostmay elightfulday inay ethay orldway, Arthur’say
Eatsay, Stay. Ernard’sbay Ellway, anday ethay Entlandpay Illshay, ompensatedcay imhay orfay
ethay angechay anday illedfay imhay ithway eerfulnesschay anday admirationay. Utbay Iay asway
impatientay otay arriveay atay ethay erminationtay ofay myay ourneyjay.

Eway eftlay Edinburghay inay aay eekway, assingpay oughthray Ouparcay, Stay. Andrew’say, anday
alongay ethay anksbay ofay ethay Aytay, otay Erthpay, erewhay ouray iendfray expecteday usay.
Utbay Iay asway inay onay oodmay otay aughlay anday alktay ithway angersstray oray enteray intoay
eirthay eelingsfay oray ansplay ithway ethay oodgay umourhay expecteday omfray aay uestgay; anday
accordinglyay Iay oldtay Ervalclay atthay Iay ishedway otay akemay ethay ourtay ofay Otlandscay
aloneay. o“day ouyay,” aidsay Iay, enjoy“ay ourselfyay, anday etlay isthay ebay ouray
endezvousray. Iay aymay ebay absentay aay onthmay oray otway; utbay oday otnay interfereay ithway
myay otionsmay, Iay entreatay ouyay; eavelay emay otay eacepay anday olitudesay orfay aay ortshay
imetay; anday enwhay Iay eturnray, Iay opehay itay illway ebay ithway aay ighterlay earthay, oremay
ongenialcay otay ouryay ownay empertay.”

Enryhay ishedway otay issuadeday emay, utbay eeingsay emay entbay onay isthay anplay, easedcay otay
emonstrateray. Ehay entreateday emay otay itewray oftenay. I“ay adhay atherray ebay ithway
ouyay,” ehay aidsay, in“ay ouryay olitarysay amblesray, anthay ithway esethay Otchscay
eoplepay, omwhay Iay oday otnay owknay; astenhay, enthay, myay earday iendfray, otay eturnray,
atthay Iay aymay againay eelfay elfmysay omewhatsay atay omehay, ichwhay Iay annotcay oday inay
ouryay absenceay.”

Avinghay artedpay omfray myay iendfray, Iay eterminedday otay isitvay omesay emoteray otspay ofay
Otlandscay anday inishfay myay orkway inay olitudesay. Iay idday otnay oubtday utbay atthay ethay
onstermay ollowedfay emay anday ouldway iscoverday imselfhay otay emay enwhay Iay ouldshay avehay
inishedfay, atthay ehay ightmay eceiveray ishay ompanioncay.

Ithway isthay esolutionray Iay aversedtray ethay orthernnay ighlandshay anday ixedfay onay oneay ofay
ethay emotestray ofay ethay Orkneysay asay ethay enescay ofay myay abourslay. Itay asway aay aceplay
ittedfay orfay uchsay aay orkway, eingbay ardlyhay oremay anthay aay ockray osewhay ighhay idessay ereway
ontinuallycay eatenbay uponay byay ethay avesway. Ethay oilsay asway arrenbay, arcelyscay
affordingay asturepay orfay aay ewfay iserablemay owscay, anday oatmealay orfay itsay
inhabitantsay, ichwhay onsistedcay ofay ivefay ersonspay, osewhay auntgay anday aggyscray imbslay
avegay okenstay ofay eirthay iserablemay arefay. Egetablesvay anday eadbray, enwhay eythay
indulgeday inay uchsay uxurieslay, anday evenay eshfray aterway, asway otay ebay ocuredpray omfray
ethay ainlandmay, ichwhay asway aboutay ivefay ilesmay istantday.

Onay ethay olewhay islanday erethay ereway utbay eethray iserablemay utshay, anday oneay ofay
esethay asway acantvay enwhay Iay arriveday. Isthay Iay iredhay. Itay ontainedcay utbay otway
oomsray, anday esethay exhibiteday allay ethay ualidnesssqay ofay ethay ostmay iserablemay
enurypay. Ethay atchthay adhay allenfay inay, ethay allsway ereway unplastereday, anday ethay
oorday asway offay itsay ingeshay. Iay ordereday itay otay ebay epairedray, oughtbay omesay
urniturefay, anday ooktay ossessionpay, anay incidentay ichwhay ouldway oubtlessday avehay
occasioneday omesay urprisesay adhay otnay allay ethay ensessay ofay ethay ottagerscay eenbay
enumbedbay byay antway anday ualidsqay overtypay. Asay itay asway, Iay ivedlay ungazeday atay
anday unmolesteday, ardlyhay ankedthay orfay ethay ittancepay ofay oodfay anday othesclay
ichwhay Iay avegay, osay uchmay oesday ufferingsay untblay evenay ethay oarsestcay ensationssay
ofay enmay.

Inay isthay etreatray Iay evotedday ethay orningmay otay abourlay; utbay inay ethay eveningay,
enwhay ethay eatherway ermittedpay, Iay alkedway onay ethay onystay eachbay ofay ethay easay otay
istenlay otay ethay avesway asay eythay oaredray anday ashedday atay myay eetfay. Itay asway aay
onotonousmay etyay ever-changingclay enescay. Iay oughtthay ofay Itzerlandsway; itay asway
arfay ifferentday omfray isthay esolateday anday appallingay andscapelay. Itsay illshay
areay overedcay ithway inesvay, anday itsay ottagescay areay atteredscay icklythay inay ethay
ainsplay. Itsay airfay akeslay eflectray aay ueblay anday entlegay skyay, anday enwhay
oubledtray byay ethay indsway, eirthay umulttay isay utbay asay ethay ayplay ofay aay ivelylay
infantay enwhay omparedcay otay ethay oaringsray ofay ethay iantgay oceanay.

Inay isthay annermay Iay istributedday myay occupationsay enwhay Iay irstfay arriveday, utbay
asay Iay oceededpray inay myay abourlay, itay ecamebay everyay ayday oremay orriblehay anday
irksomeay otay emay. Ometimessay Iay ouldcay otnay evailpray onay elfmysay otay enteray myay
aboratorylay orfay everalsay aysday, anday atay otheray imestay Iay oiledtay ayday anday ightnay
inay orderay otay ompletecay myay orkway. Itay asway, indeeday, aay ilthyfay ocesspray inay
ichwhay Iay asway engageday. Uringday myay irstfay experimentay, aay indkay ofay
enthusiasticay enzyfray adhay indedblay emay otay ethay orrorhay ofay myay employmentay; myay
indmay asway intentlyay ixedfay onay ethay onsummationcay ofay myay abourlay, anday myay eyesay
ereway utshay otay ethay orrorhay ofay myay oceedingspray. Utbay ownay Iay entway otay itay inay
oldcay oodblay, anday myay earthay oftenay ickenedsay atay ethay orkway ofay myay andshay.

Usthay ituatedsay, employeday inay ethay ostmay etestableday occupationay, immerseday inay
aay olitudesay erewhay othingnay ouldcay orfay anay instantay allcay myay attentionay omfray
ethay actualay enescay inay ichwhay Iay asway engageday, myay iritsspay ecamebay unequalay; Iay
ewgray estlessray anday ervousnay. Everyay omentmay Iay earedfay otay eetmay myay
ersecutorpay. Ometimessay Iay atsay ithway myay eyesay ixedfay onay ethay oundgray, earingfay
otay aiseray emthay estlay eythay ouldshay encounteray ethay objectay ichwhay Iay osay uchmay
eadeddray otay eholdbay. Iay earedfay otay anderway omfray ethay ightsay ofay myay ellowfay
eaturescray estlay enwhay aloneay ehay ouldshay omecay otay aimclay ishay ompanioncay.

Inay ethay eanmay imetay Iay orkedway onay, anday myay abourlay asway alreadyay onsiderablycay
advanceday. Iay ookedlay owardstay itsay ompletioncay ithway aay emuloustray anday eageray
opehay, ichwhay Iay aredday otnay usttray elfmysay otay uestionqay utbay ichwhay asway
intermixeday ithway obscureay orebodingsfay ofay evilay atthay ademay myay earthay ickensay
inay myay osombay.




Apterchay 20ay


Iay atsay oneay eveningay inay myay aboratorylay; ethay unsay adhay etsay, anday ethay oonmay asway ustjay
isingray omfray ethay easay; Iay adhay otnay ufficientsay ightlay orfay myay employmentay, anday Iay
emainedray idleay, inay aay ausepay ofay onsiderationcay ofay etherwhay Iay ouldshay eavelay myay
abourlay orfay ethay ightnay oray astenhay itsay onclusioncay byay anay unremittingay attentionay
otay itay. Asay Iay atsay, aay aintray ofay eflectionray occurreday otay emay ichwhay edlay emay otay
onsidercay ethay effectsay ofay atwhay Iay asway ownay oingday. Eethray earsyay eforebay, Iay asway
engageday inay ethay amesay annermay anday adhay eatedcray aay iendfay osewhay unparalleleday
arbaritybay adhay esolatedday myay earthay anday illedfay itay orfay everay ithway ethay itterestbay
emorseray. Iay asway ownay aboutay otay ormfay anotheray eingbay ofay osewhay ispositionsday Iay asway
alikeay ignorantay; eshay ightmay ecomebay entay ousandthay imestay oremay alignantmay anthay erhay
atemay anday elightday, orfay itsay ownay akesay, inay urdermay anday etchednesswray. Ehay adhay
ornsway otay uitqay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofay anmay anday idehay imselfhay inay esertsday, utbay eshay
adhay otnay; anday eshay, owhay inay allay obabilitypray asway otay ecomebay aay inkingthay anday
easoningray animalay, ightmay efuseray otay omplycay ithway aay ompactcay ademay eforebay erhay
eationcray. Eythay ightmay evenay atehay eachay otheray; ethay eaturecray owhay alreadyay ivedlay
oathedlay ishay ownay eformityday, anday ightmay ehay otnay onceivecay aay eatergray abhorrenceay
orfay itay enwhay itay amecay eforebay ishay eyesay inay ethay emalefay ormfay? Eshay alsoay ightmay urntay
ithway isgustday omfray imhay otay ethay uperiorsay eautybay ofay anmay; eshay ightmay uitqay imhay,
anday ehay ebay againay aloneay, exasperateday byay ethay eshfray ovocationpray ofay eingbay
esertedday byay oneay ofay ishay ownay eciesspay.

Evenay ifay eythay ereway otay eavelay Europeay anday inhabitay ethay esertsday ofay ethay ewnay orldway,
etyay oneay ofay ethay irstfay esultsray ofay osethay athiessympay orfay ichwhay ethay ondæmay
irstedthay ouldway ebay ildrenchay, anday aay aceray ofay evilsday ouldway ebay opagatedpray uponay
ethay earthay owhay ightmay akemay ethay eryvay existenceay ofay ethay eciesspay ofay anmay aay
onditioncay ecariouspray anday ullfay ofay errortay. Adhay Iay ightray, orfay myay ownay enefitbay,
otay inflictay isthay ursecay uponay everlastingay enerationsgay? Iay adhay eforebay eenbay ovedmay
byay ethay ophismssay ofay ethay eingbay Iay adhay eatedcray; Iay adhay eenbay uckstray enselesssay byay
ishay iendishfay eatsthray; utbay ownay, orfay ethay irstfay imetay, ethay ickednessway ofay myay
omisepray urstbay uponay emay; Iay udderedshay otay inkthay atthay uturefay agesay ightmay ursecay emay
asay eirthay estpay, osewhay elfishnesssay adhay otnay esitatedhay otay uybay itsay ownay eacepay atay
ethay icepray, erhapspay, ofay ethay existenceay ofay ethay olewhay umanhay aceray.

Iay embledtray anday myay earthay ailedfay ithinway emay, enwhay, onay ookinglay upay, Iay awsay byay
ethay ightlay ofay ethay oonmay ethay ondæmay atay ethay asementcay. Aay astlyghay ingray
inkledwray ishay ipslay asay ehay azedgay onay emay, erewhay Iay atsay ulfillingfay ethay asktay
ichwhay ehay adhay allotteday otay emay. Esyay, ehay adhay ollowedfay emay inay myay avelstray; ehay
adhay oiteredlay inay orestsfay, idhay imselfhay inay avescay, oray akentay efugeray inay ideway
anday esertday eathshay; anday ehay ownay amecay otay arkmay myay ogresspray anday aimclay ethay
ulfilmentfay ofay myay omisepray.

Asay Iay ookedlay onay imhay, ishay ountenancecay expresseday ethay utmostay extentay ofay
alicemay anday eacherytray. Iay oughtthay ithway aay ensationsay ofay adnessmay onay myay
omisepray ofay eatingcray anotheray ikelay otay imhay, anday emblingtray ithway assionpay,
oretay otay iecespay ethay ingthay onay ichwhay Iay asway engageday. Ethay etchwray awsay emay
estroyday ethay eaturecray onay osewhay uturefay existenceay ehay ependedday orfay
appinesshay, anday ithway aay owlhay ofay evilishday espairday anday evengeray, ithdrewway.

Iay eftlay ethay oomray, anday ockinglay ethay oorday, ademay aay olemnsay owvay inay myay ownay
earthay evernay otay esumeray myay abourslay; anday enthay, ithway emblingtray epsstay, Iay
oughtsay myay ownay apartmentay. Iay asway aloneay; onenay ereway earnay emay otay issipateday
ethay oomglay anday elieveray emay omfray ethay ickeningsay oppressionay ofay ethay ostmay
erribletay everiesray.

Everalsay ourshay assedpay, anday Iay emainedray earnay myay indowway azinggay onay ethay easay;
itay asway almostay otionlessmay, orfay ethay indsway ereway ushedhay, anday allay aturenay
eposedray underay ethay eyeay ofay ethay uietqay oonmay. Aay ewfay ishingfay esselsvay aloneay
eckedspay ethay aterway, anday ownay anday enthay ethay entlegay eezebray aftedway ethay oundsay
ofay oicesvay asay ethay ishermenfay alledcay otay oneay anotheray. Iay eltfay ethay ilencesay,
althoughay Iay asway ardlyhay onsciouscay ofay itsay extremeay ofunditypray, untilay myay earay
asway uddenlysay arresteday byay ethay addlingpay ofay oarsay earnay ethay oreshay, anday aay
ersonpay andedlay oseclay otay myay ousehay.

Inay aay ewfay inutesmay afteray, Iay eardhay ethay eakingcray ofay myay oorday, asay ifay omesay oneay
endeavoureday otay openay itay oftlysay. Iay embledtray omfray eadhay otay ootfay; Iay eltfay aay
esentimentpray ofay owhay itay asway anday ishedway otay ouseray oneay ofay ethay easantspay owhay
eltdway inay aay ottagecay otnay arfay omfray inemay; utbay Iay asway overcomeay byay ethay ensationsay
ofay elplessnesshay, osay oftenay eltfay inay ightfulfray eamsdray, enwhay ouyay inay ainvay
endeavouray otay flyay omfray anay impendingay angerday, anday asway ootedray otay ethay otspay.

Esentlypray Iay eardhay ethay oundsay ofay ootstepsfay alongay ethay assagepay; ethay oorday
openeday, anday ethay etchwray omwhay Iay eadeddray appeareday. Uttingshay ethay oorday, ehay
approacheday emay anday aidsay inay aay otheredsmay oicevay,

ou“yay avehay estroyedday ethay orkway ichwhay ouyay eganbay; atwhay isay itay atthay ouyay
intenday? Oday ouyay areday otay eakbray ouryay omisepray? Iay avehay endureday oiltay anday iserymay;
Iay eftlay Itzerlandsway ithway ouyay; Iay eptcray alongay ethay oresshay ofay ethay Inerhay, amongay
itsay illowway islandsay anday overay ethay ummitssay ofay itsay illshay. Iay avehay eltdway anymay
onthsmay inay ethay eathshay ofay Englanday anday amongay ethay esertsday ofay Otlandscay. Iay avehay
endureday incalculableay atiguefay, anday oldcay, anday ungerhay; oday ouyay areday estroyday myay
opeshay?”

egone“bay! Iay oday eakbray myay omisepray; evernay illway Iay eatecray anotheray ikelay
ourselfyay, equalay inay eformityday anday ickednessway.”

ave“slay, Iay eforebay easonedray ithway ouyay, utbay ouyay avehay ovedpray ourselfyay
unworthyay ofay myay ondescensioncay. Ememberray atthay Iay avehay owerpay; ouyay elievebay
ourselfyay iserablemay, utbay Iay ancay akemay ouyay osay etchedwray atthay ethay ightlay ofay
ayday illway ebay atefulhay otay ouyay. Ouyay areay myay eatorcray, utbay Iay amay ouryay astermay;
obeyay!”

e“thay ourhay ofay myay irresolutionay isay astpay, anday ethay eriodpay ofay ouryay owerpay isay
arriveday. Ouryay eatsthray annotcay ovemay emay otay oday anay actay ofay ickednessway; utbay
eythay onfirmcay emay inay aay eterminationday ofay otnay eatingcray ouyay aay ompanioncay inay
icevay. Allshay Iay, inay oolcay oodblay, etsay ooselay uponay ethay earthay aay ondæmay osewhay
elightday isay inay eathday anday etchednesswray? Egonebay! Iay amay irmfay, anday ouryay
ordsway illway onlyay exasperateay myay ageray.”

Ethay onstermay awsay myay eterminationday inay myay acefay anday ashedgnay ishay eethtay inay ethay
impotenceay ofay angeray. all“shay eachay anmay,” iedcray ehay, ind“fay aay
ifeway orfay ishay osombay, anday eachay eastbay avehay ishay atemay, anday Iay ebay aloneay? Iay adhay
eelingsfay ofay affectionay, anday eythay ereway equitedray byay etestationday anday ornscay.
Anmay! Ouyay aymay atehay, utbay ewarebay! Ouryay ourshay illway asspay inay eaddray anday iserymay,
anday oonsay ethay oltbay illway allfay ichwhay ustmay avishray omfray ouyay ouryay appinesshay orfay
everay. Areay ouyay otay ebay appyhay ilewhay Iay ovelgray inay ethay intensityay ofay myay
etchednesswray? Ouyay ancay astblay myay otheray assionspay, utbay evengeray
emains—revengeray, enceforthhay earerday anthay ightlay oray oodfay! Iay aymay ieday, utbay
irstfay ouyay, myay anttyray anday ormentortay, allshay ursecay ethay unsay atthay azesgay onay ouryay
iserymay. Ewarebay, orfay Iay amay earlessfay anday ereforethay owerfulpay. Iay illway atchway ithway
ethay ilinessway ofay aay akesnay, atthay Iay aymay ingstay ithway itsay enomvay. Anmay, ouyay allshay
epentray ofay ethay injuriesay ouyay inflictay.”

evil“day, easecay; anday oday otnay oisonpay ethay airay ithway esethay oundssay ofay alicemay.
Iay avehay eclaredday myay esolutionray otay ouyay, anday Iay amay onay owardcay otay endbay
eneathbay ordsway. Eavelay emay; Iay amay inexorableay.”

It“ay isay ellway. Iay ogay; utbay ememberray, Iay allshay ebay ithway ouyay onay ouryay
edding-nightclay.”

Iay artedstay orwardfay anday exclaimeday, illain“vay! Eforebay ouyay ignsay myay
eath-warrantclay, ebay uresay atthay ouyay areay ourselfyay afesay.”

Iay ouldway avehay eizedsay imhay, utbay ehay eludeday emay anday uittedqay ethay ousehay ithway
ecipitationpray. Inay aay ewfay omentsmay Iay awsay imhay inay ishay oatbay, ichwhay otshay
acrossay ethay atersway ithway anay arrowyay iftnesssway anday asway oonsay ostlay amidstay ethay
avesway.

Allay asway againay ilentsay, utbay ishay ordsway angray inay myay earsay. Iay urnedbay ithway ageray otay
ursuepay ethay urderermay ofay myay eacepay anday ecipitatepray imhay intoay ethay oceanay. Iay
alkedway upay anday ownday myay oomray astilyhay anday erturbedpay, ilewhay myay imaginationay
onjuredcay upay aay ousandthay imagesay otay ormenttay anday ingstay emay. Whyay adhay Iay otnay
ollowedfay imhay anday osedclay ithway imhay inay ortalmay ifestray? Utbay Iay adhay ufferedsay imhay
otay epartday, anday ehay adhay irectedday ishay oursecay owardstay ethay ainlandmay. Iay udderedshay
otay inkthay owhay ightmay ebay ethay extnay ictimvay acrificedsay otay ishay insatiateay evengeray.
Anday enthay Iay oughtthay againay ofay ishay ords—“_Iway illway ebay ithway ouyay onay
ouryay edding-nightclay._” Atthay, enthay, asway ethay eriodpay ixedfay orfay ethay
ulfilmentfay ofay myay estinyday. Inay atthay ourhay Iay ouldshay ieday anday atay onceay atisfysay anday
extinguishay ishay alicemay. Ethay ospectpray idday otnay ovemay emay otay earfay; etyay enwhay Iay
oughtthay ofay myay elovedbay Elizabethay, ofay erhay earstay anday endlessay orrowsay, enwhay eshay
ouldshay indfay erhay overlay osay arbarouslybay atchedsnay omfray erhay, earstay, ethay irstfay Iay
adhay edshay orfay anymay onthsmay, eamedstray omfray myay eyesay, anday Iay esolvedray otnay otay allfay
eforebay myay enemyay ithoutway aay itterbay ugglestray.

Ethay ightnay assedpay awayay, anday ethay unsay oseray omfray ethay oceanay; myay eelingsfay ecamebay
almercay, ifay itay aymay ebay alledcay almnesscay enwhay ethay iolencevay ofay ageray inkssay intoay
ethay epthsday ofay espairday. Iay eftlay ethay ousehay, ethay orridhay enescay ofay ethay astlay
ight’snay ontentioncay, anday alkedway onay ethay eachbay ofay ethay easay, ichwhay Iay
almostay egardedray asay anay insuperableay arrierbay etweenbay emay anday myay ellowfay
eaturescray; aynay, aay ishway atthay uchsay ouldshay ovepray ethay actfay olestay acrossay emay. Iay
esiredday atthay Iay ightmay asspay myay ifelay onay atthay arrenbay ockray, earilyway, itay isay uetray,
utbay uninterrupteday byay anyay uddensay ockshay ofay iserymay. Ifay Iay eturnedray, itay asway otay
ebay acrificedsay oray otay eesay osethay omwhay Iay ostmay ovedlay ieday underay ethay aspgray ofay aay
ondæmay omwhay Iay adhay elfmysay eatedcray.

Iay alkedway aboutay ethay isleay ikelay aay estlessray ectrespay, eparatedsay omfray allay itay
ovedlay anday iserablemay inay ethay eparationsay. Enwhay itay ecamebay oonnay, anday ethay
unsay oseray igherhay, Iay aylay ownday onay ethay assgray anday asway overpowereday byay aay eepday
eepslay. Iay adhay eenbay awakeay ethay olewhay ofay ethay ecedingpray ightnay, myay ervesnay
ereway agitateday, anday myay eyesay inflameday byay atchingway anday iserymay. Ethay eepslay
intoay ichwhay Iay ownay anksay efreshedray emay; anday enwhay Iay awokeay, Iay againay eltfay asay
ifay Iay elongedbay otay aay aceray ofay umanhay eingsbay ikelay elfmysay, anday Iay eganbay otay
eflectray uponay atwhay adhay assedpay ithway eatergray omposurecay; etyay illstay ethay
ordsway ofay ethay iendfay angray inay myay earsay ikelay aay eath-knellclay; eythay appeareday
ikelay aay eamdray, etyay istinctday anday oppressiveay asay aay ealityray.

Ethay unsay adhay arfay escendedday, anday Iay illstay atsay onay ethay oreshay, atisfyingsay myay
appetiteay, ichwhay adhay ecomebay avenousray, ithway anay oatenay akecay, enwhay Iay awsay aay
ishing-boatclay andlay oseclay otay emay, anday oneay ofay ethay enmay oughtbray emay aay acketpay;
itay ontainedcay etterslay omfray Enevagay, anday oneay omfray Ervalclay entreatingay emay otay
oinjay imhay. Ehay aidsay atthay ehay asway earingway awayay ishay imetay uitlesslyfray erewhay
ehay asway, atthay etterslay omfray ethay iendsfray ehay adhay ormedfay inay Ondonlay esiredday
ishay eturnray otay ompletecay ethay egotiationnay eythay adhay entereday intoay orfay ishay
Indianay enterpriseay. Ehay ouldcay otnay anyay ongerlay elayday ishay epartureday; utbay asay
ishay ourneyjay otay Ondonlay ightmay ebay ollowedfay, evenay oonersay anthay ehay ownay
onjecturedcay, byay ishay ongerlay oyagevay, ehay entreateday emay otay estowbay asay uchmay ofay
myay ocietysay onay imhay asay Iay ouldcay arespay. Ehay esoughtbay emay, ereforethay, otay
eavelay myay olitarysay isleay anday otay eetmay imhay atay Erthpay, atthay eway ightmay oceedpray
outhwardssay ogethertay. Isthay etterlay inay aay egreeday ecalledray emay otay ifelay, anday
Iay eterminedday otay uitqay myay islanday atay ethay expirationay ofay otway aysday.

Etyay, eforebay Iay epartedday, erethay asway aay asktay otay erformpay, onay ichwhay Iay udderedshay
otay eflectray; Iay ustmay ackpay upay myay emicalchay instrumentsay, anday orfay atthay urposepay Iay
ustmay enteray ethay oomray ichwhay adhay eenbay ethay enescay ofay myay odiousay orkway, anday Iay ustmay
andlehay osethay utensilsay ethay ightsay ofay ichwhay asway ickeningsay otay emay. Ethay extnay
orningmay, atay aybreakday, Iay ummonedsay ufficientsay ouragecay anday unlockeday ethay oorday
ofay myay aboratorylay. Ethay emainsray ofay ethay alf-finishedclay eaturecray, omwhay Iay adhay
estroyedday, aylay atteredscay onay ethay oorflay, anday Iay almostay eltfay asay ifay Iay adhay
angledmay ethay ivinglay eshflay ofay aay umanhay eingbay. Iay ausedpay otay ollectcay elfmysay anday
enthay entereday ethay amberchay. Ithway emblingtray andhay Iay onveyedcay ethay instrumentsay
outay ofay ethay oomray, utbay Iay eflectedray atthay Iay oughtay otnay otay eavelay ethay elicsray ofay myay
orkway otay exciteay ethay orrorhay anday uspicionsay ofay ethay easantspay; anday Iay accordinglyay
utpay emthay intoay aay asketbay, ithway aay eatgray uantityqay ofay onesstay, anday ayinglay emthay
upay, eterminedday otay owthray emthay intoay ethay easay atthay eryvay ightnay; anday inay ethay
eantimemay Iay atsay uponay ethay eachbay, employeday inay eaningclay anday arrangingay myay
emicalchay apparatusay.

Othingnay ouldcay ebay oremay ompletecay anthay ethay alterationay atthay adhay akentay aceplay
inay myay eelingsfay incesay ethay ightnay ofay ethay appearanceay ofay ethay ondæmay. Iay adhay
eforebay egardedray myay omisepray ithway aay oomyglay espairday asay aay ingthay atthay, ithway
ateverwhay onsequencescay, ustmay ebay ulfilledfay; utbay Iay ownay eltfay asay ifay aay ilmfay
adhay eenbay akentay omfray eforebay myay eyesay anday atthay Iay orfay ethay irstfay imetay awsay
earlyclay. Ethay ideaay ofay enewingray myay abourslay idday otnay orfay oneay instantay occuray
otay emay; ethay eatthray Iay adhay eardhay eighedway onay myay oughtsthay, utbay Iay idday otnay
eflectray atthay aay oluntaryvay actay ofay inemay ouldcay avertay itay. Iay adhay esolvedray inay
myay ownay indmay atthay otay eatecray anotheray ikelay ethay iendfay Iay adhay irstfay ademay
ouldway ebay anay actay ofay ethay asestbay anday ostmay atrociousay elfishnesssay, anday Iay
anishedbay omfray myay indmay everyay oughtthay atthay ouldcay eadlay otay aay ifferentday
onclusioncay.

Etweenbay otway anday eethray inay ethay orningmay ethay oonmay oseray; anday Iay enthay, uttingpay myay
asketbay aboarday aay ittlelay iffskay, ailedsay outay aboutay ourfay ilesmay omfray ethay oreshay.
Ethay enescay asway erfectlypay olitarysay; aay ewfay oatsbay ereway eturningray owardstay andlay,
utbay Iay ailedsay awayay omfray emthay. Iay eltfay asay ifay Iay asway aboutay ethay ommissioncay ofay aay
eadfuldray imecray anday avoideday ithway udderingshay anxietyay anyay encounteray ithway myay
ellowfay eaturescray. Atay oneay imetay ethay oonmay, ichwhay adhay eforebay eenbay earclay, asway
uddenlysay overspreaday byay aay ickthay oudclay, anday Iay ooktay advantageay ofay ethay omentmay ofay
arknessday anday astcay myay asketbay intoay ethay easay; Iay istenedlay otay ethay urglinggay oundsay
asay itay anksay anday enthay ailedsay awayay omfray ethay otspay. Ethay skyay ecamebay oudedclay, utbay
ethay airay asway urepay, althoughay illedchay byay ethay ortheastnay eezebray atthay asway enthay
isingray. Utbay itay efreshedray emay anday illedfay emay ithway uchsay agreeableay ensationssay
atthay Iay esolvedray otay olongpray myay aystay onay ethay aterway, anday ixingfay ethay udderray inay aay
irectday ositionpay, etchedstray elfmysay atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay oatbay. Oudsclay idhay ethay
oonmay, everythingay asway obscureay, anday Iay eardhay onlyay ethay oundsay ofay ethay oatbay asay itsay
eelkay utcay oughthray ethay avesway; ethay urmurmay ulledlay emay, anday inay aay ortshay imetay Iay
eptslay oundlysay.

Iay oday otnay owknay owhay onglay Iay emainedray inay isthay ituationsay, utbay enwhay Iay awokeay Iay
oundfay atthay ethay unsay adhay alreadyay ountedmay onsiderablycay. Ethay indway asway ighhay, anday
ethay avesway ontinuallycay eatenedthray ethay afetysay ofay myay ittlelay iffskay. Iay oundfay
atthay ethay indway asway ortheastnay anday ustmay avehay ivendray emay arfay omfray ethay oastcay omfray
ichwhay Iay adhay embarkeday. Iay endeavoureday otay angechay myay oursecay utbay uicklyqay oundfay
atthay ifay Iay againay ademay ethay attemptay ethay oatbay ouldway ebay instantlyay illedfay ithway
aterway. Usthay ituatedsay, myay onlyay esourceray asway otay ivedray eforebay ethay indway. Iay
onfesscay atthay Iay eltfay aay ewfay ensationssay ofay errortay. Iay adhay onay ompasscay ithway emay
anday asway osay enderlyslay acquainteday ithway ethay eographygay ofay isthay artpay ofay ethay
orldway atthay ethay unsay asway ofay ittlelay enefitbay otay emay. Iay ightmay ebay ivendray intoay ethay
ideway Atlanticay anday eelfay allay ethay orturestay ofay arvationstay oray ebay allowedsway upay inay
ethay immeasurableay atersway atthay oaredray anday uffetedbay arounday emay. Iay adhay alreadyay
eenbay outay anymay ourshay anday eltfay ethay ormenttay ofay aay urningbay irstthay, aay eludepray otay
myay otheray ufferingssay. Iay ookedlay onay ethay eavenshay, ichwhay ereway overedcay byay oudsclay
atthay ewflay eforebay ethay indway, onlyay otay ebay eplacedray byay othersay; Iay ookedlay uponay ethay
easay; itay asway otay ebay myay avegray. iend“fay,” Iay exclaimeday, our“yay
asktay isay alreadyay ulfilledfay!” Iay oughtthay ofay Elizabethay, ofay myay atherfay, anday
ofay Erval—allclay eftlay ehindbay, onay omwhay ethay onstermay ightmay atisfysay ishay
anguinarysay anday ercilessmay assionspay. Isthay ideaay ungedplay emay intoay aay everieray osay
espairingday anday ightfulfray atthay evenay ownay, enwhay ethay enescay isay onay ethay ointpay ofay
osingclay eforebay emay orfay everay, Iay uddershay otay eflectray onay itay.

Omesay ourshay assedpay usthay; utbay byay egreesday, asay ethay unsay eclinedday owardstay ethay
orizonhay, ethay indway iedday awayay intoay aay entlegay eezebray anday ethay easay ecamebay
eefray omfray eakersbray. Utbay esethay avegay aceplay otay aay eavyhay ellsway; Iay eltfay icksay
anday ardlyhay ableay otay oldhay ethay udderray, enwhay uddenlysay Iay awsay aay inelay ofay ighhay
andlay owardstay ethay outhsay.

Almostay entspay, asay Iay asway, byay atiguefay anday ethay eadfuldray uspensesay Iay endureday
orfay everalsay ourshay, isthay uddensay ertaintycay ofay ifelay ushedray ikelay aay oodflay ofay
armway oyjay otay myay earthay, anday earstay ushedgay omfray myay eyesay.

Owhay utablemay areay ouray eelingsfay, anday owhay angestray isay atthay ingingclay ovelay eway avehay
ofay ifelay evenay inay ethay excessay ofay iserymay! Iay onstructedcay anotheray ailsay ithway aay
artpay ofay myay essdray anday eagerlyay eeredstay myay oursecay owardstay ethay andlay. Itay adhay aay
ildway anday ockyray appearanceay, utbay asay Iay approacheday earernay Iay easilyay erceivedpay
ethay acestray ofay ultivationcay. Iay awsay esselsvay earnay ethay oreshay anday oundfay elfmysay
uddenlysay ansportedtray ackbay otay ethay eighbourhoodnay ofay ivilisedcay anmay. Iay
arefullycay acedtray ethay indingsway ofay ethay andlay anday ailedhay aay eeplestay ichwhay Iay atay
engthlay awsay issuingay omfray ehindbay aay allsmay omontorypray. Asay Iay asway inay aay atestay ofay
extremeay ebilityday, Iay esolvedray otay ailsay irectlyday owardstay ethay owntay, asay aay aceplay
erewhay Iay ouldcay ostmay easilyay ocurepray ourishmentnay. Ortunatelyfay Iay adhay oneymay ithway
emay. Asay Iay urnedtay ethay omontorypray Iay erceivedpay aay allsmay eatnay owntay anday aay oodgay
arbourhay, ichwhay Iay entereday, myay earthay oundingbay ithway oyjay atay myay unexpecteday
escapeay.

Asay Iay asway occupieday inay ixingfay ethay oatbay anday arrangingay ethay ailssay, everalsay
eoplepay owdedcray owardstay ethay otspay. Eythay eemedsay uchmay urprisedsay atay myay
appearanceay, utbay insteaday ofay offeringay emay anyay assistanceay, isperedwhay
ogethertay ithway esturesgay atthay atay anyay otheray imetay ightmay avehay oducedpray inay emay
aay ightslay ensationsay ofay alarmay. Asay itay asway, Iay erelymay emarkedray atthay eythay
okespay Englishay, anday Iay ereforethay addresseday emthay inay atthay anguagelay. “myay
oodgay iendsfray,” aidsay Iay, ill“way ouyay ebay osay indkay asay otay elltay emay ethay amenay ofay
isthay owntay anday informay emay erewhay Iay amay?”

ou“yay illway owknay atthay oonsay enoughay,” epliedray aay anmay ithway aay oarsehay oicevay.
aybe“may ouyay areay omecay otay aay aceplay atthay illway otnay ovepray uchmay otay ouryay astetay,
utbay ouyay illway otnay ebay onsultedcay asay otay ouryay uartersqay, Iay omisepray ouyay.”

Iay asway exceedinglyay urprisedsay onay eceivingray osay uderay anay answeray omfray aay
angerstray, anday Iay asway alsoay isconcertedday onay erceivingpay ethay owningfray anday
angryay ountenancescay ofay ishay ompanionscay. “whyay oday ouyay answeray emay osay
oughlyray?” Iay epliedray. urely“say itay isay otnay ethay ustomcay ofay Englishmenay otay
eceiveray angersstray osay inhospitablyay.”

I“ay oday otnay owknay,” aidsay ethay anmay, at“whay ethay ustomcay ofay ethay
Englishay aymay ebay, utbay itay isay ethay ustomcay ofay ethay Irishay otay atehay illainsvay.”

Ilewhay isthay angestray ialogueday ontinuedcay, Iay erceivedpay ethay owdcray apidlyray
increaseay. Eirthay acesfay expresseday aay ixturemay ofay uriositycay anday angeray, ichwhay
annoyeday anday inay omesay egreeday alarmeday emay. Iay inquireday ethay ayway otay ethay innay, utbay
onay oneay epliedray. Iay enthay ovedmay orwardfay, anday aay urmuringmay oundsay aroseay omfray ethay
owdcray asay eythay ollowedfay anday urroundedsay emay, enwhay anay ill-lookingclay anmay
approachingay appedtay emay onay ethay ouldershay anday aidsay, ome“cay, irsay, ouyay ustmay
ollowfay emay otay Mray. Irwin’skay otay ivegay anay accountay ofay ourselfyay.”

o“whay isay Mray. Irwinkay? Whyay amay Iay otay ivegay anay accountay ofay elfmysay? Isay otnay
isthay aay eefray ountrycay?”

Ay“ay, irsay, eefray enoughay orfay onesthay olksfay. Mray. Irwinkay isay aay agistratemay,
anday ouyay areay otay ivegay anay accountay ofay ethay eathday ofay aay entlemangay owhay asway
oundfay urderedmay erehay astlay ightnay.”

Isthay answeray artledstay emay, utbay Iay esentlypray ecoveredray elfmysay. Iay asway innocentay;
atthay ouldcay easilyay ebay ovedpray; accordinglyay Iay ollowedfay myay onductorcay inay ilencesay
anday asway edlay otay oneay ofay ethay estbay ouseshay inay ethay owntay. Iay asway eadyray otay inksay omfray
atiguefay anday ungerhay, utbay eingbay urroundedsay byay aay owdcray, Iay oughtthay itay oliticpay
otay ouseray allay myay engthstray, atthay onay icalphysay ebilityday ightmay ebay onstruedcay intoay
apprehensionay oray onsciouscay uiltgay. Ittlelay idday Iay enthay expectay ethay alamitycay atthay
asway inay aay ewfay omentsmay otay overwhelmay emay anday extinguishay inay orrorhay anday espairday
allay earfay ofay ignominyay oray eathday.

Iay ustmay ausepay erehay, orfay itay equiresray allay myay ortitudefay otay ecallray ethay emorymay ofay
ethay ightfulfray eventsay ichwhay Iay amay aboutay otay elateray, inay operpray etailday, otay myay
ecollectionray.




Apterchay 21ay


Iay asway oonsay introduceday intoay ethay esencepray ofay ethay agistratemay, anay olday
enevolentbay anmay ithway almcay anday ildmay annersmay. Ehay ookedlay uponay emay, oweverhay,
ithway omesay egreeday ofay everitysay, anday enthay, urningtay owardstay myay onductorscay,
ehay askeday owhay appeareday asay itnessesway onay isthay occasionay.

Aboutay alfhay aay ozenday enmay amecay orwardfay; anday, oneay eingbay electedsay byay ethay
agistratemay, ehay eposedday atthay ehay adhay eenbay outay ishingfay ethay ightnay eforebay ithway
ishay onsay anday other-in-lawclay, Anielday Ugentnay, enwhay, aboutay entay o’clockay,
eythay observeday aay ongstray ortherlynay astblay isingray, anday eythay accordinglyay utpay inay
orfay ortpay. Itay asway aay eryvay arkday ightnay, asay ethay oonmay adhay otnay etyay isenray; eythay idday
otnay andlay atay ethay arbourhay, utbay, asay eythay adhay eenbay accustomeday, atay aay eekcray aboutay
otway ilesmay elowbay. Ehay alkedway onay irstfay, arryingcay aay artpay ofay ethay ishingfay ackletay,
anday ishay ompanionscay ollowedfay imhay atay omesay istanceday. Asay ehay asway oceedingpray
alongay ethay andssay, ehay uckstray ishay ootfay againstay omethingsay anday ellfay atay ishay
engthlay onay ethay oundgray. Ishay ompanionscay amecay upay otay assistay imhay, anday byay ethay
ightlay ofay eirthay anternlay eythay oundfay atthay ehay adhay allenfay onay ethay odybay ofay aay anmay,
owhay asway otay allay appearanceay eadday. Eirthay irstfay uppositionsay asway atthay itay asway ethay
orpsecay ofay omesay ersonpay owhay adhay eenbay owneddray anday asway ownthray onay oreshay byay ethay
avesway, utbay onay examinationay eythay oundfay atthay ethay othesclay ereway otnay etway anday evenay
atthay ethay odybay asway otnay enthay oldcay. Eythay instantlyay arriedcay itay otay ethay ottagecay
ofay anay olday omanway earnay ethay otspay anday endeavoureday, utbay inay ainvay, otay estoreray itay
otay ifelay. Itay appeareday otay ebay aay andsomehay oungyay anmay, aboutay ivefay anday entytway
earsyay ofay ageay. Ehay adhay apparentlyay eenbay angledstray, orfay erethay asway onay ignsay ofay
anyay iolencevay exceptay ethay ackblay arkmay ofay ingersfay onay ishay ecknay.

Ethay irstfay artpay ofay isthay epositionday idday otnay inay ethay eastlay interestay emay, utbay
enwhay ethay arkmay ofay ethay ingersfay asway entionedmay Iay ememberedray ethay urdermay ofay
myay otherbray anday eltfay elfmysay extremelyay agitateday; myay imbslay embledtray, anday aay
istmay amecay overay myay eyesay, ichwhay obligeday emay otay eanlay onay aay airchay orfay
upportsay. Ethay agistratemay observeday emay ithway aay eenkay eyeay anday ofay oursecay ewdray
anay unfavourableay auguryay omfray myay annermay.

Ethay onsay onfirmedcay ishay ather’sfay accountay, utbay enwhay Anielday Ugentnay asway
alledcay ehay oresway ositivelypay atthay ustjay eforebay ethay allfay ofay ishay ompanioncay, ehay
awsay aay oatbay, ithway aay inglesay anmay inay itay, atay aay ortshay istanceday omfray ethay oreshay;
anday asay arfay asay ehay ouldcay udgejay byay ethay ightlay ofay aay ewfay arsstay, itay asway ethay amesay
oatbay inay ichwhay Iay adhay ustjay andedlay.

Aay omanway eposedday atthay eshay ivedlay earnay ethay eachbay anday asway andingstay atay ethay oorday
ofay erhay ottagecay, aitingway orfay ethay eturnray ofay ethay ishermenfay, aboutay anay ourhay
eforebay eshay eardhay ofay ethay iscoveryday ofay ethay odybay, enwhay eshay awsay aay oatbay ithway
onlyay oneay anmay inay itay ushpay offay omfray atthay artpay ofay ethay oreshay erewhay ethay orpsecay
asway afterwardsay oundfay.

Anotheray omanway onfirmedcay ethay accountay ofay ethay ishermenfay avinghay oughtbray ethay
odybay intoay erhay ousehay; itay asway otnay oldcay. Eythay utpay itay intoay aay edbay anday
ubbedray itay, anday Anielday entway otay ethay owntay orfay anay apothecaryay, utbay ifelay asway
uiteqay onegay.

Everalsay otheray enmay ereway examineday oncerningcay myay andinglay, anday eythay agreeday
atthay, ithway ethay ongstray orthnay indway atthay adhay arisenay uringday ethay ightnay, itay
asway eryvay obablepray atthay Iay adhay eatenbay aboutay orfay anymay ourshay anday adhay eenbay
obligeday otay eturnray earlynay otay ethay amesay otspay omfray ichwhay Iay adhay epartedday.
Esidesbay, eythay observeday atthay itay appeareday atthay Iay adhay oughtbray ethay odybay
omfray anotheray aceplay, anday itay asway ikelylay atthay asay Iay idday otnay appearay otay owknay
ethay oreshay, Iay ightmay avehay utpay intoay ethay arbourhay ignorantay ofay ethay istanceday
ofay ethay owntay ofay —— omfray ethay aceplay erewhay Iay adhay epositedday ethay orpsecay.

Mray. Irwinkay, onay earinghay isthay evidenceay, esiredday atthay Iay ouldshay ebay akentay intoay
ethay oomray erewhay ethay odybay aylay orfay intermentay, atthay itay ightmay ebay observeday atwhay
effectay ethay ightsay ofay itay ouldway oducepray uponay emay. Isthay ideaay asway obablypray
uggestedsay byay ethay extremeay agitationay Iay adhay exhibiteday enwhay ethay odemay ofay ethay
urdermay adhay eenbay escribedday. Iay asway accordinglyay onductedcay, byay ethay agistratemay
anday everalsay otheray ersonspay, otay ethay innay. Iay ouldcay otnay elphay eingbay uckstray byay ethay
angestray oincidencescay atthay adhay akentay aceplay uringday isthay eventfulay ightnay; utbay,
owingknay atthay Iay adhay eenbay onversingcay ithway everalsay ersonspay inay ethay islanday Iay adhay
inhabiteday aboutay ethay imetay atthay ethay odybay adhay eenbay oundfay, Iay asway erfectlypay
anquiltray asay otay ethay onsequencescay ofay ethay affairay.

Iay entereday ethay oomray erewhay ethay orpsecay aylay anday asway edlay upay otay ethay offincay. Owhay
ancay Iay escribeday myay ensationssay onay eholdingbay itay? Iay eelfay etyay archedpay ithway
orrorhay, ornay ancay Iay eflectray onay atthay erribletay omentmay ithoutway udderingshay anday
agonyay. Ethay examinationay, ethay esencepray ofay ethay agistratemay anday itnessesway,
assedpay ikelay aay eamdray omfray myay emorymay enwhay Iay awsay ethay ifelesslay ormfay ofay Enryhay
Ervalclay etchedstray eforebay emay. Iay aspedgay orfay eathbray, anday owingthray elfmysay onay
ethay odybay, Iay exclaimeday, ave“hay myay urderousmay achinationsmay eprivedday ouyay
alsoay, myay earestday Enryhay, ofay ifelay? Otway Iay avehay alreadyay estroyedday; otheray
ictimsvay awaitay eirthay estinyday; utbay ouyay, Ervalclay, myay iendfray, myay
enefactorbay—”

Ethay umanhay amefray ouldcay onay ongerlay upportsay ethay agoniesay atthay Iay endureday, anday
Iay asway arriedcay outay ofay ethay oomray inay ongstray onvulsionscay.

Aay everfay ucceededsay otay isthay. Iay aylay orfay otway onthsmay onay ethay ointpay ofay eathday; myay
avingsray, asay Iay afterwardsay eardhay, ereway ightfulfray; Iay alledcay elfmysay ethay
urderermay ofay Illiamway, ofay Ustinejay, anday ofay Ervalclay. Ometimessay Iay entreateday myay
attendantsay otay assistay emay inay ethay estructionday ofay ethay iendfay byay omwhay Iay asway
ormentedtay; anday atay othersay Iay eltfay ethay ingersfay ofay ethay onstermay alreadyay aspinggray
myay ecknay, anday eamedscray alouday ithway agonyay anday errortay. Ortunatelyfay, asay Iay okespay
myay ativenay anguagelay, Mray. Irwinkay aloneay understooday emay; utbay myay esturesgay anday
itterbay iescray ereway ufficientsay otay affrightay ethay otheray itnessesway.

Whyay idday Iay otnay ieday? Oremay iserablemay anthay anmay everay asway eforebay, whyay idday Iay otnay
inksay intoay orgetfulnessfay anday estray? Eathday atchessnay awayay anymay oomingblay
ildrenchay, ethay onlyay opeshay ofay eirthay otingday arentspay; owhay anymay idesbray anday
outhfulyay overslay avehay eenbay oneay ayday inay ethay oomblay ofay ealthhay anday opehay, anday ethay
extnay aay eypray orfay ormsway anday ethay ecayday ofay ethay ombtay! Ofay atwhay aterialsmay asway Iay
ademay atthay Iay ouldcay usthay esistray osay anymay ocksshay, ichwhay, ikelay ethay urningtay ofay
ethay eelwhay, ontinuallycay enewedray ethay orturetay?

Utbay Iay asway oomedday otay ivelay anday inay otway onthsmay oundfay elfmysay asay awakingay omfray
aay eamdray, inay aay isonpray, etchedstray onay aay etchedwray edbay, urroundedsay byay
aolersgay, urnkeystay, oltsbay, anday allay ethay iserablemay apparatusay ofay aay ungeonday.
Itay asway orningmay, Iay ememberray, enwhay Iay usthay awokeay otay understandingay; Iay adhay
orgottenfay ethay articularspay ofay atwhay adhay appenedhay anday onlyay eltfay asay ifay omesay
eatgray isfortunemay adhay uddenlysay overwhelmeday emay; utbay enwhay Iay ookedlay arounday
anday awsay ethay arredbay indowsway anday ethay ualidnesssqay ofay ethay oomray inay ichwhay Iay
asway, allay ashedflay acrossay myay emorymay anday Iay oanedgray itterlybay.

Isthay oundsay isturbedday anay olday omanway owhay asway eepingslay inay aay airchay esidebay
emay. Eshay asway aay iredhay ursenay, ethay ifeway ofay oneay ofay ethay urnkeystay, anday erhay
ountenancecay expresseday allay osethay adbay ualitiesqay ichwhay oftenay aracterisechay
atthay assclay. Ethay ineslay ofay erhay acefay ereway ardhay anday uderay, ikelay atthay ofay
ersonspay accustomeday otay eesay ithoutway athisingsympay inay ightssay ofay iserymay. Erhay
onetay expresseday erhay entireay indifferenceay; eshay addresseday emay inay Englishay,
anday ethay oicevay uckstray emay asay oneay atthay Iay adhay eardhay uringday myay ufferingssay.

Are“ay ouyay etterbay ownay, irsay?” aidsay eshay.

Iay epliedray inay ethay amesay anguagelay, ithway aay eeblefay oicevay, I“ay elievebay Iay amay;
utbay ifay itay ebay allay uetray, ifay indeeday Iay idday otnay eamdray, Iay amay orrysay atthay Iay amay
illstay aliveay otay eelfay isthay iserymay anday orrorhay.”

or“fay atthay attermay,” epliedray ethay olday omanway, if“ay ouyay eanmay aboutay ethay
entlemangay ouyay urderedmay, Iay elievebay atthay itay ereway etterbay orfay ouyay ifay ouyay
ereway eadday, orfay Iay ancyfay itay illway ogay ardhay ithway ouyay! Oweverhay, at’sthay onenay
ofay myay usinessbay; Iay amay entsay otay ursenay ouyay anday etgay ouyay ellway; Iay oday myay utyday
ithway aay afesay onsciencecay; itay ereway ellway ifay everybodyay idday ethay amesay.”

Iay urnedtay ithway oathinglay omfray ethay omanway owhay ouldcay utteray osay unfeelingay aay
eechspay otay aay ersonpay ustjay avedsay, onay ethay eryvay edgeay ofay eathday; utbay Iay eltfay
anguidlay anday unableay otay eflectray onay allay atthay adhay assedpay. Ethay olewhay eriessay
ofay myay ifelay appeareday otay emay asay aay eamdray; Iay ometimessay oubtedday ifay indeeday itay
ereway allay uetray, orfay itay evernay esentedpray itselfay otay myay indmay ithway ethay orcefay
ofay ealityray.

Asay ethay imagesay atthay oatedflay eforebay emay ecamebay oremay istinctday, Iay ewgray
everishfay; aay arknessday essedpray arounday emay; onay oneay asway earnay emay owhay oothedsay
emay ithway ethay entlegay oicevay ofay ovelay; onay earday andhay upportedsay emay. Ethay
icianphysay amecay anday escribedpray edicinesmay, anday ethay olday omanway eparedpray
emthay orfay emay; utbay utteray arelessnesscay asway isiblevay inay ethay irstfay, anday ethay
expressionay ofay utalitybray asway onglystray arkedmay inay ethay isagevay ofay ethay
econdsay. Owhay ouldcay ebay interesteday inay ethay atefay ofay aay urderermay utbay ethay
angmanhay owhay ouldway aingay ishay eefay?

Esethay ereway myay irstfay eflectionsray, utbay Iay oonsay earnedlay atthay Mray. Irwinkay adhay
ownshay emay extremeay indnesskay. Ehay adhay ausedcay ethay estbay oomray inay ethay isonpray
otay ebay eparedpray orfay emay etched(wray indeeday asway ethay estbay); anday itay asway ehay owhay
adhay ovidedpray aay icianphysay anday aay ursenay. Itay isay uetray, ehay eldomsay amecay otay
eesay emay, orfay althoughay ehay ardentlyay esiredday otay elieveray ethay ufferingssay ofay
everyay umanhay eaturecray, ehay idday otnay ishway otay ebay esentpray atay ethay agoniesay anday
iserablemay avingsray ofay aay urderermay. Ehay amecay, ereforethay, ometimessay otay eesay
atthay Iay asway otnay eglectednay, utbay ishay isitsvay ereway ortshay anday ithway onglay
intervalsay.

Oneay ayday, ilewhay Iay asway aduallygray ecoveringray, Iay asway eatedsay inay aay airchay, myay eyesay
alfhay openay anday myay eekschay ividlay ikelay osethay inay eathday. Iay asway overcomeay byay oomglay
anday iserymay anday oftenay eflectedray Iay adhay etterbay eeksay eathday anthay esireday otay
emainray inay aay orldway ichwhay otay emay asway epleteray ithway etchednesswray. Atay oneay imetay Iay
onsideredcay etherwhay Iay ouldshay otnay eclareday elfmysay uiltygay anday uffersay ethay
enaltypay ofay ethay awlay, esslay innocentay anthay oorpay Ustinejay adhay eenbay. Uchsay ereway myay
oughtsthay enwhay ethay oorday ofay myay apartmentay asway openeday anday Mray. Irwinkay entereday.
Ishay ountenancecay expresseday athysympay anday ompassioncay; ehay ewdray aay airchay oseclay otay
inemay anday addresseday emay inay Enchfray,

I“ay earfay atthay isthay aceplay isay eryvay ockingshay otay ouyay; ancay Iay oday anythingay otay
akemay ouyay oremay omfortablecay?”

I“ay ankthay ouyay, utbay allay atthay ouyay entionmay isay othingnay otay emay; onay ethay olewhay
earthay erethay isay onay omfortcay ichwhay Iay amay apablecay ofay eceivingray.”

I“ay owknay atthay ethay athysympay ofay aay angerstray ancay ebay utbay ofay ittlelay eliefray otay
oneay ornebay ownday asay ouyay areay byay osay angestray aay isfortunemay. Utbay ouyay illway, Iay
opehay, oonsay uitqay isthay elancholymay abodeay, orfay oubtlessday evidenceay ancay
easilyay ebay oughtbray otay eefray ouyay omfray ethay iminalcray argechay.”

at“thay isay myay eastlay oncerncay; Iay amay, byay aay oursecay ofay angestray eventsay, ecomebay
ethay ostmay iserablemay ofay ortalsmay. Ersecutedpay anday orturedtay asay Iay amay anday
avehay eenbay, ancay eathday ebay anyay evilay otay emay?”

othing“nay indeeday ouldcay ebay oremay unfortunateay anday agonisingay anthay ethay
angestray anceschay atthay avehay atelylay occurreday. Ouyay ereway ownthray, byay omesay
urprisingsay accidentay, onay isthay oreshay, enownedray orfay itsay ospitalityhay,
eizedsay immediatelyay, anday argedchay ithway urdermay. Ethay irstfay ightsay atthay asway
esentedpray otay ouryay eyesay asway ethay odybay ofay ouryay iendfray, urderedmay inay osay
unaccountableay aay annermay anday acedplay, asay itay ereway, byay omesay iendfay acrossay
ouryay athpay.”

Asay Mray. Irwinkay aidsay isthay, otwithstandingnay ethay agitationay Iay endureday onay
isthay etrospectray ofay myay ufferingssay, Iay alsoay eltfay onsiderablecay urprisesay atay
ethay owledgeknay ehay eemedsay otay ossesspay oncerningcay emay. Iay upposesay omesay
astonishmentay asway exhibiteday inay myay ountenancecay, orfay Mray. Irwinkay astenedhay
otay aysay,

Immediately“ay uponay ouryay eingbay akentay illay, allay ethay aperspay atthay ereway onay
ouryay ersonpay ereway oughtbray emay, anday Iay examineday emthay atthay Iay ightmay iscoverday omesay
acetray byay ichwhay Iay ouldcay endsay otay ouryay elationsray anay accountay ofay ouryay isfortunemay
anday illnessay. Iay oundfay everalsay etterslay, anday, amongay othersay, oneay ichwhay Iay
iscoveredday omfray itsay ommencementcay otay ebay omfray ouryay atherfay. Iay instantlyay otewray
otay Enevagay; earlynay otway onthsmay avehay elapseday incesay ethay epartureday ofay myay etterlay.
Utbay ouyay areay illay; evenay ownay ouyay embletray; ouyay areay unfitay orfay agitationay ofay anyay
indkay.”

is“thay uspensesay isay aay ousandthay imestay orseway anthay ethay ostmay orriblehay eventay;
elltay emay atwhay ewnay enescay ofay eathday ashay eenbay acteday, anday osewhay urdermay Iay amay
ownay otay amentlay?”

our“yay amilyfay isay erfectlypay ellway,” aidsay Mray. Irwinkay ithway
entlenessgay; and“ay omeonesay, aay iendfray, isay omecay otay isitvay ouyay.”

Iay owknay otnay byay atwhay ainchay ofay oughtthay ethay ideaay esentedpray itselfay, utbay itay
instantlyay artedday intoay myay indmay atthay ethay urderermay adhay omecay otay ockmay atay myay
iserymay anday aunttay emay ithway ethay eathday ofay Ervalclay, asay aay ewnay incitementay orfay
emay otay omplycay ithway ishay ellishhay esiresday. Iay utpay myay andhay eforebay myay eyesay,
anday iedcray outay inay agonyay,

Oh“ay! Aketay imhay awayay! Iay annotcay eesay imhay; orfay Od’sgay akesay, oday otnay
etlay imhay enteray!”

Mray. Irwinkay egardedray emay ithway aay oubledtray ountenancecay. Ehay ouldcay otnay elphay
egardingray myay exclamationay asay aay esumptionpray ofay myay uiltgay anday aidsay inay
atherray aay everesay onetay,

I“ay ouldshay avehay oughtthay, oungyay anmay, atthay ethay esencepray ofay ouryay atherfay
ouldway avehay eenbay elcomeway insteaday ofay inspiringay uchsay iolentvay epugnanceray.”

“myay atherfay!” iedcray Iay, ilewhay everyay eaturefay anday everyay usclemay asway elaxedray
omfray anguishay otay easureplay. Is“ay myay atherfay indeeday omecay? Owhay indkay, owhay
eryvay indkay! Utbay erewhay isay ehay, whyay oesday ehay otnay astenhay otay emay?”

Myay angechay ofay annermay urprisedsay anday easedplay ethay agistratemay; erhapspay ehay
oughtthay atthay myay ormerfay exclamationay asway aay omentarymay eturnray ofay eliriumday,
anday ownay ehay instantlyay esumedray ishay ormerfay enevolencebay. Ehay oseray anday
uittedqay ethay oomray ithway myay ursenay, anday inay aay omentmay myay atherfay entereday itay.

Othingnay, atay isthay omentmay, ouldcay avehay ivengay emay eatergray easureplay anthay ethay
arrivalay ofay myay atherfay. Iay etchedstray outay myay andhay otay imhay anday iedcray,

Are“ay ouyay enthay afe—andsay Elizabeth—anday Ernestay?”

Myay atherfay almedcay emay ithway assurancesay ofay eirthay elfareway anday endeavoureday, byay
ellingdway onay esethay ubjectssay osay interestingay otay myay earthay, otay aiseray myay
espondingday iritsspay; utbay ehay oonsay eltfay atthay aay isonpray annotcay ebay ethay abodeay ofay
eerfulnesschay. at“whay aay aceplay isay isthay atthay ouyay inhabitay, myay onsay!”
aidsay ehay, ookinglay ournfullymay atay ethay arredbay indowsway anday etchedwray appearanceay
ofay ethay oomray. ou“yay avelledtray otay eeksay appinesshay, utbay aay atalityfay eemssay
otay ursuepay ouyay. Anday oorpay Ervalclay—”

Ethay amenay ofay myay unfortunateay anday urderedmay iendfray asway anay agitationay ootay
eatgray otay ebay endureday inay myay eakway atestay; Iay edshay earstay.

Alas“ay! Esyay, myay atherfay,” epliedray Iay; ome“say estinyday ofay ethay
ostmay orriblehay indkay angshay overay emay, anday Iay ustmay ivelay otay ulfilfay itay, oray urelysay Iay
ouldshay avehay iedday onay ethay offincay ofay Enryhay.”

Eway ereway otnay alloweday otay onversecay orfay anyay engthlay ofay imetay, orfay ethay
ecariouspray atestay ofay myay ealthhay enderedray everyay ecautionpray ecessarynay atthay
ouldcay ensureay anquillitytray. Mray. Irwinkay amecay inay anday insisteday atthay myay
engthstray ouldshay otnay ebay exhausteday byay ootay uchmay exertionay. Utbay ethay
appearanceay ofay myay atherfay asway otay emay ikelay atthay ofay myay oodgay angelay, anday Iay
aduallygray ecoveredray myay ealthhay.

Asay myay icknesssay uittedqay emay, Iay asway absorbeday byay aay oomyglay anday ackblay
elancholymay atthay othingnay ouldcay issipateday. Ethay imageay ofay Ervalclay asway
orfay everay eforebay emay, astlyghay anday urderedmay. Oremay anthay onceay ethay agitationay
intoay ichwhay esethay eflectionsray ewthray emay ademay myay iendsfray eaddray aay angerousday
elapseray. Alasay! Whyay idday eythay eservepray osay iserablemay anday etestedday aay
ifelay? Itay asway urelysay atthay Iay ightmay ulfilfay myay estinyday, ichwhay isay ownay
awingdray otay aay oseclay. Oonsay, ohay, eryvay oonsay, illway eathday extinguishay esethay
obbingsthray anday elieveray emay omfray ethay ightymay eightway ofay anguishay atthay earsbay
emay otay ethay ustday; anday, inay executingay ethay awarday ofay usticejay, Iay allshay alsoay
inksay otay estray. Enthay ethay appearanceay ofay eathday asway istantday, althoughay ethay
ishway asway everay esentpray otay myay oughtsthay; anday Iay oftenay atsay orfay ourshay
otionlessmay anday eechlessspay, ishingway orfay omesay ightymay evolutionray atthay
ightmay urybay emay anday myay estroyerday inay itsay uinsray.

Ethay easonsay ofay ethay assizesay approacheday. Iay adhay alreadyay eenbay eethray onthsmay
inay isonpray, anday althoughay Iay asway illstay eakway anday inay ontinualcay angerday ofay aay
elapseray, Iay asway obligeday otay aveltray earlynay aay undredhay ilesmay otay ethay ountrycay
owntay erewhay ethay ourtcay asway eldhay. Mray. Irwinkay argedchay imselfhay ithway everyay
arecay ofay ollectingcay itnessesway anday arrangingay myay efenceday. Iay asway aredspay
ethay isgraceday ofay appearingay ubliclypay asay aay iminalcray, asay ethay asecay asway otnay
oughtbray eforebay ethay ourtcay atthay ecidesday onay ifelay anday eathday. Ethay andgray
uryjay ejectedray ethay illbay, onay itsay eingbay ovedpray atthay Iay asway onay ethay Orkneyay
Islandsay atay ethay ourhay ethay odybay ofay myay iendfray asway oundfay; anday aay ortnightfay
afteray myay emovalray Iay asway iberatedlay omfray isonpray.

Myay atherfay asway enraptureday onay indingfay emay eedfray omfray ethay exationsvay ofay aay
iminalcray argechay, atthay Iay asway againay alloweday otay eathebray ethay eshfray
atmosphereay anday ermittedpay otay eturnray otay myay ativenay ountrycay. Iay idday otnay
articipatepay inay esethay eelingsfay, orfay otay emay ethay allsway ofay aay ungeonday oray aay
alacepay ereway alikeay atefulhay. Ethay upcay ofay ifelay asway oisonedpay orfay everay, anday
althoughay ethay unsay oneshay uponay emay, asay uponay ethay appyhay anday aygay ofay earthay, Iay
awsay arounday emay othingnay utbay aay enseday anday ightfulfray arknessday, enetratedpay byay
onay ightlay utbay ethay immerglay ofay otway eyesay atthay aredglay uponay emay. Ometimessay
eythay ereway ethay expressiveay eyesay ofay Enryhay, anguishinglay inay eathday, ethay arkday
orbsay earlynay overedcay byay ethay idslay anday ethay onglay ackblay asheslay atthay ingedfray
emthay; ometimessay itay asway ethay ateryway, oudedclay eyesay ofay ethay onstermay, asay Iay
irstfay awsay emthay inay myay amberchay atay Ingolstadtay.

Myay atherfay iedtray otay awakenay inay emay ethay eelingsfay ofay affectionay. Ehay alkedtay
ofay Enevagay, ichwhay Iay ouldshay oonsay isitvay, ofay Elizabethay anday Ernestay; utbay
esethay ordsway onlyay ewdray eepday oansgray omfray emay. Ometimessay, indeeday, Iay eltfay aay
ishway orfay appinesshay anday oughtthay ithway elancholymay elightday ofay myay elovedbay
ousincay oray ongedlay, ithway aay evouringday aladie_may uday ayspay_, otay eesay onceay oremay
ethay ueblay akelay anday apidray Onerhay, atthay adhay eenbay osay earday otay emay inay earlyay
ildhoodchay; utbay myay eneralgay atestay ofay eelingfay asway aay orportay inay ichwhay aay
isonpray asway asay elcomeway aay esidenceray asay ethay ivinestday enescay inay aturenay; anday
esethay itsfay ereway eldomsay interrupteday utbay byay aroxysmspay ofay anguishay anday
espairday. Atay esethay omentsmay Iay oftenay endeavoureday otay utpay anay enday otay ethay
existenceay Iay oathedlay, anday itay equiredray unceasingay attendanceay anday igilancevay
otay estrainray emay omfray ommittingcay omesay eadfuldray actay ofay iolencevay.

Etyay oneay utyday emainedray otay emay, ethay ecollectionray ofay ichwhay inallyfay
iumphedtray overay myay elfishsay espairday. Itay asway ecessarynay atthay Iay ouldshay
eturnray ithoutway elayday otay Enevagay, erethay otay atchway overay ethay iveslay ofay osethay
Iay osay ondlyfay ovedlay anday otay ielay inay aitway orfay ethay urderermay, atthay ifay anyay
ancechay edlay emay otay ethay aceplay ofay ishay oncealmentcay, oray ifay ehay aredday againay otay
astblay emay byay ishay esencepray, Iay ightmay, ithway unfailingay aimay, utpay anay enday otay
ethay existenceay ofay ethay onstrousmay imageay ichwhay Iay adhay endueday ithway ethay
ockerymay ofay aay oulsay illstay oremay onstrousmay. Myay atherfay illstay esiredday otay
elayday ouray epartureday, earfulfay atthay Iay ouldcay otnay ustainsay ethay atiguesfay ofay aay
ourneyjay, orfay Iay asway aay atteredshay eck—thewray adowshay ofay aay umanhay eingbay. Myay
engthstray asway onegay. Iay asway aay eremay eletonskay, anday everfay ightnay anday ayday
eyedpray uponay myay astedway amefray.

Illstay, asay Iay urgeday ouray eavinglay Irelanday ithway uchsay inquietudeay anday impatienceay,
myay atherfay oughtthay itay estbay otay ieldyay. Eway ooktay ouray assagepay onay oardbay aay esselvay
oundbay orfay avre-de-Graceclay anday ailedsay ithway aay airfay indway omfray ethay Irishay oresshay.
Itay asway idnightmay. Iay aylay onay ethay eckday ookinglay atay ethay arsstay anday isteninglay otay
ethay ashingday ofay ethay avesway. Iay ailedhay ethay arknessday atthay utshay Irelanday omfray myay
ightsay, anday myay ulsepay eatbay ithway aay everishfay oyjay enwhay Iay eflectedray atthay Iay ouldshay
oonsay eesay Enevagay. Ethay astpay appeareday otay emay inay ethay ightlay ofay aay ightfulfray eamdray;
etyay ethay esselvay inay ichwhay Iay asway, ethay indway atthay ewblay emay omfray ethay etestedday
oreshay ofay Irelanday, anday ethay easay ichwhay urroundedsay emay, oldtay emay ootay orciblyfay
atthay Iay asway eceivedday byay onay isionvay anday atthay Ervalclay, myay iendfray anday earestday
ompanioncay, adhay allenfay aay ictimvay otay emay anday ethay onstermay ofay myay eationcray. Iay
epassedray, inay myay emorymay, myay olewhay ifelay; myay uietqay appinesshay ilewhay esidingray
ithway myay amilyfay inay Enevagay, ethay eathday ofay myay othermay, anday myay epartureday orfay
Ingolstadtay. Iay ememberedray, udderingshay, ethay admay enthusiasmay atthay urriedhay emay onay
otay ethay eationcray ofay myay ideoushay enemyay, anday Iay alledcay otay indmay ethay ightnay inay
ichwhay ehay irstfay ivedlay. Iay asway unableay otay ursuepay ethay aintray ofay oughtthay; aay
ousandthay eelingsfay essedpray uponay emay, anday Iay eptway itterlybay.

Everay incesay myay ecoveryray omfray ethay everfay, Iay adhay eenbay inay ethay ustomcay ofay akingtay
everyay ightnay aay allsmay uantityqay ofay audanumlay, orfay itay asway byay eansmay ofay isthay ugdray
onlyay atthay Iay asway enableday otay aingay ethay estray ecessarynay orfay ethay eservationpray ofay
ifelay. Oppresseday byay ethay ecollectionray ofay myay ariousvay isfortunesmay, Iay ownay
allowedsway oubleday myay usualay uantityqay anday oonsay eptslay ofoundlypray. Utbay eepslay idday
otnay afforday emay espiteray omfray oughtthay anday iserymay; myay eamsdray esentedpray aay
ousandthay objectsay atthay aredscay emay. Owardstay orningmay Iay asway ossessedpay byay aay indkay
ofay ightmarenay; Iay eltfay ethay iend’sfay aspgray inay myay ecknay anday ouldcay otnay eefray
elfmysay omfray itay; oansgray anday iescray angray inay myay earsay. Myay atherfay, owhay asway
atchingway overay emay, erceivingpay myay estlessnessray, awokeay emay; ethay ashingday avesway
ereway arounday, ethay oudyclay skyay aboveay, ethay iendfay asway otnay erehay: aay ensesay ofay
ecuritysay, aay eelingfay atthay aay ucetray asway establisheday etweenbay ethay esentpray ourhay
anday ethay irresistibleay, isastrousday uturefay imparteday otay emay aay indkay ofay almcay
orgetfulnessfay, ofay ichwhay ethay umanhay indmay isay byay itsay ucturestray eculiarlypay
usceptiblesay.




Apterchay 22ay


Ethay oyagevay amecay otay anay enday. Eway andedlay, anday oceededpray otay Arispay. Iay oonsay
oundfay atthay Iay adhay overtaxeday myay engthstray anday atthay Iay ustmay eposeray eforebay Iay
ouldcay ontinuecay myay ourneyjay. Myay ather’sfay arecay anday attentionsay ereway
indefatigableay, utbay ehay idday otnay owknay ethay originay ofay myay ufferingssay anday
oughtsay erroneousay ethodsmay otay emedyray ethay incurableay illay. Ehay ishedway emay otay
eeksay amusementay inay ocietysay. Iay abhorreday ethay acefay ofay anmay. Ohay, otnay
abhorreday! Eythay ereway myay ethrenbray, myay ellowfay eingsbay, anday Iay eltfay
attracteday evenay otay ethay ostmay epulsiveray amongay emthay, asay otay eaturescray ofay anay
angelicay aturenay anday elestialcay echanismmay. Utbay Iay eltfay atthay Iay adhay onay ightray
otay areshay eirthay intercourseay. Iay adhay unchaineday anay enemyay amongay emthay osewhay
oyjay itay asway otay edshay eirthay oodblay anday otay evelray inay eirthay oansgray. Owhay eythay
ouldway, eachay anday allay, abhoray emay anday unthay emay omfray ethay orldway, idday eythay owknay
myay unhalloweday actsay anday ethay imescray ichwhay adhay eirthay ourcesay inay emay!

Myay atherfay ieldedyay atay engthlay otay myay esireday otay avoiday ocietysay anday ovestray byay
ariousvay argumentsay otay anishbay myay espairday. Ometimessay ehay oughtthay atthay Iay
eltfay eeplyday ethay egradationday ofay eingbay obligeday otay answeray aay argechay ofay
urdermay, anday ehay endeavoureday otay ovepray otay emay ethay utilityfay ofay idepray.

Alas“ay! Myay atherfay,” aidsay Iay, ow“hay ittlelay oday ouyay owknay emay.
Umanhay eingsbay, eirthay eelingsfay anday assionspay, ouldway indeeday ebay egradedday ifay uchsay
aay etchwray asay Iay eltfay idepray. Ustinejay, oorpay unhappyay Ustinejay, asway asay innocentay
asay Iay, anday eshay ufferedsay ethay amesay argechay; eshay iedday orfay itay; anday Iay amay ethay ausecay
ofay is—Ithay urderedmay erhay. Illiamway, Ustinejay, anday Enry—theyhay allay
iedday byay myay andshay.”

Myay atherfay adhay oftenay, uringday myay imprisonmentay, eardhay emay akemay ethay amesay
assertionay; enwhay Iay usthay accuseday elfmysay, ehay ometimessay eemedsay otay esireday anay
explanationay, anday atay othersay ehay appeareday otay onsidercay itay asay ethay offspringay ofay
eliriumday, anday atthay, uringday myay illnessay, omesay ideaay ofay isthay indkay adhay esentedpray
itselfay otay myay imaginationay, ethay emembranceray ofay ichwhay Iay eservedpray inay myay
onvalescencecay. Iay avoideday explanationay anday aintainedmay aay ontinualcay ilencesay
oncerningcay ethay etchwray Iay adhay eatedcray. Iay adhay aay ersuasionpay atthay Iay ouldshay ebay
upposedsay admay, anday isthay inay itselfay ouldway orfay everay avehay ainedchay myay onguetay. Utbay,
esidesbay, Iay ouldcay otnay ingbray elfmysay otay iscloseday aay ecretsay ichwhay ouldway illfay myay
earerhay ithway onsternationcay anday akemay earfay anday unnaturalay orrorhay ethay inmatesay ofay
ishay eastbray. Iay eckedchay, ereforethay, myay impatientay irstthay orfay athysympay anday asway
ilentsay enwhay Iay ouldway avehay ivengay ethay orldway otay avehay onfidedcay ethay atalfay ecretsay.
Etyay, illstay, ordsway ikelay osethay Iay avehay ecordedray ouldway urstbay uncontrollablyay
omfray emay. Iay ouldcay offeray onay explanationay ofay emthay, utbay eirthay uthtray inay artpay
elievedray ethay urdenbay ofay myay eriousmystay oeway.

Uponay isthay occasionay myay atherfay aidsay, ithway anay expressionay ofay unboundeday onderway,
“myay earestday Ictorvay, atwhay infatuationay isay isthay? Myay earday onsay, Iay entreatay
ouyay evernay otay akemay uchsay anay assertionay againay.”

I“ay amay otnay admay,” Iay iedcray energeticallyay; e“thay unsay anday ethay eavenshay, owhay
avehay iewedvay myay operationsay, ancay earbay itnessway ofay myay uthtray. Iay amay ethay
assassinay ofay osethay ostmay innocentay ictimsvay; eythay iedday byay myay achinationsmay.
Aay ousandthay imestay ouldway Iay avehay edshay myay ownay oodblay, opdray byay opdray, otay avehay
avedsay eirthay iveslay; utbay Iay ouldcay otnay, myay atherfay, indeeday Iay ouldcay otnay
acrificesay ethay olewhay umanhay aceray.”

Ethay onclusioncay ofay isthay eechspay onvincedcay myay atherfay atthay myay ideasay ereway
erangedday, anday ehay instantlyay angedchay ethay ubjectsay ofay ouray onversationcay anday
endeavoureday otay alteray ethay oursecay ofay myay oughtsthay. Ehay ishedway asay uchmay asay
ossiblepay otay obliterateay ethay emorymay ofay ethay enesscay atthay adhay akentay aceplay inay
Irelanday anday evernay alludeday otay emthay oray ufferedsay emay otay eakspay ofay myay
isfortunesmay.

Asay imetay assedpay awayay Iay ecamebay oremay almcay; iserymay adhay erhay ellingdway inay myay
earthay, utbay Iay onay ongerlay alkedtay inay ethay amesay incoherentay annermay ofay myay ownay
imescray; ufficientsay orfay emay asway ethay onsciousnesscay ofay emthay. Byay ethay utmostay
elf-violenceclay Iay urbedcay ethay imperiousay oicevay ofay etchednesswray, ichwhay
ometimessay esiredday otay eclareday itselfay otay ethay olewhay orldway, anday myay annersmay
ereway almercay anday oremay omposedcay anthay eythay adhay everay eenbay incesay myay ourneyjay
otay ethay easay ofay iceay.

Aay ewfay aysday eforebay eway eftlay Arispay onay ouray ayway otay Itzerlandsway, Iay eceivedray ethay
ollowingfay etterlay omfray Elizabethay:

“myay earday Iendfray,

It“ay avegay emay ethay eatestgray easureplay otay eceiveray aay etterlay omfray myay uncleay
atedday atay Arispay; ouyay areay onay ongerlay atay aay ormidablefay istanceday, anday Iay aymay
opehay otay eesay ouyay inay esslay anthay aay ortnightfay. Myay oorpay ousincay, owhay uchmay ouyay
ustmay avehay ufferedsay! Iay expectay otay eesay ouyay ookinglay evenay oremay illay anthay
enwhay ouyay uittedqay Enevagay. Isthay interway ashay eenbay assedpay ostmay iserablymay,
orturedtay asay Iay avehay eenbay byay anxiousay uspensesay; etyay Iay opehay otay eesay eacepay inay
ouryay ountenancecay anday otay indfay atthay ouryay earthay isay otnay otallytay oidvay ofay
omfortcay anday anquillitytray.

et“yay Iay earfay atthay ethay amesay eelingsfay ownay existay atthay ademay ouyay osay iserablemay
aay earyay agoay, evenay erhapspay augmenteday byay imetay. Iay ouldway otnay isturbday ouyay atay
isthay eriodpay, enwhay osay anymay isfortunesmay eighway uponay ouyay, utbay aay
onversationcay atthay Iay adhay ithway myay uncleay eviouspray otay ishay epartureday endersray
omesay explanationay ecessarynay eforebay eway eetmay.

Explanationay! Ouyay aymay ossiblypay aysay, Atwhay ancay Elizabethay avehay otay explainay? Ifay
ouyay eallyray aysay isthay, myay uestionsqay areay answereday anday allay myay oubtsday atisfiedsay.
Utbay ouyay areay istantday omfray emay, anday itay isay ossiblepay atthay ouyay aymay eaddray anday etyay
ebay easedplay ithway isthay explanationay; anday inay aay obabilitypray ofay isthay eingbay ethay
asecay, Iay areday otnay anyay ongerlay ostponepay itingwray atwhay, uringday ouryay absenceay, Iay
avehay oftenay ishedway otay expressay otay ouyay utbay avehay evernay adhay ethay ouragecay otay eginbay.

ou“yay ellway owknay, Ictorvay, atthay ouray unionay adhay eenbay ethay avouritefay anplay ofay
ouryay arentspay everay incesay ouray infancyay. Eway ereway oldtay isthay enwhay oungyay, anday
aughttay otay ooklay orwardfay otay itay asay anay eventay atthay ouldway ertainlycay aketay
aceplay. Eway ereway affectionateay ayfellowsplay uringday ildhoodchay, anday, Iay
elievebay, earday anday aluedvay iendsfray otay oneay anotheray asay eway ewgray olderay. Utbay
asay otherbray anday istersay oftenay entertainay aay ivelylay affectionay owardstay eachay
otheray ithoutway esiringday aay oremay intimateay unionay, aymay otnay uchsay alsoay ebay ouray
asecay? Elltay emay, earestday Ictorvay. Answeray emay, Iay onjurecay ouyay byay ouray utualmay
appinesshay, ithway implesay uth—Dotray ouyay otnay ovelay anotheray?

ou“yay avehay avelledtray; ouyay avehay entspay everalsay earsyay ofay ouryay ifelay atay
Ingolstadtay; anday Iay onfesscay otay ouyay, myay iendfray, atthay enwhay Iay awsay ouyay astlay
autumnay osay unhappyay, ingflyay otay olitudesay omfray ethay ocietysay ofay everyay
eaturecray, Iay ouldcay otnay elphay upposingsay atthay ouyay ightmay egretray ouray
onnectioncay anday elievebay ourselfyay oundbay inay onourhay otay ulfilfay ethay ishesway ofay
ouryay arentspay, althoughay eythay opposeday emselvesthay otay ouryay inclinationsay.
Utbay isthay isay alsefay easoningray. Iay onfesscay otay ouyay, myay iendfray, atthay Iay ovelay
ouyay anday atthay inay myay airyay eamsdray ofay uturityfay ouyay avehay eenbay myay onstantcay
iendfray anday ompanioncay. Utbay itay isay ouryay appinesshay Iay esireday asay ellway asay myay
ownay enwhay Iay eclareday otay ouyay atthay ouray arriagemay ouldway enderray emay eternallyay
iserablemay unlessay itay ereway ethay ictateday ofay ouryay ownay eefray oicechay. Evenay ownay
Iay eepway otay inkthay atthay, ornebay ownday asay ouyay areay byay ethay uellestcray
isfortunesmay, ouyay aymay iflestay, byay ethay ordway onour_hay_, allay opehay ofay atthay
ovelay anday appinesshay ichwhay ouldway aloneay estoreray ouyay otay ourselfyay. Iay, owhay
avehay osay isinterestedday anay affectionay orfay ouyay, aymay increaseay ouryay iseriesmay
enfoldtay byay eingbay anay obstacleay otay ouryay ishesway. Ahay! Ictorvay, ebay assureday
atthay ouryay ousincay anday aymateplay ashay ootay inceresay aay ovelay orfay ouyay otnay otay ebay
ademay iserablemay byay isthay uppositionsay. Ebay appyhay, myay iendfray; anday ifay ouyay
obeyay emay inay isthay oneay equestray, emainray atisfiedsay atthay othingnay onay earthay
illway avehay ethay owerpay otay interruptay myay anquillitytray.

o“day otnay etlay isthay etterlay isturbday ouyay; oday otnay answeray omorrowtay, oray ethay
extnay ayday, oray evenay untilay ouyay omecay, ifay itay illway ivegay ouyay ainpay. Myay uncleay
illway endsay emay ewsnay ofay ouryay ealthhay, anday ifay Iay eesay utbay oneay ilesmay onay ouryay
ipslay enwhay eway eetmay, occasioneday byay isthay oray anyay otheray exertionay ofay inemay, Iay
allshay eednay onay otheray appinesshay.

Elizabeth“ay Avenzalay.



eneva“gay, Aymay 18thay, 17ay—”



Isthay etterlay evivedray inay myay emorymay atwhay Iay adhay eforebay orgottenfay, ethay eatthray ofay
ethay iend—“_Ifay illway ebay ithway ouyay onay ouryay
edding-nightclay!_” Uchsay asway myay entencesay, anday onay atthay ightnay ouldway ethay
ondæmay employay everyay artay otay estroyday emay anday eartay emay omfray ethay impseglay ofay
appinesshay ichwhay omisedpray artlypay otay onsolecay myay ufferingssay. Onay atthay ightnay ehay
adhay eterminedday otay onsummatecay ishay imescray byay myay eathday. Ellway, ebay itay osay; aay
eadlyday ugglestray ouldway enthay assuredlyay aketay aceplay, inay ichwhay ifay ehay ereway
ictoriousvay Iay ouldshay ebay atay eacepay anday ishay owerpay overay emay ebay atay anay enday. Ifay ehay
ereway anquishedvay, Iay ouldshay ebay aay eefray anmay. Alasay! Atwhay eedomfray? Uchsay asay ethay
easantpay enjoysay enwhay ishay amilyfay avehay eenbay assacredmay eforebay ishay eyesay, ishay
ottagecay urntbay, ishay andslay aidlay asteway, anday ehay isay urnedtay adriftay, omelesshay,
ennilesspay, anday aloneay, utbay eefray. Uchsay ouldway ebay myay ibertylay exceptay atthay inay myay
Elizabethay Iay ossessedpay aay easuretray, alasay, alancedbay byay osethay orrorshay ofay
emorseray anday uiltgay ichwhay ouldway ursuepay emay untilay eathday.

Eetsway anday elovedbay Elizabethay! Iay eadray anday ereadray erhay etterlay, anday omesay
oftenedsay eelingsfay olestay intoay myay earthay anday aredday otay isperwhay aradisiacalpay
eamsdray ofay ovelay anday oyjay; utbay ethay appleay asway alreadyay eatenay, anday ethay
angel’say armay aredbay otay ivedray emay omfray allay opehay. Etyay Iay ouldway ieday otay akemay
erhay appyhay. Ifay ethay onstermay executeday ishay eatthray, eathday asway inevitableay; etyay,
againay, Iay onsideredcay etherwhay myay arriagemay ouldway astenhay myay atefay. Myay
estructionday ightmay indeeday arriveay aay ewfay onthsmay oonersay, utbay ifay myay orturertay
ouldshay uspectsay atthay Iay ostponedpay itay, influenceday byay ishay enacesmay, ehay ouldway
urelysay indfay otheray anday erhapspay oremay eadfuldray eansmay ofay evengeray. Ehay adhay owedvay
o_tay ebay ithway emay onay myay edding-nightclay_, etyay ehay idday otnay onsidercay atthay
eatthray asay indingbay imhay otay eacepay inay ethay eantimemay, orfay asay ifay otay owshay emay atthay
ehay asway otnay etyay atiatedsay ithway oodblay, ehay adhay urderedmay Ervalclay immediatelyay
afteray ethay enunciationay ofay ishay eatsthray. Iay esolvedray, ereforethay, atthay ifay myay
immediateay unionay ithway myay ousincay ouldway onducecay eitheray otay ershay oray myay
ather’sfay appinesshay, myay adversary’say esignsday againstay myay ifelay
ouldshay otnay etardray itay aay inglesay ourhay.

Inay isthay atestay ofay indmay Iay otewray otay Elizabethay. Myay etterlay asway almcay anday
affectionateay. I“ay earfay, myay elovedbay irlgay,” Iay aidsay, ittle“lay appinesshay
emainsray orfay usay onay earthay; etyay allay atthay Iay aymay oneay ayday enjoyay isay entredcay inay
ouyay. Asechay awayay ouryay idleay earsfay; otay ouyay aloneay oday Iay onsecratecay myay ifelay
anday myay endeavoursay orfay ontentmentcay. Iay avehay oneay ecretsay, Elizabethay, aay
eadfuldray oneay; enwhay evealedray otay ouyay, itay illway illchay ouryay amefray ithway
orrorhay, anday enthay, arfay omfray eingbay urprisedsay atay myay iserymay, ouyay illway onlyay
onderway atthay Iay urvivesay atwhay Iay avehay endureday. Iay illway onfidecay isthay aletay ofay
iserymay anday errortay otay ouyay ethay ayday afteray ouray arriagemay allshay aketay aceplay,
orfay, myay eetsway ousincay, erethay ustmay ebay erfectpay onfidencecay etweenbay usay. Utbay
untilay enthay, Iay onjurecay ouyay, oday otnay entionmay oray alludeay otay itay. Isthay Iay ostmay
earnestlyay entreatay, anday Iay owknay ouyay illway omplycay.”

Inay aboutay aay eekway afteray ethay arrivalay ofay Elizabeth’say etterlay eway eturnedray
otay Enevagay. Ethay eetsway irlgay elcomedway emay ithway armway affectionay, etyay earstay ereway
inay erhay eyesay asay eshay eheldbay myay emaciateday amefray anday everishfay eekschay. Iay awsay aay
angechay inay erhay alsoay. Eshay asway innerthay anday adhay ostlay uchmay ofay atthay eavenlyhay
ivacityvay atthay adhay eforebay armedchay emay; utbay erhay entlenessgay anday oftsay ookslay ofay
ompassioncay ademay erhay aay oremay itfay ompanioncay orfay oneay astedblay anday iserablemay asay Iay
asway.

Ethay anquillitytray ichwhay Iay ownay enjoyeday idday otnay endureay. Emorymay oughtbray adnessmay
ithway itay, anday enwhay Iay oughtthay ofay atwhay adhay assedpay, aay ealray insanityay ossessedpay
emay; ometimessay Iay asway uriousfay anday urntbay ithway ageray, ometimessay owlay anday
espondentday. Iay eithernay okespay ornay ookedlay atay anyoneay, utbay atsay otionlessmay,
ewilderedbay byay ethay ultitudemay ofay iseriesmay atthay overcameay emay.

Elizabethay aloneay adhay ethay owerpay otay awdray emay omfray esethay itsfay; erhay entlegay oicevay
ouldway oothesay emay enwhay ansportedtray byay assionpay anday inspireay emay ithway umanhay
eelingsfay enwhay unksay inay orportay. Eshay eptway ithway emay anday orfay emay. Enwhay easonray
eturnedray, eshay ouldway emonstrateray anday endeavouray otay inspireay emay ithway
esignationray. Ahay! Itay isay ellway orfay ethay unfortunateay otay ebay esignedray, utbay orfay ethay
uiltygay erethay isay onay eacepay. Ethay agoniesay ofay emorseray oisonpay ethay uxurylay erethay isay
otherwiseay ometimessay oundfay inay indulgingay ethay excessay ofay iefgray.

Oonsay afteray myay arrivalay myay atherfay okespay ofay myay immediateay arriagemay ithway
Elizabethay. Iay emainedray ilentsay.

ave“hay ouyay, enthay, omesay otheray attachmentay?”

one“nay onay earthay. Iay ovelay Elizabethay anday ooklay orwardfay otay ouray unionay ithway
elightday. Etlay ethay ayday ereforethay ebay ixedfay; anday onay itay Iay illway onsecratecay
elfmysay, inay ifelay oray eathday, otay ethay appinesshay ofay myay ousincay.”

“myay earday Ictorvay, oday otnay eakspay usthay. Eavyhay isfortunesmay avehay efallenbay
usay, utbay etlay usay onlyay ingclay oserclay otay atwhay emainsray anday ansfertray ouray ovelay
orfay osethay omwhay eway avehay ostlay otay osethay owhay etyay ivelay. Ouray irclecay illway ebay
allsmay utbay oundbay oseclay byay ethay iestay ofay affectionay anday utualmay isfortunemay.
Anday enwhay imetay allshay avehay oftenedsay ouryay espairday, ewnay anday earday objectsay ofay
arecay illway ebay ornbay otay eplaceray osethay ofay omwhay eway avehay eenbay osay uellycray
eprivedday.”

Uchsay ereway ethay essonslay ofay myay atherfay. Utbay otay emay ethay emembranceray ofay ethay
eatthray eturnedray; ornay ancay ouyay onderway atthay, omnipotentay asay ethay iendfay adhay
etyay eenbay inay ishay eedsday ofay oodblay, Iay ouldshay almostay egardray imhay asay
invincibleay, anday atthay enwhay ehay adhay onouncedpray ethay ordsway I“_ay allshay ebay ithway
ouyay onay ouryay edding-nightclay_,” Iay ouldshay egardray ethay eatenedthray atefay asay
unavoidableay. Utbay eathday asway onay evilay otay emay ifay ethay osslay ofay Elizabethay ereway
alancedbay ithway itay, anday Iay ereforethay, ithway aay ontentedcay anday evenay eerfulchay
ountenancecay, agreeday ithway myay atherfay atthay ifay myay ousincay ouldway onsentcay, ethay
eremonycay ouldshay aketay aceplay inay entay aysday, anday usthay utpay, asay Iay imagineday,
ethay ealsay otay myay atefay.
