Eatgray Odgay! Ifay orfay oneay instantay Iay adhay oughtthay atwhay ightmay ebay ethay ellishhay
intentionay ofay myay iendishfay adversaryay, Iay ouldway atherray avehay anishedbay elfmysay
orfay everay omfray myay ativenay ountrycay anday anderedway aay iendlessfray outcastay overay
ethay earthay anthay avehay onsentedcay otay isthay iserablemay arriagemay. Utbay, asay ifay
ossessedpay ofay agicmay owerspay, ethay onstermay adhay indedblay emay otay ishay ealray
intentionsay; anday enwhay Iay oughtthay atthay Iay adhay eparedpray onlyay myay ownay eathday, Iay
astenedhay atthay ofay aay arfay earerday ictimvay.

Asay ethay eriodpay ixedfay orfay ouray arriagemay ewdray earernay, etherwhay omfray owardicecay oray
aay opheticpray eelingfay, Iay eltfay myay earthay inksay ithinway emay. Utbay Iay oncealedcay myay
eelingsfay byay anay appearanceay ofay ilarityhay atthay oughtbray ilessmay anday oyjay otay ethay
ountenancecay ofay myay atherfay, utbay ardlyhay eceivedday ethay ever-watchfulclay anday icernay
eyeay ofay Elizabethay. Eshay ookedlay orwardfay otay ouray unionay ithway acidplay ontentmentcay,
otnay unmingleday ithway aay ittlelay earfay, ichwhay astpay isfortunesmay adhay impresseday,
atthay atwhay ownay appeareday ertaincay anday angibletay appinesshay ightmay oonsay issipateday
intoay anay airyay eamdray anday eavelay onay acetray utbay eepday anday everlastingay egretray.

Eparationspray ereway ademay orfay ethay eventay, ongratulatorycay isitsvay ereway eceivedray,
anday allay oreway aay ilingsmay appearanceay. Iay utshay upay, asay ellway asay Iay ouldcay, inay myay ownay
earthay ethay anxietyay atthay eyedpray erethay anday entereday ithway eemingsay earnestnessay
intoay ethay ansplay ofay myay atherfay, althoughay eythay ightmay onlyay ervesay asay ethay
ecorationsday ofay myay agedytray. Oughthray myay ather’sfay exertionsay aay artpay ofay
ethay inheritanceay ofay Elizabethay adhay eenbay estoredray otay erhay byay ethay Austrianay
overnmentgay. Aay allsmay ossessionpay onay ethay oresshay ofay Omocay elongedbay otay erhay. Itay
asway agreeday atthay, immediatelyay afteray ouray unionay, eway ouldshay oceedpray otay Illavay
Avenzalay anday endspay ouray irstfay aysday ofay appinesshay esidebay ethay eautifulbay akelay
earnay ichwhay itay oodstay.

Inay ethay eantimemay Iay ooktay everyay ecautionpray otay efendday myay ersonpay inay asecay ethay
iendfay ouldshay openlyay attackay emay. Iay arriedcay istolspay anday aay aggerday
onstantlycay aboutay emay anday asway everay onay ethay atchway otay eventpray artificeay, anday
byay esethay eansmay ainedgay aay eatergray egreeday ofay anquillitytray. Indeeday, asay ethay
eriodpay approacheday, ethay eatthray appeareday oremay asay aay elusionday, otnay otay ebay
egardedray asay orthyway otay isturbday myay eacepay, ilewhay ethay appinesshay Iay opedhay orfay
inay myay arriagemay oreway aay eatergray appearanceay ofay ertaintycay asay ethay ayday ixedfay
orfay itsay olemnisationsay ewdray earernay anday Iay eardhay itay ontinuallycay okenspay ofay
asay anay occurrenceay ichwhay onay accidentay ouldcay ossiblypay eventpray.

Elizabethay eemedsay appyhay; myay anquiltray emeanourday ontributedcay eatlygray otay
almcay erhay indmay. Utbay onay ethay ayday atthay asway otay ulfilfay myay ishesway anday myay
estinyday, eshay asway elancholymay, anday aay esentimentpray ofay evilay ervadedpay erhay;
anday erhapspay alsoay eshay oughtthay ofay ethay eadfuldray ecretsay ichwhay Iay adhay
omisedpray otay evealray otay erhay onay ethay ollowingfay ayday. Myay atherfay asway inay ethay
eantimemay overjoyeday, anday, inay ethay ustlebay ofay eparationpray, onlyay ecognisedray inay
ethay elancholymay ofay ishay iecenay ethay iffidenceday ofay aay idebray.

Afteray ethay eremonycay asway erformedpay aay argelay artypay assembleday atay myay
ather’sfay, utbay itay asway agreeday atthay Elizabethay anday Iay ouldshay ommencecay ouray
ourneyjay byay aterway, eepingslay atthay ightnay atay Evianay anday ontinuingcay ouray
oyagevay onay ethay ollowingfay ayday. Ethay ayday asway airfay, ethay indway avourablefay;
allay iledsmay onay ouray uptialnay embarkationay.

Osethay ereway ethay astlay omentsmay ofay myay ifelay uringday ichwhay Iay enjoyeday ethay
eelingfay ofay appinesshay. Eway assedpay apidlyray alongay; ethay unsay asway othay, utbay eway
ereway elteredshay omfray itsay aysray byay aay indkay ofay anopycay ilewhay eway enjoyeday ethay
eautybay ofay ethay enescay, ometimessay onay oneay idesay ofay ethay akelay, erewhay eway awsay
Ontmay Alêvesay, ethay easantplay anksbay ofay Ontalègremay, anday atay aay istanceday,
urmountingsay allay, ethay eautifulbay Ontmay Ancblay, anday ethay assemblageay ofay owysnay
ountainsmay atthay inay ainvay endeavouray otay emulateay erhay; ometimessay oastingcay ethay
oppositeay anksbay, eway awsay ethay ightymay Urajay opposingay itsay arkday idesay otay ethay
ambitionay atthay ouldway uitqay itsay ativenay ountrycay, anday anay almostay
insurmountableay arrierbay otay ethay invaderay owhay ouldshay ishway otay enslaveay itay.

Iay ooktay ethay andhay ofay Elizabethay. ou“yay areay orrowfulsay, myay ovelay. Ahay! Ifay
ouyay ewknay atwhay Iay avehay ufferedsay anday atwhay Iay aymay etyay endureay, ouyay ouldway
endeavouray otay etlay emay astetay ethay uietqay anday eedomfray omfray espairday atthay isthay
oneay ayday atay eastlay ermitspay emay otay enjoyay.”

e“bay appyhay, myay earday Ictorvay,” epliedray Elizabethay; ere“thay isay, Iay opehay,
othingnay otay istressday ouyay; anday ebay assureday atthay ifay aay ivelylay oyjay isay otnay
aintedpay inay myay acefay, myay earthay isay ontentedcay. Omethingsay isperswhay otay emay
otnay otay ependday ootay uchmay onay ethay ospectpray atthay isay openeday eforebay usay, utbay Iay
illway otnay istenlay otay uchsay aay inistersay oicevay. Observeay owhay astfay eway ovemay
alongay anday owhay ethay oudsclay, ichwhay ometimessay obscureay anday ometimessay iseray
aboveay ethay omeday ofay Ontmay Ancblay, enderray isthay enescay ofay eautybay illstay oremay
interestingay. Ooklay alsoay atay ethay innumerableay ishfay atthay areay immingsway inay
ethay earclay atersway, erewhay eway ancay istinguishday everyay ebblepay atthay ieslay atay
ethay ottombay. Atwhay aay ivineday ayday! Owhay appyhay anday erenesay allay aturenay
appearsay!”

Usthay Elizabethay endeavoureday otay ivertday erhay oughtsthay anday inemay omfray allay
eflectionray uponay elancholymay ubjectssay. Utbay erhay empertay asway uctuatingflay;
oyjay orfay aay ewfay instantsay oneshay inay erhay eyesay, utbay itay ontinuallycay avegay aceplay
otay istractionday anday everieray.

Ethay unsay anksay owerlay inay ethay eavenshay; eway assedpay ethay iverray Ancedray anday
observeday itsay athpay oughthray ethay asmschay ofay ethay igherhay anday ethay ensglay ofay ethay
owerlay illshay. Ethay Alpsay erehay omecay oserclay otay ethay akelay, anday eway approacheday
ethay amphitheatreay ofay ountainsmay ichwhay ormsfay itsay easternay oundarybay. Ethay
irespay ofay Evianay oneshay underay ethay oodsway atthay urroundedsay itay anday ethay angeray
ofay ountainmay aboveay ountainmay byay ichwhay itay asway overhungay.

Ethay indway, ichwhay adhay ithertohay arriedcay usay alongay ithway amazingay apidityray,
anksay atay unsetsay otay aay ightlay eezebray; ethay oftsay airay ustjay uffledray ethay aterway
anday ausedcay aay easantplay otionmay amongay ethay eestray asay eway approacheday ethay
oreshay, omfray ichwhay itay aftedway ethay ostmay elightfulday entscay ofay owersflay anday
ayhay. Ethay unsay anksay eneathbay ethay orizonhay asay eway andedlay, anday asay Iay ouchedtay
ethay oreshay Iay eltfay osethay arescay anday earsfay eviveray ichwhay oonsay ereway otay aspclay
emay anday ingclay otay emay orfay everay.




Apterchay 23ay


Itay asway eightay o’clockay enwhay eway andedlay; eway alkedway orfay aay ortshay imetay onay ethay
oreshay, enjoyingay ethay ansitorytray ightlay, anday enthay etiredray otay ethay innay anday
ontemplatedcay ethay ovelylay enescay ofay atersway, oodsway, anday ountainsmay, obscureday
inay arknessday, etyay illstay isplayingday eirthay ackblay outlinesay.

Ethay indway, ichwhay adhay allenfay inay ethay outhsay, ownay oseray ithway eatgray iolencevay
inay ethay estway. Ethay oonmay adhay eachedray erhay ummitsay inay ethay eavenshay anday asway
eginningbay otay escendday; ethay oudsclay eptsway acrossay itay iftersway anthay ethay
ightflay ofay ethay ulturevay anday immedday erhay aysray, ilewhay ethay akelay eflectedray ethay
enescay ofay ethay usybay eavenshay, enderedray illstay usierbay byay ethay estlessray avesway
atthay ereway eginningbay otay iseray. Uddenlysay aay eavyhay ormstay ofay ainray escendedday.

Iay adhay eenbay almcay uringday ethay ayday, utbay osay oonsay asay ightnay obscureday ethay
apesshay ofay objectsay, aay ousandthay earsfay aroseay inay myay indmay. Iay asway anxiousay
anday atchfulway, ilewhay myay ightray andhay aspedgray aay istolpay ichwhay asway iddenhay inay
myay osombay; everyay oundsay errifiedtay emay, utbay Iay esolvedray atthay Iay ouldway ellsay myay
ifelay earlyday anday otnay inkshray omfray ethay onflictcay untilay myay ownay ifelay oray atthay
ofay myay adversaryay asway extinguisheday.

Elizabethay observeday myay agitationay orfay omesay imetay inay imidtay anday earfulfay ilencesay,
utbay erethay asway omethingsay inay myay anceglay ichwhay ommunicatedcay errortay otay erhay, anday
emblingtray, eshay askeday, at“whay isay itay atthay agitatesay ouyay, myay earday Ictorvay?
Atwhay isay itay ouyay earfay?”

Oh“ay! Eacepay, eacepay, myay ovelay,” epliedray Iay; is“thay ightnay, anday
allay illway ebay afesay; utbay isthay ightnay isay eadfuldray, eryvay eadfuldray.”

Iay assedpay anay ourhay inay isthay atestay ofay indmay, enwhay uddenlysay Iay eflectedray owhay
earfulfay ethay ombatcay ichwhay Iay omentarilymay expecteday ouldway ebay otay myay ifeway,
anday Iay earnestlyay entreateday erhay otay etireray, esolvingray otnay otay oinjay erhay
untilay Iay adhay obtaineday omesay owledgeknay asay otay ethay ituationsay ofay myay enemyay.

Eshay eftlay emay, anday Iay ontinuedcay omesay imetay alkingway upay anday ownday ethay assagespay
ofay ethay ousehay anday inspectingay everyay ornercay atthay ightmay afforday aay etreatray otay
myay adversaryay. Utbay Iay iscoveredday onay acetray ofay imhay anday asway eginningbay otay
onjecturecay atthay omesay ortunatefay ancechay adhay interveneday otay eventpray ethay
executionay ofay ishay enacesmay enwhay uddenlysay Iay eardhay aay illshray anday eadfuldray
eamscray. Itay amecay omfray ethay oomray intoay ichwhay Elizabethay adhay etiredray. Asay Iay
eardhay itay, ethay olewhay uthtray ushedray intoay myay indmay, myay armsay oppeddray, ethay
otionmay ofay everyay usclemay anday ibrefay asway uspendedsay; Iay ouldcay eelfay ethay oodblay
icklingtray inay myay einsvay anday inglingtay inay ethay extremitiesay ofay myay imbslay. Isthay
atestay astedlay utbay orfay anay instantay; ethay eamscray asway epeatedray, anday Iay ushedray
intoay ethay oomray.

Eatgray Odgay! Whyay idday Iay otnay enthay expireay! Whyay amay Iay erehay otay elateray ethay
estructionday ofay ethay estbay opehay anday ethay urestpay eaturecray onay earthay? Eshay asway
erethay, ifelesslay anday inanimateay, ownthray acrossay ethay edbay, erhay eadhay anginghay ownday
anday erhay alepay anday istortedday eaturesfay alfhay overedcay byay erhay airhay. Everywhereay Iay
urntay Iay eesay ethay amesay igure—herfay oodlessblay armsay anday elaxedray ormfay ungflay
byay ethay urderermay onay itsay idalbray ierbay. Ouldcay Iay eholdbay isthay anday ivelay? Alasay!
Ifelay isay obstinateay anday ingsclay osestclay erewhay itay isay ostmay atedhay. Orfay aay omentmay
onlyay idday Iay oselay ecollectionray; Iay ellfay enselesssay onay ethay oundgray.

Enwhay Iay ecoveredray Iay oundfay elfmysay urroundedsay byay ethay eoplepay ofay ethay innay; eirthay
ountenancescay expresseday aay eathlessbray errortay, utbay ethay orrorhay ofay othersay
appeareday onlyay asay aay ockerymay, aay adowshay ofay ethay eelingsfay atthay oppresseday emay. Iay
escapeday omfray emthay otay ethay oomray erewhay aylay ethay odybay ofay Elizabethay, myay ovelay, myay
ifeway, osay atelylay ivinglay, osay earday, osay orthyway. Eshay adhay eenbay ovedmay omfray ethay
osturepay inay ichwhay Iay adhay irstfay eheldbay erhay, anday ownay, asay eshay aylay, erhay eadhay uponay
erhay armay anday aay andkerchiefhay ownthray acrossay erhay acefay anday ecknay, Iay ightmay avehay
upposedsay erhay asleepay. Iay ushedray owardstay erhay anday embraceday erhay ithway ardouray, utbay
ethay eadlyday anguorlay anday oldnesscay ofay ethay imbslay oldtay emay atthay atwhay Iay ownay eldhay
inay myay armsay adhay easedcay otay ebay ethay Elizabethay omwhay Iay adhay ovedlay anday erishedchay.
Ethay urderousmay arkmay ofay ethay iend’sfay aspgray asway onay erhay ecknay, anday ethay
eathbray adhay easedcay otay issueay omfray erhay ipslay.

Ilewhay Iay illstay unghay overay erhay inay ethay agonyay ofay espairday, Iay appenedhay otay ooklay upay.
Ethay indowsway ofay ethay oomray adhay eforebay eenbay arkenedday, anday Iay eltfay aay indkay ofay
anicpay onay eeingsay ethay alepay ellowyay ightlay ofay ethay oonmay illuminateay ethay amberchay.
Ethay uttersshay adhay eenbay ownthray ackbay, anday ithway aay ensationsay ofay orrorhay otnay otay ebay
escribedday, Iay awsay atay ethay openay indowway aay igurefay ethay ostmay ideoushay anday abhorreday.
Aay ingray asway onay ethay acefay ofay ethay onstermay; ehay eemedsay otay eerjay, asay ithway ishay
iendishfay ingerfay ehay ointedpay owardstay ethay orpsecay ofay myay ifeway. Iay ushedray owardstay
ethay indowway, anday awingdray aay istolpay omfray myay osombay, iredfay; utbay ehay eludeday emay,
eapedlay omfray ishay ationstay, anday unningray ithway ethay iftnesssway ofay ightninglay,
ungedplay intoay ethay akelay.

Ethay eportray ofay ethay istolpay oughtbray aay owdcray intoay ethay oomray. Iay ointedpay otay
ethay otspay erewhay ehay adhay isappearedday, anday eway ollowedfay ethay acktray ithway
oatsbay; etsnay ereway astcay, utbay inay ainvay. Afteray assingpay everalsay ourshay, eway
eturnedray opelesshay, ostmay ofay myay ompanionscay elievingbay itay otay avehay eenbay aay
ormfay onjuredcay upay byay myay ancyfay. Afteray avinghay andedlay, eythay oceededpray otay
earchsay ethay ountrycay, artiespay oinggay inay ifferentday irectionsday amongay ethay
oodsway anday inesvay.

Iay attempteday otay accompanyay emthay anday oceededpray aay ortshay istanceday omfray ethay
ousehay, utbay myay eadhay irledwhay oundray, myay epsstay ereway ikelay osethay ofay aay unkendray
anmay, Iay ellfay atay astlay inay aay atestay ofay utteray exhaustionay; aay ilmfay overedcay myay
eyesay, anday myay inskay asway archedpay ithway ethay eathay ofay everfay. Inay isthay atestay Iay
asway arriedcay ackbay anday acedplay onay aay edbay, ardlyhay onsciouscay ofay atwhay adhay
appenedhay; myay eyesay anderedway oundray ethay oomray asay ifay otay eeksay omethingsay atthay
Iay adhay ostlay.

Afteray anay intervalay Iay aroseay, anday asay ifay byay instinctay, awledcray intoay ethay oomray
erewhay ethay orpsecay ofay myay elovedbay aylay. Erethay ereway omenway eepingway arounday; Iay
unghay overay itay anday oinedjay myay adsay earstay otay eirsthay; allay isthay imetay onay
istinctday ideaay esentedpray itselfay otay myay indmay, utbay myay oughtsthay ambledray otay
ariousvay ubjectssay, eflectingray onfusedlycay onay myay isfortunesmay anday eirthay
ausecay. Iay asway ewilderedbay, inay aay oudclay ofay onderway anday orrorhay. Ethay eathday
ofay Illiamway, ethay executionay ofay Ustinejay, ethay urdermay ofay Ervalclay, anday astlylay
ofay myay ifeway; evenay atay atthay omentmay Iay ewknay otnay atthay myay onlyay emainingray
iendsfray ereway afesay omfray ethay alignitymay ofay ethay iendfay; myay atherfay evenay ownay
ightmay ebay ithingwray underay ishay aspgray, anday Ernestay ightmay ebay eadday atay ishay
eetfay. Isthay ideaay ademay emay uddershay anday ecalledray emay otay actionay. Iay artedstay
upay anday esolvedray otay eturnray otay Enevagay ithway allay ossiblepay eedspay.

Erethay ereway onay orseshay otay ebay ocuredpray, anday Iay ustmay eturnray byay ethay akelay; utbay ethay
indway asway unfavourableay, anday ethay ainray ellfay inay orrentstay. Oweverhay, itay asway
ardlyhay orningmay, anday Iay ightmay easonablyray opehay otay arriveay byay ightnay. Iay iredhay enmay
otay owray anday ooktay anay oaray elfmysay, orfay Iay adhay alwaysay experienceday eliefray omfray
entalmay ormenttay inay odilybay exerciseay. Utbay ethay overflowingay iserymay Iay ownay eltfay,
anday ethay excessay ofay agitationay atthay Iay endureday enderedray emay incapableay ofay anyay
exertionay. Iay ewthray ownday ethay oaray, anday eaninglay myay eadhay uponay myay andshay, avegay ayway
otay everyay oomyglay ideaay atthay aroseay. Ifay Iay ookedlay upay, Iay awsay enesscay ichwhay ereway
amiliarfay otay emay inay myay appierhay imetay anday ichwhay Iay adhay ontemplatedcay utbay ethay ayday
eforebay inay ethay ompanycay ofay erhay owhay asway ownay utbay aay adowshay anday aay ecollectionray.
Earstay eamedstray omfray myay eyesay. Ethay ainray adhay easedcay orfay aay omentmay, anday Iay awsay
ethay ishfay ayplay inay ethay atersway asay eythay adhay oneday aay ewfay ourshay eforebay; eythay adhay
enthay eenbay observeday byay Elizabethay. Othingnay isay osay ainfulpay otay ethay umanhay indmay asay
aay eatgray anday uddensay angechay. Ethay unsay ightmay ineshay oray ethay oudsclay ightmay owerlay,
utbay othingnay ouldcay appearay otay emay asay itay adhay oneday ethay ayday eforebay. Aay iendfay adhay
atchedsnay omfray emay everyay opehay ofay uturefay appinesshay; onay eaturecray adhay everay eenbay
osay iserablemay asay Iay asway; osay ightfulfray anay eventay isay inglesay inay ethay istoryhay ofay
anmay.

Utbay whyay ouldshay Iay elldway uponay ethay incidentsay atthay ollowedfay isthay astlay
overwhelmingay eventay? Inemay ashay eenbay aay aletay ofay orrorshay; Iay avehay eachedray eirthay
acme_ay_, anday atwhay Iay ustmay ownay elateray ancay utbay ebay edioustay otay ouyay. Owknay
atthay, oneay byay oneay, myay iendsfray ereway atchedsnay awayay; Iay asway eftlay esolateday. Myay
ownay engthstray isay exhausteday, anday Iay ustmay elltay, inay aay ewfay ordsway, atwhay emainsray ofay
myay ideoushay arrationnay.

Iay arriveday atay Enevagay. Myay atherfay anday Ernestay etyay ivedlay, utbay ethay ormerfay unksay
underay ethay idingstay atthay Iay orebay. Iay eesay imhay ownay, excellentay anday enerablevay olday
anmay! Ishay eyesay anderedway inay acancyvay, orfay eythay adhay ostlay eirthay armchay anday eirthay
elight—hisday Elizabethay, ishay oremay anthay aughterday, omwhay ehay otedday onay ithway
allay atthay affectionay ichwhay aay anmay eelsfay, owhay inay ethay eclineday ofay ifelay, avinghay
ewfay affectionsay, ingsclay oremay earnestlyay otay osethay atthay emainray. Ursedcay, ursedcay
ebay ethay iendfay atthay oughtbray iserymay onay ishay eygray airshay anday oomedday imhay otay asteway
inay etchednesswray! Ehay ouldcay otnay ivelay underay ethay orrorshay atthay ereway accumulateday
arounday imhay; ethay ingsspray ofay existenceay uddenlysay avegay ayway; ehay asway unableay otay
iseray omfray ishay edbay, anday inay aay ewfay aysday ehay iedday inay myay armsay.

Atwhay enthay ecamebay ofay emay? Iay owknay otnay; Iay ostlay ensationsay, anday ainschay anday
arknessday ereway ethay onlyay objectsay atthay essedpray uponay emay. Ometimessay,
indeeday, Iay eamtdray atthay Iay anderedway inay oweryflay eadowsmay anday easantplay alesvay
ithway ethay iendsfray ofay myay outhyay, utbay Iay awokeay anday oundfay elfmysay inay aay
ungeonday. Elancholymay ollowedfay, utbay byay egreesday Iay ainedgay aay earclay
onceptioncay ofay myay iseriesmay anday ituationsay anday asway enthay eleasedray omfray myay
isonpray. Orfay eythay adhay alledcay emay admay, anday uringday anymay onthsmay, asay Iay
understooday, aay olitarysay ellcay adhay eenbay myay abitationhay.

Ibertylay, oweverhay, adhay eenbay aay uselessay iftgay otay emay, adhay Iay otnay, asay Iay
awakeneday otay easonray, atay ethay amesay imetay awakeneday otay evengeray. Asay ethay
emorymay ofay astpay isfortunesmay essedpray uponay emay, Iay eganbay otay eflectray onay eirthay
ause—thecay onstermay omwhay Iay adhay eatedcray, ethay iserablemay ondæmay omwhay Iay adhay
entsay abroaday intoay ethay orldway orfay myay estructionday. Iay asway ossessedpay byay aay
addeningmay ageray enwhay Iay oughtthay ofay imhay, anday esiredday anday ardentlyay ayedpray
atthay Iay ightmay avehay imhay ithinway myay aspgray otay eakwray aay eatgray anday ignalsay
evengeray onay ishay ursedcay eadhay.

Ornay idday myay atehay onglay onfinecay itselfay otay uselessay ishesway; Iay eganbay otay
eflectray onay ethay estbay eansmay ofay ecuringsay imhay; anday orfay isthay urposepay, aboutay
aay onthmay afteray myay eleaseray, Iay epairedray otay aay iminalcray udgejay inay ethay owntay
anday oldtay imhay atthay Iay adhay anay accusationay otay akemay, atthay Iay ewknay ethay
estroyerday ofay myay amilyfay, anday atthay Iay equiredray imhay otay exertay ishay olewhay
authorityay orfay ethay apprehensionay ofay ethay urderermay.

Ethay agistratemay istenedlay otay emay ithway attentionay anday indnesskay. e“bay
assureday, irsay,” aidsay ehay, o“nay ainspay oray exertionsay onay myay artpay allshay
ebay aredspay otay iscoverday ethay illainvay.”

I“ay ankthay ouyay,” epliedray Iay; isten“lay, ereforethay, otay ethay
epositionday atthay Iay avehay otay akemay. Itay isay indeeday aay aletay osay angestray atthay Iay
ouldshay earfay ouyay ouldway otnay editcray itay ereway erethay otnay omethingsay inay uthtray
ichwhay, oweverhay onderfulway, orcesfay onvictioncay. Ethay orystay isay ootay onnectedcay otay
ebay istakenmay orfay aay eamdray, anday Iay avehay onay otivemay orfay alsehoodfay.” Myay
annermay asay Iay usthay addresseday imhay asway impressiveay utbay almcay; Iay adhay ormedfay inay myay
ownay earthay aay esolutionray otay ursuepay myay estroyerday otay eathday, anday isthay urposepay
uietedqay myay agonyay anday orfay anay intervalay econciledray emay otay ifelay. Iay ownay elatedray
myay istoryhay ieflybray utbay ithway irmnessfay anday ecisionpray, arkingmay ethay atesday ithway
accuracyay anday evernay eviatingday intoay invectiveay oray exclamationay.

Ethay agistratemay appeareday atay irstfay erfectlypay incredulousay, utbay asay Iay ontinuedcay
ehay ecamebay oremay attentiveay anday interesteday; Iay awsay imhay ometimessay uddershay ithway
orrorhay; atay othersay aay ivelylay urprisesay, unmingleday ithway isbeliefday, asway aintedpay
onay ishay ountenancecay.

Enwhay Iay adhay oncludedcay myay arrationnay, Iay aidsay, is“thay isay ethay eingbay omwhay Iay
accuseay anday orfay osewhay eizuresay anday unishmentpay Iay allcay uponay ouyay otay exertay ouryay
olewhay owerpay. Itay isay ouryay utyday asay aay agistratemay, anday Iay elievebay anday opehay atthay
ouryay eelingsfay asay aay anmay illway otnay evoltray omfray ethay executionay ofay osethay
unctionsfay onay isthay occasionay.”

Isthay addressay ausedcay aay onsiderablecay angechay inay ethay iognomyphysay ofay myay ownay
auditoray. Ehay adhay eardhay myay orystay ithway atthay alfhay indkay ofay eliefbay atthay isay ivengay
otay aay aletay ofay iritsspay anday upernaturalsay eventsay; utbay enwhay ehay asway alledcay uponay
otay actay officiallyay inay onsequencecay, ethay olewhay idetay ofay ishay incredulityay
eturnedray. Ehay, oweverhay, answereday ildlymay, I“ay ouldway illinglyway afforday ouyay
everyay aiday inay ouryay ursuitpay, utbay ethay eaturecray ofay omwhay ouyay eakspay appearsay otay
avehay owerspay ichwhay ouldway utpay allay myay exertionsay otay efianceday. Owhay ancay ollowfay anay
animalay ichwhay ancay aversetray ethay easay ofay iceay anday inhabitay avescay anday ensday erewhay
onay anmay ouldway enturevay otay intrudeay? Esidesbay, omesay onthsmay avehay elapseday incesay
ethay ommissioncay ofay ishay imescray, anday onay oneay ancay onjecturecay otay atwhay aceplay ehay
ashay anderedway oray atwhay egionray ehay aymay ownay inhabitay.”

I“ay oday otnay oubtday atthay ehay overshay earnay ethay otspay ichwhay Iay inhabitay, anday ifay
ehay ashay indeeday akentay efugeray inay ethay Alpsay, ehay aymay ebay untedhay ikelay ethay amoischay
anday estroyedday asay aay eastbay ofay eypray. Utbay Iay erceivepay ouryay oughtsthay; ouyay oday otnay
editcray myay arrativenay anday oday otnay intenday otay ursuepay myay enemyay ithway ethay
unishmentpay ichwhay isay ishay esertday.”

Asay Iay okespay, ageray arkledspay inay myay eyesay; ethay agistratemay asway intimidateday.
ou“yay areay istakenmay,” aidsay ehay. I“ay illway exertay elfmysay, anday ifay
itay isay inay myay owerpay otay eizesay ethay onstermay, ebay assureday atthay ehay allshay uffersay
unishmentpay oportionatepray otay ishay imescray. Utbay Iay earfay, omfray atwhay ouyay avehay
ourselfyay escribedday otay ebay ishay opertiespray, atthay isthay illway ovepray
impracticableay; anday usthay, ilewhay everyay operpray easuremay isay ursuedpay, ouyay ouldshay
akemay upay ouryay indmay otay isappointmentday.”

at“thay annotcay ebay; utbay allay atthay Iay ancay aysay illway ebay ofay ittlelay availay. Myay
evengeray isay ofay onay omentmay otay ouyay; etyay, ilewhay Iay alloway itay otay ebay aay icevay, Iay
onfesscay atthay itay isay ethay evouringday anday onlyay assionpay ofay myay oulsay. Myay ageray
isay unspeakableay enwhay Iay eflectray atthay ethay urderermay, omwhay Iay avehay urnedtay
ooselay uponay ocietysay, illstay existsay. Ouyay efuseray myay ustjay emandday; Iay avehay
utbay oneay esourceray, anday Iay evoteday elfmysay, eitheray inay myay ifelay oray eathday, otay
ishay estructionday.”

Iay embledtray ithway excessay ofay agitationay asay Iay aidsay isthay; erethay asway aay enzyfray
inay myay annermay, anday omethingsay, Iay oubtday otnay, ofay atthay aughtyhay iercenessfay
ichwhay ethay artyrsmay ofay olday areay aidsay otay avehay ossessedpay. Utbay otay aay Enevangay
agistratemay, osewhay indmay asway occupieday byay arfay otheray ideasay anthay osethay ofay
evotionday anday eroismhay, isthay elevationay ofay indmay adhay uchmay ethay appearanceay ofay
adnessmay. Ehay endeavoureday otay oothesay emay asay aay ursenay oesday aay ildchay anday
evertedray otay myay aletay asay ethay effectsay ofay eliriumday.

an“may,” Iay iedcray, ow“hay ignorantay artay outhay inay thyay idepray ofay
isdomway! Easecay; ouyay owknay otnay atwhay itay isay ouyay aysay.”

Iay okebray omfray ethay ousehay angryay anday isturbedday anday etiredray otay editatemay onay
omesay otheray odemay ofay actionay.




Apterchay 24ay


Myay esentpray ituationsay asway oneay inay ichwhay allay oluntaryvay oughtthay asway
allowedsway upay anday ostlay. Iay asway urriedhay awayay byay uryfay; evengeray aloneay
endoweday emay ithway engthstray anday omposurecay; itay ouldedmay myay eelingsfay anday
alloweday emay otay ebay alculatingcay anday almcay atay eriodspay enwhay otherwiseay
eliriumday oray eathday ouldway avehay eenbay myay ortionpay.

Myay irstfay esolutionray asway otay uitqay Enevagay orfay everay; myay ountrycay, ichwhay, enwhay Iay
asway appyhay anday elovedbay, asway earday otay emay, ownay, inay myay adversityay, ecamebay
atefulhay. Iay ovidedpray elfmysay ithway aay umsay ofay oneymay, ogethertay ithway aay ewfay ewelsjay
ichwhay adhay elongedbay otay myay othermay, anday epartedday.

Anday ownay myay anderingsway eganbay ichwhay areay otay easecay utbay ithway ifelay. Iay avehay
aversedtray aay astvay ortionpay ofay ethay earthay anday avehay endureday allay ethay ardshipshay
ichwhay avellerstray inay esertsday anday arbarousbay ountriescay areay ontway otay eetmay. Owhay Iay
avehay ivedlay Iay ardlyhay owknay; anymay imestay avehay Iay etchedstray myay ailingfay imbslay uponay
ethay andysay ainplay anday ayedpray orfay eathday. Utbay evengeray eptkay emay aliveay; Iay aredday
otnay ieday anday eavelay myay adversaryay inay eingbay.

Enwhay Iay uittedqay Enevagay myay irstfay abourlay asway otay aingay omesay ueclay byay ichwhay Iay
ightmay acetray ethay epsstay ofay myay iendishfay enemyay. Utbay myay anplay asway unsettleday,
anday Iay anderedway anymay ourshay oundray ethay onfinescay ofay ethay owntay, uncertainay
atwhay athpay Iay ouldshay ursuepay. Asay ightnay approacheday Iay oundfay elfmysay atay ethay
entranceay ofay ethay emeterycay erewhay Illiamway, Elizabethay, anday myay atherfay
eposedray. Iay entereday itay anday approacheday ethay ombtay ichwhay arkedmay eirthay
avesgray. Everythingay asway ilentsay exceptay ethay eaveslay ofay ethay eestray, ichwhay
ereway entlygay agitateday byay ethay indway; ethay ightnay asway earlynay arkday, anday ethay
enescay ouldway avehay eenbay olemnsay anday affectingay evenay otay anay uninteresteday
observeray. Ethay iritsspay ofay ethay epartedday eemedsay otay itflay arounday anday otay
astcay aay adowshay, ichwhay asway eltfay utbay otnay eensay, arounday ethay eadhay ofay ethay
ournermay.

Ethay eepday iefgray ichwhay isthay enescay adhay atay irstfay exciteday uicklyqay avegay ayway otay
ageray anday espairday. Eythay ereway eadday, anday Iay ivedlay; eirthay urderermay alsoay ivedlay,
anday otay estroyday imhay Iay ustmay agdray outay myay earyway existenceay. Iay eltknay onay ethay assgray
anday issedkay ethay earthay anday ithway uiveringqay ipslay exclaimeday, “byay ethay
acredsay earthay onay ichwhay Iay eelknay, byay ethay adesshay atthay anderway earnay emay, byay ethay
eepday anday eternalay iefgray atthay Iay eelfay, Iay earsway; anday byay eethay, Oay Ightnay, anday ethay
iritsspay atthay esidepray overay eethay, otay ursuepay ethay ondæmay owhay ausedcay isthay iserymay,
untilay ehay oray Iay allshay erishpay inay ortalmay onflictcay. Orfay isthay urposepay Iay illway
eservepray myay ifelay; otay executeay isthay earday evengeray illway Iay againay eholdbay ethay unsay
anday eadtray ethay eengray erbagehay ofay earthay, ichwhay otherwiseay ouldshay anishvay omfray myay
eyesay orfay everay. Anday Iay allcay onay ouyay, iritsspay ofay ethay eadday, anday onay ouyay, anderingway
inistersmay ofay engeancevay, otay aiday anday onductcay emay inay myay orkway. Etlay ethay ursedcay
anday ellishhay onstermay inkdray eepday ofay agonyay; etlay imhay eelfay ethay espairday atthay ownay
ormentstay emay.”

Iay adhay egunbay myay adjurationay ithway olemnitysay anday anay aweay ichwhay almostay assureday emay
atthay ethay adesshay ofay myay urderedmay iendsfray eardhay anday approveday myay evotionday, utbay
ethay uriesfay ossessedpay emay asay Iay oncludedcay, anday ageray okedchay myay utteranceay.

Iay asway answereday oughthray ethay illnessstay ofay ightnay byay aay oudlay anday iendishfay
aughlay. Itay angray onay myay earsay onglay anday eavilyhay; ethay ountainsmay e-echoedclay
itay, anday Iay eltfay asay ifay allay ellhay urroundedsay emay ithway ockerymay anday aughterlay.
Urelysay inay atthay omentmay Iay ouldshay avehay eenbay ossessedpay byay enzyfray anday avehay
estroyedday myay iserablemay existenceay utbay atthay myay owvay asway eardhay anday atthay Iay
asway eservedray orfay engeancevay. Ethay aughterlay iedday awayay, enwhay aay ell-knownclay
anday abhorreday oicevay, apparentlyay oseclay otay myay earay, addresseday emay inay anay
audibleay isperwhay, I“ay amay atisfiedsay, iserablemay etchwray! Ouyay avehay
eterminedday otay ivelay, anday Iay amay atisfiedsay.”

Iay artedday owardstay ethay otspay omfray ichwhay ethay oundsay oceededpray, utbay ethay evilday
eludeday myay aspgray. Uddenlysay ethay oadbray iskday ofay ethay oonmay aroseay anday oneshay
ullfay uponay ishay astlyghay anday istortedday apeshay asay ehay edflay ithway oremay anthay
ortalmay eedspay.

Iay ursuedpay imhay, anday orfay anymay onthsmay isthay ashay eenbay myay asktay. Uidedgay byay aay
ightslay ueclay, Iay ollowedfay ethay indingsway ofay ethay Onerhay, utbay ainlyvay. Ethay
ueblay Editerraneanmay appeareday, anday byay aay angestray ancechay, Iay awsay ethay iendfay
enteray byay ightnay anday idehay imselfhay inay aay esselvay oundbay orfay ethay Ackblay Easay. Iay
ooktay myay assagepay inay ethay amesay ipshay, utbay ehay escapeday, Iay owknay otnay owhay.

Amidstay ethay ildsway ofay Artarytay anday Ussiaray, althoughay ehay illstay evadeday emay, Iay
avehay everay ollowedfay inay ishay acktray. Ometimessay ethay easantspay, aredscay byay
isthay orridhay apparitionay, informeday emay ofay ishay athpay; ometimessay ehay imselfhay,
owhay earedfay atthay ifay Iay ostlay allay acetray ofay imhay Iay ouldshay espairday anday ieday,
eftlay omesay arkmay otay uidegay emay. Ethay owssnay escendedday onay myay eadhay, anday Iay awsay
ethay intpray ofay ishay ugehay epstay onay ethay itewhay ainplay. Otay ouyay irstfay enteringay
onay ifelay, otay omwhay arecay isay ewnay anday agonyay unknownay, owhay ancay ouyay understanday
atwhay Iay avehay eltfay anday illstay eelfay? Oldcay, antway, anday atiguefay ereway ethay
eastlay ainspay ichwhay Iay asway estinedday otay endureay; Iay asway ursedcay byay omesay evilday
anday arriedcay aboutay ithway emay myay eternalay ellhay; etyay illstay aay iritspay ofay oodgay
ollowedfay anday irectedday myay epsstay anday enwhay Iay ostmay urmuredmay ouldway uddenlysay
extricateay emay omfray eeminglysay insurmountableay ifficultiesday. Ometimessay,
enwhay aturenay, overcomeay byay ungerhay, anksay underay ethay exhaustionay, aay epastray
asway eparedpray orfay emay inay ethay esertday atthay estoredray anday inspiriteday emay. Ethay
arefay asway, indeeday, oarsecay, uchsay asay ethay easantspay ofay ethay ountrycay ateay, utbay
Iay illway otnay oubtday atthay itay asway etsay erethay byay ethay iritsspay atthay Iay adhay
invokeday otay aiday emay. Oftenay, enwhay allay asway dryay, ethay eavenshay oudlessclay, anday
Iay asway archedpay byay irstthay, aay ightslay oudclay ouldway edimbay ethay skyay, edshay ethay
ewfay opsdray atthay evivedray emay, anday anishvay.

Iay ollowedfay, enwhay Iay ouldcay, ethay oursescay ofay ethay iversray; utbay ethay ondæmay
enerallygay avoideday esethay, asay itay asway erehay atthay ethay opulationpay ofay ethay
ountrycay ieflychay ollectedcay. Inay otheray acesplay umanhay eingsbay ereway eldomsay
eensay, anday Iay enerallygay ubsistedsay onay ethay ildway animalsay atthay ossedcray myay
athpay. Iay adhay oneymay ithway emay anday ainedgay ethay iendshipfray ofay ethay illagersvay
byay istributingday itay; oray Iay oughtbray ithway emay omesay oodfay atthay Iay adhay illedkay,
ichwhay, afteray akingtay aay allsmay artpay, Iay alwaysay esentedpray otay osethay owhay adhay
ovidedpray emay ithway irefay anday utensilsay orfay ookingcay.

Myay ifelay, asay itay assedpay usthay, asway indeeday atefulhay otay emay, anday itay asway uringday
eepslay aloneay atthay Iay ouldcay astetay oyjay. Oay essedblay eepslay! Oftenay, enwhay ostmay
iserablemay, Iay anksay otay eposeray, anday myay eamsdray ulledlay emay evenay otay aptureray. Ethay
iritsspay atthay uardedgay emay adhay ovidedpray esethay omentsmay, oray atherray ourshay, ofay
appinesshay atthay Iay ightmay etainray engthstray otay ulfilfay myay ilgrimagepay. Eprivedday ofay
isthay espiteray, Iay ouldshay avehay unksay underay myay ardshipshay. Uringday ethay ayday Iay asway
ustainedsay anday inspiriteday byay ethay opehay ofay ightnay, orfay inay eepslay Iay awsay myay
iendsfray, myay ifeway, anday myay elovedbay ountrycay; againay Iay awsay ethay enevolentbay
ountenancecay ofay myay atherfay, eardhay ethay ilversay onestay ofay myay Elizabeth’say
oicevay, anday eheldbay Ervalclay enjoyingay ealthhay anday outhyay. Oftenay, enwhay eariedway byay
aay oilsometay archmay, Iay ersuadedpay elfmysay atthay Iay asway eamingdray untilay ightnay ouldshay
omecay anday atthay Iay ouldshay enthay enjoyay ealityray inay ethay armsay ofay myay earestday
iendsfray. Atwhay agonisingay ondnessfay idday Iay eelfay orfay emthay! Owhay idday Iay ingclay otay
eirthay earday ormsfay, asay ometimessay eythay auntedhay evenay myay akingway ourshay, anday
ersuadepay elfmysay atthay eythay illstay ivedlay! Atay uchsay omentsmay engeancevay, atthay
urnedbay ithinway emay, iedday inay myay earthay, anday Iay ursuedpay myay athpay owardstay ethay
estructionday ofay ethay ondæmay oremay asay aay asktay enjoineday byay eavenhay, asay ethay
echanicalmay impulseay ofay omesay owerpay ofay ichwhay Iay asway unconsciousay, anthay asay ethay
ardentay esireday ofay myay oulsay.

Atwhay ishay eelingsfay ereway omwhay Iay ursuedpay Iay annotcay owknay. Ometimessay, indeeday, ehay
eftlay arksmay inay itingwray onay ethay arksbay ofay ethay eestray oray utcay inay onestay atthay uidedgay
emay anday instigateday myay uryfay. “myay eignray isay otnay etyay
over”—theseay ordsway ereway egiblelay inay oneay ofay esethay
inscriptions—“youay ivelay, anday myay owerpay isay ompletecay. Ollowfay emay; Iay
eeksay ethay everlastingay icesay ofay ethay orthnay, erewhay ouyay illway eelfay ethay iserymay ofay
oldcay anday ostfray, otay ichwhay Iay amay impassiveay. Ouyay illway indfay earnay isthay aceplay, ifay
ouyay ollowfay otnay ootay ardilytay, aay eadday arehay; eatay anday ebay efreshedray. Omecay onay, myay
enemyay; eway avehay etyay otay estlewray orfay ouray iveslay, utbay anymay ardhay anday iserablemay
ourshay ustmay ouyay endureay untilay atthay eriodpay allshay arriveay.”

Offingscay evilday! Againay oday Iay owvay engeancevay; againay oday Iay evoteday eethay,
iserablemay iendfay, otay orturetay anday eathday. Evernay illway Iay ivegay upay myay earchsay
untilay ehay oray Iay erishpay; anday enthay ithway atwhay ecstasyay allshay Iay oinjay myay
Elizabethay anday myay epartedday iendsfray, owhay evenay ownay eparepray orfay emay ethay
ewardray ofay myay edioustay oiltay anday orriblehay ilgrimagepay!

Asay Iay illstay ursuedpay myay ourneyjay otay ethay orthwardnay, ethay owssnay ickenedthay anday ethay
oldcay increaseday inay aay egreeday almostay ootay everesay otay upportsay. Ethay easantspay ereway
utshay upay inay eirthay ovelshay, anday onlyay aay ewfay ofay ethay ostmay ardyhay enturedvay orthfay otay
eizesay ethay animalsay omwhay arvationstay adhay orcedfay omfray eirthay iding-placesclay otay
eeksay orfay eypray. Ethay iversray ereway overedcay ithway iceay, anday onay ishfay ouldcay ebay
ocuredpray; anday usthay Iay asway utcay offay omfray myay iefchay articleay ofay aintenancemay.

Ethay iumphtray ofay myay enemyay increaseday ithway ethay ifficultyday ofay myay abourslay. Oneay
inscriptionay atthay ehay eftlay asway inay esethay ordsway: epare“pray! Ouryay oilstay
onlyay eginbay; apwray ourselfyay inay ursfay anday ovidepray oodfay, orfay eway allshay oonsay enteray
uponay aay ourneyjay erewhay ouryay ufferingssay illway atisfysay myay everlastingay
atredhay.”

Myay ouragecay anday erseverancepay ereway invigorateday byay esethay offingscay ordsway; Iay
esolvedray otnay otay ailfay inay myay urposepay, anday allingcay onay Eavenhay otay upportsay
emay, Iay ontinuedcay ithway unabateday ervourfay otay aversetray immenseay esertsday,
untilay ethay oceanay appeareday atay aay istanceday anday ormedfay ethay utmostay oundarybay
ofay ethay orizonhay. Ohay! Owhay unlikeay itay asway otay ethay ueblay easonssay ofay ethay
outhsay! Overedcay ithway iceay, itay asway onlyay otay ebay istinguishedday omfray andlay byay
itsay uperiorsay ildnessway anday uggednessray. Ethay Eeksgray eptway orfay oyjay enwhay
eythay eheldbay ethay Editerraneanmay omfray ethay illshay ofay Asiaay, anday ailedhay ithway
aptureray ethay oundarybay ofay eirthay oilstay. Iay idday otnay eepway, utbay Iay eltknay ownday
anday ithway aay ullfay earthay ankedthay myay uidinggay iritspay orfay onductingcay emay inay
afetysay otay ethay aceplay erewhay Iay opedhay, otwithstandingnay myay adversary’say ibegay,
otay eetmay anday applegray ithway imhay.

Omesay eeksway eforebay isthay eriodpay Iay adhay ocuredpray aay edgeslay anday ogsday anday usthay
aversedtray ethay owssnay ithway inconceivableay eedspay. Iay owknay otnay etherwhay ethay
iendfay ossessedpay ethay amesay advantagesay, utbay Iay oundfay atthay, asay eforebay Iay adhay
ailyday ostlay oundgray inay ethay ursuitpay, Iay ownay ainedgay onay imhay, osay uchmay osay atthay
enwhay Iay irstfay awsay ethay oceanay ehay asway utbay oneay ay’sday ourneyjay inay advanceay, anday
Iay opedhay otay interceptay imhay eforebay ehay ouldshay eachray ethay eachbay. Ithway ewnay
ouragecay, ereforethay, Iay essedpray onay, anday inay otway aysday arriveday atay aay etchedwray
amlethay onay ethay eashoresay. Iay inquireday ofay ethay inhabitantsay oncerningcay ethay
iendfay anday ainedgay accurateay informationay. Aay iganticgay onstermay, eythay aidsay,
adhay arriveday ethay ightnay eforebay, armeday ithway aay ungay anday anymay istolspay,
uttingpay otay ightflay ethay inhabitantsay ofay aay olitarysay ottagecay oughthray earfay ofay
ishay errifictay appearanceay. Ehay adhay arriedcay offay eirthay orestay ofay interway
oodfay, anday acingplay itay inay aay edgeslay, otay awdray ichwhay ehay adhay eizedsay onay aay
umerousnay ovedray ofay ainedtray ogsday, ehay adhay arnessedhay emthay, anday ethay amesay
ightnay, otay ethay oyjay ofay ethay orror-struckclay illagersvay, adhay ursuedpay ishay
ourneyjay acrossay ethay easay inay aay irectionday atthay edlay otay onay andlay; anday eythay
onjecturedcay atthay ehay ustmay eedilyspay ebay estroyedday byay ethay eakingbray ofay ethay
iceay oray ozenfray byay ethay eternalay ostsfray.

Onay earinghay isthay informationay Iay ufferedsay aay emporarytay accessay ofay espairday.
Ehay adhay escapeday emay, anday Iay ustmay ommencecay aay estructiveday anday almostay endlessay
ourneyjay acrossay ethay ountainousmay icesay ofay ethay oceanay, amidstay oldcay atthay ewfay
ofay ethay inhabitantsay ouldcay onglay endureay anday ichwhay Iay, ethay ativenay ofay aay
enialgay anday unnysay imateclay, ouldcay otnay opehay otay urvivesay. Etyay atay ethay ideaay
atthay ethay iendfay ouldshay ivelay anday ebay iumphanttray, myay ageray anday engeancevay
eturnedray, anday ikelay aay ightymay idetay, overwhelmeday everyay otheray eelingfay.
Afteray aay ightslay eposeray, uringday ichwhay ethay iritsspay ofay ethay eadday overedhay
oundray anday instigateday emay otay oiltay anday evengeray, Iay eparedpray orfay myay ourneyjay.

Iay exchangeday myay and-sledgeclay orfay oneay ashionedfay orfay ethay inequalitiesay ofay
ethay Ozenfray Oceanay, anday urchasingpay aay entifulplay ockstay ofay ovisionspray, Iay
epartedday omfray andlay.

Iay annotcay uessgay owhay anymay aysday avehay assedpay incesay enthay, utbay Iay avehay endureday
iserymay ichwhay othingnay utbay ethay eternalay entimentsay ofay aay ustjay etributionray
urningbay ithinway myay earthay ouldcay avehay enableday emay otay upportsay. Immenseay anday
uggedray ountainsmay ofay iceay oftenay arredbay upay myay assagepay, anday Iay oftenay eardhay
ethay underthay ofay ethay oundgray easay, ichwhay eatenedthray myay estructionday. Utbay
againay ethay ostfray amecay anday ademay ethay athspay ofay ethay easay ecuresay.

Byay ethay uantityqay ofay ovisionpray ichwhay Iay adhay onsumedcay, Iay ouldshay uessgay atthay
Iay adhay assedpay eethray eeksway inay isthay ourneyjay; anday ethay ontinualcay otractionpray
ofay opehay, eturningray ackbay uponay ethay earthay, oftenay ungwray itterbay opsdray ofay
espondencyday anday iefgray omfray myay eyesay. Espairday adhay indeeday almostay ecuredsay
erhay eypray, anday Iay ouldshay oonsay avehay unksay eneathbay isthay iserymay. Onceay, afteray
ethay oorpay animalsay atthay onveyedcay emay adhay ithway incredibleay oiltay ainedgay ethay
ummitsay ofay aay opingslay iceay ountainmay, anday oneay, inkingsay underay ishay atiguefay,
iedday, Iay iewedvay ethay expanseay eforebay emay ithway anguishay, enwhay uddenlysay myay eyeay
aughtcay aay arkday eckspay uponay ethay uskyday ainplay. Iay ainedstray myay ightsay otay
iscoverday atwhay itay ouldcay ebay anday uttereday aay ildway cryay ofay ecstasyay enwhay Iay
istinguishedday aay edgeslay anday ethay istortedday oportionspray ofay aay ell-knownclay
ormfay ithinway. Ohay! Ithway atwhay aay urningbay ushgay idday opehay evisitray myay earthay!
Armway earstay illedfay myay eyesay, ichwhay Iay astilyhay ipedway awayay, atthay eythay ightmay
otnay interceptay ethay iewvay Iay adhay ofay ethay ondæmay; utbay illstay myay ightsay asway
immedday byay ethay urningbay opsdray, untilay, ivinggay ayway otay ethay emotionsay atthay
oppresseday emay, Iay eptway alouday.

Utbay isthay asway otnay ethay imetay orfay elayday; Iay isencumberedday ethay ogsday ofay eirthay
eadday ompanioncay, avegay emthay aay entifulplay ortionpay ofay oodfay, anday afteray anay
our’shay estray, ichwhay asway absolutelyay ecessarynay, anday etyay ichwhay asway itterlybay
irksomeay otay emay, Iay ontinuedcay myay outeray. Ethay edgeslay asway illstay isiblevay, ornay
idday Iay againay oselay ightsay ofay itay exceptay atay ethay omentsmay enwhay orfay aay ortshay
imetay omesay ice-rockclay oncealedcay itay ithway itsay interveningay agscray. Iay indeeday
erceptiblypay ainedgay onay itay, anday enwhay, afteray earlynay otway aysday’ ourneyjay, Iay
eheldbay myay enemyay atay onay oremay anthay aay ilemay istantday, myay earthay oundedbay ithinway
emay.

Utbay ownay, enwhay Iay appeareday almostay ithinway aspgray ofay myay oefay, myay opeshay ereway
uddenlysay extinguisheday, anday Iay ostlay allay acetray ofay imhay oremay utterlyay anthay Iay adhay
everay oneday eforebay. Aay oundgray easay asway eardhay; ethay underthay ofay itsay ogresspray, asay
ethay atersway olledray anday elledsway eneathbay emay, ecamebay everyay omentmay oremay ominousay
anday errifictay. Iay essedpray onay, utbay inay ainvay. Ethay indway aroseay; ethay easay oaredray;
anday, asay ithway ethay ightymay ockshay ofay anay earthquakeay, itay itsplay anday ackedcray ithway aay
emendoustray anday overwhelmingay oundsay. Ethay orkway asway oonsay inishedfay; inay aay ewfay
inutesmay aay umultuoustay easay olledray etweenbay emay anday myay enemyay, anday Iay asway eftlay
iftingdray onay aay atteredscay iecepay ofay iceay atthay asway ontinuallycay esseninglay anday
usthay eparingpray orfay emay aay ideoushay eathday.

Inay isthay annermay anymay appallingay ourshay assedpay; everalsay ofay myay ogsday iedday, anday Iay
elfmysay asway aboutay otay inksay underay ethay accumulationay ofay istressday enwhay Iay awsay ouryay
esselvay idingray atay anchoray anday oldinghay orthfay otay emay opeshay ofay uccoursay anday ifelay.
Iay adhay onay onceptioncay atthay esselsvay everay amecay osay arfay orthnay anday asway astoundeday
atay ethay ightsay. Iay uicklyqay estroyedday artpay ofay myay edgeslay otay onstructcay oarsay, anday
byay esethay eansmay asway enableday, ithway infiniteay atiguefay, otay ovemay myay iceay aftray inay
ethay irectionday ofay ouryay ipshay. Iay adhay eterminedday, ifay ouyay ereway oinggay outhwardssay,
illstay otay usttray elfmysay otay ethay ercymay ofay ethay eassay atherray anthay abandonay myay
urposepay. Iay opedhay otay induceay ouyay otay antgray emay aay oatbay ithway ichwhay Iay ouldcay ursuepay
myay enemyay. Utbay ouryay irectionday asway orthwardsnay. Ouyay ooktay emay onay oardbay enwhay myay
igourvay asway exhausteday, anday Iay ouldshay oonsay avehay unksay underay myay ultipliedmay
ardshipshay intoay aay eathday ichwhay Iay illstay eaddray, orfay myay asktay isay unfulfilleday.

Ohay! Enwhay illway myay uidinggay iritspay, inay onductingcay emay otay ethay ondæmay, alloway
emay ethay estray Iay osay uchmay esireday; oray ustmay Iay ieday, anday ehay etyay ivelay? Ifay Iay oday,
earsway otay emay, Altonway, atthay ehay allshay otnay escapeay, atthay ouyay illway eeksay imhay
anday atisfysay myay engeancevay inay ishay eathday. Anday oday Iay areday otay askay ofay ouyay otay
undertakeay myay ilgrimagepay, otay endureay ethay ardshipshay atthay Iay avehay undergoneay?
Onay; Iay amay otnay osay elfishsay. Etyay, enwhay Iay amay eadday, ifay ehay ouldshay appearay, ifay
ethay inistersmay ofay engeancevay ouldshay onductcay imhay otay ouyay, earsway atthay ehay
allshay otnay ive—swearlay atthay ehay allshay otnay iumphtray overay myay accumulateday
oesway anday urvivesay otay adday otay ethay istlay ofay ishay arkday imescray. Ehay isay eloquentay
anday ersuasivepay, anday onceay ishay ordsway adhay evenay owerpay overay myay earthay; utbay
usttray imhay otnay. Ishay oulsay isay asay ellishhay asay ishay ormfay, ullfay ofay eacherytray
anday iend-likeclay alicemay. Earhay imhay otnay; allcay onay ethay amesnay ofay Illiamway,
Ustinejay, Ervalclay, Elizabethay, myay atherfay, anday ofay ethay etchedwray Ictorvay, anday
ustthray ouryay ordsway intoay ishay earthay. Iay illway overhay earnay anday irectday ethay
eelstay arightay.

Altonway, in_ay ontinuationcay._


Augustay 26thay, 17ay—.


Ouyay avehay eadray isthay angestray anday errifictay orystay, Argaretmay; anday oday ouyay otnay
eelfay ouryay oodblay ongealcay ithway orrorhay, ikelay atthay ichwhay evenay ownay urdlescay
inemay? Ometimessay, eizedsay ithway uddensay agonyay, ehay ouldcay otnay ontinuecay ishay
aletay; atay othersay, ishay oicevay okenbray, etyay iercingpay, uttereday ithway
ifficultyday ethay ordsway osay epleteray ithway anguishay. Ishay inefay anday ovelylay eyesay
ereway ownay ightedlay upay ithway indignationay, ownay ubduedsay otay owncastday orrowsay
anday uenchedqay inay infiniteay etchednesswray. Ometimessay ehay ommandedcay ishay
ountenancecay anday onestay anday elatedray ethay ostmay orriblehay incidentsay ithway aay
anquiltray oicevay, uppressingsay everyay arkmay ofay agitationay; enthay, ikelay aay
olcanovay urstingbay orthfay, ishay acefay ouldway uddenlysay angechay otay anay expressionay
ofay ethay ildestway ageray asay ehay iekedshray outay imprecationsay onay ishay ersecutorpay.

Ishay aletay isay onnectedcay anday oldtay ithway anay appearanceay ofay ethay implestsay uthtray,
etyay Iay ownay otay ouyay atthay ethay etterslay ofay Elixfay anday Afiesay, ichwhay ehay owedshay emay,
anday ethay apparitionay ofay ethay onstermay eensay omfray ouray ipshay, oughtbray otay emay aay
eatergray onvictioncay ofay ethay uthtray ofay ishay arrativenay anthay ishay asseverationsay,
oweverhay earnestay anday onnectedcay. Uchsay aay onstermay ashay, enthay, eallyray existenceay!
Iay annotcay oubtday itay, etyay Iay amay ostlay inay urprisesay anday admirationay. Ometimessay Iay
endeavoureday otay aingay omfray Ankensteinfray ethay articularspay ofay ishay
eature’scray ormationfay, utbay onay isthay ointpay ehay asway impenetrableay.

Are“ay ouyay admay, myay iendfray?” aidsay ehay. Or“ay itherwhay oesday ouryay
enselesssay uriositycay eadlay ouyay? Ouldway ouyay alsoay eatecray orfay ourselfyay anday ethay
orldway aay emoniacalday enemyay? Eacepay, eacepay! Earnlay myay iseriesmay anday oday otnay eeksay
otay increaseay ouryay ownay.”

Ankensteinfray iscoveredday atthay Iay ademay otesnay oncerningcay ishay istoryhay; ehay askeday
otay eesay emthay anday enthay imselfhay orrectedcay anday augmenteday emthay inay anymay acesplay,
utbay incipallypray inay ivinggay ethay ifelay anday iritspay otay ethay onversationscay ehay eldhay
ithway ishay enemyay. ince“say ouyay avehay eservedpray myay arrationnay,” aidsay
ehay, I“ay ouldway otnay atthay aay utilatedmay oneay ouldshay ogay ownday otay
osteritypay.”

Usthay ashay aay eekway assedpay awayay, ilewhay Iay avehay istenedlay otay ethay angeststray
aletay atthay everay imaginationay ormedfay. Myay oughtsthay anday everyay eelingfay ofay myay
oulsay avehay eenbay unkdray upay byay ethay interestay orfay myay uestgay ichwhay isthay aletay
anday ishay ownay elevateday anday entlegay annersmay avehay eatedcray. Iay ishway otay oothesay
imhay, etyay ancay Iay ounselcay oneay osay infinitelyay iserablemay, osay estituteday ofay
everyay opehay ofay onsolationcay, otay ivelay? Ohay, onay! Ethay onlyay oyjay atthay ehay ancay
ownay owknay illway ebay enwhay ehay omposescay ishay atteredshay iritspay otay eacepay anday
eathday. Etyay ehay enjoysay oneay omfortcay, ethay offspringay ofay olitudesay anday
eliriumday; ehay elievesbay atthay enwhay inay eamsdray ehay oldshay onversecay ithway ishay
iendsfray anday erivesday omfray atthay ommunioncay onsolationcay orfay ishay iseriesmay oray
excitementsay otay ishay engeancevay, atthay eythay areay otnay ethay eationscray ofay ishay
ancyfay, utbay ethay eingsbay emselvesthay owhay isitvay imhay omfray ethay egionsray ofay aay
emoteray orldway. Isthay aithfay ivesgay aay olemnitysay otay ishay everiesray atthay enderray
emthay otay emay almostay asay imposingay anday interestingay asay uthtray.

Ouray onversationscay areay otnay alwaysay onfinedcay otay ishay ownay istoryhay anday
isfortunesmay. Onay everyay ointpay ofay eneralgay iteraturelay ehay isplaysday
unboundeday owledgeknay anday aay uickqay anday iercingpay apprehensionay. Ishay
eloquenceay isay orciblefay anday ouchingtay; ornay ancay Iay earhay imhay, enwhay ehay elatesray
aay atheticpay incidentay oray endeavoursay otay ovemay ethay assionspay ofay itypay oray ovelay,
ithoutway earstay. Atwhay aay oriousglay eaturecray ustmay ehay avehay eenbay inay ethay aysday
ofay ishay osperitypray, enwhay ehay isay usthay oblenay anday odlikegay inay uinray! Ehay eemssay
otay eelfay ishay ownay orthway anday ethay eatnessgray ofay ishay allfay.

en“whay oungeryay,” aidsay ehay, I“ay elievedbay elfmysay estinedday orfay
omesay eatgray enterpriseay. Myay eelingsfay areay ofoundpray, utbay Iay ossessedpay aay oolnesscay
ofay udgmentjay atthay ittedfay emay orfay illustriousay achievementsay. Isthay entimentsay ofay
ethay orthway ofay myay aturenay upportedsay emay enwhay othersay ouldway avehay eenbay oppresseday,
orfay Iay eemedday itay iminalcray otay owthray awayay inay uselessay iefgray osethay alentstay atthay
ightmay ebay usefulay otay myay ellowfay eaturescray. Enwhay Iay eflectedray onay ethay orkway Iay adhay
ompletedcay, onay esslay aay oneay anthay ethay eationcray ofay aay ensitivesay anday ationalray
animalay, Iay ouldcay otnay ankray elfmysay ithway ethay erdhay ofay ommoncay ojectorspray. Utbay
isthay oughtthay, ichwhay upportedsay emay inay ethay ommencementcay ofay myay areercay, ownay
ervessay onlyay otay ungeplay emay owerlay inay ethay ustday. Allay myay eculationsspay anday opeshay
areay asay othingnay, anday ikelay ethay archangelay owhay aspireday otay omnipotenceay, Iay amay
ainedchay inay anay eternalay ellhay. Myay imaginationay asway ividvay, etyay myay owerspay ofay
analysisay anday applicationay ereway intenseay; byay ethay unionay ofay esethay ualitiesqay Iay
onceivedcay ethay ideaay anday executeday ethay eationcray ofay aay anmay. Evenay ownay Iay annotcay
ecollectray ithoutway assionpay myay everiesray ilewhay ethay orkway asway incompleteay. Iay odtray
eavenhay inay myay oughtsthay, ownay exultingay inay myay owerspay, ownay urningbay ithway ethay ideaay
ofay eirthay effectsay. Omfray myay infancyay Iay asway imbueday ithway ighhay opeshay anday aay oftylay
ambitionay; utbay owhay amay Iay unksay! Ohay! Myay iendfray, ifay ouyay adhay ownknay emay asay Iay onceay
asway, ouyay ouldway otnay ecogniseray emay inay isthay atestay ofay egradationday. Espondencyday
arelyray isitedvay myay earthay; aay ighhay estinyday eemedsay otay earbay emay onay, untilay Iay ellfay,
evernay, evernay againay otay iseray.”

Ustmay Iay enthay oselay isthay admirableay eingbay? Iay avehay ongedlay orfay aay iendfray; Iay avehay
oughtsay oneay owhay ouldway athisesympay ithway anday ovelay emay. Eholdbay, onay esethay esertday
eassay Iay avehay oundfay uchsay aay oneay, utbay Iay earfay Iay avehay ainedgay imhay onlyay otay owknay ishay
aluevay anday oselay imhay. Iay ouldway econcileray imhay otay ifelay, utbay ehay epulsesray ethay ideaay.

I“ay ankthay ouyay, Altonway,” ehay aidsay, or“fay ouryay indkay intentionsay owardstay osay
iserablemay aay etchwray; utbay enwhay ouyay eakspay ofay ewnay iestay anday eshfray
affectionsay, inkthay ouyay atthay anyay ancay eplaceray osethay owhay areay onegay? Ancay anyay
anmay ebay otay emay asay Ervalclay asway, oray anyay omanway anotheray Elizabethay? Evenay
erewhay ethay affectionsay areay otnay onglystray ovedmay byay anyay uperiorsay excellenceay,
ethay ompanionscay ofay ouray ildhoodchay alwaysay ossesspay aay ertaincay owerpay overay ouray
indsmay ichwhay ardlyhay anyay aterlay iendfray ancay obtainay. Eythay owknay ouray
infantineay ispositionsday, ichwhay, oweverhay eythay aymay ebay afterwardsay odifiedmay,
areay evernay eradicateday; anday eythay ancay udgejay ofay ouray actionsay ithway oremay
ertaincay onclusionscay asay otay ethay integrityay ofay ouray otivesmay. Aay istersay oray aay
otherbray ancay evernay, unlessay indeeday uchsay omssymptay avehay eenbay ownshay earlyay,
uspectsay ethay otheray ofay audfray oray alsefay ealingday, enwhay anotheray iendfray,
oweverhay onglystray ehay aymay ebay attacheday, aymay, inay itespay ofay imselfhay, ebay
ontemplatedcay ithway uspicionsay. Utbay Iay enjoyeday iendsfray, earday otnay onlyay
oughthray abithay anday associationay, utbay omfray eirthay ownay eritsmay; anday ereverwhay
Iay amay, ethay oothingsay oicevay ofay myay Elizabethay anday ethay onversationcay ofay
Ervalclay illway ebay everay isperedwhay inay myay earay. Eythay areay eadday, anday utbay oneay
eelingfay inay uchsay aay olitudesay ancay ersuadepay emay otay eservepray myay ifelay. Ifay Iay
ereway engageday inay anyay ighhay undertakingay oray esignday, aughtfray ithway extensiveay
utilityay otay myay ellowfay eaturescray, enthay ouldcay Iay ivelay otay ulfilfay itay. Utbay
uchsay isay otnay myay estinyday; Iay ustmay ursuepay anday estroyday ethay eingbay otay omwhay Iay
avegay existenceay; enthay myay otlay onay earthay illway ebay ulfilledfay anday Iay aymay ieday.”

Myay elovedbay Istersay,

Eptembersay 2day.


Iay itewray otay ouyay, encompasseday byay erilpay anday ignorantay etherwhay Iay amay everay
oomedday otay eesay againay earday Englanday anday ethay earerday iendsfray atthay inhabitay
itay. Iay amay urroundedsay byay ountainsmay ofay iceay ichwhay admitay ofay onay escapeay anday
eatenthray everyay omentmay otay ushcray myay esselvay. Ethay avebray ellowsfay omwhay Iay
avehay ersuadedpay otay ebay myay ompanionscay ooklay owardstay emay orfay aiday, utbay Iay avehay
onenay otay estowbay. Erethay isay omethingsay erriblytay appallingay inay ouray
ituationsay, etyay myay ouragecay anday opeshay oday otnay esertday emay. Etyay itay isay
erribletay otay eflectray atthay ethay iveslay ofay allay esethay enmay areay endangereday
oughthray emay. Ifay eway areay ostlay, myay admay emesschay areay ethay ausecay.

Anday atwhay, Argaretmay, illway ebay ethay atestay ofay ouryay indmay? Ouyay illway otnay earhay ofay myay
estructionday, anday ouyay illway anxiouslyay awaitay myay eturnray. Earsyay illway asspay, anday
ouyay illway avehay isitingsvay ofay espairday anday etyay ebay orturedtay byay opehay. Ohay! Myay
elovedbay istersay, ethay ickeningsay ailingfay ofay ouryay eart-feltclay expectationsay isay,
inay ospectpray, oremay erribletay otay emay anthay myay ownay eathday. Utbay ouyay avehay aay usbandhay
anday ovelylay ildrenchay; ouyay aymay ebay appyhay. Eavenhay essblay ouyay anday akemay ouyay osay!

Myay unfortunateay uestgay egardsray emay ithway ethay enderesttay ompassioncay. Ehay
endeavoursay otay illfay emay ithway opehay anday alkstay asay ifay ifelay ereway aay ossessionpay
ichwhay ehay aluedvay. Ehay emindsray emay owhay oftenay ethay amesay accidentsay avehay
appenedhay otay otheray avigatorsnay owhay avehay attempteday isthay easay, anday inay itespay
ofay elfmysay, ehay illsfay emay ithway eerfulchay auguriesay. Evenay ethay ailorssay eelfay
ethay owerpay ofay ishay eloquenceay; enwhay ehay eaksspay, eythay onay ongerlay espairday; ehay
ousesray eirthay energiesay, anday ilewhay eythay earhay ishay oicevay eythay elievebay esethay
astvay ountainsmay ofay iceay areay ole-hillsclay ichwhay illway anishvay eforebay ethay
esolutionsray ofay anmay. Esethay eelingsfay areay ansitorytray; eachay ayday ofay
expectationay elayedday illsfay emthay ithway earfay, anday Iay almostay eaddray aay utinymay
ausedcay byay isthay espairday.

Eptembersay 5thay.


Aay enescay ashay ustjay assedpay ofay uchsay uncommonay interestay atthay, althoughay itay isay
ighlyhay obablepray atthay esethay aperspay aymay evernay eachray ouyay, etyay Iay annotcay
orbearfay ecordingray itay.

Eway areay illstay urroundedsay byay ountainsmay ofay iceay, illstay inay imminentay angerday
ofay eingbay ushedcray inay eirthay onflictcay. Ethay oldcay isay excessiveay, anday anymay ofay
myay unfortunateay omradescay avehay alreadyay oundfay aay avegray amidstay isthay enescay ofay
esolationday. Ankensteinfray ashay ailyday eclinedday inay ealthhay; aay everishfay irefay
illstay immersglay inay ishay eyesay, utbay ehay isay exhausteday, anday enwhay uddenlysay
ousedray otay anyay exertionay, ehay eedilyspay inkssay againay intoay apparentay
ifelessnesslay.

Iay entionedmay inay myay astlay etterlay ethay earsfay Iay entertaineday ofay aay utinymay.
Isthay orningmay, asay Iay atsay atchingway ethay anway ountenancecay ofay myay iend—hisfray
eyesay alfhay osedclay anday ishay imbslay anginghay istlessly—Ilay asway ousedray byay alfhay
aay ozenday ofay ethay ailorssay, owhay emandedday admissionay intoay ethay abincay. Eythay
entereday, anday eirthay eaderlay addresseday emay. Ehay oldtay emay atthay ehay anday ishay
ompanionscay adhay eenbay osenchay byay ethay otheray ailorssay otay omecay inay eputationday
otay emay otay akemay emay aay equisitionray ichwhay, inay usticejay, Iay ouldcay otnay efuseray.
Eway ereway immureday inay iceay anday ouldshay obablypray evernay escapeay, utbay eythay
earedfay atthay ifay, asay asway ossiblepay, ethay iceay ouldshay issipateday anday aay eefray
assagepay ebay openeday, Iay ouldshay ebay ashray enoughay otay ontinuecay myay oyagevay anday
eadlay emthay intoay eshfray angersday, afteray eythay ightmay appilyhay avehay urmountedsay
isthay. Eythay insisteday, ereforethay, atthay Iay ouldshay engageay ithway aay olemnsay
omisepray atthay ifay ethay esselvay ouldshay ebay eedfray Iay ouldway instantlyay irectday myay
oursecay outhwardssay.

Isthay eechspay oubledtray emay. Iay adhay otnay espairedday, ornay adhay Iay etyay onceivedcay
ethay ideaay ofay eturningray ifay etsay eefray. Etyay ouldcay Iay, inay usticejay, oray evenay inay
ossibilitypay, efuseray isthay emandday? Iay esitatedhay eforebay Iay answereday, enwhay
Ankensteinfray, owhay adhay atay irstfay eenbay ilentsay, anday indeeday appeareday ardlyhay
otay avehay orcefay enoughay otay attenday, ownay ousedray imselfhay; ishay eyesay arkledspay,
anday ishay eekschay ushedflay ithway omentarymay igourvay. Urningtay owardstay ethay enmay,
ehay aidsay,

at“whay oday ouyay eanmay? Atwhay oday ouyay emandday ofay ouryay aptaincay? Areay ouyay, enthay,
osay easilyay urnedtay omfray ouryay esignday? Idday ouyay otnay allcay isthay aay oriousglay
expeditionay? And“ay ereforewhay asway itay oriousglay? Otnay ecausebay ethay ayway asway
oothsmay anday acidplay asay aay outhernsay easay, utbay ecausebay itay asway ullfay ofay angersday anday
errortay, ecausebay atay everyay ewnay incidentay ouryay ortitudefay asway otay ebay alledcay orthfay
anday ouryay ouragecay exhibiteday, ecausebay angerday anday eathday urroundedsay itay, anday
esethay ouyay ereway otay avebray anday overcomeay. Orfay isthay asway itay aay oriousglay, orfay isthay
asway itay anay onourablehay undertakingay. Ouyay ereway ereafterhay otay ebay ailedhay asay ethay
enefactorsbay ofay ouryay eciesspay, ouryay amesnay adoreday asay elongingbay otay avebray enmay
owhay encountereday eathday orfay onourhay anday ethay enefitbay ofay ankindmay. Anday ownay,
eholdbay, ithway ethay irstfay imaginationay ofay angerday, oray, ifay ouyay illway, ethay irstfay
ightymay anday errifictay ialtray ofay ouryay ouragecay, ouyay inkshray awayay anday areay ontentcay
otay ebay andedhay ownday asay enmay owhay adhay otnay engthstray enoughay otay endureay oldcay anday
erilpay; anday osay, oorpay oulssay, eythay ereway illychay anday eturnedray otay eirthay armway
iresidesfay. Whyay, atthay equiresray otnay isthay eparationpray; eyay eednay otnay avehay omecay
usthay arfay anday aggeddray ouryay aptaincay otay ethay ameshay ofay aay efeatday erelymay otay ovepray
ourselvesyay owardscay. Ohay! Ebay enmay, oray ebay oremay anthay enmay. Ebay eadystay otay ouryay
urposespay anday irmfay asay aay ockray. Isthay iceay isay otnay ademay ofay uchsay uffstay asay ouryay
eartshay aymay ebay; itay isay utablemay anday annotcay ithstandway ouyay ifay ouyay aysay atthay itay
allshay otnay. Oday otnay eturnray otay ouryay amiliesfay ithway ethay igmastay ofay isgraceday
arkedmay onay ouryay owsbray. Eturnray asay eroeshay owhay avehay oughtfay anday onqueredcay anday
owhay owknay otnay atwhay itay isay otay urntay eirthay acksbay onay ethay oefay.”

Ehay okespay isthay ithway aay oicevay osay odulatedmay otay ethay ifferentday eelingsfay expresseday
inay ishay eechspay, ithway anay eyeay osay ullfay ofay oftylay esignday anday eroismhay, atthay ancay
ouyay onderway atthay esethay enmay ereway ovedmay? Eythay ookedlay atay oneay anotheray anday ereway
unableay otay eplyray. Iay okespay; Iay oldtay emthay otay etireray anday onsidercay ofay atwhay adhay
eenbay aidsay, atthay Iay ouldway otnay eadlay emthay artherfay orthnay ifay eythay enuouslystray
esiredday ethay ontrarycay, utbay atthay Iay opedhay atthay, ithway eflectionray, eirthay ouragecay
ouldway eturnray.

Eythay etiredray anday Iay urnedtay owardstay myay iendfray, utbay ehay asway unksay inay anguorlay anday
almostay eprivedday ofay ifelay.

Owhay allay isthay illway erminatetay, Iay owknay otnay, utbay Iay adhay atherray ieday anthay
eturnray amefullyshay, myay urposepay unfulfilleday. Etyay Iay earfay uchsay illway ebay myay
atefay; ethay enmay, unsupporteday byay ideasay ofay oryglay anday onourhay, ancay evernay
illinglyway ontinuecay otay endureay eirthay esentpray ardshipshay.

Eptembersay 7thay.


Ethay ieday isay astcay; Iay avehay onsentedcay otay eturnray ifay eway areay otnay estroyedday.
Usthay areay myay opeshay astedblay byay owardicecay anday indecisionay; Iay omecay ackbay
ignorantay anday isappointedday. Itay equiresray oremay ilosophyphay anthay Iay ossesspay
otay earbay isthay injusticeay ithway atiencepay.

Eptembersay 12thay.


Itay isay astpay; Iay amay eturningray otay Englanday. Iay avehay ostlay myay opeshay ofay utilityay
anday oryglay; Iay avehay ostlay myay iendfray. Utbay Iay illway endeavouray otay etailday esethay
itterbay ircumstancescay otay ouyay, myay earday istersay; anday ilewhay Iay amay aftedway
owardstay Englanday anday owardstay ouyay, Iay illway otnay espondday.

Eptembersay 9thay, ethay iceay eganbay otay ovemay, anday oaringsray ikelay underthay ereway eardhay
atay aay istanceday asay ethay islandsay itsplay anday ackedcray inay everyay irectionday. Eway ereway
inay ethay ostmay imminentay erilpay, utbay asay eway ouldcay onlyay emainray assivepay, myay iefchay
attentionay asway occupieday byay myay unfortunateay uestgay osewhay illnessay increaseday inay
uchsay aay egreeday atthay ehay asway entirelyay onfinedcay otay ishay edbay. Ethay iceay ackedcray
ehindbay usay anday asway ivendray ithway orcefay owardstay ethay orthnay; aay eezebray angspray omfray
ethay estway, anday onay ethay 11thay ethay assagepay owardstay ethay outhsay ecamebay erfectlypay
eefray. Enwhay ethay ailorssay awsay isthay anday atthay eirthay eturnray otay eirthay ativenay
ountrycay asway apparentlyay assureday, aay outshay ofay umultuoustay oyjay okebray omfray emthay,
oudlay anday ong-continuedclay. Ankensteinfray, owhay asway ozingday, awokeay anday askeday ethay
ausecay ofay ethay umulttay. ey“thay outshay,” Iay aidsay, ecause“bay eythay
illway oonsay eturnray otay Englanday.”

o“day ouyay, enthay, eallyray eturnray?”

Alas“ay! Esyay; Iay annotcay ithstandway eirthay emandsday. Iay annotcay eadlay emthay
unwillinglyay otay angerday, anday Iay ustmay eturnray.”

o“day osay, ifay ouyay illway; utbay Iay illway otnay. Ouyay aymay ivegay upay ouryay urposepay, utbay
inemay isay assigneday otay emay byay Eavenhay, anday Iay areday otnay. Iay amay eakway, utbay
urelysay ethay iritsspay owhay assistay myay engeancevay illway endoway emay ithway
ufficientsay engthstray.” Ayingsay isthay, ehay endeavoureday otay ingspray omfray ethay
edbay, utbay ethay exertionay asway ootay eatgray orfay imhay; ehay ellfay ackbay anday aintedfay.

Itay asway onglay eforebay ehay asway estoredray, anday Iay oftenay oughtthay atthay ifelay asway
entirelyay extinctay. Atay engthlay ehay openeday ishay eyesay; ehay eathedbray ithway
ifficultyday anday asway unableay otay eakspay. Ethay urgeonsay avegay imhay aay omposingcay
aughtdray anday ordereday usay otay eavelay imhay undisturbeday. Inay ethay eantimemay ehay
oldtay emay atthay myay iendfray adhay ertainlycay otnay anymay ourshay otay ivelay.

Ishay entencesay asway onouncedpray, anday Iay ouldcay onlyay ievegray anday ebay atientpay. Iay atsay
byay ishay edbay, atchingway imhay; ishay eyesay ereway osedclay, anday Iay oughtthay ehay eptslay; utbay
esentlypray ehay alledcay otay emay inay aay eeblefay oicevay, anday iddingbay emay omecay earnay,
aidsay, Alas“ay! Ethay engthstray Iay eliedray onay isay onegay; Iay eelfay atthay Iay allshay
oonsay ieday, anday ehay, myay enemyay anday ersecutorpay, aymay illstay ebay inay eingbay. Inkthay
otnay, Altonway, atthay inay ethay astlay omentsmay ofay myay existenceay Iay eelfay atthay urningbay
atredhay anday ardentay esireday ofay evengeray Iay onceay expresseday; utbay Iay eelfay elfmysay
ustifiedjay inay esiringday ethay eathday ofay myay adversaryay. Uringday esethay astlay aysday Iay
avehay eenbay occupieday inay examiningay myay astpay onductcay; ornay oday Iay indfay itay amableblay.
Inay aay itfay ofay enthusiasticay adnessmay Iay eatedcray aay ationalray eaturecray anday asway
oundbay owardstay imhay otay assureay, asay arfay asay asway inay myay owerpay, ishay appinesshay anday
ell-beingclay. Isthay asway myay utyday, utbay erethay asway anotheray illstay aramountpay otay
atthay. Myay utiesday owardstay ethay eingsbay ofay myay ownay eciesspay adhay eatergray aimsclay otay
myay attentionay ecausebay eythay includeday aay eatergray oportionpray ofay appinesshay oray
iserymay. Urgeday byay isthay iewvay, Iay efusedray, anday Iay idday ightray inay efusingray, otay
eatecray aay ompanioncay orfay ethay irstfay eaturecray. Ehay owedshay unparalleleday alignitymay
anday elfishnesssay inay evilay; ehay estroyedday myay iendsfray; ehay evotedday otay estructionday
eingsbay owhay ossessedpay exquisiteay ensationssay, appinesshay, anday isdomway; ornay oday Iay
owknay erewhay isthay irstthay orfay engeancevay aymay enday. Iserablemay imselfhay atthay ehay aymay
enderray onay otheray etchedwray, ehay oughtay otay ieday. Ethay asktay ofay ishay estructionday asway
inemay, utbay Iay avehay ailedfay. Enwhay actuateday byay elfishsay anday iciousvay otivesmay, Iay
askeday ouyay otay undertakeay myay unfinisheday orkway, anday Iay enewray isthay equestray ownay,
enwhay Iay amay onlyay induceday byay easonray anday irtuevay.

et“yay Iay annotcay askay ouyay otay enounceray ouryay ountrycay anday iendsfray otay ulfilfay
isthay asktay; anday ownay atthay ouyay areay eturningray otay Englanday, ouyay illway avehay
ittlelay ancechay ofay eetingmay ithway imhay. Utbay ethay onsiderationcay ofay esethay
ointspay, anday ethay ellway alancingbay ofay atwhay ouyay aymay esteemay ouryay utiesday, Iay
eavelay otay ouyay; myay udgmentjay anday ideasay areay alreadyay isturbedday byay ethay earnay
approachay ofay eathday. Iay areday otnay askay ouyay otay oday atwhay Iay inkthay ightray, orfay Iay
aymay illstay ebay isledmay byay assionpay.

at“thay ehay ouldshay ivelay otay ebay anay instrumentay ofay ischiefmay isturbsday emay; inay
otheray espectsray, isthay ourhay, enwhay Iay omentarilymay expectay myay eleaseray, isay ethay
onlyay appyhay oneay ichwhay Iay avehay enjoyeday orfay everalsay earsyay. Ethay ormsfay ofay
ethay elovedbay eadday itflay eforebay emay, anday Iay astenhay otay eirthay armsay. Arewellfay,
Altonway! Eeksay appinesshay inay anquillitytray anday avoiday ambitionay, evenay ifay itay
ebay onlyay ethay apparentlyay innocentay oneay ofay istinguishingday ourselfyay inay
iencescay anday iscoveriesday. Etyay whyay oday Iay aysay isthay? Iay avehay elfmysay eenbay
astedblay inay esethay opeshay, etyay anotheray aymay ucceedsay.”

Ishay oicevay ecamebay ainterfay asay ehay okespay, anday atay engthlay, exhausteday byay ishay
effortay, ehay anksay intoay ilencesay. Aboutay alfhay anay ourhay afterwardsay ehay
attempteday againay otay eakspay utbay asway unableay; ehay essedpray myay andhay eeblyfay, anday
ishay eyesay osedclay orfay everay, ilewhay ethay irradiationay ofay aay entlegay ilesmay assedpay
awayay omfray ishay ipslay.

Argaretmay, atwhay ommentcay ancay Iay akemay onay ethay untimelyay extinctionay ofay isthay
oriousglay iritspay? Atwhay ancay Iay aysay atthay illway enableay ouyay otay understanday ethay
epthday ofay myay orrowsay? Allay atthay Iay ouldshay expressay ouldway ebay inadequateay anday
eeblefay. Myay earstay owflay; myay indmay isay overshadoweday byay aay oudclay ofay
isappointmentday. Utbay Iay ourneyjay owardstay Englanday, anday Iay aymay erethay indfay
onsolationcay.

Iay amay interrupteday. Atwhay oday esethay oundssay ortendpay? Itay isay idnightmay; ethay
eezebray owsblay airlyfay, anday ethay atchway onay eckday arcelyscay irstay. Againay erethay
isay aay oundsay asay ofay aay umanhay oicevay, utbay oarserhay; itay omescay omfray ethay abincay
erewhay ethay emainsray ofay Ankensteinfray illstay ielay. Iay ustmay ariseay anday examineay.
Oodgay ightnay, myay istersay.

Eatgray Odgay! atwhay aay enescay ashay ustjay akentay aceplay! Iay amay etyay izzyday ithway ethay
emembranceray ofay itay. Iay ardlyhay owknay etherwhay Iay allshay avehay ethay owerpay otay etailday
itay; etyay ethay aletay ichwhay Iay avehay ecordedray ouldway ebay incompleteay ithoutway isthay
inalfay anday onderfulway atastrophecay.

Iay entereday ethay abincay erewhay aylay ethay emainsray ofay myay ill-fatedclay anday admirableay
iendfray. Overay imhay unghay aay ormfay ichwhay Iay annotcay indfay ordsway otay
escribe—giganticday inay aturestay, etyay uncouthay anday istortedday inay itsay
oportionspray. Asay ehay unghay overay ethay offincay, ishay acefay asway oncealedcay byay onglay
ockslay ofay aggedray airhay; utbay oneay astvay andhay asway extendeday, inay olourcay anday
apparentay exturetay ikelay atthay ofay aay ummymay. Enwhay ehay eardhay ethay oundsay ofay myay
approachay, ehay easedcay otay utteray exclamationsay ofay iefgray anday orrorhay anday ungspray
owardstay ethay indowway. Evernay idday Iay eholdbay aay isionvay osay orriblehay asay ishay acefay, ofay
uchsay oathsomelay etyay appallingay ideousnesshay. Iay utshay myay eyesay involuntarilyay anday
endeavoureday otay ecollectray atwhay ereway myay utiesday ithway egardray otay isthay estroyerday.
Iay alledcay onay imhay otay aystay.

Ehay ausedpay, ookinglay onay emay ithway onderway, anday againay urningtay owardstay ethay
ifelesslay ormfay ofay ishay eatorcray, ehay eemedsay otay orgetfay myay esencepray, anday
everyay eaturefay anday esturegay eemedsay instigateday byay ethay ildestway ageray ofay omesay
uncontrollableay assionpay.

at“thay isay alsoay myay ictimvay!” ehay exclaimeday. In“ay ishay urdermay myay
imescray areay onsummatedcay; ethay iserablemay eriessay ofay myay eingbay isay oundway otay itsay
oseclay! Ohay, Ankensteinfray! Enerousgay anday elf-devotedclay eingbay! Atwhay oesday itay
availay atthay Iay ownay askay eethay otay ardonpay emay? Iay, owhay irretrievablyay estroyedday eethay
byay estroyingday allay outhay ovedstlay. Alasay! Ehay isay oldcay, ehay annotcay answeray
emay.”

Ishay oicevay eemedsay uffocatedsay, anday myay irstfay impulsesay, ichwhay adhay uggestedsay otay
emay ethay utyday ofay obeyingay ethay ingdyay equestray ofay myay iendfray inay estroyingday ishay
enemyay, ereway ownay uspendedsay byay aay ixturemay ofay uriositycay anday ompassioncay. Iay
approacheday isthay emendoustray eingbay; Iay aredday otnay againay aiseray myay eyesay otay ishay
acefay, erethay asway omethingsay osay aringscay anday unearthlyay inay ishay uglinessay. Iay
attempteday otay eakspay, utbay ethay ordsway iedday awayay onay myay ipslay. Ethay onstermay
ontinuedcay otay utteray ildway anday incoherentay elf-reproachesclay. Atay engthlay Iay
atheredgay esolutionray otay addressay imhay inay aay ausepay ofay ethay empesttay ofay ishay assionpay.

our“yay epentanceray,” Iay aidsay, is“ay ownay uperfluoussay. Ifay ouyay
adhay istenedlay otay ethay oicevay ofay onsciencecay anday eededhay ethay ingsstay ofay emorseray
eforebay ouyay adhay urgeday ouryay iabolicalday engeancevay otay isthay extremityay,
Ankensteinfray ouldway etyay avehay ivedlay.”

And“ay oday ouyay eamdray?” aidsay ethay ondæmay. o“day ouyay inkthay atthay Iay asway enthay
eadday otay agonyay anday emorseray? Ehay,” ehay ontinuedcay, ointingpay otay ethay orpsecay,
e“hay ufferedsay otnay inay ethay onsummationcay ofay ethay eedday. Ohay! Otnay ethay
en-thousandthclay ortionpay ofay ethay anguishay atthay asway inemay uringday ethay
ingeringlay etailday ofay itsay executionay. Aay ightfulfray elfishnesssay urriedhay emay
onay, ilewhay myay earthay asway oisonedpay ithway emorseray. Inkthay ouyay atthay ethay
oansgray ofay Ervalclay ereway usicmay otay myay earsay? Myay earthay asway ashionedfay otay ebay
usceptiblesay ofay ovelay anday athysympay, anday enwhay enchedwray byay iserymay otay icevay
anday atredhay, itay idday otnay endureay ethay iolencevay ofay ethay angechay ithoutway
orturetay uchsay asay ouyay annotcay evenay imagineay.

After“ay ethay urdermay ofay Ervalclay Iay eturnedray otay Itzerlandsway, eart-brokenclay
anday overcomeay. Iay itiedpay Ankensteinfray; myay itypay amounteday otay orrorhay; Iay
abhorreday elfmysay. Utbay enwhay Iay iscoveredday atthay ehay, ethay authoray atay onceay ofay
myay existenceay anday ofay itsay unspeakableay ormentstay, aredday otay opehay orfay
appinesshay, atthay ilewhay ehay accumulateday etchednesswray anday espairday uponay emay
ehay oughtsay ishay ownay enjoymentay inay eelingsfay anday assionspay omfray ethay
indulgenceay ofay ichwhay Iay asway orfay everay arredbay, enthay impotentay envyay anday itterbay
indignationay illedfay emay ithway anay insatiableay irstthay orfay engeancevay. Iay
ecollectedray myay eatthray anday esolvedray atthay itay ouldshay ebay accomplisheday. Iay
ewknay atthay Iay asway eparingpray orfay elfmysay aay eadlyday orturetay, utbay Iay asway ethay
aveslay, otnay ethay astermay, ofay anay impulseay ichwhay Iay etestedday etyay ouldcay otnay
isobeyday. Etyay enwhay eshay iedday! Aynay, enthay Iay asway otnay iserablemay. Iay adhay
astcay offay allay eelingfay, ubduedsay allay anguishay, otay iotray inay ethay excessay ofay myay
