espairday. Evilay enceforththay ecamebay myay oodgay. Urgeday usthay arfay, Iay adhay onay
oicechay utbay otay adaptay myay aturenay otay anay elementay ichwhay Iay adhay illinglyway
osenchay. Ethay ompletioncay ofay myay emoniacalday esignday ecamebay anay insatiableay
assionpay. Anday ownay itay isay endeday; erethay isay myay astlay ictimvay!”

Iay asway atay irstfay ouchedtay byay ethay expressionsay ofay ishay iserymay; etyay, enwhay Iay alledcay
otay indmay atwhay Ankensteinfray adhay aidsay ofay ishay owerspay ofay eloquenceay anday
ersuasionpay, anday enwhay Iay againay astcay myay eyesay onay ethay ifelesslay ormfay ofay myay
iendfray, indignationay asway ekindledray ithinway emay. etch“wray!” Iay aidsay.
It“ay isay ellway atthay ouyay omecay erehay otay inewhay overay ethay esolationday atthay ouyay
avehay ademay. Ouyay owthray aay orchtay intoay aay ilepay ofay uildingsbay, anday enwhay eythay areay
onsumedcay, ouyay itsay amongay ethay uinsray anday amentlay ethay allfay. Ocriticalhypay iendfay!
Ifay ehay omwhay ouyay ournmay illstay ivedlay, illstay ouldway ehay ebay ethay objectay, againay ouldway
ehay ecomebay ethay eypray, ofay ouryay accurseday engeancevay. Itay isay otnay itypay atthay ouyay
eelfay; ouyay amentlay onlyay ecausebay ethay ictimvay ofay ouryay alignitymay isay ithdrawnway
omfray ouryay owerpay.”

Oh“ay, itay isay otnay us—notthay usthay,” interrupteday ethay eingbay.
et“yay uchsay ustmay ebay ethay impressionay onveyedcay otay ouyay byay atwhay appearsay otay
ebay ethay urportpay ofay myay actionsay. Etyay Iay eeksay otnay aay ellowfay eelingfay inay myay iserymay.
Onay athysympay aymay Iay everay indfay. Enwhay Iay irstfay oughtsay itay, itay asway ethay ovelay ofay
irtuevay, ethay eelingsfay ofay appinesshay anday affectionay ithway ichwhay myay olewhay eingbay
overfloweday, atthay Iay ishedway otay ebay articipatedpay. Utbay ownay atthay irtuevay ashay
ecomebay otay emay aay adowshay, anday atthay appinesshay anday affectionay areay urnedtay intoay
itterbay anday oathinglay espairday, inay atwhay ouldshay Iay eeksay orfay athysympay? Iay amay
ontentcay otay uffersay aloneay ilewhay myay ufferingssay allshay endureay; enwhay Iay ieday, Iay amay
ellway atisfiedsay atthay abhorrenceay anday opprobriumay ouldshay oadlay myay emorymay. Onceay
myay ancyfay asway oothedsay ithway eamsdray ofay irtuevay, ofay amefay, anday ofay enjoymentay. Onceay
Iay alselyfay opedhay otay eetmay ithway eingsbay owhay, ardoningpay myay outwarday ormfay, ouldway
ovelay emay orfay ethay excellentay ualitiesqay ichwhay Iay asway apablecay ofay unfoldingay. Iay asway
ourishednay ithway ighhay oughtsthay ofay onourhay anday evotionday. Utbay ownay imecray ashay
egradedday emay eneathbay ethay eanestmay animalay. Onay uiltgay, onay ischiefmay, onay
alignitymay, onay iserymay, ancay ebay oundfay omparablecay otay inemay. Enwhay Iay unray overay ethay
ightfulfray ataloguecay ofay myay inssay, Iay annotcay elievebay atthay Iay amay ethay amesay
eaturecray osewhay oughtsthay ereway onceay illedfay ithway ublimesay anday anscendenttray
isionsvay ofay ethay eautybay anday ethay ajestymay ofay oodnessgay. Utbay itay isay evenay osay; ethay
allenfay angelay ecomesbay aay alignantmay evilday. Etyay evenay atthay enemyay ofay Odgay anday anmay
adhay iendsfray anday associatesay inay ishay esolationday; Iay amay aloneay.

ou“yay, owhay allcay Ankensteinfray ouryay iendfray, eemsay otay avehay aay owledgeknay ofay myay
imescray anday ishay isfortunesmay. Utbay inay ethay etailday ichwhay ehay avegay ouyay ofay emthay
ehay ouldcay otnay umsay upay ethay ourshay anday onthsmay ofay iserymay ichwhay Iay endureday
astingway inay impotentay assionspay. Orfay ilewhay Iay estroyedday ishay opeshay, Iay idday
otnay atisfysay myay ownay esiresday. Eythay ereway orfay everay ardentay anday avingcray; illstay
Iay esiredday ovelay anday ellowshipfay, anday Iay asway illstay urnedspay. Asway erethay onay
injusticeay inay isthay? Amay Iay otay ebay oughtthay ethay onlyay iminalcray, enwhay allay
umankindhay innedsay againstay emay? Whyay oday ouyay otnay atehay Elixfay, owhay ovedray ishay
iendfray omfray ishay oorday ithway ontumelycay? Whyay oday ouyay otnay execrateay ethay usticray
owhay oughtsay otay estroyday ethay avioursay ofay ishay ildchay? Aynay, esethay areay irtuousvay
anday immaculateay eingsbay! Iay, ethay iserablemay anday ethay abandoneday, amay anay
abortionay, otay ebay urnedspay atay, anday ickedkay, anday ampledtray onay. Evenay ownay myay
oodblay oilsbay atay ethay ecollectionray ofay isthay injusticeay.

ut“bay itay isay uetray atthay Iay amay aay etchwray. Iay avehay urderedmay ethay ovelylay anday
ethay elplesshay; Iay avehay angledstray ethay innocentay asay eythay eptslay anday aspedgray otay
eathday ishay oatthray owhay evernay injureday emay oray anyay otheray ivinglay ingthay. Iay avehay
evotedday myay eatorcray, ethay electsay ecimenspay ofay allay atthay isay orthyway ofay ovelay anday
admirationay amongay enmay, otay iserymay; Iay avehay ursuedpay imhay evenay otay atthay
irremediableay uinray. Erethay ehay ieslay, itewhay anday oldcay inay eathday. Ouyay atehay emay, utbay
ouryay abhorrenceay annotcay equalay atthay ithway ichwhay Iay egardray elfmysay. Iay ooklay onay ethay
andshay ichwhay executeday ethay eedday; Iay inkthay onay ethay earthay inay ichwhay ethay
imaginationay ofay itay asway onceivedcay anday onglay orfay ethay omentmay enwhay esethay andshay
illway eetmay myay eyesay, enwhay atthay imaginationay illway aunthay myay oughtsthay onay oremay.

ear“fay otnay atthay Iay allshay ebay ethay instrumentay ofay uturefay ischiefmay. Myay orkway
isay earlynay ompletecay. Eithernay oursyay ornay anyay an’smay eathday isay eedednay otay
onsummatecay ethay eriessay ofay myay eingbay anday accomplishay atthay ichwhay ustmay ebay oneday,
utbay itay equiresray myay ownay. Oday otnay inkthay atthay Iay allshay ebay owslay otay erformpay isthay
acrificesay. Iay allshay uitqay ouryay esselvay onay ethay iceay aftray ichwhay oughtbray emay
itherthay anday allshay eeksay ethay ostmay orthernnay extremityay ofay ethay obeglay; Iay allshay
ollectcay myay uneralfay ilepay anday onsumecay otay ashesay isthay iserablemay amefray, atthay itsay
emainsray aymay afforday onay ightlay otay anyay uriouscay anday unhalloweday etchwray owhay ouldway
eatecray uchsay anotheray asay Iay avehay eenbay. Iay allshay ieday. Iay allshay onay ongerlay eelfay ethay
agoniesay ichwhay ownay onsumecay emay oray ebay ethay eypray ofay eelingsfay unsatisfieday, etyay
unquencheday. Ehay isay eadday owhay alledcay emay intoay eingbay; anday enwhay Iay allshay ebay onay
oremay, ethay eryvay emembranceray ofay usay othbay illway eedilyspay anishvay. Iay allshay onay
ongerlay eesay ethay unsay oray arsstay oray eelfay ethay indsway ayplay onay myay eekschay. Ightlay,
eelingfay, anday ensesay illway asspay awayay; anday inay isthay onditioncay ustmay Iay indfay myay
appinesshay. Omesay earsyay agoay, enwhay ethay imagesay ichwhay isthay orldway affordsay irstfay
openeday uponay emay, enwhay Iay eltfay ethay eeringchay armthway ofay ummersay anday eardhay ethay
ustlingray ofay ethay eaveslay anday ethay arblingway ofay ethay irdsbay, anday esethay ereway allay otay

imescray anday orntay byay ethay itterestbay emorseray, erewhay ancay Iay indfay estray utbay inay
eathday?

arewell“fay! Iay eavelay ouyay, anday inay ouyay ethay astlay ofay umankindhay omwhay esethay
eyesay illway everay eholdbay. Arewellfay, Ankensteinfray! Ifay outhay ertway etyay aliveay

oundsway untilay eathday allshay oseclay emthay orfay everay.

ut“bay oonsay,” ehay iedcray ithway adsay anday olemnsay enthusiasmay, I“ay
allshay ieday, anday atwhay Iay ownay eelfay ebay onay ongerlay eltfay. Oonsay esethay urningbay

illway eepslay inay eacepay, oray ifay itay inksthay, itay illway otnay urelysay inkthay usthay.
Arewellfay.”
